
//   :TITLE: New Testament According to the Egyptian Greek Text. 
//    NTEG 1.00 (2005.October.27)
//   
//    NOTE: Best viewed in Wordpad(R) with View/Options set to No wrap. 
//   -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    Representing thw New Testament in the original Greek according to the Egyptian text, upon which the Sahidic was based.
//    This Greek text was based on the CCAT lemmatized version of the United Bible Societies text corrected by James Tauber.
//   -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//   :TITLE NOTES
//   -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    "Egyptian" means the Greek text type Aland calls Alexandrian/Egyptian and Metzger calls Proto-Alexandrian/Alexandrian.
//    The term "in the Original Greek" is often misunderstood to mean this represents the text as it was originally written.
//    It does not imply that. It means this is "a version" of the New Testament in the language the original was written in.
//   -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//   :TEXT NOTES
//   -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    Character representation in the Greek and Coptic texts.
//    (These characters are mapped in the UncialSS font, which 
//    is freely available on the www.sahidica.org website.)
//   ------------------------------------------------------------------
//    a alpha    i iota     r rho      S shai
//    b beta     k kappa    s sigma    F fai
//    g gamma    l lambda   t tau      H hori
//    d delta    m mu       u upsilon  J janjia
//    e epsilon  n nu       f phi      C chima
//    z zeta     x xi       c khi      T ti
//    h eta      o omicron  y psi      Q chi (Bo)*
//    q theta    p pi       w omega    X stauros *
//   ------------------------------------------------------------------
//    * Neither "chi" (Bohairic) nor "stauros" are used in the 
//      Sahidica text. V is reserved for final Greek sigma.
//   ------------------------------------------------------------------
//   
//    Note: "UBS" herein means The Greek New Testament of the United Bible Societies, fourth revised edition (1994).
//   
//    Sections and Paragraphs
//   
//    Following each book-ch-vs, there may appear encoding: where "=" is a section break, and "-" is a paragraph break.
//    These are aligned, but not identical, to those found in the UBS text where sections have headings.
//   
//    Purpose and Criteria
//   
//    The purpose is to provide a parallel Greek text for students and researchers who work with the Sahidic version.
//    At the same time fabricating a hypothetical version of the Greek to correspond to the Sahidic has been avoided.
//    To accomplish, this the CCAT lemmatized version of the UBS text corrected by James Tauber, was used as a basis.
//    That Greek text has been altered to correspond to the Sahidic only where there is support in the UBS apparatus.
//    This is a simplified text. The following marks are omitted: Accent, breathing, dieresis, subscript and elision.
//    Punctuation marks have been removed except for periods and Greek question marks (";") which have been retained.
//    This allows the student or researcher to compare differences between the Sahidic and the standard Greek texts. 
//    As a result this Greek text is encoded to be viewable with the Symbol font available in Microsoft Windows(R).
//   
//    To better serve the student or researcher, the following steps have been taken in modifying the Greek text.
//   
//    Brackets in the UBS/NA have been removed. Double brackets have been left. Commas have also been removed.
//    Single brackets mark where the Sahidic witnesses read differently than the standard Greek text.
//    Single brackets with hyphens within [--] indicates the Sahidic omits one or more words found in the Greek text.
//    Where single brackets with hyphens within stand alone by a verse number, the Sahidic omits the entire verse.
//    Double brackets with hyphens mark where the Greek text is not represented in the Sahidic witnesses.
//    Double brackets with hyphens within [[--]] indicates the Sahidic omits a major section found in the UBS Greek.
//   
//    Interpolations
//   
//    The shorter and longer endings of Mark appear in most Sahidic mss. Herein the longer is given first.
//    The pericope of the adultress (John 7:53 - 8:11) does not appear in any Sahidic mss. Herein it is omitted.
//   -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    NTAEG - New Testament According to the Egyptian Greek Text. Copyright (c)2005 by J. Warren Wells. All rights reserved.
//   -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//   Prepared with permission for use with BibleWorks by Jim Darlack.
//   August 2007 (http://bibleworks.oldinthenew.org)
//   The text has been encoded for use with the BibleWorks bwgrkl.

mat 1:1 biblos genesews ihsou xristou uiou dauid uiou abraam.
mat 1:2 abraam egennhsen ton isaak isaak de egennhsen ton iakwb iakwb de egennhsen ton ioudan kai tous adelfous autou
mat 1:3 ioudas de egennhsen ton fares kai ton zara ek ths qamar fares de egennhsen ton esrwm esrwm de egennhsen ton aram
mat 1:4 aram de egennhsen ton aminadab aminadab de egennhsen ton naasswn naasswn de egennhsen ton salmwn
mat 1:5 salmwn de egennhsen ton boes ek ths raxab boes de egennhsen ton iwbhd ek ths rouq iwbhd de egennhsen ton iessai
mat 1:6 iessai de egennhsen ton dauid ton basilea. dauid de egennhsen ton solomwna ek ths tou ouriou
mat 1:7 solomwn de egennhsen ton roboam roboam de egennhsen ton abia abia de egennhsen ton asaf
mat 1:8 asaf de egennhsen ton iwsafat iwsafat de egennhsen ton iwram iwram de egennhsen ton ozian
mat 1:9 ozias de egennhsen ton iwaqam iwaqam de egennhsen ton axaz axaz de egennhsen ton ezekian
mat 1:10 ezekias de egennhsen ton manassh manasshs de egennhsen ton amws amws de egennhsen ton iwsian
mat 1:11 iwsias de egennhsen ton iexonian kai tous adelfous autou epi ths metoikesias babulwnos.
mat 1:12 meta de thn metoikesian babulwnos iexonias egennhsen ton salaqihl salaqihl de egennhsen ton zorobabel
mat 1:13 zorobabel de egennhsen ton abioud abioud de egennhsen ton eliakim eliakim de egennhsen ton azwr
mat 1:14 azwr de egennhsen ton sadwk sadwk de egennhsen ton axim axim de egennhsen ton elioud
mat 1:15 elioud de egennhsen ton eleazar eleazar de egennhsen ton matqan matqan de egennhsen ton iakwb
mat 1:16 iakwb de egennhsen ton iwshf ton andra marias ec hs egennhqh ihsous o legomenos xristos.
mat 1:17 pasai oun ai geneai apo abraam ews dauid geneai dekatessares kai apo dauid ews ths metoikesias babulwnos geneai dekatessares kai apo ths metoikesias babulwnos ews tou xristou geneai dekatessares.
mat 1:18 tou de ihsou xristou h genesis outws hn. mnhsteuqeishs ths mhtros autou marias tw iwshf prin h sunelqein autous eureqh en gastri exousa ek pneumatos agiou.
mat 1:19 iwshf de o anhr auths dikaios wn kai mh qelwn authn deigmatisai eboulhqh laqra apolusai authn.
mat 1:20 tauta de autou enqumhqentos idou aggelos kuriou kat onar efanh autw legwn iwshf uios dauid mh fobhqhs paralabein mariam thn gunaika sou to gar en auth gennhqen ek pneumatos estin agiou
mat 1:21 tecetai de uion kai kaleseis to onoma autou ihsoun autos gar swsei ton laon autou apo twn amartiwn autwn.
mat 1:22 touto de olon gegonen ina plhrwqh to rhqen upo kuriou dia tou profhtou legontos
mat 1:23 idou h parqenos en gastri ecei kai tecetai uion kai kalesousin to onoma autou emmanouhl o estin meqermhneuomenon meq hmwn o qeos.
mat 1:24 egerqeis de o iwshf apo tou upnou epoihsen ws prosetacen autw o aggelos kuriou kai parelaben thn gunaika autou
mat 1:25 kai ouk eginwsken authn ews ou eteken uion kai ekalesen to onoma autou ihsoun.
mat 2:1 tou de ihsou gennhqentos en bhqleem ths ioudaias en hmerais hrwdou tou basilews idou magoi apo anatolwn paregenonto eis ierosoluma
mat 2:2 legontes pou estin o texqeis basileus twn ioudaiwn; eidomen gar autou ton astera en th anatolh kai hlqomen proskunhsai autw.
mat 2:3 akousas de o basileus hrwdhs etaraxqh kai pasa ierosoluma met autou
mat 2:4 kai sunagagwn pantas tous arxiereis kai grammateis tou laou epunqaneto par autwn pou o xristos gennatai.
mat 2:5 oi de eipan autw en bhqleem ths ioudaias outws gar gegraptai dia tou profhtou
mat 2:6 kai su bhqleem gh iouda oudamws elaxisth ei en tois hgemosin iouda ek sou gar eceleusetai hgoumenos ostis poimanei ton laon mou ton israhl.
mat 2:7 tote hrwdhs laqra kalesas tous magous hkribwsen par autwn ton xronon tou fainomenou asteros
mat 2:8 kai pemyas autous eis bhqleem eipen poreuqentes ecetasate akribws peri tou paidiou epan de eurhte apaggeilate moi opws kagw elqwn proskunhsw autw.
mat 2:9 oi de akousantes tou basilews eporeuqhsan kai idou o asthr on eidon en th anatolh prohgen autous ews elqwn estaqh epanw ou hn to paidion.
mat 2:10 idontes de ton astera exarhsan xaran megalhn sfodra.
mat 2:11 kai elqontes eis thn oikian eidon to paidion meta marias ths mhtros autou kai pesontes prosekunhsan autw kai anoicantes tous qhsaurous autwn proshnegkan autw dwra xruson kai libanon kai smurnan.
mat 2:12 kai xrhmatisqentes kat onar mh anakamyai pros hrwdhn di allhs odou anexwrhsan eis thn xwran autwn.
mat 2:13 anaxwrhsantwn de autwn idou aggelos kuriou fainetai kat onar tw iwshf legwn egerqeis paralabe to paidion kai thn mhtera autou kai feuge eis aigupton kai isqi ekei ews an eipw soi mellei gar hrwdhs zhtein to paidion tou apolesai auto.
mat 2:14 o de egerqeis parelaben to paidion kai thn mhtera autou nuktos kai anexwrhsen eis aigupton
mat 2:15 kai hn ekei ews ths teleuths hrwdou ina plhrwqh to rhqen upo kuriou dia tou profhtou legontos ec aiguptou ekalesa ton uion mou.
mat 2:16 tote hrwdhs idwn oti enepaixqh upo twn magwn equmwqh lian kai aposteilas aneilen pantas tous paidas tous en bhqleem kai en pasi tois oriois auths apo dietous kai katwterw kata ton xronon on hkribwsen para twn magwn.
mat 2:17 tote eplhrwqh to rhqen dia ieremiou tou profhtou legontos
mat 2:18 fwnh en rama hkousqh klauqmos kai odurmos polus raxhl klaiousa ta tekna auths kai ouk hqelen paraklhqhnai oti ouk eisin.
mat 2:19 teleuthsantos de tou hrwdou idou aggelos kuriou fainetai kat onar tw iwshf en aiguptw
mat 2:20 legwn egerqeis paralabe to paidion kai thn mhtera autou kai poreuou eis ghn israhl teqnhkasin gar oi zhtountes thn yuxhn tou paidiou.
mat 2:21 o de egerqeis parelaben to paidion kai thn mhtera autou kai eishlqen eis ghn israhl.
mat 2:22 akousas de oti arxelaos basileuei ths ioudaias anti tou patros autou hrwdou efobhqh ekei apelqein xrhmatisqeis de kat onar anexwrhsen eis ta merh ths galilaias
mat 2:23 kai elqwn katwkhsen eis polin legomenhn nazaret opws plhrwqh to rhqen dia twn profhtwn oti nazwraios klhqhsetai.
mat 3:1 en de tais hmerais ekeinais paraginetai iwannhs o baptisths khrusswn en th erhmw ths ioudaias
mat 3:2 kai legwn metanoeite hggiken gar h basileia twn ouranwn.
mat 3:3 outos gar estin o rhqeis dia hsaiou tou profhtou legontos fwnh bowntos en th erhmw etoimasate thn odon kuriou euqeias poieite tas tribous autou.
mat 3:4 autos de o iwannhs eixen to enduma autou apo trixwn kamhlou kai zwnhn dermatinhn peri thn osfun autou h de trofh hn autou akrides kai meli agrion.
mat 3:5 tote eceporeueto pros auton ierosoluma kai pasa h ioudaia kai pasa h perixwros tou iordanou
mat 3:6 kai ebaptizonto en tw iordanh potamw up autou ecomologoumenoi tas amartias autwn.
mat 3:7 idwn de pollous twn farisaiwn kai saddoukaiwn erxomenous epi to baptisma autou eipen autois gennhmata exidnwn tis upedeicen umin fugein apo ths melloushs orghs;
mat 3:8 poihsate oun karpon acion ths metanoias
mat 3:9 kai mh dochte legein en eautois patera exomen ton abraam legw gar umin oti dunatai o qeos ek twn liqwn toutwn egeirai tekna tw abraam.
mat 3:10 hdh de h acinh pros thn rizan twn dendrwn keitai pan oun dendron mh poioun karpon kalon ekkoptetai kai eis pur balletai.
mat 3:11 egw men umas baptizw en udati eis metanoian o de opisw mou erxomenos isxuroteros mou estin ou ouk eimi ikanos ta upodhmata bastasai autos umas baptisei en pneumati agiw kai puri
mat 3:12 ou to ptuon en th xeiri autou kai diakaqariei thn alwna autou kai sunacei ton siton autou eis thn apoqhkhn to de axuron katakausei puri asbestw.
mat 3:13 tote paraginetai o ihsous apo ths galilaias epi ton iordanhn pros ton iwannhn tou baptisqhnai up autou.
mat 3:14 o de iwannhs diekwluen auton legwn egw xreian exw upo sou baptisqhnai kai su erxh pros me;
mat 3:15 apokriqeis de o ihsous eipen pros auton afes arti outws gar prepon estin hmin plhrwsai pasan dikaiosunhn. tote afihsin auton.
mat 3:16 baptisqeis de o ihsous euqus anebh apo tou udatos kai idou hnewxqhsan [-] oi ouranoi kai eiden to pneuma tou qeou katabainon [-] ep auton
mat 3:17 kai idou fwnh ek twn ouranwn legousa outos estin o uios mou o agaphtos en w eudokhsa.
mat 4:1 tote o ihsous anhxqh eis thn erhmon upo tou pneumatos peirasqhnai upo tou diabolou.
mat 4:2 kai nhsteusas hmeras tesserakonta kai nuktas tesserakonta usteron epeinasen.
mat 4:3 kai proselqwn o peirazwn eipen autw ei uios ei tou qeou eipe ina oi liqoi outoi artoi genwntai.
mat 4:4 o de apokriqeis eipen gegraptai ouk ep artw monw zhsetai o anqrwpos all epi panti rhmati ekporeuomenw dia stomatos qeou.
mat 4:5 tote paralambanei auton o diabolos eis thn agian polin kai esthsen auton epi to pterugion tou ierou
mat 4:6 kai legei autw ei uios ei tou qeou bale seauton katw gegraptai gar oti tois aggelois autou enteleitai peri sou kai epi xeirwn arousin se mhpote proskoyhs pros liqon ton poda sou.
mat 4:7 efh autw o ihsous palin gegraptai ouk ekpeiraseis kurion ton qeon sou.
mat 4:8 palin paralambanei auton o diabolos eis oros uyhlon lian kai deiknusin autw pasas tas basileias tou kosmou kai thn docan autwn
mat 4:9 kai eipen autw tauta soi panta dwsw ean peswn proskunhshs moi.
mat 4:10 tote legei autw o ihsous upage satana gegraptai gar kurion ton qeon sou proskunhseis kai autw monw latreuseis.
mat 4:11 tote afihsin auton o diabolos kai idou aggeloi proshlqon kai dihkonoun autw.
mat 4:12 akousas de oti iwannhs paredoqh anexwrhsen eis thn galilaian.
mat 4:13 kai katalipwn thn nazara elqwn katwkhsen eis kafarnaoum thn paraqalassian en oriois zaboulwn kai nefqalim
mat 4:14 ina plhrwqh to rhqen dia hsaiou tou profhtou legontos
mat 4:15 gh zaboulwn kai gh nefqalim odon qalasshs peran tou iordanou galilaia twn eqnwn
mat 4:16 o laos o kaqhmenos en skotei fws eiden mega kai tois kaqhmenois en xwra kai skia qanatou fws aneteilen autois.
mat 4:17 apo tote hrcato o ihsous khrussein kai legein metanoeite hggiken gar h basileia twn ouranwn.
mat 4:18 peripatwn de para thn qalassan ths galilaias eiden duo adelfous simwna ton legomenon petron kai andrean ton adelfon autou ballontas amfiblhstron eis thn qalassan hsan gar alieis.
mat 4:19 kai legei autois deute opisw mou kai poihsw umas alieis anqrwpwn.
mat 4:20 oi de euqews afentes ta diktua hkolouqhsan autw.
mat 4:21 kai probas ekeiqen eiden allous duo adelfous iakwbon ton tou zebedaiou kai iwannhn ton adelfon autou en tw ploiw meta zebedaiou tou patros autwn katartizontas ta diktua autwn kai ekalesen autous.
mat 4:22 oi de euqews afentes to ploion kai ton patera autwn hkolouqhsan autw.
mat 4:23 kai perihgen en olh th galilaia didaskwn en tais sunagwgais autwn kai khrusswn to euaggelion ths basileias kai qerapeuwn pasan noson kai pasan malakian en tw law.
mat 4:24 kai aphlqen h akoh autou eis olhn thn surian kai proshnegkan autw pantas tous kakws exontas poikilais nosois kai basanois sunexomenous kai daimonizomenous kai selhniazomenous kai paralutikous kai eqerapeusen autous.
mat 4:25 kai hkolouqhsan autw oxloi polloi apo ths galilaias kai dekapolews kai ierosolumwn kai ioudaias kai peran tou iordanou.
mat 5:1 idwn de tous oxlous anebh eis to oros kai kaqisantos autou proshlqan autw oi maqhtai autou
mat 5:2 kai anoicas to stoma autou edidasken autous legwn
mat 5:3 makarioi oi ptwxoi tw pneumati oti autwn estin h basileia twn ouranwn.
mat 5:4 makarioi oi penqountes oti autoi paraklhqhsontai.
mat 5:5 makarioi oi praeis oti autoi klhronomhsousin thn ghn.
mat 5:6 makarioi oi peinwntes kai diywntes thn dikaiosunhn oti autoi xortasqhsontai.
mat 5:7 makarioi oi elehmones oti autoi elehqhsontai.
mat 5:8 makarioi oi kaqaroi th kardia oti autoi ton qeon oyontai.
mat 5:9 makarioi oi eirhnopoioi oti autoi uioi qeou klhqhsontai.
mat 5:10 makarioi oi dediwgmenoi eneken dikaiosunhs oti autwn estin h basileia twn ouranwn.
mat 5:11 makarioi este otan oneidiswsin umas kai diwcwsin kai eipwsin pan ponhron kaq umwn yeudomenoi eneken emou
mat 5:12 xairete kai agalliasqe oti o misqos umwn polus en tois ouranois outws gar ediwcan tous profhtas tous pro umwn.
mat 5:13 umeis este to alas ths ghs ean de to alas mwranqh en tini alisqhsetai; eis ouden isxuei eti ei mh blhqen ecw katapateisqai upo twn anqrwpwn.
mat 5:14 umeis este to fws tou kosmou. ou dunatai polis krubhnai epanw orous keimenh
mat 5:15 oude kaiousin luxnon kai tiqeasin auton upo ton modion all epi thn luxnian kai lampei pasin tois en th oikia.
mat 5:16 outws lamyatw to fws umwn emprosqen twn anqrwpwn opws idwsin umwn ta kala erga kai docaswsin ton patera umwn ton en tois ouranois.
mat 5:17 mh nomishte oti hlqon katalusai ton nomon h tous profhtas ouk hlqon katalusai alla plhrwsai.
mat 5:18 amhn gar legw umin ews an parelqh o ouranos kai h gh iwta en h mia keraia ou mh parelqh apo tou nomou ews an panta genhtai.
mat 5:19 os ean oun lush mian twn entolwn toutwn twn elaxistwn kai didach outws tous anqrwpous elaxistos klhqhsetai en th basileia twn ouranwn os d an poihsh kai didach outos megas klhqhsetai en th basileia twn ouranwn.
mat 5:20 legw gar umin oti ean mh perisseush umwn h dikaiosunh pleion twn grammatewn kai farisaiwn ou mh eiselqhte eis thn basileian twn ouranwn.
mat 5:21 hkousate oti erreqh tois arxaiois ou foneuseis os d an foneush enoxos estai th krisei.
mat 5:22 egw de legw umin oti pas o orgizomenos tw adelfw autou [eikh] enoxos estai th krisei os d an eiph tw adelfw autou raka enoxos estai tw sunedriw os d an eiph mwre enoxos estai eis thn geennan tou puros.
mat 5:23 ean oun prosferhs to dwron sou epi to qusiasthrion kakei mnhsqhs oti o adelfos sou exei ti kata sou
mat 5:24 afes ekei to dwron sou emprosqen tou qusiasthriou kai upage prwton diallaghqi tw adelfw sou kai tote elqwn prosfere to dwron sou.
mat 5:25 isqi eunown tw antidikw sou taxu ews otou ei met autou en th odw mhpote se paradw o antidikos tw krith kai o kriths tw uphreth kai eis fulakhn blhqhsh
mat 5:26 amhn legw soi ou mh ecelqhs ekeiqen ews an apodws ton esxaton kodranthn.
mat 5:27 hkousate oti erreqh ou moixeuseis.
mat 5:28 egw de legw umin oti pas o blepwn gunaika pros to epiqumhsai authn hdh emoixeusen authn en th kardia autou.
mat 5:29 ei de o ofqalmos sou o decios skandalizei se ecele auton kai bale apo sou sumferei gar soi ina apolhtai en twn melwn sou kai mh olon to swma sou blhqh eis geennan.
mat 5:30 kai ei h decia sou xeir skandalizei se ekkoyon authn kai bale apo sou sumferei gar soi ina apolhtai en twn melwn sou kai mh olon to swma sou eis geennan apelqh.
mat 5:31 erreqh de os an apolush thn gunaika autou dotw auth apostasion.
mat 5:32 egw de legw umin oti pas o apoluwn thn gunaika autou parektos logou porneias poiei authn moixeuqhnai kai [os apolelumenhn gamhsas] moixatai.
mat 5:33 palin hkousate oti erreqh tois arxaiois ouk epiorkhseis apodwseis de tw kuriw tous orkous sou.
mat 5:34 egw de legw umin mh omosai olws mhte en tw ouranw oti qronos estin tou qeou
mat 5:35 mhte en th gh oti upopodion estin twn podwn autou mhte eis ierosoluma oti polis estin tou megalou basilews
mat 5:36 mhte en th kefalh sou omoshs oti ou dunasai mian trixa leukhn poihsai h melainan.
mat 5:37 estw de o logos umwn nai nai ou ou to de perisson toutwn ek tou ponhrou estin.
mat 5:38 hkousate oti erreqh ofqalmon anti ofqalmou kai odonta anti odontos.
mat 5:39 egw de legw umin mh antisthnai tw ponhrw all ostis se rapizei eis thn decian siagona sou streyon autw kai thn allhn
mat 5:40 kai tw qelonti soi kriqhnai kai ton xitwna sou labein afes autw kai to imation
mat 5:41 kai ostis se aggareusei milion en upage met autou duo.
mat 5:42 tw aitounti se dos kai ton qelonta apo sou danisasqai mh apostrafhs.
mat 5:43 hkousate oti erreqh agaphseis ton plhsion sou kai mishseis ton exqron sou.
mat 5:44 egw de legw umin agapate tous exqrous umwn kai proseuxesqe uper twn diwkontwn umas
mat 5:45 opws genhsqe uioi tou patros umwn tou en ouranois oti ton hlion autou anatellei epi ponhrous kai agaqous kai brexei epi dikaious kai adikous.
mat 5:46 ean gar agaphshte tous agapwntas umas tina misqon exete; ouxi kai oi telwnai to auto poiousin;
mat 5:47 kai ean aspashsqe tous adelfous umwn monon ti perisson poieite; ouxi kai oi eqnikoi to auto poiousin;
mat 5:48 esesqe oun umeis teleioi ws o pathr umwn o ouranios teleios estin.
mat 6:1 prosexete de thn dikaiosunhn umwn mh poiein emprosqen twn anqrwpwn pros to qeaqhnai autois ei de mh ge misqon ouk exete para tw patri umwn tw en tois ouranois.
mat 6:2 otan oun poihs elehmosunhn mh salpishs emprosqen sou wsper oi upokritai poiousin en tais sunagwgais kai en tais rumais opws docasqwsin upo twn anqrwpwn amhn legw umin apexousin ton misqon autwn.
mat 6:3 sou de poiountos elehmosunhn mh gnwtw h aristera sou ti poiei h decia sou
mat 6:4 opws h sou h elehmosunh en tw kruptw kai o pathr sou o blepwn en tw kruptw apodwsei soi.
mat 6:5 kai otan proseuxhsqe ouk esesqe ws oi upokritai oti filousin en tais sunagwgais kai en tais gwniais twn plateiwn estwtes proseuxesqai opws fanwsin tois anqrwpois amhn legw umin apexousin ton misqon autwn.
mat 6:6 su de otan proseuxh eiselqe eis to tameion sou kai kleisas thn quran sou proseucai tw patri sou tw en tw kruptw kai o pathr sou o blepwn en tw kruptw apodwsei soi.
mat 6:7 proseuxomenoi de mh battaloghshte wsper oi eqnikoi dokousin gar oti en th polulogia autwn eisakousqhsontai.
mat 6:8 mh oun omoiwqhte autois oiden gar [o qeos] o pathr umwn wn xreian exete pro tou umas aithsai auton.
mat 6:9 outws oun proseuxesqe umeis pater hmwn o en tois ouranois agiasqhtw to onoma sou
mat 6:10 elqetw h basileia sou genhqhtw to qelhma sou ws en ouranw kai epi ghs.
mat 6:11 ton arton hmwn ton epiousion dos hmin shmeron
mat 6:12 kai afes hmin ta ofeilhmata hmwn ws kai hmeis afhkamen tois ofeiletais hmwn
mat 6:13 kai mh eisenegkhs hmas eis peirasmon alla rusai hmas apo tou ponhrou.
mat 6:14 ean gar afhte tois anqrwpois [ta paraptwmata autwn] ta paraptwmata autwn afhsei kai umin o pathr umwn o ouranios
mat 6:15 ean de mh afhte tois anqrwpois oude o pathr umwn afhsei ta paraptwmata umwn.
mat 6:16 otan de nhsteuhte mh ginesqe ws oi upokritai skuqrwpoi afanizousin gar ta proswpa autwn opws fanwsin tois anqrwpois nhsteuontes amhn legw umin apexousin ton misqon autwn.
mat 6:17 su de nhsteuwn aleiyai sou thn kefalhn kai to proswpon sou niyai
mat 6:18 opws mh fanhs tois anqrwpois nhsteuwn alla tw patri sou tw en tw krufaiw kai o pathr sou o blepwn en tw krufaiw apodwsei soi.
mat 6:19 mh qhsaurizete umin qhsaurous epi ths ghs opou shs kai brwsis afanizei kai opou kleptai diorussousin kai kleptousin
mat 6:20 qhsaurizete de umin qhsaurous en ouranw opou oute shs oute brwsis afanizei kai opou kleptai ou diorussousin oude kleptousin
mat 6:21 opou gar estin o qhsauros sou ekei estai kai h kardia sou.
mat 6:22 o luxnos tou swmatos estin o ofqalmos. ean oun h o ofqalmos sou aplous olon to swma sou fwteinon estai
mat 6:23 ean de o ofqalmos sou ponhros h olon to swma sou skoteinon estai. ei oun to fws to en soi skotos estin to skotos poson.
mat 6:24 oudeis dunatai dusi kuriois douleuein h gar ton ena mishsei kai ton eteron agaphsei h enos anqecetai kai tou eterou katafronhsei ou dunasqe qew douleuein kai mamwna.
mat 6:25 dia touto legw umin mh merimnate th yuxh umwn ti faghte h ti pihte mhde tw swmati umwn ti endushsqe ouxi h yuxh pleion estin ths trofhs kai to swma tou endumatos;
mat 6:26 embleyate eis ta peteina tou ouranou oti ou speirousin oude qerizousin oude sunagousin eis apoqhkas kai o pathr umwn o ouranios trefei auta oux umeis mallon diaferete autwn;
mat 6:27 tis de ec umwn merimnwn dunatai prosqeinai epi thn hlikian autou phxun ena;
mat 6:28 kai peri endumatos ti merimnate; katamaqete ta krina tou agrou pws aucanousin ou kopiwsin oude nhqousin
mat 6:29 legw de umin oti oude solomwn en pash th doch autou periebaleto ws en toutwn.
mat 6:30 ei de ton xorton tou agrou shmeron onta kai aurion eis klibanon ballomenon o qeos outws amfiennusin ou pollw mallon umas oligopistoi;
mat 6:31 mh oun merimnhshte legontes ti fagwmen; h ti piwmen; h ti peribalwmeqa;
mat 6:32 panta gar tauta ta eqnh epizhtousin oiden gar o pathr umwn o ouranios oti xrhzete toutwn apantwn.
mat 6:33 zhteite de prwton thn basileian tou [autou] kai thn dikaiosunhn autou kai tauta panta prosteqhsetai umin.
mat 6:34 mh oun merimnhshte eis thn aurion h gar aurion merimnhsei eauths arketon th hmera h kakia auths.
mat 7:1 mh krinete ina mh kriqhte
mat 7:2 en w gar krimati krinete kriqhsesqe kai en w metrw metreite metrhqhsetai umin.
mat 7:3 ti de blepeis to karfos to en tw ofqalmw tou adelfou sou thn de en tw sw ofqalmw dokon ou katanoeis;
mat 7:4 h pws ereis tw adelfw sou afes ekbalw to karfos ek tou ofqalmou sou kai idou h dokos en tw ofqalmw sou;
mat 7:5 upokrita ekbale prwton ek tou ofqalmou sou thn dokon kai tote diableyeis ekbalein to karfos ek tou ofqalmou tou adelfou sou.
mat 7:6 mh dwte to agion tois kusin mhde balhte tous margaritas umwn emprosqen twn xoirwn mhpote katapathsousin autous en tois posin autwn kai strafentes rhcwsin umas.
mat 7:7 aiteite kai doqhsetai umin zhteite kai eurhsete krouete kai anoighsetai umin.
mat 7:8 pas gar o aitwn lambanei kai o zhtwn euriskei kai tw krouonti anoighsetai.
mat 7:9 h tis estin ec umwn anqrwpos on aithsei o uios autou arton mh liqon epidwsei autw;
mat 7:10 h kai ixqun aithsei mh ofin epidwsei autw;
mat 7:11 ei oun umeis ponhroi ontes oidate domata agaqa didonai tois teknois umwn posw mallon o pathr umwn o en tois ouranois dwsei agaqa tois aitousin auton.
mat 7:12 panta oun osa ean qelhte ina poiwsin umin oi anqrwpoi outws kai umeis poieite autois outos gar estin o nomos kai oi profhtai.
mat 7:13 eiselqate dia ths stenhs pulhs oti plateia h pulh kai euruxwros h odos h apagousa eis thn apwleian kai polloi eisin oi eiserxomenoi di auths
mat 7:14 [oti] stenh h pulh kai teqlimmenh h odos h apagousa eis thn zwhn kai oligoi eisin oi euriskontes authn.
mat 7:15 prosexete apo twn yeudoprofhtwn oitines erxontai pros umas en endumasin probatwn eswqen de eisin lukoi arpages.
mat 7:16 apo twn karpwn autwn epignwsesqe autous mhti sullegousin apo akanqwn stafulas h apo tribolwn suka;
mat 7:17 outws pan dendron agaqon karpous kalous poiei to de sapron dendron karpous ponhrous poiei
mat 7:18 ou dunatai dendron agaqon karpous ponhrous poiein oude dendron sapron karpous kalous poiein.
mat 7:19 pan dendron mh poioun karpon kalon ekkoptetai kai eis pur balletai.
mat 7:20 ara ge apo twn karpwn autwn epignwsesqe autous.
mat 7:21 ou pas o legwn moi kurie kurie eiseleusetai eis thn basileian twn ouranwn all o poiwn to qelhma tou patros mou tou en tois ouranois.
mat 7:22 polloi erousin moi en ekeinh th hmera kurie kurie ou tw sw onomati eprofhteusamen kai tw sw onomati daimonia ecebalomen kai tw sw onomati dunameis pollas epoihsamen;
mat 7:23 kai tote omologhsw autois oti oudepote egnwn umas apoxwreite ap emou oi ergazomenoi thn anomian.
mat 7:24 pas oun ostis akouei mou tous logous toutous kai poiei autous omoiwqhsetai andri fronimw ostis wkodomhsen autou thn oikian epi thn petran.
mat 7:25 kai katebh h broxh kai hlqon oi potamoi kai epneusan oi anemoi kai prosepesan th oikia ekeinh kai ouk epesen teqemeliwto gar epi thn petran.
mat 7:26 kai pas o akouwn mou tous logous toutous kai mh poiwn autous omoiwqhsetai andri mwrw ostis wkodomhsen autou thn oikian epi thn ammon.
mat 7:27 kai katebh h broxh kai hlqon oi potamoi kai epneusan oi anemoi kai prosekoyan th oikia ekeinh kai epesen kai hn h ptwsis auths megalh.
mat 7:28 kai egeneto ote etelesen o ihsous tous logous toutous eceplhssonto oi oxloi epi th didaxh autou
mat 7:29 hn gar didaskwn autous ws ecousian exwn kai oux ws oi grammateis autwn.
mat 8:1 katabantos de autou apo tou orous hkolouqhsan autw oxloi polloi.
mat 8:2 kai idou lepros proselqwn prosekunei autw legwn kurie ean qelhs dunasai me kaqarisai.
mat 8:3 kai ekteinas thn xeira hyato autou legwn qelw kaqarisqhti kai euqews ekaqarisqh autou h lepra.
mat 8:4 kai legei autw o ihsous ora mhdeni eiphs alla upage seauton deicon tw ierei kai prosenegkon to dwron o prosetacen mwushs eis marturion autois.
mat 8:5 eiselqontos de autou eis kafarnaoum proshlqen autw ekatontarxos parakalwn auton
mat 8:6 kai legwn kurie o pais mou beblhtai en th oikia paralutikos deinws basanizomenos.
mat 8:7 kai legei autw egw elqwn qerapeusw auton.
mat 8:8 kai apokriqeis o ekatontarxos efh kurie ouk eimi ikanos ina mou upo thn steghn eiselqhs alla monon eipe logw kai iaqhsetai o pais mou.
mat 8:9 kai gar egw anqrwpos eimi upo ecousian exwn up emauton stratiwtas kai legw toutw poreuqhti kai poreuetai kai allw erxou kai erxetai kai tw doulw mou poihson touto kai poiei.
mat 8:10 akousas de o ihsous eqaumasen kai eipen tois akolouqousin amhn legw umin par oudeni tosauthn pistin en tw israhl euron.
mat 8:11 legw de umin oti polloi apo anatolwn kai dusmwn hcousin kai anakliqhsontai meta abraam kai isaak kai iakwb en th basileia twn ouranwn
mat 8:12 oi de uioi ths basileias ekblhqhsontai eis to skotos to ecwteron ekei estai o klauqmos kai o brugmos twn odontwn.
mat 8:13 kai eipen o ihsous tw ekatontarxh upage ws episteusas genhqhtw soi. kai iaqh o pais autou en th wra ekeinh.
mat 8:14 kai elqwn o ihsous eis thn oikian petrou eiden thn penqeran autou beblhmenhn kai puressousan
mat 8:15 kai hyato ths xeiros auths kai afhken authn o puretos kai hgerqh kai dihkonei autw.
mat 8:16 oyias de genomenhs proshnegkan autw daimonizomenous pollous kai ecebalen ta pneumata logw kai pantas tous kakws exontas eqerapeusen
mat 8:17 opws plhrwqh to rhqen dia hsaiou tou profhtou legontos autos tas asqeneias hmwn elaben kai tas nosous ebastasen.
mat 8:18 idwn de o ihsous oxlon peri auton ekeleusen apelqein eis to peran.
mat 8:19 kai proselqwn eis grammateus eipen autw didaskale akolouqhsw soi opou ean aperxh.
mat 8:20 kai legei autw o ihsous ai alwpekes fwleous exousin kai ta peteina tou ouranou kataskhnwseis o de uios tou anqrwpou ouk exei pou thn kefalhn klinh.
mat 8:21 eteros de twn maqhtwn [-] eipen autw kurie epitreyon moi prwton apelqein kai qayai ton patera mou.
mat 8:22 o de ihsous legei autw akolouqei moi kai afes tous nekrous qayai tous eautwn nekrous.
mat 8:23 kai embanti autw eis to ploion hkolouqhsan autw oi maqhtai autou.
mat 8:24 kai idou seismos megas egeneto en th qalassh wste to ploion kaluptesqai upo twn kumatwn autos de ekaqeuden.
mat 8:25 kai proselqontes hgeiran auton legontes kurie swson [hmas] apollumeqa.
mat 8:26 kai legei autois ti deiloi este oligopistoi; tote egerqeis epetimhsen tois anemois kai th qalassh kai egeneto galhnh megalh.
mat 8:27 oi de anqrwpoi eqaumasan legontes potapos estin outos oti kai oi anemoi kai h qalassa autw upakouousin;
mat 8:28 kai elqontos autou eis to peran eis thn xwran twn [gerashnwn] uphnthsan autw duo daimonizomenoi ek twn mnhmeiwn ecerxomenoi xalepoi lian wste mh isxuein tina parelqein dia ths odou ekeinhs.
mat 8:29 kai idou ekracan legontes ti hmin kai soi uie tou qeou; hlqes wde pro kairou basanisai hmas;
mat 8:30 hn de makran ap autwn agelh xoirwn pollwn boskomenh.
mat 8:31 oi de daimones parekaloun auton legontes ei ekballeis hmas aposteilon hmas eis thn agelhn twn xoirwn.
mat 8:32 kai eipen autois upagete. oi de ecelqontes aphlqon eis tous xoirous kai idou wrmhsen pasa h agelh kata tou krhmnou eis thn qalassan kai apeqanon en tois udasin.
mat 8:33 oi de boskontes efugon kai apelqontes eis thn polin aphggeilan panta kai ta twn daimonizomenwn.
mat 8:34 kai idou pasa h polis echlqen eis upanthsin tw ihsou kai idontes auton parekalesan opws metabh apo twn oriwn autwn.
mat 9:1 kai embas eis ploion dieperasen kai hlqen eis thn idian polin.
mat 9:2 kai idou proseferon autw paralutikon epi klinhs beblhmenon. kai idwn o ihsous thn pistin autwn eipen tw paralutikw qarsei teknon afientai sou ai amartiai.
mat 9:3 kai idou tines twn grammatewn eipan en eautois outos blasfhmei.
mat 9:4 [eidws] o ihsous tas enqumhseis autwn eipen inati enqumeisqe ponhra en tais kardiais umwn;
mat 9:5 ti gar estin eukopwteron eipein afientai sou ai amartiai h eipein egeire kai peripatei;
mat 9:6 ina de eidhte oti ecousian exei o uios tou anqrwpou epi ths ghs afienai amartias tote legei tw paralutikw egerqeis aron sou thn klinhn kai upage eis ton oikon sou.
mat 9:7 kai egerqeis aphlqen eis ton oikon autou.
mat 9:8 idontes de oi oxloi efobhqhsan kai edocasan ton qeon ton donta ecousian toiauthn tois anqrwpois.
mat 9:9 kai paragwn o ihsous ekeiqen eiden anqrwpon kaqhmenon epi to telwnion maqqaion legomenon kai legei autw akolouqei moi. kai anastas hkolouqhsen autw.
mat 9:10 kai egeneto autou anakeimenou en th oikia kai idou polloi telwnai kai amartwloi elqontes sunanekeinto tw ihsou kai tois maqhtais autou.
mat 9:11 kai idontes oi farisaioi elegon tois maqhtais autou dia ti meta twn telwnwn kai amartwlwn esqiei o didaskalos umwn;
mat 9:12 o de akousas eipen ou xreian exousin oi isxuontes iatrou all oi kakws exontes.
mat 9:13 poreuqentes de maqete ti estin eleos qelw kai ou qusian ou gar hlqon kalesai dikaious alla amartwlous.
mat 9:14 tote proserxontai autw oi maqhtai iwannou legontes dia ti hmeis kai oi farisaioi nhsteuomen [-] oi de maqhtai sou ou nhsteuousin;
mat 9:15 kai eipen autois o ihsous mh dunantai oi uioi tou numfwnos penqein ef oson met autwn estin o numfios; eleusontai de hmerai otan aparqh ap autwn o numfios kai tote nhsteusousin.
mat 9:16 oudeis de epiballei epiblhma rakous agnafou epi imatiw palaiw airei gar to plhrwma autou apo tou imatiou kai xeiron sxisma ginetai.
mat 9:17 oude ballousin oinon neon eis askous palaious ei de mh ge rhgnuntai oi askoi kai o oinos ekxeitai kai oi askoi apolluntai alla ballousin oinon neon eis askous kainous kai amfoteroi sunthrountai.
mat 9:18 tauta autou lalountos autois idou arxwn eis elqwn prosekunei autw legwn oti h qugathr mou arti eteleuthsen alla elqwn epiqes thn xeira sou ep authn kai zhsetai.
mat 9:19 kai egerqeis o ihsous hkolouqhsen autw kai oi maqhtai autou.
mat 9:20 kai idou gunh aimorroousa dwdeka eth proselqousa opisqen hyato tou kraspedou tou imatiou autou
mat 9:21 elegen gar en eauth ean monon aywmai tou imatiou autou swqhsomai.
mat 9:22 o de ihsous strafeis kai idwn authn eipen qarsei qugater h pistis sou seswken se. kai eswqh h gunh apo ths wras ekeinhs.
mat 9:23 kai elqwn o ihsous eis thn oikian tou arxontos kai idwn tous aulhtas kai ton oxlon qoruboumenon
mat 9:24 elegen anaxwreite ou gar apeqanen to korasion alla kaqeudei. kai kategelwn autou.
mat 9:25 ote de eceblhqh o oxlos eiselqwn ekrathsen ths xeiros auths kai hgerqh to korasion.
mat 9:26 kai echlqen h fhmh auth eis olhn thn ghn ekeinhn.
mat 9:27 kai paragonti ekeiqen tw ihsou hkolouqhsan autw duo tufloi krazontes kai legontes elehson hmas uios dauid.
mat 9:28 elqonti de eis thn oikian proshlqon autw oi tufloi kai legei autois o ihsous pisteuete oti dunamai touto poihsai; legousin autw nai kurie.
mat 9:29 tote hyato twn ofqalmwn autwn legwn kata thn pistin umwn genhqhtw umin.
mat 9:30 kai hnewxqhsan autwn oi ofqalmoi. kai enebrimhqh autois o ihsous legwn orate mhdeis ginwsketw.
mat 9:31 oi de ecelqontes diefhmisan auton en olh th gh ekeinh.
mat 9:32 autwn de ecerxomenwn idou proshnegkan autw anqrwpon kwfon daimonizomenon
mat 9:33 kai ekblhqentos tou daimoniou elalhsen o kwfos. kai eqaumasan oi oxloi legontes oudepote efanh outws en tw israhl.
mat 9:34 oi de farisaioi elegon en tw arxonti twn daimoniwn ekballei ta daimonia.
mat 9:35 kai perihgen o ihsous tas poleis pasas kai tas kwmas didaskwn en tais sunagwgais autwn kai khrusswn to euaggelion ths basileias kai qerapeuwn pasan noson kai pasan malakian.
mat 9:36 idwn de tous oxlous esplagxnisqh peri autwn oti hsan eskulmenoi kai errimmenoi wsei probata mh exonta poimena.
mat 9:37 tote legei tois maqhtais autou o men qerismos polus oi de ergatai oligoi
mat 9:38 dehqhte oun tou kuriou tou qerismou opws ekbalh ergatas eis ton qerismon autou.
mat 10:1 kai proskalesamenos tous dwdeka maqhtas autou edwken autois ecousian pneumatwn akaqartwn wste ekballein auta kai qerapeuein pasan noson kai pasan malakian.
mat 10:2 twn de dwdeka apostolwn ta onomata estin tauta prwtos simwn o legomenos petros kai andreas o adelfos autou kai iakwbos o tou zebedaiou kai iwannhs o adelfos autou
mat 10:3 filippos kai barqolomaios qwmas kai maqqaios o telwnhs iakwbos o tou alfaiou kai qaddaios
mat 10:4 simwn o kananaios kai ioudas o iskariwths o kai paradous auton.
mat 10:5 toutous tous dwdeka apesteilen o ihsous paraggeilas autois legwn eis odon eqnwn mh apelqhte kai eis polin samaritwn mh eiselqhte
mat 10:6 poreuesqe de mallon pros ta probata ta apolwlota oikou israhl.
mat 10:7 poreuomenoi de khrussete legontes oti hggiken h basileia twn ouranwn.
mat 10:8 asqenountas qerapeuete nekrous egeirete leprous kaqarizete daimonia ekballete dwrean elabete dwrean dote.
mat 10:9 mh kthshsqe xruson mhde arguron mhde xalkon eis tas zwnas umwn
mat 10:10 mh phran eis odon mhde duo xitwnas mhde upodhmata mhde rabdon acios gar o ergaths ths trofhs autou.
mat 10:11 eis hn d an polin h kwmhn eiselqhte ecetasate tis en auth acios estin kakei meinate ews an ecelqhte.
mat 10:12 eiserxomenoi de eis thn oikian aspasasqe authn
mat 10:13 kai ean men h h oikia acia elqatw h eirhnh umwn ep authn ean de mh h acia h eirhnh umwn pros umas epistrafhtw.
mat 10:14 kai os an mh dechtai umas mhde akoush tous logous umwn ecerxomenoi ecw ths oikias h ths polews ekeinhs ektinacate ton koniorton twn podwn umwn.
mat 10:15 amhn legw umin anektoteron estai gh sodomwn kai gomorrwn en hmera krisews h th polei ekeinh.
mat 10:16 idou egw apostellw umas ws probata en mesw lukwn ginesqe oun fronimoi ws oi ofeis kai akeraioi ws ai peristerai.
mat 10:17 prosexete de apo twn anqrwpwn paradwsousin gar umas eis sunedria kai en tais sunagwgais autwn mastigwsousin umas
mat 10:18 kai epi hgemonas de kai basileis axqhsesqe eneken emou eis marturion autois kai tois eqnesin.
mat 10:19 otan de paradwsin umas mh merimnhshte pws h ti lalhshte doqhsetai gar umin en ekeinh th wra ti lalhshte
mat 10:20 ou gar umeis este oi lalountes alla to pneuma tou patros umwn to laloun en umin.
mat 10:21 paradwsei de adelfos adelfon eis qanaton kai pathr teknon kai epanasthsontai tekna epi goneis kai qanatwsousin autous.
mat 10:22 kai esesqe misoumenoi upo pantwn dia to onoma mou o de upomeinas eis telos outos swqhsetai.
mat 10:23 otan de diwkwsin umas en th polei tauth feugete eis thn [allhn] amhn gar legw umin ou mh teleshte tas poleis tou israhl ews an elqh o uios tou anqrwpou.
mat 10:24 ouk estin maqhths uper ton didaskalon oude doulos uper ton kurion autou.
mat 10:25 arketon tw maqhth ina genhtai ws o didaskalos autou kai o doulos ws o kurios autou. ei ton oikodespothn beelzeboul epekalesan posw mallon tous oikiakous autou.
mat 10:26 mh oun fobhqhte autous ouden gar estin kekalummenon o ouk apokalufqhsetai kai krupton o ou gnwsqhsetai.
mat 10:27 o legw umin en th skotia eipate en tw fwti kai o eis to ous akouete khrucate epi twn dwmatwn.
mat 10:28 kai mh fobeisqe apo twn apoktennontwn to swma thn de yuxhn mh dunamenwn apokteinai fobeisqe de mallon ton dunamenon kai yuxhn kai swma apolesai en geennh.
mat 10:29 ouxi duo strouqia assariou pwleitai; kai en ec autwn ou peseitai epi thn ghn aneu tou patros umwn.
mat 10:30 umwn de kai ai trixes ths kefalhs pasai hriqmhmenai eisin.
mat 10:31 mh oun fobeisqe pollwn strouqiwn diaferete umeis.
mat 10:32 pas oun ostis omologhsei en emoi emprosqen twn anqrwpwn omologhsw kagw en autw emprosqen tou patros mou tou en tois ouranois
mat 10:33 ostis d an arnhshtai me emprosqen twn anqrwpwn arnhsomai kagw auton emprosqen tou patros mou tou en tois ouranois.
mat 10:34 mh nomishte oti hlqon balein eirhnhn epi thn ghn ouk hlqon balein eirhnhn alla maxairan.
mat 10:35 hlqon gar dixasai anqrwpon kata tou patros autou kai qugatera kata ths mhtros auths kai numfhn kata ths penqeras auths
mat 10:36 kai exqroi tou anqrwpou oi oikiakoi autou.
mat 10:37 o filwn patera h mhtera uper eme ouk estin mou acios kai o filwn uion h qugatera uper eme ouk estin mou acios
mat 10:38 kai os ou lambanei ton stauron autou kai akolouqei opisw mou ouk estin mou acios.
mat 10:39 o eurwn thn yuxhn autou apolesei authn kai o apolesas thn yuxhn autou eneken emou eurhsei authn.
mat 10:40 o dexomenos umas eme dexetai kai o eme dexomenos dexetai ton aposteilanta me.
mat 10:41 o dexomenos profhthn eis onoma profhtou misqon profhtou lhmyetai kai o dexomenos dikaion eis onoma dikaiou misqon dikaiou lhmyetai.
mat 10:42 kai os an potish ena twn mikrwn toutwn pothrion yuxrou monon eis onoma maqhtou amhn legw umin ou mh apolesh ton misqon autou.
mat 11:1 kai egeneto ote etelesen o ihsous diatasswn tois dwdeka maqhtais autou metebh ekeiqen tou didaskein kai khrussein en tais polesin autwn.
mat 11:2 o de iwannhs akousas en tw desmwthriw ta erga tou xristou pemyas dia twn maqhtwn autou
mat 11:3 eipen autw su ei o erxomenos h eteron prosdokwmen;
mat 11:4 kai apokriqeis o ihsous eipen autois poreuqentes apaggeilate iwannh a akouete kai blepete
mat 11:5 tufloi anablepousin kai xwloi peripatousin leproi kaqarizontai kai kwfoi akouousin kai nekroi egeirontai kai ptwxoi euaggelizontai
mat 11:6 kai makarios estin os ean mh skandalisqh en emoi.
mat 11:7 toutwn de poreuomenwn hrcato o ihsous legein tois oxlois peri iwannou ti echlqate eis thn erhmon qeasasqai; kalamon upo anemou saleuomenon;
mat 11:8 alla ti echlqate idein; anqrwpon en malakois hmfiesmenon; idou oi ta malaka forountes en tois oikois twn basilewn eisin.
mat 11:9 alla ti echlqate idein; profhthn; nai legw umin kai perissoteron profhtou.
mat 11:10 outos estin peri ou gegraptai idou egw apostellw ton aggelon mou pro proswpou sou os kataskeuasei thn odon sou emprosqen sou.
mat 11:11 amhn legw umin ouk eghgertai en gennhtois gunaikwn meizwn iwannou tou baptistou o de mikroteros en th basileia twn ouranwn meizwn autou estin.
mat 11:12 apo de twn hmerwn iwannou tou baptistou ews arti h basileia twn ouranwn biazetai kai biastai arpazousin authn.
mat 11:13 pantes gar oi profhtai kai o nomos ews iwannou eprofhteusan
mat 11:14 kai ei qelete decasqai autos estin hlias o mellwn erxesqai.
mat 11:15 o exwn wta [akouein] akouetw.
mat 11:16 tini de omoiwsw thn genean tauthn; omoia estin paidiois kaqhmenois en tais agorais a prosfwnounta tois eterois
mat 11:17 legousin hulhsamen umin kai ouk wrxhsasqe eqrhnhsamen kai ouk ekoyasqe.
mat 11:18 hlqen gar iwannhs mhte esqiwn mhte pinwn kai legousin daimonion exei
mat 11:19 hlqen o uios tou anqrwpou esqiwn kai pinwn kai legousin idou anqrwpos fagos kai oinopoths telwnwn filos kai amartwlwn. kai edikaiwqh h sofia apo [pantwn] twn ergwn auths.
mat 11:20 tote hrcato oneidizein tas poleis en ais egenonto ai pleistai dunameis autou oti ou metenohsan
mat 11:21 ouai soi xorazin ouai soi bhqsaida oti ei en turw kai sidwni egenonto ai dunameis ai genomenai en umin palai an en sakkw kai spodw metenohsan.
mat 11:22 plhn legw umin turw kai sidwni anektoteron estai en hmera krisews h umin.
mat 11:23 kai su kafarnaoum mh ews ouranou uywqhsh; ews adou katabhsh. oti ei en sodomois egenhqhsan ai dunameis ai genomenai en soi emeinen an mexri ths shmeron.
mat 11:24 plhn legw umin oti gh sodomwn anektoteron estai en hmera krisews h soi.
mat 11:25 en ekeinw tw kairw apokriqeis o ihsous eipen ecomologoumai soi pater kurie tou ouranou kai ths ghs oti ekruyas tauta apo sofwn kai sunetwn kai apekaluyas auta nhpiois
mat 11:26 nai o pathr oti outws eudokia egeneto emprosqen sou.
mat 11:27 panta moi paredoqh upo tou patros mou kai oudeis epiginwskei ton uion ei mh o pathr oude ton patera tis epiginwskei ei mh o uios kai w ean boulhtai o uios apokaluyai.
mat 11:28 deute pros me pantes oi kopiwntes kai pefortismenoi kagw anapausw umas.
mat 11:29 arate ton zugon mou ef umas kai maqete ap emou oti praus eimi kai tapeinos th kardia kai eurhsete anapausin tais yuxais umwn
mat 11:30 o gar zugos mou xrhstos kai to fortion mou elafron estin.
mat 12:1 en ekeinw tw kairw eporeuqh o ihsous tois sabbasin dia twn sporimwn oi de maqhtai autou epeinasan kai hrcanto tillein staxuas kai esqiein.
mat 12:2 oi de farisaioi idontes eipan autw idou oi maqhtai sou poiousin o ouk ecestin poiein en sabbatw.
mat 12:3 o de eipen autois ouk anegnwte ti epoihsen dauid ote epeinasen kai oi met autou;
mat 12:4 pws eishlqen eis ton oikon tou qeou kai tous artous ths proqesews [efagen] o ouk econ hn autw fagein oude tois met autou ei mh tois iereusin monois;
mat 12:5 h ouk anegnwte en tw nomw oti tois sabbasin oi iereis en tw ierw to sabbaton bebhlousin kai anaitioi eisin;
mat 12:6 legw de umin oti tou ierou meizon estin wde.
mat 12:7 ei de egnwkeite ti estin eleos qelw kai ou qusian ouk an katedikasate tous anaitious.
mat 12:8 kurios gar estin tou sabbatou o uios tou anqrwpou.
mat 12:9 kai metabas ekeiqen hlqen eis thn sunagwghn autwn
mat 12:10 kai idou anqrwpos xeira exwn chran. kai ephrwthsan auton legontes ei ecestin tois sabbasin qerapeusai; ina kathgorhswsin autou.
mat 12:11 o de eipen autois tis estai ec umwn anqrwpos os ecei probaton en kai ean empesh touto tois sabbasin eis boqunon ouxi krathsei auto kai egerei;
mat 12:12 posw oun diaferei anqrwpos probatou. wste ecestin tois sabbasin kalws poiein.
mat 12:13 tote legei tw anqrwpw ekteinon sou thn xeira. kai eceteinen kai apekatestaqh ugihs ws h allh.
mat 12:14 ecelqontes de oi farisaioi sumboulion elabon kat autou opws auton apoleswsin.
mat 12:15 o de ihsous gnous anexwrhsen ekeiqen. kai hkolouqhsan autw oxloi polloi kai eqerapeusen autous pantas
mat 12:16 kai epetimhsen autois ina mh faneron auton poihswsin
mat 12:17 ina plhrwqh to rhqen dia hsaiou tou profhtou legontos
mat 12:18 idou o pais mou on hretisa o agaphtos mou eis on eudokhsen h yuxh mou qhsw to pneuma mou ep auton kai krisin tois eqnesin apaggelei.
mat 12:19 ouk erisei oude kraugasei oude akousei tis en tais plateiais thn fwnhn autou.
mat 12:20 kalamon suntetrimmenon ou kateacei kai linon tufomenon ou sbesei ews an ekbalh eis nikos thn krisin.
mat 12:21 kai tw onomati autou eqnh elpiousin.
mat 12:22 tote proshnexqh autw daimonizomenos tuflos kai kwfos kai eqerapeusen auton wste ton kwfon lalein kai blepein.
mat 12:23 kai ecistanto pantes oi oxloi kai elegon mhti outos estin o uios dauid;
mat 12:24 oi de farisaioi akousantes eipon outos ouk ekballei ta daimonia ei mh en tw beelzeboul arxonti twn daimoniwn.
mat 12:25 eidws de tas enqumhseis autwn eipen autois pasa basileia merisqeisa kaq eauths erhmoutai kai pasa polis h oikia merisqeisa kaq eauths ou staqhsetai.
mat 12:26 kai ei o satanas ton satanan ekballei ef eauton emerisqh pws oun staqhsetai h basileia autou;
mat 12:27 kai ei egw en beelzeboul ekballw ta daimonia oi uioi umwn en tini ekballousin; dia touto autoi kritai esontai umwn.
mat 12:28 ei de en pneumati qeou egw ekballw ta daimonia ara efqasen ef umas h basileia tou qeou.
mat 12:29 h pws dunatai tis eiselqein eis thn oikian tou isxurou kai ta skeuh autou arpasai ean mh prwton dhsh ton isxuron; kai tote thn oikian autou diarpasei.
mat 12:30 o mh wn met emou kat emou estin kai o mh sunagwn met emou skorpizei.
mat 12:31 dia touto legw umin pasa amartia kai blasfhmia afeqhsetai tois anqrwpois h de tou pneumatos blasfhmia ouk afeqhsetai.
mat 12:32 kai os ean eiph logon kata tou uiou tou anqrwpou afeqhsetai autw os d an eiph kata tou pneumatos tou agiou ouk afeqhsetai autw oute en toutw tw aiwni oute en tw mellonti.
mat 12:33 h poihsate to dendron kalon kai ton karpon autou kalon h poihsate to dendron sapron kai ton karpon autou sapron ek gar tou karpou to dendron ginwsketai.
mat 12:34 gennhmata exidnwn pws dunasqe agaqa lalein ponhroi ontes; ek gar tou perisseumatos ths kardias to stoma lalei.
mat 12:35 o agaqos anqrwpos ek tou agaqou qhsaurou ekballei agaqa kai o ponhros anqrwpos ek tou ponhrou qhsaurou ekballei ponhra.
mat 12:36 legw de umin oti pan rhma argon o lalhsousin oi anqrwpoi apodwsousin peri autou logon en hmera krisews
mat 12:37 ek gar twn logwn sou dikaiwqhsh kai ek twn logwn sou katadikasqhsh.
mat 12:38 tote apekriqhsan autw tines twn grammatewn kai farisaiwn legontes didaskale qelomen apo sou shmeion idein.
mat 12:39 o de apokriqeis eipen autois genea ponhra kai moixalis shmeion epizhtei kai shmeion ou doqhsetai auth ei mh to shmeion iwna tou profhtou.
mat 12:40 wsper gar hn iwnas en th koilia tou khtous treis hmeras kai treis nuktas outws estai o uios tou anqrwpou en th kardia ths ghs treis hmeras kai treis nuktas.
mat 12:41 andres nineuitai anasthsontai en th krisei meta ths geneas tauths kai katakrinousin authn oti metenohsan eis to khrugma iwna kai idou pleion iwna wde.
mat 12:42 basilissa notou egerqhsetai en th krisei meta ths geneas tauths kai katakrinei authn oti hlqen ek twn peratwn ths ghs akousai thn sofian solomwnos kai idou pleion solomwnos wde.
mat 12:43 otan de to akaqarton pneuma ecelqh apo tou anqrwpou dierxetai di anudrwn topwn zhtoun anapausin kai oux euriskei.
mat 12:44 tote legei eis ton oikon mou epistreyw oqen echlqon kai elqon euriskei sxolazonta sesarwmenon kai kekosmhmenon.
mat 12:45 tote poreuetai kai paralambanei meq eautou epta etera pneumata ponhrotera eautou kai eiselqonta katoikei ekei kai ginetai ta esxata tou anqrwpou ekeinou xeirona twn prwtwn. outws estai kai th genea tauth th ponhra.
mat 12:46 eti autou lalountos tois oxlois idou h mhthr kai oi adelfoi autou eisthkeisan ecw zhtountes autw lalhsai.
mat 12:47 [--]
mat 12:48 o de apokriqeis eipen tw legonti autw tis estin h mhthr mou kai tines eisin oi adelfoi mou;
mat 12:49 kai ekteinas thn xeira autou epi tous maqhtas autou eipen idou h mhthr mou kai oi adelfoi mou
mat 12:50 ostis gar an poihsh to qelhma tou patros mou tou en ouranois autos mou adelfos kai adelfh kai mhthr estin.
mat 13:1 en th hmera ekeinh ecelqwn o ihsous ths oikias ekaqhto para thn qalassan
mat 13:2 kai sunhxqhsan pros auton oxloi polloi wste auton eis ploion embanta kaqhsqai kai pas o oxlos epi ton aigialon eisthkei.
mat 13:3 kai elalhsen autois polla en parabolais legwn idou echlqen o speirwn tou speirein.
mat 13:4 kai en tw speirein auton a men epesen para thn odon kai elqonta ta peteina katefagen auta.
mat 13:5 alla de epesen epi ta petrwdh opou ouk eixen ghn pollhn kai euqews ecaneteilen dia to mh exein baqos ghs.
mat 13:6 hliou de anateilantos ekaumatisqh kai dia to mh exein rizan echranqh.
mat 13:7 alla de epesen epi tas akanqas kai anebhsan ai akanqai kai epnican auta.
mat 13:8 alla de epesen epi thn ghn thn kalhn kai edidou karpon o men ekaton o de echkonta o de triakonta.
mat 13:9 o exwn wta [akouein] akouetw.
mat 13:10 kai proselqontes oi maqhtai eipan autw dia ti en parabolais laleis autois;
mat 13:11 o de apokriqeis eipen autois oti umin dedotai gnwnai ta musthria ths basileias twn ouranwn ekeinois de ou dedotai.
mat 13:12 ostis gar exei doqhsetai autw kai perisseuqhsetai ostis de ouk exei kai o exei arqhsetai ap autou.
mat 13:13 dia touto en parabolais autois lalw [ina blepontes mh blepwsin kai akouontes mh akouwsin kai mh sunwsin mhpote epistreywsin.
mat 13:14 kai anaplhroutai autois h profhteia hsaiou h legousa akoh akousete kai ou mh sunhte kai blepontes bleyete kai ou mh idhte.
mat 13:15 epaxunqh gar h kardia tou laou toutou kai tois wsin barews hkousan kai tous ofqalmous autwn ekammusan mhpote idwsin tois ofqalmois kai tois wsin akouswsin kai th kardia sunwsin kai epistreywsin kai iasomai autous.
mat 13:16 umwn de makarioi oi ofqalmoi oti blepousin kai ta wta umwn oti akouousin.
mat 13:17 amhn gar legw umin oti polloi profhtai kai dikaioi epequmhsan idein a blepete kai ouk eidan kai akousai a akouete kai ouk hkousan.
mat 13:18 umeis oun akousate thn parabolhn tou speirantos.
mat 13:19 pantos akouontos ton logon ths basileias kai mh sunientos erxetai o ponhros kai arpazei to esparmenon en th kardia autou outos estin o para thn odon spareis.
mat 13:20 o de epi ta petrwdh spareis outos estin o ton logon akouwn kai euqus meta xaras lambanwn auton
mat 13:21 ouk exei de rizan en eautw alla proskairos estin genomenhs de qliyews h diwgmou dia ton logon euqus skandalizetai.
mat 13:22 o de eis tas akanqas spareis outos estin o ton logon akouwn kai h merimna tou aiwnos kai h apath tou ploutou sumpnigei ton logon kai akarpos ginetai.
mat 13:23 o de epi thn kalhn ghn spareis outos estin o ton logon akouwn kai sunieis os dh karpoforei kai poiei o men ekaton o de echkonta o de triakonta.
mat 13:24 allhn parabolhn pareqhken autois legwn wmoiwqh h basileia twn ouranwn anqrwpw speiranti kalon sperma en tw agrw autou.
mat 13:25 en de tw kaqeudein tous anqrwpous hlqen autou o exqros kai epespeiren zizania ana meson tou sitou kai aphlqen.
mat 13:26 ote de eblasthsen o xortos kai karpon epoihsen tote efanh kai ta zizania.
mat 13:27 proselqontes de oi douloi tou oikodespotou eipon autw kurie ouxi kalon sperma espeiras en tw sw agrw; poqen oun exei zizania;
mat 13:28 o de efh autois exqros anqrwpos touto epoihsen. oi de douloi legousin autw qeleis oun apelqontes sullecwmen auta;
mat 13:29 o de fhsin ou mhpote sullegontes ta zizania ekrizwshte ama autois ton siton.
mat 13:30 afete sunaucanesqai amfotera ews tou qerismou kai en kairw tou qerismou erw tois qeristais sullecate prwton ta zizania kai dhsate auta eis desmas pros to katakausai auta ton de siton sunagagete eis thn apoqhkhn mou.
mat 13:31 allhn parabolhn pareqhken autois legwn omoia estin h basileia twn ouranwn kokkw sinapews on labwn anqrwpos espeiren en tw agrw autou
mat 13:32 o mikroteron men estin pantwn twn spermatwn otan de auchqh meizon twn laxanwn estin kai ginetai dendron wste elqein ta peteina tou ouranou kai kataskhnoun en tois kladois autou.
mat 13:33 allhn parabolhn elalhsen autois omoia estin h basileia twn ouranwn zumh hn labousa gunh enekruyen eis aleurou sata tria ews ou ezumwqh olon.
mat 13:34 tauta panta elalhsen o ihsous en parabolais tois oxlois kai xwris parabolhs ouden elalei autois
mat 13:35 opws plhrwqh to rhqen dia tou profhtou legontos anoicw en parabolais to stoma mou ereucomai kekrummena apo katabolhs kosmou.
mat 13:36 tote afeis tous oxlous hlqen eis thn oikian. kai proshlqon autw oi maqhtai autou legontes diasafhson hmin thn parabolhn twn zizaniwn tou agrou.
mat 13:37 o de apokriqeis eipen o speirwn to kalon sperma estin o uios tou anqrwpou
mat 13:38 o de agros estin o kosmos to de kalon sperma outoi eisin oi uioi ths basileias ta de zizania eisin oi uioi tou ponhrou
mat 13:39 o de exqros o speiras auta estin o diabolos o de qerismos sunteleia aiwnos estin oi de qeristai aggeloi eisin.
mat 13:40 wsper oun sullegetai ta zizania kai puri katakaietai outws estai en th sunteleia tou aiwnos
mat 13:41 apostelei o uios tou anqrwpou tous aggelous autou kai sullecousin ek ths basileias autou panta ta skandala kai tous poiountas thn anomian
mat 13:42 kai balousin autous eis thn kaminon tou puros ekei estai o klauqmos kai o brugmos twn odontwn.
mat 13:43 tote oi dikaioi eklamyousin ws o hlios en th basileia tou patros autwn. o exwn wta [akouein] akouetw.
mat 13:44 omoia estin h basileia twn ouranwn qhsaurw kekrummenw en tw agrw on eurwn anqrwpos ekruyen kai apo ths xaras autou upagei kai pwlei panta osa exei kai agorazei ton agron ekeinon.
mat 13:45 palin omoia estin h basileia twn ouranwn anqrwpw emporw zhtounti kalous margaritas
mat 13:46 eurwn de ena polutimon margarithn apelqwn pepraken panta osa eixen kai hgorasen auton.
mat 13:47 palin omoia estin h basileia twn ouranwn saghnh blhqeish eis thn qalassan kai ek pantos genous sunagagoush
mat 13:48 hn ote eplhrwqh anabibasantes epi ton aigialon kai kaqisantes sunelecan ta kala eis aggh ta de sapra ecw ebalon.
mat 13:49 outws estai en th sunteleia tou aiwnos eceleusontai oi aggeloi kai aforiousin tous ponhrous ek mesou twn dikaiwn
mat 13:50 kai balousin autous eis thn kaminon tou puros ekei estai o klauqmos kai o brugmos twn odontwn.
mat 13:51 sunhkate tauta panta; legousin autw nai.
mat 13:52 o de eipen autois dia touto pas grammateus maqhteuqeis th basileia twn ouranwn omoios estin anqrwpw oikodespoth ostis ekballei ek tou qhsaurou autou kaina kai palaia.
mat 13:53 kai egeneto ote etelesen o ihsous tas parabolas tautas methren ekeiqen.
mat 13:54 kai elqwn eis thn patrida autou edidasken autous en th sunagwgh autwn wste ekplhssesqai autous kai legein poqen toutw h sofia auth kai ai dunameis;
mat 13:55 oux outos estin o tou tektonos uios; oux h mhthr autou legetai mariam kai oi adelfoi autou iakwbos kai [iwshs] kai simwn kai ioudas;
mat 13:56 kai ai adelfai autou ouxi pasai pros hmas eisin; poqen oun toutw tauta panta;
mat 13:57 kai eskandalizonto en autw. o de ihsous eipen autois ouk estin profhths atimos ei mh en th patridi kai en th oikia autou.
mat 13:58 kai ouk epoihsen ekei dunameis pollas dia thn apistian autwn.
mat 14:1 en ekeinw tw kairw hkousen hrwdhs o tetraarxhs thn akohn ihsou
mat 14:2 kai eipen tois paisin autou outos estin iwannhs o baptisths autos hgerqh apo twn nekrwn kai dia touto ai dunameis energousin en autw.
mat 14:3 o gar hrwdhs krathsas ton iwannhn edhsen auton kai en fulakh apeqeto dia hrwdiada thn gunaika filippou tou adelfou autou
mat 14:4 elegen gar o iwannhs autw ouk ecestin soi exein authn.
mat 14:5 kai qelwn auton apokteinai efobhqh ton oxlon oti ws profhthn auton eixon.
mat 14:6 genesiois de genomenois tou hrwdou wrxhsato h qugathr ths hrwdiados en tw mesw kai hresen tw hrwdh
mat 14:7 oqen meq orkou wmologhsen auth dounai o ean aithshtai.
mat 14:8 h de probibasqeisa upo ths mhtros auths dos moi fhsin wde epi pinaki thn kefalhn iwannou tou baptistou.
mat 14:9 kai [eluphqh] o basileus dia [de] tous orkous kai tous sunanakeimenous ekeleusen doqhnai
mat 14:10 kai pemyas apekefalisen ton iwannhn en th fulakh
mat 14:11 kai hnexqh h kefalh autou epi pinaki kai edoqh tw korasiw kai hnegken th mhtri auths.
mat 14:12 kai proselqontes oi maqhtai autou hran to ptwma kai eqayan auton kai elqontes aphggeilan tw ihsou.
mat 14:13 akousas de o ihsous anexwrhsen ekeiqen en ploiw eis erhmon topon kat idian kai akousantes oi oxloi hkolouqhsan autw pezh apo twn polewn.
mat 14:14 kai ecelqwn eiden polun oxlon kai esplagxnisqh ep autois kai eqerapeusen tous arrwstous autwn.
mat 14:15 oyias de genomenhs proshlqon autw oi maqhtai legontes erhmos estin o topos kai h wra hdh parhlqen apoluson tous oxlous ina apelqontes eis tas kwmas agoraswsin eautois brwmata.
mat 14:16 o de ihsous eipen autois ou xreian exousin apelqein dote autois umeis fagein.
mat 14:17 oi de legousin autw ouk exomen wde ei mh pente artous kai duo ixquas.
mat 14:18 o de eipen ferete moi wde autous.
mat 14:19 kai keleusas tous oxlous anakliqhnai epi tou xortou labwn tous pente artous kai tous duo ixquas anableyas eis ton ouranon euloghsen kai klasas edwken tois maqhtais tous artous oi de maqhtai tois oxlois.
mat 14:20 kai efagon pantes kai exortasqhsan kai hran to perisseuon twn klasmatwn dwdeka kofinous plhreis.
mat 14:21 oi de esqiontes hsan andres wsei pentakisxilioi xwris gunaikwn kai paidiwn.
mat 14:22 kai euqews hnagkasen tous maqhtas embhnai eis to ploion kai proagein auton eis to peran ews ou apolush tous oxlous.
mat 14:23 kai apolusas tous oxlous anebh eis to oros kat idian proseucasqai. oyias de genomenhs monos hn ekei.
mat 14:24 to de ploion hdh stadious pollous apo ths ghs apeixen basanizomenon upo twn kumatwn hn gar enantios o anemos.
mat 14:25 tetarth de fulakh ths nuktos hlqen pros autous peripatwn epi thn qalassan.
mat 14:26 oi de maqhtai idontes auton epi ths qalasshs peripatounta etaraxqhsan legontes oti fantasma estin kai apo tou fobou ekracan.
mat 14:27 euqus de elalhsen o ihsous autois legwn qarseite egw eimi mh fobeisqe.
mat 14:28 apokriqeis de autw o petros eipen kurie ei su ei keleuson me elqein pros se epi ta udata
mat 14:29 o de eipen elqe. kai katabas apo tou ploiou o petros periepathsen epi ta udata [elqein] pros ton ihsoun.
mat 14:30 blepwn de ton anemon [-] efobhqh kai arcamenos katapontizesqai ekracen legwn kurie swson me.
mat 14:31 euqews de o ihsous ekteinas thn xeira epelabeto autou kai legei autw oligopiste eis ti edistasas;
mat 14:32 kai anabantwn autwn eis to ploion ekopasen o anemos.
mat 14:33 oi de en tw ploiw prosekunhsan autw legontes alhqws qeou uios ei.
mat 14:34 kai diaperasantes hlqon epi thn ghn eis gennhsaret.
mat 14:35 kai epignontes auton oi andres tou topou ekeinou apesteilan eis olhn thn perixwron ekeinhn kai proshnegkan autw pantas tous kakws exontas
mat 14:36 kai parekaloun auton ina monon aywntai tou kraspedou tou imatiou autou kai osoi hyanto dieswqhsan.
mat 15:1 tote proserxontai tw ihsou apo ierosolumwn farisaioi kai grammateis legontes
mat 15:2 dia ti oi maqhtai sou parabainousin thn paradosin twn presbuterwn; ou gar niptontai tas xeiras autwn otan arton esqiwsin.
mat 15:3 o de apokriqeis eipen autois dia ti kai umeis parabainete thn entolhn tou qeou dia thn paradosin umwn;
mat 15:4 o gar qeos eipen tima ton patera kai thn mhtera kai o kakologwn patera h mhtera qanatw teleutatw
mat 15:5 umeis de legete os an eiph tw patri h th mhtri dwron o ean ec emou wfelhqhs
mat 15:6 ou mh timhsei ton patera autou kai hkurwsate ton logon tou qeou dia thn paradosin umwn.
mat 15:7 upokritai kalws eprofhteusen peri umwn hsaias legwn
mat 15:8 o laos outos tois xeilesin me tima h de kardia autwn porrw apexei ap emou
mat 15:9 mathn de sebontai me didaskontes didaskalias entalmata anqrwpwn.
mat 15:10 kai proskalesamenos ton oxlon eipen autois akouete kai suniete
mat 15:11 ou to eiserxomenon eis to stoma koinoi ton anqrwpon alla to ekporeuomenon ek tou stomatos touto koinoi ton anqrwpon.
mat 15:12 tote proselqontes oi maqhtai legousin autw oidas oti oi farisaioi akousantes ton logon eskandalisqhsan;
mat 15:13 o de apokriqeis eipen pasa futeia hn ouk efuteusen o pathr mou o ouranios ekrizwqhsetai.
mat 15:14 afete autous [tufloi eisin odhgoi] tuflos de tuflon ean odhgh amfoteroi eis boqunon pesountai.
mat 15:15 apokriqeis de o petros eipen autw frason hmin thn parabolhn [-].
mat 15:16 o de eipen akmhn kai umeis asunetoi este;
mat 15:17 ou noeite oti pan to eisporeuomenon eis to stoma eis thn koilian xwrei kai eis afedrwna ekballetai;
mat 15:18 ta de ekporeuomena ek tou stomatos ek ths kardias ecerxetai kakeina koinoi ton anqrwpon.
mat 15:19 ek gar ths kardias ecerxontai dialogismoi ponhroi fonoi moixeiai porneiai klopai yeudomarturiai blasfhmiai.
mat 15:20 tauta estin ta koinounta ton anqrwpon to de aniptois xersin fagein ou koinoi ton anqrwpon.
mat 15:21 kai ecelqwn ekeiqen o ihsous anexwrhsen eis ta merh turou kai sidwnos.
mat 15:22 kai idou gunh xananaia apo twn oriwn ekeinwn ecelqousa ekrazen legousa elehson me kurie uios dauid h qugathr mou kakws daimonizetai.
mat 15:23 o de ouk apekriqh auth logon. kai proselqontes oi maqhtai autou hrwtoun auton legontes apoluson authn oti krazei opisqen hmwn.
mat 15:24 o de apokriqeis eipen ouk apestalhn ei mh eis ta probata ta apolwlota oikou israhl.
mat 15:25 h de elqousa prosekunei autw legousa kurie bohqei moi.
mat 15:26 o de apokriqeis eipen ouk estin kalon labein ton arton twn teknwn kai balein tois kunariois.
mat 15:27 h de eipen nai kurie kai gar ta kunaria esqiei apo twn yixiwn twn piptontwn apo ths trapezhs twn kuriwn autwn.
mat 15:28 tote apokriqeis o ihsous eipen auth w gunai megalh sou h pistis genhqhtw soi ws qeleis. kai iaqh h qugathr auths apo ths wras ekeinhs.
mat 15:29 kai metabas ekeiqen o ihsous hlqen para thn qalassan ths galilaias kai anabas eis to oros ekaqhto ekei.
mat 15:30 kai proshlqon autw oxloi polloi exontes meq eautwn xwlous tuflous kullous kwfous kai eterous pollous kai erriyan autous para tous podas autou kai eqerapeusen autous
mat 15:31 wste ton oxlon qaumasai blepontas kwfous lalountas kullous ugieis kai xwlous peripatountas kai tuflous blepontas kai edocasan ton qeon israhl.
mat 15:32 o de ihsous proskalesamenos tous maqhtas autou eipen splagxnizomai epi ton oxlon oti hdh hmerai treis prosmenousin moi kai ouk exousin ti fagwsin kai apolusai autous nhsteis ou qelw mhpote ekluqwsin en th odw.
mat 15:33 kai legousin autw oi maqhtai poqen hmin en erhmia artoi tosoutoi wste xortasai oxlon tosouton;
mat 15:34 kai legei autois o ihsous posous artous exete; oi de eipan epta kai oliga ixqudia.
mat 15:35 kai paraggeilas tw oxlw anapesein epi thn ghn
mat 15:36 elaben tous epta artous kai tous ixquas kai euxaristhsas eklasen kai edidou tois maqhtais oi de maqhtai tois oxlois.
mat 15:37 kai efagon pantes kai exortasqhsan kai to perisseuon twn klasmatwn hran epta spuridas plhreis.
mat 15:38 oi de esqiontes hsan tetrakisxilioi andres xwris gunaikwn kai paidiwn.
mat 15:39 kai apolusas tous oxlous enebh eis to ploion kai hlqen eis ta oria magadan.
mat 16:1 kai proselqontes oi farisaioi kai saddoukaioi peirazontes ephrwthsan auton shmeion ek tou ouranou epideicai autois.
mat 16:2 o de apokriqeis eipen autois [-]
mat 16:3 [--]
mat 16:4 genea ponhra kai moixalis shmeion epizhtei kai shmeion ou doqhsetai auth ei mh to shmeion iwna. kai katalipwn autous aphlqen.
mat 16:5 kai elqontes oi maqhtai eis to peran epelaqonto artous labein.
mat 16:6 o de ihsous eipen autois orate kai prosexete apo ths zumhs twn farisaiwn kai saddoukaiwn.
mat 16:7 oi de dielogizonto en eautois legontes oti artous ouk elabomen.
mat 16:8 gnous de o ihsous eipen ti dialogizesqe en eautois oligopistoi oti artous ouk exete;
mat 16:9 oupw noeite oude mnhmoneuete tous pente artous twn pentakisxiliwn kai posous kofinous elabete;
mat 16:10 oude tous epta artous twn tetrakisxiliwn kai posas spuridas elabete;
mat 16:11 pws ou noeite oti ou peri artwn eipon umin; prosexete de apo ths zumhs twn farisaiwn kai saddoukaiwn.
mat 16:12 tote sunhkan oti ouk eipen prosexein apo ths zumhs twn artwn alla apo ths didaxhs twn farisaiwn kai saddoukaiwn.
mat 16:13 elqwn de o ihsous eis ta merh kaisareias ths filippou hrwta tous maqhtas autou legwn tina legousin oi anqrwpoi einai ton uion tou anqrwpou;
mat 16:14 oi de eipan oi men iwannhn ton baptisthn alloi de hlian eteroi de ieremian h ena twn profhtwn.
mat 16:15 legei autois umeis de tina me legete einai;
mat 16:16 apokriqeis de simwn petros eipen su ei o xristos o uios tou qeou tou zwntos.
mat 16:17 apokriqeis de o ihsous eipen autw makarios ei simwn bariwna oti sarc kai aima ouk apekaluyen soi all o pathr mou o en tois ouranois.
mat 16:18 kagw de soi legw oti su ei petros kai epi tauth th petra oikodomhsw mou thn ekklhsian kai pulai adou ou katisxusousin auths.
mat 16:19 dwsw soi tas kleidas ths basileias twn ouranwn kai o ean dhshs epi ths ghs estai dedemenon en tois ouranois kai o ean lushs epi ths ghs estai lelumenon en tois ouranois.
mat 16:20 tote diesteilato tois maqhtais ina mhdeni eipwsin oti autos estin o xristos.
mat 16:21 apo tote hrcato o ihsous deiknuein tois maqhtais autou oti dei auton eis ierosoluma apelqein kai polla paqein apo twn presbuterwn kai arxierewn kai grammatewn kai apoktanqhnai kai th trith hmera egerqhnai.
mat 16:22 kai proslabomenos auton o petros hrcato epitiman autw legwn ilews soi kurie ou mh estai soi touto.
mat 16:23 o de strafeis eipen tw petrw upage opisw mou satana skandalon ei emou oti ou froneis ta tou qeou alla ta twn anqrwpwn.
mat 16:24 tote o ihsous eipen tois maqhtais autou ei tis qelei opisw mou elqein aparnhsasqw eauton kai aratw ton stauron autou kai akolouqeitw moi.
mat 16:25 os gar ean qelh thn yuxhn autou swsai apolesei authn os d an apolesh thn yuxhn autou eneken emou eurhsei authn.
mat 16:26 ti gar wfelhqhsetai anqrwpos ean ton kosmon olon kerdhsh thn de yuxhn autou zhmiwqh; h ti dwsei anqrwpos antallagma ths yuxhs autou;
mat 16:27 mellei gar o uios tou anqrwpou erxesqai en th doch tou patros autou meta twn aggelwn autou kai tote apodwsei ekastw kata [ta erga] autou.
mat 16:28 amhn legw umin oti eisin tines twn wde estwtwn oitines ou mh geuswntai qanatou ews an idwsin ton uion tou anqrwpou erxomenon en th basileia autou.
mat 17:1 kai meq hmeras ec paralambanei o ihsous ton petron kai iakwbon kai iwannhn ton adelfon autou kai anaferei autous eis oros uyhlon kat idian.
mat 17:2 kai metemorfwqh emprosqen autwn kai elamyen to proswpon autou ws o hlios ta de imatia autou egeneto leuka ws to fws.
mat 17:3 kai idou wfqh autois mwushs kai hlias sullalountes met autou.
mat 17:4 apokriqeis de o petros eipen tw ihsou kurie kalon estin hmas wde einai ei qeleis [poihswmen] wde treis skhnas soi mian kai mwusei mian kai hlia mian.
mat 17:5 eti autou lalountos idou nefelh fwteinh epeskiasen autous kai idou fwnh ek ths nefelhs legousa outos estin o uios mou o agaphtos en w eudokhsa akouete autou.
mat 17:6 kai akousantes oi maqhtai epesan epi proswpon autwn kai efobhqhsan sfodra.
mat 17:7 kai proshlqen o ihsous kai ayamenos autwn eipen egerqhte kai mh fobeisqe.
mat 17:8 eparantes de tous ofqalmous autwn oudena eidon ei mh auton ihsoun monon.
mat 17:9 kai katabainontwn autwn ek tou orous eneteilato autois o ihsous legwn mhdeni eiphte to orama ews ou o uios tou anqrwpou ek nekrwn egerqh.
mat 17:10 kai ephrwthsan auton oi maqhtai legontes ti oun oi grammateis legousin oti hlian dei elqein prwton;
mat 17:11 o de apokriqeis eipen hlias men erxetai kai apokatasthsei panta
mat 17:12 legw de umin oti hlias hdh hlqen kai ouk epegnwsan auton alla epoihsan en autw osa hqelhsan outws kai o uios tou anqrwpou mellei pasxein up autwn.
mat 17:13 tote sunhkan oi maqhtai oti peri iwannou tou baptistou eipen autois.
mat 17:14 kai elqontwn pros ton oxlon proshlqen autw anqrwpos gonupetwn auton
mat 17:15 kai legwn kurie elehson mou ton uion oti selhniazetai kai kakws pasxei pollakis gar piptei eis to pur kai pollakis eis to udwr.
mat 17:16 kai proshnegka auton tois maqhtais sou kai ouk hdunhqhsan auton qerapeusai.
mat 17:17 apokriqeis de o ihsous eipen w genea apistos kai diestrammenh ews pote meq umwn esomai; ews pote anecomai umwn; ferete moi auton wde.
mat 17:18 kai epetimhsen autw o ihsous kai echlqen ap autou to daimonion kai eqerapeuqh o pais apo ths wras ekeinhs.
mat 17:19 tote proselqontes oi maqhtai tw ihsou kat idian eipon dia ti hmeis ouk hdunhqhmen ekbalein auto;
mat 17:20 o de legei autois dia thn oligopistian umwn amhn gar legw umin ean exhte pistin ws kokkon sinapews ereite tw orei toutw metaba enqen ekei kai metabhsetai kai ouden adunathsei umin.
mat 17:21 [--]
mat 17:22 [anastrefomenwn] de autwn en th galilaia eipen autois o ihsous mellei o uios tou anqrwpou paradidosqai eis xeiras anqrwpwn
mat 17:23 kai apoktenousin auton kai th trith hmera egerqhsetai. kai eluphqhsan sfodra.
mat 17:24 elqontwn de autwn eis kafarnaoum proshlqon oi ta didraxma lambanontes tw petrw kai eipan o didaskalos umwn ou telei ta didraxma;
mat 17:25 legei nai. kai elqonta eis thn oikian proefqasen auton o ihsous legwn ti soi dokei simwn; oi basileis ths ghs apo tinwn lambanousin telh h khnson; apo twn uiwn autwn h apo twn allotriwn;
mat 17:26 eipontos de apo twn allotriwn efh autw o ihsous ara ge eleuqeroi eisin oi uioi.
mat 17:27 ina de mh skandaliswmen autous poreuqeis eis qalassan bale agkistron kai ton anabanta prwton ixqun aron kai anoicas to stoma autou eurhseis stathra ekeinon labwn dos autois anti emou kai sou.
mat 18:1 en ekeinh th wra proshlqon oi maqhtai tw ihsou legontes tis ara meizwn estin en th basileia twn ouranwn;
mat 18:2 kai proskalesamenos paidion esthsen auto en mesw autwn
mat 18:3 kai eipen amhn legw umin ean mh strafhte kai genhsqe ws ta paidia ou mh eiselqhte eis thn basileian twn ouranwn.
mat 18:4 ostis oun tapeinwsei eauton ws to paidion touto outos estin o meizwn en th basileia twn ouranwn.
mat 18:5 kai os ean dechtai en paidion toiouto epi tw onomati mou eme dexetai.
mat 18:6 os d an skandalish ena twn mikrwn toutwn twn pisteuontwn eis eme sumferei autw ina kremasqh mulos onikos peri ton traxhlon autou kai katapontisqh en tw pelagei ths qalasshs.
mat 18:7 ouai tw kosmw apo twn skandalwn anagkh gar elqein ta skandala plhn ouai tw anqrwpw di ou to skandalon erxetai.
mat 18:8 ei de h xeir sou h o pous sou skandalizei se ekkoyon auton kai bale apo sou kalon soi estin eiselqein eis thn zwhn kullon h xwlon h duo xeiras h duo podas exonta blhqhnai eis to pur to aiwnion.
mat 18:9 kai ei o ofqalmos sou skandalizei se ecele auton kai bale apo sou kalon soi estin monofqalmon eis thn zwhn eiselqein h duo ofqalmous exonta blhqhnai eis thn geennan tou puros.
mat 18:10 orate mh katafronhshte enos twn mikrwn toutwn legw gar umin oti oi aggeloi autwn en ouranois dia pantos blepousi to proswpon tou patros mou tou en ouranois.
mat 18:11 [--]
mat 18:12 ti umin dokei; ean genhtai tini anqrwpw ekaton probata kai planhqh en ec autwn ouxi afhsei ta enenhkonta ennea epi ta orh kai poreuqeis zhtei to planwmenon;
mat 18:13 kai ean genhtai eurein auto amhn legw umin oti xairei ep autw mallon h epi tois enenhkonta ennea tois mh peplanhmenois.
mat 18:14 outws ouk estin qelhma emprosqen tou patros [mou] tou en ouranois ina apolhtai en twn mikrwn toutwn.
mat 18:15 ean de amarthsh eis se o adelfos sou upage elegcon auton metacu sou kai autou monou. ean sou akoush ekerdhsas ton adelfon sou
mat 18:16 ean de mh akoush paralabe meta sou eti ena h duo ina epi stomatos duo marturwn h triwn staqh pan rhma
mat 18:17 ean de parakoush autwn eipe th ekklhsia ean de kai ths ekklhsias parakoush estw soi wsper o eqnikos kai o telwnhs.
mat 18:18 amhn legw umin osa ean dhshte epi ths ghs estai dedemena en ouranw kai osa ean lushte epi ths ghs estai lelumena en ouranw.
mat 18:19 palin amhn legw umin oti ean duo sumfwnhswsin ec umwn epi ths ghs peri pantos pragmatos ou ean aithswntai genhsetai autois para tou patros mou tou en ouranois.
mat 18:20 ou gar eisin duo h treis sunhgmenoi eis to emon onoma ekei eimi en mesw autwn.
mat 18:21 tote proselqwn o petros eipen autw kurie posakis amarthsei eis eme o adelfos mou kai afhsw autw; ews eptakis;
mat 18:22 legei autw o ihsous ou legw soi ews eptakis alla ews ebdomhkontakis epta.
mat 18:23 dia touto wmoiwqh h basileia twn ouranwn anqrwpw basilei os hqelhsen sunarai logon meta twn doulwn autou.
mat 18:24 arcamenou de autou sunairein proshnexqh autw eis ofeileths muriwn talantwn.
mat 18:25 mh exontos de autou apodounai ekeleusen auton o kurios praqhnai kai thn gunaika kai ta tekna kai panta osa exei kai apodoqhnai.
mat 18:26 peswn oun o doulos prosekunei autw legwn [kurie] makroqumhson ep emoi kai panta apodwsw soi.
mat 18:27 splagxnisqeis de o kurios tou doulou ekeinou apelusen auton kai to daneion afhken autw.
mat 18:28 ecelqwn de o doulos ekeinos euren ena twn sundoulwn autou os wfeilen autw ekaton dhnaria kai krathsas auton epnigen legwn apodos ei ti ofeileis.
mat 18:29 peswn oun o sundoulos autou parekalei auton legwn makroqumhson ep emoi kai apodwsw soi.
mat 18:30 o de ouk hqelen alla apelqwn ebalen auton eis fulakhn ews apodw to ofeilomenon.
mat 18:31 idontes oun oi sundouloi autou ta genomena eluphqhsan sfodra kai elqontes diesafhsan tw kuriw eautwn panta ta genomena.
mat 18:32 tote proskalesamenos auton o kurios autou legei autw doule ponhre pasan thn ofeilhn ekeinhn afhka soi epei parekalesas me
mat 18:33 ouk edei kai se elehsai ton sundoulon sou ws kagw se hlehsa;
mat 18:34 kai orgisqeis o kurios autou paredwken auton tois basanistais ews ou apodw pan to ofeilomenon.
mat 18:35 outws kai o pathr mou o ouranios poihsei umin ean mh afhte ekastos tw adelfw autou apo twn kardiwn umwn.
mat 19:1 kai egeneto ote etelesen o ihsous tous logous toutous methren apo ths galilaias kai hlqen eis ta oria ths ioudaias peran tou iordanou.
mat 19:2 kai hkolouqhsan autw oxloi polloi kai eqerapeusen autous ekei.
mat 19:3 kai proshlqon autw farisaioi peirazontes auton kai legontes ei ecestin anqrwpw apolusai thn gunaika autou kata pasan aitian;
mat 19:4 o de apokriqeis eipen ouk anegnwte oti o ktisas ap arxhs arsen kai qhlu epoihsen autous;
mat 19:5 kai eipen eneka toutou kataleiyei anqrwpos ton patera kai thn mhtera kai kollhqhsetai th gunaiki autou kai esontai oi duo eis sarka mian.
mat 19:6 wste ouketi eisin duo alla sarc mia. o oun o qeos sunezeucen anqrwpos mh xwrizetw.
mat 19:7 legousin autw ti oun mwushs eneteilato dounai biblion apostasiou kai apolusai authn;
mat 19:8 legei autois oti mwushs pros thn sklhrokardian umwn epetreyen umin apolusai tas gunaikas umwn ap arxhs de ou gegonen outws.
mat 19:9 legw de umin oti os an apolush thn gunaika autou [parektos logou porneias] kai gamhsh allhn moixatai.
mat 19:10 legousin autw oi maqhtai autou ei outws estin h aitia tou anqrwpou meta ths gunaikos ou sumferei gamhsai.
mat 19:11 o de eipen autois ou pantes xwrousin ton logon touton all ois dedotai.
mat 19:12 eisin gar eunouxoi oitines ek koilias mhtros egennhqhsan outws kai eisin eunouxoi oitines eunouxisqhsan upo twn anqrwpwn kai eisin eunouxoi oitines eunouxisan eautous dia thn basileian twn ouranwn. o dunamenos xwrein xwreitw.
mat 19:13 tote proshnexqhsan autw paidia ina tas xeiras epiqh autois kai proseuchtai oi de maqhtai epetimhsan autois.
mat 19:14 o de ihsous eipen afete ta paidia kai mh kwluete auta elqein pros me twn gar toioutwn estin h basileia twn ouranwn.
mat 19:15 kai epiqeis tas xeiras autois eporeuqh ekeiqen.
mat 19:16 kai idou eis proselqwn autw eipen didaskale [agaqe] ti agaqon poihsw ina sxw zwhn aiwnion;
mat 19:17 o de eipen autw ti me [erwtas peri tou agaqou; oudeis agaqos ei mh eis o qeos]. ei de qeleis eis thn zwhn eiselqein thrhson tas entolas.
mat 19:18 legei autw poias; o de ihsous eipen to ou foneuseis ou moixeuseis ou kleyeis ou yeudomarturhseis
mat 19:19 tima ton patera kai thn mhtera kai agaphseis ton plhsion sou ws seauton.
mat 19:20 legei autw o neaniskos panta tauta [efulacamhn ek neothtos mou] ti eti usterw;
mat 19:21 efh autw o ihsous ei qeleis teleios einai upage pwlhson sou ta uparxonta kai dos tois ptwxois kai eceis qhsauron en ouranois kai deuro akolouqei moi.
mat 19:22 akousas de o neaniskos ton logon aphlqen lupoumenos hn gar exwn kthmata polla.
mat 19:23 o de ihsous eipen tois maqhtais autou amhn legw umin oti plousios duskolws eiseleusetai eis thn basileian twn ouranwn.
mat 19:24 palin de legw umin eukopwteron estin kamhlon dia truphmatos rafidos dielqein h plousion eiselqein eis thn basileian tou qeou.
mat 19:25 akousantes de oi maqhtai eceplhssonto sfodra legontes tis ara dunatai swqhnai;
mat 19:26 embleyas de o ihsous eipen autois para anqrwpois touto adunaton estin para de qew panta dunata.
mat 19:27 tote apokriqeis o petros eipen autw idou hmeis afhkamen panta kai hkolouqhsamen soi ti ara estai hmin;
mat 19:28 o de ihsous eipen autois amhn legw umin oti umeis oi akolouqhsantes moi en th paliggenesia otan kaqish o uios tou anqrwpou epi qronou dochs autou kaqhsesqe kai umeis epi dwdeka qronous krinontes tas dwdeka fulas tou israhl.
