mat 19:29 kai pas ostis afhken oikias h adelfous h adelfas h patera h mhtera [h gunaika] h tekna h agrous eneken tou onomatos mou [pollaplasiona] lhmyetai kai zwhn aiwnion klhronomhsei.
mat 19:30 polloi de esontai prwtoi esxatoi kai esxatoi prwtoi.
mat 20:1 omoia gar estin h basileia twn ouranwn anqrwpw oikodespoth ostis echlqen ama prwi misqwsasqai ergatas eis ton ampelwna autou
mat 20:2 sumfwnhsas de meta twn ergatwn ek dhnariou thn hmeran apesteilen autous eis ton ampelwna autou.
mat 20:3 kai ecelqwn peri trithn wran eiden allous estwtas en th agora argous
mat 20:4 kai ekeinois eipen upagete kai umeis eis ton ampelwna kai o ean h dikaion dwsw umin.
mat 20:5 oi de aphlqon. palin de ecelqwn peri ekthn kai enathn wran epoihsen wsautws.
mat 20:6 peri de thn endekathn ecelqwn euren allous estwtas kai legei autois ti wde esthkate olhn thn hmeran argoi;
mat 20:7 legousin autw oti oudeis hmas emisqwsato. legei autois upagete kai umeis eis ton ampelwna.

mat 20:11 labontes de egogguzon kata tou oikodespotou

mat 20:14 aron to son kai upage qelw de toutw tw esxatw dounai ws kai soi.

mat 20:16 outws esontai oi esxatoi prwtoi kai oi prwtoi esxatoi.

mat 20:19 kai paradwsousin auton tois eqnesin eis to empaicai kai mastigwsai kai staurwsai kai th trith hmera egerqhsetai.

mat 20:24 kai akousantes oi deka hganakthsan peri twn duo adelfwn.

mat 20:27 kai os an qelh en umin einai prwtos estai umwn doulos

mat 21:12 kai eishlqen ihsous eis to ieron kai ecebalen pantas tous pwlountas kai agorazontas en tw ierw kai tas trapezas twn kollubistwn katestreyen kai tas kaqedras twn pwlountwn tas peristeras

mat 21:15 idontes de oi arxiereis kai oi grammateis ta qaumasia a epoihsen kai tous paidas tous krazontas en tw ierw kai legontas wsanna tw uiw dauid hganakthsan

mat 21:17 kai katalipwn autous echlqen ecw ths polews eis bhqanian kai hulisqh ekei.
mat 21:18 prwi de epanagwn eis thn polin epeinasen.
mat 21:19 kai idwn sukhn mian epi ths odou hlqen ep authn kai ouden euren en auth ei mh fulla monon kai legei auth mhketi ek sou karpos genhtai eis ton aiwna. kai echranqh paraxrhma h sukh.
mat 21:20 kai idontes oi maqhtai eqaumasan legontes pws paraxrhma echranqh h sukh;
mat 21:21 apokriqeis de o ihsous eipen autois amhn legw umin ean exhte pistin kai mh diakriqhte ou monon to ths sukhs poihsete alla kan tw orei toutw eiphte arqhti kai blhqhti eis thn qalassan genhsetai
mat 21:22 kai panta osa an aithshte en th proseuxh pisteuontes lhmyesqe.

mat 21:24 apokriqeis de o ihsous eipen autois erwthsw umas kagw logon ena on ean eiphte moi kagw umin erw en poia ecousia tauta poiw
mat 21:25 to baptisma to iwannou poqen hn; ec ouranou h ec anqrwpwn; oi de dielogizonto en eautois legontes ean eipwmen ec ouranou erei hmin dia ti oun ouk episteusate autw;
mat 21:26 ean de eipwmen ec anqrwpwn foboumeqa ton oxlon pantes gar ws profhthn exousin ton iwannhn.
mat 21:27 kai apokriqentes tw ihsou eipan ouk oidamen. efh autois kai autos oude egw legw umin en poia ecousia tauta poiw.
mat 21:28 ti de umin dokei; anqrwpos eixen tekna duo. kai proselqwn tw prwtw eipen teknon upage shmeron ergazou en tw ampelwni.

mat 21:30 proselqwn de tw eterw eipen wsautws. o de apokriqeis eipen egw kurie kai ouk aphlqen.
mat 21:31 tis ek twn duo epoihsen to qelhma tou patros; legousin o prwtos. legei autois o ihsous amhn legw umin oti oi telwnai kai ai pornai proagousin umas eis thn basileian tou qeou.
mat 21:32 hlqen gar iwannhs pros umas en odw dikaiosunhs kai ouk episteusate autw oi de telwnai kai ai pornai episteusan autw umeis de idontes oude metemelhqhte usteron tou pisteusai autw.
mat 21:33 allhn parabolhn akousate. anqrwpos hn oikodespoths ostis efuteusen ampelwna kai fragmon autw perieqhken kai wrucen en autw lhnon kai wkodomhsen purgon kai ecedeto auton gewrgois kai apedhmhsen.

mat 21:35 kai labontes oi gewrgoi tous doulous autou on men edeiran on de apekteinan on de eliqobolhsan.

mat 21:37 usteron de apesteilen pros autous ton uion autou legwn entraphsontai ton uion mou.
mat 21:38 oi de gewrgoi idontes ton uion eipon en eautois outos estin o klhronomos deute apokteinwmen auton kai sxwmen thn klhronomian autou.
mat 21:39 kai labontes auton ecebalon ecw tou ampelwnos kai apekteinan.
mat 21:40 otan oun elqh o kurios tou ampelwnos ti poihsei tois gewrgois ekeinois;
mat 21:41 legousin autw kakous kakws apolesei autous kai ton ampelwna ekdwsetai allois gewrgois oitines apodwsousin autw tous karpous en tois kairois autwn.
mat 21:42 legei autois o ihsous oudepote anegnwte en tais grafais liqon on apedokimasan oi oikodomountes outos egenhqh eis kefalhn gwnias para kuriou egeneto auth kai estin qaumasth en ofqalmois hmwn;

mat 22:1 kai apokriqeis o ihsous palin eipen en parabolais autois legwn

mat 22:3 kai apesteilen tous doulous autou kalesai tous keklhmenous eis tous gamous kai ouk hqelon elqein.
mat 22:4 palin apesteilen allous doulous legwn eipate tois keklhmenois idou to ariston mou htoimaka oi tauroi mou kai ta sitista tequmena kai panta etoima deute eis tous gamous.
mat 22:5 oi de amelhsantes aphlqon os men eis ton idion agron os de epi thn emporian autou
mat 22:6 oi de loipoi krathsantes tous doulous autou ubrisan kai apekteinan.

mat 22:13 tote o basileus eipen tois diakonois dhsantes autou podas kai xeiras ekbalete auton eis to skotos to ecwteron ekei estai o klauqmos kai o brugmos twn odontwn.

mat 22:25 hsan de par hmin epta adelfoi kai o prwtos ghmas eteleuthsen kai mh exwn sperma afhken thn gunaika autou tw adelfw autou
mat 22:26 omoiws kai o deuteros kai o tritos ews twn epta.
mat 22:27 usteron de pantwn apeqanen h gunh.
mat 22:28 en th anastasei oun tinos twn epta estai gunh; pantes gar esxon authn.

mat 22:30 en gar th anastasei oute gamousin oute gamizontai all ws [oi] aggeloi en tw ouranw eisin.
mat 22:31 peri de ths anastasews twn nekrwn ouk anegnwte to rhqen umin upo tou qeou legontos
mat 22:32 egw eimi o qeos abraam kai o qeos isaak kai o qeos iakwb; ouk estin o qeos nekrwn alla zwntwn.

mat 23:1 tote o ihsous elalhsen tois oxlois kai tois maqhtais autou
mat 23:2 legwn epi ths mwusews kaqedras ekaqisan oi grammateis kai oi farisaioi.
mat 23:3 panta oun osa ean eipwsin umin poihsate kai threite kata de ta erga autwn mh poieite legousin gar kai ou poiousin.
mat 23:4 desmeuousin de fortia barea kai dusbastakta kai epitiqeasin epi tous wmous twn anqrwpwn autoi de tw daktulw autwn ou qelousin kinhsai auta.
mat 23:5 panta de ta erga autwn poiousin pros to qeaqhnai tois anqrwpois platunousin gar ta fulakthria autwn kai megalunousin ta kraspeda
mat 23:6 filousin de thn prwtoklisian en tois deipnois kai tas prwtokaqedrias en tais sunagwgais
mat 23:7 kai tous aspasmous en tais agorais kai kaleisqai upo twn anqrwpwn rabbi.
mat 23:8 umeis de mh klhqhte rabbi eis gar estin umwn o didaskalos pantes de umeis adelfoi este.
mat 23:9 kai patera mh kaleshte [umin] epi ths ghs eis gar estin umwn o pathr o ouranios.
mat 23:10 mhde klhqhte kaqhghtai oti kaqhghths umwn estin eis o xristos.
mat 23:11 o de meizwn umwn estai umwn diakonos.
mat 23:12 ostis de uywsei eauton tapeinwqhsetai kai ostis tapeinwsei eauton uywqhsetai.
mat 23:13 ouai de umin grammateis kai farisaioi upokritai oti kleiete thn basileian twn ouranwn emprosqen twn anqrwpwn umeis gar ouk eiserxesqe oude tous eiserxomenous afiete eiselqein.
mat 23:14 [--]
mat 23:15 ouai umin grammateis kai farisaioi upokritai oti periagete thn qalassan kai thn chran poihsai ena proshluton kai otan genhtai poieite auton uion geennhs diploteron umwn.
mat 23:16 ouai umin odhgoi tufloi oi legontes os an omosh en tw naw ouden estin os d an omosh en tw xrusw tou naou ofeilei.
mat 23:17 mwroi kai tufloi tis gar meizwn estin o xrusos h o naos o agiasas ton xruson;
mat 23:18 kai os an omosh en tw qusiasthriw ouden estin os d an omosh en tw dwrw tw epanw autou ofeilei.
mat 23:19 [mwroi kai] tufloi ti gar meizon to dwron h to qusiasthrion to agiazon to dwron;
mat 23:20 o oun omosas en tw qusiasthriw omnuei en autw kai en pasi tois epanw autou
mat 23:21 kai o omosas en tw naw omnuei en autw kai en tw katoikounti auton
mat 23:22 kai o omosas en tw ouranw omnuei en tw qronw tou qeou kai en tw kaqhmenw epanw autou.
mat 23:23 ouai umin grammateis kai farisaioi upokritai oti apodekatoute to hduosmon kai to anhqon kai to kuminon kai afhkate ta barutera tou nomou thn krisin kai to eleos kai thn pistin tauta de edei poihsai kakeina mh afienai.
mat 23:24 odhgoi tufloi oi diulizontes ton kwnwpa thn de kamhlon katapinontes.
mat 23:25 ouai umin grammateis kai farisaioi upokritai oti kaqarizete to ecwqen tou pothriou kai ths paroyidos eswqen de gemousin ec arpaghs kai akrasias.
mat 23:26 farisaie tufle kaqarison prwton to entos tou pothriou [kai ths paroyidos] ina genhtai kai to ektos autou kaqaron.
mat 23:27 ouai umin grammateis kai farisaioi upokritai oti paromoiazete tafois kekoniamenois oitines ecwqen men fainontai wraioi eswqen de gemousin ostewn nekrwn kai pashs akaqarsias.
mat 23:28 outws kai umeis ecwqen men fainesqe tois anqrwpois dikaioi eswqen de este mestoi upokrisews kai anomias.
mat 23:29 ouai umin grammateis kai farisaioi upokritai oti oikodomeite tous tafous twn profhtwn kai kosmeite ta mnhmeia twn dikaiwn
mat 23:30 kai legete ei hmeqa en tais hmerais twn paterwn hmwn ouk an hmeqa autwn koinwnoi en tw aimati twn profhtwn.
mat 23:31 wste martureite eautois oti uioi este twn foneusantwn tous profhtas.
mat 23:32 kai umeis plhrwsate to metron twn paterwn umwn.

mat 25:1 tote omoiwqhsetai h basileia twn ouranwn deka parqenois aitines labousai tas lampadas eautwn echlqon eis upanthsin tou numfiou.

mat 25:4 ai de fronimoi elabon elaion en tois aggeiois meta twn lampadwn eautwn.

mat 25:42 epeinasa gar kai ouk edwkate moi fagein ediyhsa kai ouk epotisate me

mat 26:19 kai epoihsan oi maqhtai ws sunetacen autois o ihsous kai htoimasan to pasxa.

mat 26:23 o de apokriqeis eipen o embayas met emou thn xeira en tw trubliw outos me paradwsei.
mat 26:24 o men uios tou anqrwpou upagei kaqws gegraptai peri autou ouai de tw anqrwpw ekeinw di ou o uios tou anqrwpou paradidotai kalon hn autw ei ouk egennhqh o anqrwpos ekeinos.
mat 26:25 apokriqeis de ioudas o paradidous auton eipen mhti egw eimi rabbi; legei autw su eipas.
mat 26:26 esqiontwn de autwn labwn o ihsous arton kai euloghsas eklasen kai dous tois maqhtais eipen labete fagete touto estin to swma mou.
mat 26:27 kai labwn pothrion kai euxaristhsas edwken autois legwn piete ec autou pantes

mat 26:31 tote legei autois o ihsous pantes umeis skandalisqhsesqe en emoi en th nukti tauth gegraptai gar patacw ton poimena kai diaskorpisqhsontai ta probata ths poimnhs
mat 26:32 meta de to egerqhnai me proacw umas eis thn galilaian.

mat 26:39 kai proelqwn mikron epesen epi proswpon autou proseuxomenos kai legwn pater mou ei dunaton estin parelqatw ap emou to pothrion touto plhn oux ws egw qelw all ws su.
mat 26:40 kai erxetai pros tous maqhtas kai euriskei autous kaqeudontas kai legei tw petrw outws ouk isxusate mian wran grhgorhsai met emou;

mat 26:43 kai elqwn palin euren autous kaqeudontas hsan gar autwn oi ofqalmoi bebarhmenoi.
mat 26:44 kai afeis autous palin apelqwn proshucato ek tritou ton auton logon eipwn palin.
mat 26:45 tote erxetai pros tous maqhtas kai legei autois kaqeudete to loipon kai anapauesqe; idou hggiken h wra kai o uios tou anqrwpou paradidotai eis xeiras amartwlwn.
mat 26:46 egeiresqe agwmen idou hggiken o paradidous me.
mat 26:47 kai eti autou lalountos idou ioudas eis twn dwdeka hlqen kai met autou oxlos polus meta maxairwn kai culwn apo twn arxierewn kai presbuterwn tou laou.
mat 26:48 o de paradidous auton edwken autois shmeion legwn on an filhsw autos estin krathsate auton.
mat 26:49 kai euqews proselqwn tw ihsou eipen xaire rabbi kai katefilhsen auton.
mat 26:50 o de ihsous eipen autw etaire ef o parei. tote proselqontes epebalon tas xeiras epi ton ihsoun kai ekrathsan auton.
mat 26:51 kai idou eis twn meta ihsou ekteinas thn xeira apespasen thn maxairan autou kai patacas ton doulon tou arxierews afeilen autou to wtion.
mat 26:52 tote legei autw o ihsous apostreyon thn maxairan sou eis ton topon auths pantes gar oi labontes maxairan en maxairh apolountai.
mat 26:53 h dokeis oti ou dunamai parakalesai ton patera mou kai parasthsei moi arti pleiw dwdeka legiwnas aggelwn;
mat 26:54 pws oun plhrwqwsin ai grafai oti outws dei genesqai;
mat 26:55 en ekeinh th wra eipen o ihsous tois oxlois ws epi lhsthn echlqate meta maxairwn kai culwn sullabein me; kaq hmeran en tw ierw ekaqezomhn didaskwn kai ouk ekrathsate me.
mat 26:56 touto de olon gegonen ina plhrwqwsin ai grafai twn profhtwn. tote oi maqhtai pantes afentes auton efugon.
mat 26:57 oi de krathsantes ton ihsoun aphgagon pros kaiafan ton arxierea opou oi grammateis kai oi presbuteroi sunhxqhsan.
mat 26:58 o de petros hkolouqei autw apo makroqen ews ths aulhs tou arxierews kai eiselqwn esw ekaqhto meta twn uphretwn idein to telos.
mat 26:59 oi de arxiereis kai to sunedrion olon ezhtoun yeudomarturian kata tou ihsou opws auton qanatwswsin
mat 26:60 kai oux euron pollwn proselqontwn yeudomarturwn. usteron de proselqontes duo
