mat 26:63 o de ihsous esiwpa. kai o arxiereus eipen autw ecorkizw se kata tou qeou tou zwntos ina hmin eiphs ei su ei o xristos o uios tou qeou.
mat 26:64 legei autw o ihsous su eipas plhn legw umin ap arti oyesqe ton uion tou anqrwpou kaqhmenon ek deciwn ths dunamews kai erxomenon epi twn nefelwn tou ouranou.
mat 26:65 tote o arxiereus dierrhcen ta imatia autou legwn eblasfhmhsen ti eti xreian exomen marturwn; ide nun hkousate thn blasfhmian
mat 26:66 ti umin dokei; oi de apokriqentes eipan enoxos qanatou estin.
mat 26:67 tote eneptusan eis to proswpon autou kai ekolafisan auton oi de erapisan
mat 26:68 legontes profhteuson hmin xriste tis estin o paisas se;
mat 26:69 o de petros ekaqhto ecw en th aulh kai proshlqen autw mia paidiskh legousa kai su hsqa meta ihsou tou galilaiou.
mat 26:70 o de hrnhsato emprosqen pantwn legwn ouk oida ti legeis.
mat 26:71 ecelqonta de eis ton pulwna eiden auton allh kai legei tois ekei outos hn meta ihsou tou nazwraiou.
mat 26:72 kai palin hrnhsato meta orkou oti ouk oida ton anqrwpon.
mat 26:73 meta mikron de proselqontes oi estwtes eipon tw petrw alhqws kai su ec autwn ei kai gar h lalia sou dhlon se poiei.
mat 26:74 tote hrcato kataqematizein kai omnuein oti ouk oida ton anqrwpon. kai euqews alektwr efwnhsen.
mat 26:75 kai emnhsqh o petros tou rhmatos ihsou eirhkotos oti prin alektora fwnhsai tris aparnhsh me kai ecelqwn ecw eklausen pikrws.
mat 27:1 prwias de genomenhs sumboulion elabon pantes oi arxiereis kai oi presbuteroi tou laou kata tou ihsou wste qanatwsai auton
mat 27:2 kai dhsantes auton aphgagon kai paredwkan pilatw tw hgemoni.
mat 27:3 tote idwn ioudas o paradidous auton oti katekriqh metamelhqeis estreyen ta triakonta arguria tois arxiereusin kai presbuterois
mat 27:4 legwn hmarton paradous aima [diaion]. oi de eipan ti pros hmas; su oyh.
mat 27:5 kai riyas ta arguria eis ton naon anexwrhsen kai apelqwn aphgcato.
mat 27:6 oi de arxiereis labontes ta arguria eipan ouk ecestin balein auta eis ton korbanan epei timh aimatos estin.
mat 27:7 sumboulion de labontes hgorasan ec autwn ton agron tou keramews eis tafhn tois cenois.
mat 27:8 dio eklhqh o agros ekeinos agros aimatos ews ths shmeron.
mat 27:9 tote eplhrwqh to rhqen dia ieremiou tou profhtou legontos kai elabon ta triakonta arguria thn timhn tou tetimhmenou on etimhsanto apo uiwn israhl
mat 27:10 kai edwkan auta eis ton agron tou keramews kaqa sunetacen moi kurios.
mat 27:11 o de ihsous estaqh emprosqen tou hgemonos kai ephrwthsen auton o hgemwn legwn su ei o basileus twn ioudaiwn; o de ihsous efh su legeis.
mat 27:12 kai en tw kathgoreisqai auton upo twn arxierewn kai presbuterwn ouden apekrinato.
mat 27:13 tote legei autw o pilatos ouk akoueis posa sou katamarturousin;
mat 27:14 kai ouk apekriqh autw pros oude en rhma wste qaumazein ton hgemona lian.
mat 27:15 kata de eorthn eiwqei o hgemwn apoluein ena tw oxlw desmion on hqelon.
mat 27:16 eixon de tote desmion epishmon legomenon [--] barabban.
mat 27:17 sunhgmenwn oun autwn eipen autois o pilatos tina qelete apolusw umin [--] ton barabban h ihsoun ton legomenon xriston;
mat 27:18 hdei gar oti dia fqonon paredwkan auton.
mat 27:19 kaqhmenou de autou epi tou bhmatos apesteilen pros auton h gunh autou legousa mhden soi kai tw dikaiw ekeinw polla gar epaqon shmeron kat onar di auton.
mat 27:20 oi de arxiereis kai oi presbuteroi epeisan tous oxlous ina aithswntai ton barabban ton de ihsoun apoleswsin.
mat 27:21 apokriqeis de o hgemwn eipen autois tina qelete apo twn duo apolusw umin; oi de eipan ton barabban.
mat 27:22 legei autois o pilatos ti oun poihsw ihsoun ton legomenon xriston; legousin pantes staurwqhtw.
mat 27:23 o de efh ti gar kakon epoihsen; oi de perissws ekrazon legontes staurwqhtw.
mat 27:24 idwn de o pilatos oti ouden wfelei alla mallon qorubos ginetai labwn udwr apeniyato tas xeiras apenanti tou oxlou legwn aqwos eimi apo tou aimatos toutou umeis oyesqe.
mat 27:25 kai apokriqeis pas o laos eipen to aima autou ef hmas kai epi ta tekna hmwn.
mat 27:26 tote apelusen autois ton barabban ton de ihsoun fragellwsas paredwken ina staurwqh.
mat 27:27 tote oi stratiwtai tou hgemonos paralabontes ton ihsoun eis to praitwrion sunhgagon ep auton olhn thn speiran.
mat 27:28 kai ekdusantes auton xlamuda kokkinhn perieqhkan autw
mat 27:29 kai plecantes stefanon ec akanqwn epeqhkan epi ths kefalhs autou kai kalamon en th decia autou kai gonupethsantes emprosqen autou enepaican autw legontes xaire basileu twn ioudaiwn
mat 27:30 kai emptusantes eis auton elabon ton kalamon kai etupton eis thn kefalhn autou.
mat 27:31 kai ote enepaican autw ecedusan auton thn xlamuda kai enedusan auton ta imatia autou kai aphgagon auton eis to staurwsai.
mat 27:32 ecerxomenoi de euron anqrwpon kurhnaion onomati simwna touton hggareusan ina arh ton stauron autou.
mat 27:33 kai elqontes eis topon legomenon golgoqa o estin kraniou topos legomenos
mat 27:34 edwkan autw piein oinon meta xolhs memigmenon kai geusamenos ouk hqelhsen piein.
mat 27:35 staurwsantes de auton diemerisanto ta imatia autou ballontes klhron
mat 27:36 kai kaqhmenoi ethroun auton ekei.
mat 27:37 kai epeqhkan epanw ths kefalhs autou thn aitian autou gegrammenhn outos estin ihsous o basileus twn ioudaiwn.
mat 27:38 tote staurountai sun autw duo lhstai eis ek deciwn kai eis ec euwnumwn.
mat 27:39 oi de paraporeuomenoi eblasfhmoun auton kinountes tas kefalas autwn
mat 27:40 kai legontes o kataluwn ton naon kai en trisin hmerais oikodomwn swson seauton ei uios ei tou qeou [--] katabhqi apo tou staurou.
mat 27:41 omoiws kai oi arxiereis empaizontes meta twn grammatewn kai presbuterwn elegon
mat 27:42 allous eswsen eauton ou dunatai swsai basileus israhl estin katabatw nun apo tou staurou kai pisteusomen ep auton.
mat 27:43 pepoiqen epi ton qeon rusasqw nun ei qelei auton eipen gar oti qeou eimi uios.
mat 27:44 to d auto kai oi lhstai oi sustaurwqentes sun autw wneidizon auton.
mat 27:45 apo de ekths wras skotos egeneto epi pasan thn ghn ews wras enaths.
mat 27:46 peri de thn enathn wran anebohsen o ihsous fwnh megalh legwn hli hli lema sabaxqani; tout estin qee mou qee mou inati me egkatelipes;
mat 27:47 tines de twn ekei esthkotwn akousantes elegon oti hlian fwnei outos.
mat 27:48 kai euqews dramwn eis ec autwn kai labwn spoggon plhsas te ocous kai periqeis kalamw epotizen auton.
mat 27:49 oi de loipoi elegon afes idwmen ei erxetai hlias swswn auton.
mat 27:50 o de ihsous palin kracas fwnh megalh afhken to pneuma.
mat 27:51 kai idou to katapetasma tou naou esxisqh ap anwqen ews katw eis duo kai h gh eseisqh kai ai petrai esxisqhsan
mat 27:52 kai ta mnhmeia anewxqhsan kai polla swmata twn kekoimhmenwn agiwn hgerqhsan
mat 27:53 kai ecelqontes ek twn mnhmeiwn meta thn egersin autou eishlqon eis thn agian polin kai enefanisqhsan pollois.
mat 27:54 o de ekatontarxos kai oi met autou thrountes ton ihsoun idontes ton seismon kai ta genomena efobhqhsan sfodra legontes alhqws qeou uios hn outos.
mat 27:55 hsan de ekei gunaikes pollai apo makroqen qewrousai aitines hkolouqhsan tw ihsou apo ths galilaias diakonousai autw
mat 27:56 en ais hn maria h magdalhnh kai maria h tou iakwbou kai iwshf mhthr kai h mhthr twn uiwn zebedaiou.
mat 27:57 oyias de genomenhs hlqen anqrwpos plousios apo arimaqaias tounoma iwshf os kai autos emaqhteuqh tw ihsou
mat 27:58 outos proselqwn tw pilatw hthsato to swma tou ihsou. tote o pilatos ekeleusen apodoqhnai.
mat 27:59 kai labwn to swma o iwshf enetulicen auto en sindoni kaqara
mat 27:60 kai eqhken auto en tw kainw autou mnhmeiw o elatomhsen en th petra kai proskulisas liqon megan th qura tou mnhmeiou aphlqen.
mat 27:61 hn de ekei mariam h magdalhnh kai h allh maria kaqhmenai apenanti tou tafou.
mat 27:62 th de epaurion htis estin meta thn paraskeuhn sunhxqhsan oi arxiereis kai oi farisaioi pros pilaton
mat 27:63 legontes kurie emnhsqhmen oti ekeinos o planos eipen eti zwn meta treis hmeras egeiromai.
mat 27:64 keleuson oun asfalisqhnai ton tafon ews ths triths hmeras mhpote elqontes oi maqhtai autou kleywsin auton kai eipwsin tw law hgerqh apo twn nekrwn kai estai h esxath planh xeirwn ths prwths.
mat 27:65 efh autois o pilatos exete koustwdian upagete asfalisasqe ws oidate.
mat 27:66 oi de poreuqentes hsfalisanto ton tafon sfragisantes ton liqon meta ths koustwdias.
mat 28:1 oye de sabbatwn th epifwskoush eis mian sabbatwn hlqen mariam h magdalhnh kai h allh maria qewrhsai ton tafon.
mat 28:2 kai idou seismos egeneto megas aggelos gar kuriou katabas ec ouranou kai proselqwn apekulisen ton liqon kai ekaqhto epanw autou.
mat 28:3 hn de h eidea autou ws astraph kai to enduma autou leukon ws xiwn.
mat 28:4 apo de tou fobou autou eseisqhsan oi thrountes kai egenhqhsan ws nekroi.
mat 28:5 apokriqeis de o aggelos eipen tais gunaicin mh fobeisqe umeis oida gar oti ihsoun ton estaurwmenon zhteite
mat 28:6 ouk estin wde hgerqh gar kaqws eipen deute idete ton topon opou ekeito.
mat 28:7 kai taxu poreuqeisai eipate tois maqhtais autou oti hgerqh apo twn nekrwn kai idou proagei umas eis thn galilaian ekei auton oyesqe idou eipon umin.
mat 28:8 kai apelqousai taxu apo tou mnhmeiou meta fobou kai xaras megalhs edramon apaggeilai tois maqhtais autou.
mat 28:9 kai idou ihsous uphnthsen autais legwn xairete. ai de proselqousai ekrathsan autou tous podas kai prosekunhsan autw.
mat 28:10 tote legei autais o ihsous mh fobeisqe upagete apaggeilate tois adelfois mou ina apelqwsin eis thn galilaian kakei me oyontai.
mat 28:11 poreuomenwn de autwn idou tines ths koustwdias elqontes eis thn polin aphggeilan tois arxiereusin apanta ta genomena.
mat 28:12 kai sunaxqentes meta twn presbuterwn sumboulion te labontes arguria ikana edwkan tois stratiwtais
mat 28:13 legontes eipate oti oi maqhtai autou nuktos elqontes ekleyan auton hmwn koimwmenwn.
mat 28:14 kai ean akousqh touto epi tou hgemonos hmeis peisomen auton kai umas amerimnous poihsomen.
mat 28:15 oi de labontes ta arguria epoihsan ws edidaxqhsan. kai diefhmisqh o logos outos para ioudaiois mexri ths shmeron hmeras.
mat 28:16 oi de endeka maqhtai eporeuqhsan eis thn galilaian eis to oros ou etacato autois o ihsous
mat 28:17 kai idontes auton prosekunhsan oi de edistasan.
mat 28:18 kai proselqwn o ihsous elalhsen autois legwn edoqh moi pasa ecousia en ouranw kai epi ths ghs.
mat 28:19 poreuqentes oun maqhteusate panta ta eqnh baptizontes autous eis to onoma tou patros kai tou uiou kai tou agiou pneumatos
mat 28:20 didaskontes autous threin panta osa eneteilamhn umin kai idou egw meq umwn eimi pasas tas hmeras ews ths sunteleias tou aiwnos.
mar 1:1 arxh tou euaggeliou ihsou xristou [uiou tou qeou].
mar 1:2 kaqws gegraptai en tw hsaia tw profhth idou apostellw ton aggelon mou pro proswpou sou os kataskeuasei thn odon sou
mar 1:3 fwnh bowntos en th erhmw etoimasate thn odon kuriou euqeias poieite tas tribous autou 
mar 1:4 egeneto iwannhs [--] baptizwn en th erhmw [--] khrusswn baptisma metanoias eis afesin amartiwn.
mar 1:5 kai eceporeueto pros auton pasa h ioudaia xwra kai oi ierosolumitai pantes kai ebaptizonto up autou en tw iordanh potamw ecomologoumenoi tas amartias autwn.
mar 1:6 kai hn o iwannhs endedumenos trixas kamhlou kai zwnhn dermatinhn peri thn osfun autou kai esqiwn akridas kai meli agrion.
mar 1:7 kai ekhrussen legwn erxetai o isxuroteros mou opisw mou ou ouk eimi ikanos kuyas lusai ton imanta twn upodhmatwn autou
mar 1:8 egw ebaptisa umas udati autos de baptisei umas en pneumati agiw.
mar 1:9 kai egeneto en ekeinais tais hmerais hlqen ihsous apo nazaret ths galilaias kai ebaptisqh eis ton iordanhn upo iwannou.
mar 1:10 kai euqus anabainwn ek tou udatos eiden sxizomenous tous ouranous kai to pneuma ws peristeran katabainon eis auton
mar 1:11 kai fwnh egeneto ek twn ouranwn su ei o uios mou o agaphtos en soi eudokhsa.
mar 1:12 kai euqus to pneuma auton ekballei eis thn erhmon.
mar 1:13 kai hn en th erhmw tesserakonta hmeras peirazomenos upo tou satana kai hn meta twn qhriwn kai oi aggeloi dihkonoun autw.
mar 1:14 meta de to paradoqhnai ton iwannhn hlqen o ihsous eis thn galilaian khrusswn to euaggelion tou qeou
mar 1:15 kai legwn oti peplhrwtai o kairos kai hggiken h basileia tou qeou metanoeite kai pisteuete en tw euaggeliw.
mar 1:16 kai paragwn para thn qalassan ths galilaias eiden simwna kai andrean ton adelfon simwnos amfiballontas en th qalassh hsan gar alieis.
mar 1:17 kai eipen autois o ihsous deute opisw mou kai poihsw umas genesqai alieis anqrwpwn.
mar 1:18 kai euqus afentes ta diktua hkolouqhsan autw.
mar 1:19 kai probas oligon eiden iakwbon ton tou zebedaiou kai iwannhn ton adelfon autou kai autous en tw ploiw katartizontas ta diktua
mar 1:20 kai euqus ekalesen autous. kai afentes ton patera autwn zebedaion en tw ploiw meta twn misqwtwn aphlqon opisw autou.
mar 1:21 kai eisporeuontai eis kafarnaoum. kai euqus tois sabbasin eiselqwn eis thn sunagwghn edidasken.
mar 1:22 kai eceplhssonto epi th didaxh autou hn gar didaskwn autous ws ecousian exwn kai oux ws oi grammateis.
mar 1:23 kai euqus hn en th sunagwgh autwn anqrwpos en pneumati akaqartw kai anekracen
mar 1:24 legwn ti hmin kai soi ihsou nazarhne; hlqes apolesai hmas; oida se tis ei o agios tou qeou.
mar 1:25 kai epetimhsen autw o ihsous legwn fimwqhti kai ecelqe ec autou.
mar 1:26 kai sparacan auton to pneuma to akaqarton kai fwnhsan fwnh megalh echlqen ec autou.
mar 1:27 kai eqambhqhsan apantes wste suzhtein pros eautous legontas ti estin touto; didaxh kainh kat ecousian kai tois pneumasi tois akaqartois epitassei kai upakouousin autw.
mar 1:28 kai echlqen h akoh autou euqus pantaxou eis olhn thn perixwron ths galilaias.
mar 1:29 kai euqus ek ths sunagwghs ecelqontes hlqon eis thn oikian simwnos kai andreou meta iakwbou kai iwannou.
mar 1:30 h de penqera simwnos katekeito puressousa kai euqus legousin autw peri auths.
mar 1:31 kai proselqwn hgeiren authn krathsas ths xeiros kai afhken authn o puretos kai dihkonei autois.
mar 1:32 oyias de genomenhs ote edu o hlios eferon pros auton pantas tous kakws exontas kai tous daimonizomenous
mar 1:33 kai hn olh h polis episunhgmenh pros thn quran.
mar 1:34 kai eqerapeusen pollous kakws exontas poikilais nosois kai daimonia polla ecebalen kai ouk hfien lalein ta daimonia oti hdeisan auton.
mar 1:35 kai prwi ennuxa lian anastas echlqen kai aphlqen eis erhmon topon kakei proshuxeto.
mar 1:36 kai katediwcen auton simwn kai oi met autou
mar 1:37 kai euron auton kai legousin autw oti pantes zhtousin se.
mar 1:38 kai legei autois agwmen allaxou eis tas exomenas kwmopoleis ina kai ekei khrucw eis touto gar echlqon.
mar 1:39 kai hlqen khrusswn eis tas sunagwgas autwn eis olhn thn galilaian kai ta daimonia ekballwn.
mar 1:40 kai erxetai pros auton lepros parakalwn auton [--] kai legwn autw oti ean qelhs dunasai me kaqarisai.
mar 1:41 kai splagxnisqeis ekteinas thn xeira autou hyato kai legei autw qelw kaqarisqhti
mar 1:42 kai euqus aphlqen ap autou h lepra kai ekaqarisqh.
mar 1:43 kai embrimhsamenos autw euqus ecebalen auton
mar 1:44 kai legei autw ora mhdeni mhden eiphs alla upage seauton deicon tw ierei kai prosenegke peri tou kaqarismou sou a prosetacen mwushs eis marturion autois.
mar 1:45 o de ecelqwn hrcato khrussein polla kai diafhmizein ton logon wste mhketi auton dunasqai fanerws eis polin eiselqein all ecw ep erhmois topois hn kai hrxonto pros auton pantoqen.
mar 2:1 kai eiselqwn palin eis kafarnaoum di hmerwn hkousqh oti en oikw estin.
mar 2:2 kai sunhxqhsan polloi wste mhketi xwrein mhde ta pros thn quran kai elalei autois ton logon.
mar 2:3 kai erxontai ferontes pros auton paralutikon airomenon upo tessarwn.
mar 2:4 kai mh dunamenoi prosenegkai autw dia ton oxlon apestegasan thn steghn opou hn kai ecorucantes xalwsi ton krabatton opou o paralutikos katekeito.
mar 2:5 kai idwn o ihsous thn pistin autwn legei tw paralutikw teknon afientai sou ai amartiai.
mar 2:6 hsan de tines twn grammatewn ekei kaqhmenoi kai dialogizomenoi en tais kardiais autwn
mar 2:7 ti outos outws lalei; blasfhmei tis dunatai afienai amartias ei mh eis o qeos;
mar 2:8 kai euqus epignous o ihsous tw pneumati autou oti outws dialogizontai en eautois legei autois ti tauta dialogizesqe en tais kardiais umwn;
mar 2:9 ti estin eukopwteron eipein tw paralutikw afientai sou ai amartiai h eipein egeire kai aron ton krabatton sou kai peripatei;
mar 2:10 ina de eidhte oti ecousian exei o uios tou anqrwpou afienai amartias epi ths ghs legei tw paralutikw
mar 2:11 soi legw egeire aron ton krabatton sou kai upage eis ton oikon sou.
mar 2:12 kai hgerqh kai euqus aras ton krabatton echlqen emprosqen pantwn wste ecistasqai pantas kai docazein ton qeon legontas oti outws oudepote eidomen.
mar 2:13 kai echlqen palin para thn qalassan kai pas o oxlos hrxeto pros auton kai edidasken autous.
mar 2:14 kai paragwn eiden [leui] ton tou alfaiou kaqhmenon epi to telwnion kai legei autw akolouqei moi. kai anastas hkolouqhsen autw.
mar 2:15 kai ginetai katakeisqai auton en th oikia autou kai polloi telwnai kai amartwloi sunanekeinto tw ihsou kai tois maqhtais autou hsan gar polloi kai hkolouqoun autw.
mar 2:16 kai oi grammateis [kai oi farisaioi] idontes oti esqiei meta twn amartwlwn kai telwnwn elegon tois maqhtais autou oti meta twn telwnwn kai amartwlwn [o didaskalos umwn esqiei kai pinei];
mar 2:17 kai akousas o ihsous legei autois oti ou xreian exousin oi isxuontes iatrou all oi kakws exontes ouk hlqon kalesai dikaious alla amartwlous.
mar 2:18 kai hsan oi maqhtai iwannou kai oi farisaioi nhsteuontes. kai erxontai kai legousin autw dia ti oi maqhtai iwannou kai oi maqhtai twn farisaiwn nhsteuousin oi de soi maqhtai ou nhsteuousin;
mar 2:19 kai eipen autois o ihsous mh dunantai oi uioi tou numfwnos en w o numfios met autwn estin nhsteuein; oson xronon exousin ton numfion met autwn ou dunantai nhsteuein
mar 2:20 eleusontai de hmerai otan aparqh ap autwn o numfios kai tote nhsteusousin en ekeinh th hmera.
mar 2:21 oudeis epiblhma rakous agnafou epiraptei epi imation palaion ei de mh airei to plhrwma ap autou to kainon tou palaiou kai xeiron sxisma ginetai.
mar 2:22 kai oudeis ballei oinon neon eis askous palaious ei de mh rhcei o oinos tous askous kai o oinos [ekeitai] kai oi askoi alla oinon neon eis askous kainous.
mar 2:23 kai egeneto auton en tois sabbasin paraporeuesqai dia twn sporimwn kai oi maqhtai autou hrcanto odon poiein tillontes tous staxuas.
mar 2:24 kai oi farisaioi elegon autw ide ti poiousin tois sabbasin o ouk ecestin;
mar 2:25 kai legei autois oudepote anegnwte ti epoihsen dauid ote xreian esxen kai epeinasen autos kai oi met autou;
mar 2:26 pws eishlqen eis ton oikon tou qeou epi abiaqar arxierews kai tous artous ths proqesews efagen ous ouk ecestin fagein ei mh tous iereis kai edwken kai tois sun autw ousin;
mar 2:27 kai elegen autois to sabbaton dia ton anqrwpon egeneto kai oux o anqrwpos dia to sabbaton
mar 2:28 wste kurios estin o uios tou anqrwpou kai tou sabbatou.
mar 3:1 kai eishlqen palin eis thn sunagwghn. kai hn ekei anqrwpos echrammenhn exwn thn xeira
mar 3:2 kai parethroun auton ei tois sabbasin qerapeusei auton ina kathgorhswsin autou.
mar 3:3 kai legei tw anqrwpw tw thn chran xeira exonti egeire eis to meson.
mar 3:4 kai legei autois ecestin tois sabbasin agaqon poihsai h kakopoihsai yuxhn swsai h apokteinai; oi de esiwpwn.
mar 3:5 kai peribleyamenos autous met orghs sullupoumenos epi th pwrwsei ths kardias autwn legei tw anqrwpw ekteinon thn xeira. kai eceteinen kai apekatestaqh h xeir autou.
mar 3:6 kai ecelqontes oi farisaioi euqus meta twn hrwdianwn sumboulion edidoun kat autou opws auton apoleswsin.
mar 3:7 kai o ihsous meta twn maqhtwn autou anexwrhsen pros thn qalassan kai polu plhqos apo ths galilaias hkolouqhsen kai apo ths ioudaias
mar 3:8 kai apo ierosolumwn kai apo ths idoumaias kai peran tou iordanou kai peri turon kai sidwna plhqos polu akouontes osa epoiei hlqon pros auton.
mar 3:9 kai eipen tois maqhtais autou ina ploiarion proskarterh autw dia ton oxlon ina mh qlibwsin auton
mar 3:10 pollous gar eqerapeusen wste epipiptein autw ina autou aywntai osoi eixon mastigas.
mar 3:11 kai ta pneumata ta akaqarta otan auton eqewroun prosepipton autw kai ekrazon legontes oti su ei o uios tou qeou.
mar 3:12 kai polla epetima autois ina mh auton faneron poihswsin.
mar 3:13 kai anabainei eis to oros kai proskaleitai ous hqelen autos kai aphlqon pros auton.
mar 3:14 kai epoihsen dwdeka ous kai apostolous wnomasen ina wsin met autou kai ina apostellh autous khrussein
mar 3:15 kai exein ecousian ekballein ta daimonia
mar 3:16 kai epoihsen tous dwdeka kai epeqhken onoma tw simwni petron
mar 3:17 kai iakwbon ton tou zebedaiou kai iwannhn ton adelfon tou iakwbou kai epeqhken autois onomata boanhrges o estin uioi bronths
mar 3:18 kai andrean kai filippon kai barqolomaion kai maqqaion kai qwman kai iakwbon ton tou alfaiou kai qaddaion kai simwna ton kananaion
mar 3:19 kai ioudan iskariwq os kai paredwken auton.
mar 3:20 kai erxetai eis oikon kai sunerxetai palin o oxlos wste mh dunasqai autous mhde arton fagein.
mar 3:21 kai akousantes oi par autou echlqon krathsai auton elegon gar oti ecesth.
mar 3:22 kai oi grammateis oi apo ierosolumwn katabantes elegon oti beelzeboul exei kai oti en tw arxonti twn daimoniwn ekballei ta daimonia.
mar 3:23 kai proskalesamenos autous en parabolais elegen autois pws dunatai satanas satanan ekballein;
mar 3:24 kai ean basileia ef eauthn merisqh ou dunatai staqhnai h basileia ekeinh
mar 3:25 kai ean oikia ef eauthn merisqh ou dunhsetai h oikia ekeinh staqhnai.
mar 3:26 kai ei o satanas anesth ef eauton kai emerisqh ou dunatai sthnai alla telos exei.
mar 3:27 all ou dunatai oudeis eis thn oikian tou isxurou eiselqwn ta skeuh autou diarpasai ean mh prwton ton isxuron dhsh kai tote thn oikian autou diarpasei.
mar 3:28 amhn legw umin oti panta afeqhsetai tois uiois twn anqrwpwn ta amarthmata kai ai blasfhmiai osa ean blasfhmhswsin
mar 3:29 os d an blasfhmhsh eis to pneuma to agion ouk exei afesin eis ton aiwna alla enoxos estin aiwniou amarthmatos 
mar 3:30 oti elegon pneuma akaqarton exei.
mar 3:31 kai erxetai h mhthr autou kai oi adelfoi autou kai ecw sthkontes apesteilan pros auton kalountes auton.
mar 3:32 kai ekaqhto peri auton oxlos kai legousin autw idou h mhthr sou kai oi adelfoi sou [--] ecw zhtousin se.
mar 3:33 kai apokriqeis autois legei tis estin h mhthr mou kai oi adelfoi mou;
mar 3:34 kai peribleyamenos tous peri auton kuklw kaqhmenous legei ide h mhthr mou kai oi adelfoi mou.
mar 3:35 os gar an poihsh to qelhma tou qeou outos adelfos mou kai adelfh kai mhthr estin.
mar 4:1 kai palin hrcato didaskein para thn qalassan. kai sunagetai pros auton oxlos pleistos wste auton eis ploion embanta kaqhsqai en th qalassh kai pas o oxlos pros thn qalassan epi ths ghs hsan.
mar 4:2 kai edidasken autous en parabolais polla kai elegen autois en th didaxh autou
mar 4:3 akouete. idou echlqen o speirwn speirai.
mar 4:4 kai egeneto en tw speirein o men epesen para thn odon kai hlqen ta peteina kai katefagen auto.
mar 4:5 kai allo epesen epi to petrwdes opou ouk eixen ghn pollhn kai euqus ecaneteilen dia to mh exein baqos ghs
mar 4:6 kai ote aneteilen o hlios ekaumatisqh kai dia to mh exein rizan echranqh.
mar 4:7 kai allo epesen eis tas akanqas kai anebhsan ai akanqai kai sunepnican auto kai karpon ouk edwken.
mar 4:8 kai alla epesen eis thn ghn thn kalhn kai edidou karpon anabainonta kai aucanomena kai eferen en triakonta kai en echkonta kai en ekaton.
mar 4:9 kai elegen os exei wta akouein akouetw.
mar 4:10 kai ote egeneto kata monas hrwtwn auton oi peri auton sun tois dwdeka tas parabolas.
mar 4:11 kai elegen autois umin to musthrion dedotai ths basileias tou qeou ekeinois de tois ecw en parabolais ta panta ginetai
mar 4:12 ina blepontes blepwsin kai mh idwsin kai akouontes akouwsin kai mh suniwsin mhpote epistreywsin kai afeqh autois.
mar 4:13 kai legei autois ouk oidate thn parabolhn tauthn kai pws pasas tas parabolas gnwsesqe;
mar 4:14 o speirwn ton logon speirei.
mar 4:15 outoi de eisin oi para thn odon opou speiretai o logos kai otan akouswsin euqus erxetai o satanas kai airei ton logon ton esparmenon [en autois].
mar 4:16 kai outoi eisin oi epi ta petrwdh speiromenoi oi otan akouswsin ton logon euqus meta xaras lambanousin auton
mar 4:17 kai ouk exousin rizan en eautois alla proskairoi eisin eita genomenhs qliyews h diwgmou dia ton logon euqus skandalizontai.
mar 4:18 kai alloi eisin oi eis tas akanqas speiromenoi outoi eisin oi ton logon akousantes
mar 4:19 kai ai merimnai tou aiwnos kai h apath tou ploutou kai ai peri ta loipa epiqumiai eisporeuomenai sumpnigousin ton logon kai akarpos ginetai.
mar 4:20 kai ekeinoi eisin oi epi thn ghn thn kalhn sparentes oitines akouousin ton logon kai paradexontai kai karpoforousin en triakonta kai en echkonta kai en ekaton.
mar 4:21 kai elegen autois mhti erxetai o luxnos ina upo ton modion teqh h upo thn klinhn; oux ina epi thn luxnian teqh;
mar 4:22 ou gar estin krupton ean mh ina fanerwqh oude egeneto apokrufon all ina elqh eis faneron.
mar 4:23 ei tis exei wta akouein akouetw.
mar 4:24 kai elegen autois blepete ti akouete. en w metrw metreite metrhqhsetai umin kai prosteqhsetai umin [tois akouousin].
mar 4:25 os gar exei doqhsetai autw kai os ouk exei kai o exei arqhsetai ap autou.
mar 4:26 kai elegen outws estin h basileia tou qeou ws anqrwpos balh ton sporon epi ths ghs
mar 4:27 kai kaqeudh kai egeirhtai nukta kai hmeran kai o sporos blasta kai mhkunhtai ws ouk oiden autos.
mar 4:28 automath h gh karpoforei prwton xorton eita staxun eita plhrhs siton en tw staxui.
mar 4:29 otan de paradoi o karpos euqus apostellei to drepanon oti paresthken o qerismos.
mar 4:30 kai elegen pws omoiwswmen thn basileian tou qeou h en tini authn parabolh qwmen;
mar 4:31 ws kokkw sinapews os otan sparh epi ths ghs mikroteron on pantwn twn spermatwn twn epi ths ghs
mar 4:32 kai otan sparh anabainei kai ginetai meizon pantwn twn laxanwn kai poiei kladous megalous wste dunasqai upo thn skian autou ta peteina tou ouranou kataskhnoun.
mar 4:33 kai toiautais parabolais pollais elalei autois ton logon kaqws hdunanto akouein
mar 4:34 xwris de parabolhs ouk elalei autois kat idian de tois idiois maqhtais epeluen panta.
mar 4:35 kai legei autois en ekeinh th hmera oyias genomenhs dielqwmen eis to peran.
mar 4:36 kai afentes ton oxlon paralambanousin auton ws hn en tw ploiw kai alla ploia hn met autou.
mar 4:37 kai ginetai lailay megalh anemou kai ta kumata epeballen eis to ploion wste hdh gemizesqai to ploion.
mar 4:38 kai autos hn en th prumnh epi to proskefalaion kaqeudwn kai egeirousin auton kai legousin autw didaskale ou melei soi oti apollumeqa;
mar 4:39 kai diegerqeis epetimhsen tw anemw kai eipen th qalassh siwpa pefimwso. kai ekopasen o anemos kai egeneto galhnh megalh.
mar 4:40 kai eipen autois ti deiloi este; oupw exete pistin;
mar 4:41 kai efobhqhsan fobon megan kai elegon pros allhlous tis ara outos estin oti kai o anemos kai h qalassa upakouei autw;
mar 5:1 kai hlqon eis to peran ths qalasshs eis thn xwran twn gerashnwn.
mar 5:2 kai ecelqontos autou ek tou ploiou euqus uphnthsen autw ek twn mnhmeiwn anqrwpos en pneumati akaqartw
mar 5:3 os thn katoikhsin eixen en tois mnhmasin kai oude alusei ouketi oudeis edunato auton dhsai
mar 5:4 dia to auton pollakis pedais kai alusesin dedesqai kai diespasqai up autou tas aluseis kai tas pedas suntetrifqai kai oudeis isxuen auton damasai
mar 5:5 kai dia pantos nuktos kai hmeras en tois mnhmasin kai en tois oresin hn krazwn kai katakoptwn eauton liqois.
mar 5:6 kai idwn ton ihsoun apo makroqen edramen kai prosekunhsen autw
mar 5:7 kai kracas fwnh megalh legei ti emoi kai soi ihsou uie tou qeou tou uyistou; orkizw se ton qeon mh me basanishs.
mar 5:8 elegen gar autw ecelqe to pneuma to akaqarton ek tou anqrwpou.
mar 5:9 kai ephrwta auton ti onoma soi; kai legei autw legiwn onoma moi oti polloi esmen.
mar 5:10 kai parekalei auton polla ina mh auta aposteilh ecw ths xwras.
mar 5:11 hn de ekei pros tw orei agelh xoirwn megalh boskomenh
mar 5:12 kai parekalesan auton legontes pemyon hmas eis tous xoirous ina eis autous eiselqwmen.
mar 5:13 kai epetreyen autois. kai ecelqonta ta pneumata ta akaqarta eishlqon eis tous xoirous kai wrmhsen h agelh kata tou krhmnou eis thn qalassan ws disxilioi kai epnigonto en th qalassh.
mar 5:14 kai oi boskontes autous efugon kai aphggeilan eis thn polin kai eis tous agrous kai hlqon idein ti estin to gegonos.
mar 5:15 kai erxontai pros ton ihsoun kai qewrousin ton daimonizomenon kaqhmenon imatismenon kai swfronounta ton esxhkota ton legiwna kai efobhqhsan.
mar 5:16 kai dihghsanto autois oi idontes pws egeneto tw daimonizomenw kai peri twn xoirwn.
mar 5:17 kai hrcanto parakalein auton apelqein apo twn oriwn autwn.
mar 5:18 kai embainontos autou eis to ploion parekalei auton o daimonisqeis ina met autou h.
mar 5:19 kai ouk afhken auton alla legei autw upage eis ton oikon sou pros tous sous kai apaggeilon autois osa o kurios soi pepoihken kai hlehsen se.
mar 5:20 kai aphlqen kai hrcato khrussein en th dekapolei osa epoihsen autw o ihsous kai pantes eqaumazon.
mar 5:21 kai diaperasantos tou ihsou en tw ploiw palin eis to peran sunhxqh oxlos polus ep auton kai hn para thn qalassan.
mar 5:22 kai erxetai eis twn arxisunagwgwn onomati iairos kai idwn auton piptei pros tous podas autou
mar 5:23 kai parakalei auton polla legwn oti to qugatrion mou esxatws exei ina elqwn epiqhs tas xeiras auth ina swqh kai zhsh.
mar 5:24 kai aphlqen met autou. kai hkolouqei autw oxlos polus kai suneqlibon auton.
mar 5:25 kai gunh ousa en rusei aimatos dwdeka eth
mar 5:26 kai polla paqousa upo pollwn iatrwn kai dapanhsasa ta par auths panta kai mhden wfelhqeisa alla mallon eis to xeiron elqousa
mar 5:27 akousasa peri tou ihsou elqousa en tw oxlw opisqen hyato tou imatiou autou
mar 5:28 elegen gar oti ean aywmai kan twn imatiwn autou swqhsomai.
mar 5:29 kai euqus echranqh h phgh tou aimatos auths kai egnw tw swmati oti iatai apo ths mastigos.
mar 5:30 kai euqus o ihsous epignous en eautw thn ec autou dunamin ecelqousan epistrafeis en tw oxlw elegen tis mou hyato twn imatiwn;
mar 5:31 kai elegon autw oi maqhtai autou blepeis ton oxlon sunqlibonta se kai legeis tis mou hyato;
mar 5:32 kai perieblepeto idein thn touto poihsasan.
mar 5:33 h de gunh fobhqeisa kai tremousa eiduia o gegonen auth hlqen kai prosepesen autw kai eipen autw pasan thn alhqeian.
mar 5:34 o de eipen auth qugathr h pistis sou seswken se upage eis eirhnhn kai isqi ugihs apo ths mastigos sou.
mar 5:35 eti autou lalountos erxontai apo tou arxisunagwgou legontes oti h qugathr sou apeqanen ti eti skulleis ton didaskalon;
mar 5:36 o de ihsous [akousas] ton logon laloumenon legei tw arxisunagwgw mh fobou monon pisteue.
mar 5:37 kai ouk afhken oudena met autou sunakolouqhsai ei mh ton petron kai iakwbon kai iwannhn ton adelfon iakwbou.
mar 5:38 kai erxontai eis ton oikon tou arxisunagwgou kai qewrei qorubon kai klaiontas kai alalazontas polla
mar 5:39 kai eiselqwn legei autois ti qorubeisqe kai klaiete; to paidion ouk apeqanen alla kaqeudei.
mar 5:40 kai kategelwn autou. autos de ekbalwn pantas paralambanei ton patera tou paidiou kai thn mhtera kai tous met autou kai eisporeuetai opou hn to paidion
mar 5:41 kai krathsas ths xeiros tou paidiou legei auth taliqa koum o estin meqermhneuomenon to korasion soi legw egeire.
mar 5:42 kai euqus anesth to korasion kai periepatei hn gar etwn dwdeka. kai ecesthsan euqus ekstasei megalh.
mar 5:43 kai diesteilato autois polla ina mhdeis gnoi touto kai eipen doqhnai auth fagein.
mar 6:1 kai echlqen ekeiqen kai erxetai eis thn patrida autou kai akolouqousin autw oi maqhtai autou.
mar 6:2 kai genomenou sabbatou hrcato didaskein en th sunagwgh kai polloi akouontes eceplhssonto legontes poqen toutw tauta kai tis h sofia h doqeisa toutw kai ai dunameis toiautai dia twn xeirwn autou ginomenai;
mar 6:3 oux outos estin o tektwn o uios ths marias kai adelfos iakwbou kai iwshtos kai iouda kai simwnos; kai ouk eisin ai adelfai autou wde pros hmas; kai eskandalizonto en autw.
mar 6:4 kai elegen autois o ihsous oti ouk estin profhths atimos ei mh en th patridi autou kai en tois suggeneusin autou kai en th oikia autou.
mar 6:5 kai ouk edunato ekei poihsai oudemian dunamin ei mh oligois arrwstois epiqeis tas xeiras eqerapeusen
mar 6:6 kai eqaumazen dia thn apistian autwn. kai perihgen tas kwmas kuklw didaskwn.
mar 6:7 kai proskaleitai tous dwdeka kai hrcato autous apostellein duo duo kai edidou autois ecousian twn pneumatwn twn akaqartwn
mar 6:8 kai parhggeilen autois ina mhden airwsin eis odon ei mh rabdon monon mh arton mh phran mh eis thn zwnhn xalkon
mar 6:9 alla upodedemenous sandalia kai mh endushsqe duo xitwnas.
mar 6:10 kai elegen autois opou ean eiselqhte eis oikian ekei menete ews an ecelqhte ekeiqen.
mar 6:11 kai os an topos mh dechtai umas mhde akouswsin umwn ekporeuomenoi ekeiqen ektinacate ton xoun ton upokatw twn podwn umwn eis marturion autois.
mar 6:12 kai ecelqontes ekhrucan ina metanowsin
mar 6:13 kai daimonia polla eceballon kai hleifon elaiw pollous arrwstous kai eqerapeuon.
mar 6:14 kai hkousen o basileus hrwdhs faneron gar egeneto to onoma autou kai elegon oti iwannhs o baptizwn eghgertai ek nekrwn kai dia touto energousin ai dunameis en autw.
mar 6:15 alloi de elegon oti hlias estin alloi de elegon oti profhths ws eis twn profhtwn.
mar 6:16 akousas de o hrwdhs elegen on egw apekefalisa iwannhn outos hgerqh.
mar 6:17 autos gar o hrwdhs aposteilas ekrathsen ton iwannhn kai edhsen auton en fulakh dia hrwdiada thn gunaika filippou tou adelfou autou oti authn egamhsen
mar 6:18 elegen gar o iwannhs tw hrwdh oti ouk ecestin soi exein thn gunaika tou adelfou sou.
mar 6:19 h de hrwdias eneixen autw kai hqelen auton apokteinai kai ouk hdunato
mar 6:20 o gar hrwdhs efobeito ton iwannhn eidws auton andra dikaion kai agion kai sunethrei auton kai akousas autou polla hporei kai hdews autou hkouen.
mar 6:21 kai genomenhs hmeras eukairou ote hrwdhs tois genesiois autou deipnon epoihsen tois megistasin autou kai tois xiliarxois kai tois prwtois ths galilaias
mar 6:22 kai eiselqoushs ths qugatros [ths] hrwdiados kai orxhsamenhs hresen tw hrwdh kai tois sunanakeimenois. eipen o basileus tw korasiw aithson me o ean qelhs kai dwsw soi
mar 6:23 kai wmosen auth [--] o ti ean me aithshs dwsw soi ews hmisous ths basileias mou.
mar 6:24 kai ecelqousa eipen th mhtri auths ti aithswmai; h de eipen thn kefalhn iwannou tou baptizontos.
mar 6:25 kai eiselqousa euqus meta spoudhs pros ton basilea hthsato legousa qelw ina ecauths dws moi epi pinaki thn kefalhn iwannou tou baptistou.
mar 6:26 kai perilupos genomenos o basileus dia tous orkous kai tous anakeimenous ouk hqelhsen aqethsai authn
mar 6:27 kai euqus aposteilas o basileus spekoulatora epetacen enegkai thn kefalhn autou. kai apelqwn apekefalisen auton en th fulakh
mar 6:28 kai hnegken thn kefalhn autou epi pinaki kai edwken authn tw korasiw kai to korasion edwken authn th mhtri auths.
mar 6:29 kai akousantes oi maqhtai autou hlqon kai hran to ptwma autou kai eqhkan auto en mnhmeiw.
mar 6:30 kai sunagontai oi apostoloi pros ton ihsoun kai aphggeilan autw panta osa epoihsan kai osa edidacan.
mar 6:31 kai legei autois deute umeis autoi kat idian eis erhmon topon kai anapausasqe oligon. hsan gar oi erxomenoi kai oi upagontes polloi kai oude fagein eukairoun.
mar 6:32 kai aphlqon en tw ploiw eis erhmon topon kat idian.
mar 6:33 kai eidon autous upagontas kai epegnwsan polloi kai pezh apo paswn twn polewn sunedramon ekei kai prohlqon autous.
mar 6:34 kai ecelqwn eiden polun oxlon kai esplagxnisqh ep autous oti hsan ws probata mh exonta poimena kai hrcato didaskein autous polla.
mar 6:35 kai hdh wras pollhs genomenhs proselqontes autw oi maqhtai autou elegon oti erhmos estin o topos kai hdh wra pollh
mar 6:36 apoluson autous ina apelqontes eis tous kuklw agrous kai kwmas agoraswsin eautois ti fagwsin.
mar 6:37 o de apokriqeis eipen autois dote autois umeis fagein. kai legousin autw apelqontes agoraswmen dhnariwn diakosiwn artous kai dwsomen autois fagein;
mar 6:38 o de legei autois posous artous exete; upagete idete. kai gnontes legousin pente kai duo ixquas.
mar 6:39 kai epetacen autois anaklinai pantas sumposia sumposia epi tw xlwrw xortw.
mar 6:40 kai anepesan prasiai prasiai kata ekaton kai kata penthkonta.
mar 6:41 kai labwn tous pente artous kai tous duo ixquas anableyas eis ton ouranon euloghsen kai kateklasen tous artous kai edidou tois maqhtais autou ina paratiqwsin autois kai tous duo ixquas emerisen pasin.
mar 6:42 kai efagon pantes kai exortasqhsan
mar 6:43 kai hran klasmata dwdeka kofinwn plhrwmata kai apo twn ixquwn.
mar 6:44 kai hsan oi fagontes [--] pentakisxilioi andres.
mar 6:45 kai euqus hnagkasen tous maqhtas autou embhnai eis to ploion kai proagein eis to peran pros bhqsaidan ews autos apoluei ton oxlon.
mar 6:46 kai apotacamenos autois aphlqen eis to oros proseucasqai.
mar 6:47 kai oyias genomenhs hn to ploion en mesw ths qalasshs kai autos monos epi ths ghs.
mar 6:48 kai idwn autous basanizomenous en tw elaunein hn gar o anemos enantios autois peri tetarthn fulakhn ths nuktos erxetai pros autous peripatwn epi ths qalasshs kai hqelen parelqein autous.
mar 6:49 oi de idontes auton epi ths qalasshs peripatounta edocan oti fantasma estin kai anekracan
mar 6:50 pantes gar auton eidon kai etaraxqhsan. o de euqus elalhsen met autwn kai legei autois qarseite egw eimi mh fobeisqe.
mar 6:51 kai anebh pros autous eis to ploion kai ekopasen o anemos. kai lian ek perissou en eautois ecistanto
mar 6:52 ou gar sunhkan epi tois artois all hn autwn h kardia pepwrwmenh.
mar 6:53 kai diaperasantes epi thn ghn hlqon eis gennhsaret kai proswrmisqhsan.
mar 6:54 kai ecelqontwn autwn ek tou ploiou euqus epignontes auton
mar 6:55 periedramon olhn thn xwran ekeinhn kai hrcanto epi tois krabattois tous kakws exontas periferein opou hkouon oti estin.
mar 6:56 kai opou an eiseporeueto eis kwmas h eis poleis h eis agrous en tais agorais etiqesan tous asqenountas kai parekaloun auton ina kan tou kraspedou tou imatiou autou aywntai kai osoi an hyanto autou eswzonto.
mar 7:1 kai sunagontai pros auton oi farisaioi kai tines twn grammatewn elqontes apo ierosolumwn
mar 7:2 kai idontes tinas twn maqhtwn autou oti koinais xersin tout estin aniptois esqiousin tous artous
mar 7:3 oi gar farisaioi kai pantes oi ioudaioi ean mh [--] niywntai tas xeiras ouk esqiousin kratountes thn paradosin twn presbuterwn
mar 7:4 kai ap agoras ean mh [ravtiswvtai] ouk esqiousin kai alla polla estin a parelabon kratein baptismous pothriwn kai cestwn kai xalkiwn kai klinwn 
mar 7:5 kai eperwtwsin auton oi farisaioi kai oi grammateis dia ti ou peripatousin oi maqhtai sou kata thn paradosin twn presbuterwn alla koinais xersin esqiousin ton arton;
mar 7:6 o de eipen autois kalws eprofhteusen hsaias peri umwn twn upokritwn ws gegraptai oti outos o laos tois xeilesin me tima h de kardia autwn porrw apexei ap emou
mar 7:7 mathn de sebontai me didaskontes didaskalias entalmata anqrwpwn.
mar 7:8 afentes thn entolhn tou qeou krateite thn paradosin twn anqrwpwn.
mar 7:9 kai elegen autois kalws aqeteite thn entolhn tou qeou ina thn paradosin umwn [thrnshte].
mar 7:10 mwushs gar eipen tima ton patera sou kai thn mhtera sou kai o kakologwn patera h mhtera qanatw teleutatw
mar 7:11 umeis de legete ean eiph anqrwpos tw patri h th mhtri korban o estin dwron o ean ec emou wfelhqhs
mar 7:12 ouketi afiete auton ouden poihsai tw patri h th mhtri
mar 7:13 akurountes ton logon tou qeou th paradosei umwn h paredwkate kai paromoia toiauta polla poieite.
mar 7:14 kai proskalesamenos palin ton oxlon elegen autois akousate mou pantes kai sunete.
mar 7:15 ouden estin ecwqen tou anqrwpou eisporeuomenon eis auton o dunatai koinwsai auton alla ta ek tou anqrwpou ekporeuomena estin ta koinounta ton anqrwpon.
mar 7:16 [--]
mar 7:17 kai ote eishlqen eis oikon apo tou oxlou ephrwtwn auton oi maqhtai autou thn parabolhn.
mar 7:18 kai legei autois outws kai umeis asunetoi este; ou noeite oti pan to ecwqen eisporeuomenon eis ton anqrwpon ou dunatai auton koinwsai
mar 7:19 oti ouk eisporeuetai autou eis thn kardian all eis thn koilian kai eis ton afedrwna ekporeuetai; kaqarizwn panta ta brwmata.
mar 7:20 elegen de oti to ek tou anqrwpou ekporeuomenon ekeino koinoi ton anqrwpon
mar 7:21 eswqen gar ek ths kardias twn anqrwpwn oi dialogismoi oi kakoi ekporeuontai porneiai klopai fonoi
mar 7:22 moixeiai pleoneciai ponhriai dolos aselgeia ofqalmos ponhros blasfhmia uperhfania afrosunh
mar 7:23 panta tauta ta ponhra eswqen ekporeuetai kai koinoi ton anqrwpon.
mar 7:24 ekeiqen de anastas aphlqen eis ta oria turou [kai sidwnos]. kai eiselqwn eis oikian oudena hqelen gnwnai kai ouk hdunhqh laqein
mar 7:25 all euqus akousasa gunh peri autou hs eixen to qugatrion auths pneuma akaqarton elqousa prosepesen pros tous podas autou
mar 7:26 h de gunh hn ellhnis surofoinikissa tw genei kai hrwta auton ina to daimonion ekbalh ek ths qugatros auths.
mar 7:27 kai elegen auth afes prwton xortasqhnai ta tekna ou gar estin kalon labein ton arton twn teknwn kai tois kunariois balein.
mar 7:28 h de apekriqh kai legei autw [nai] kurie kai ta kunaria upokatw ths trapezhs esqiousin apo twn yixiwn twn paidiwn.
mar 7:29 kai eipen auth dia touton ton logon upage ecelhluqen ek ths qugatros sou to daimonion.
mar 7:30 kai apelqousa eis ton oikon auths euren to paidion beblhmenon epi thn klinhn kai to daimonion ecelhluqos.
mar 7:31 kai palin ecelqwn ek twn oriwn turou hlqen dia sidwnos eis thn qalassan ths galilaias ana meson twn oriwn dekapolews.
mar 7:32 kai ferousin autw kwfon kai mogilalon kai parakalousin auton ina epiqh autw thn xeira.
mar 7:33 kai apolabomenos auton apo tou oxlou kat idian ebalen tous daktulous autou eis ta wta autou kai ptusas hyato ths glwsshs autou
mar 7:34 kai anableyas eis ton ouranon estenacen kai legei autw effaqa o estin dianoixqhti.
mar 7:35 kai euqews hnoighsan autou ai akoai kai eluqh o desmos ths glwsshs autou kai elalei orqws.
mar 7:36 kai diesteilato autois ina mhdeni legwsin oson de autois diestelleto autoi mallon perissoteron ekhrusson.
mar 7:37 kai uperperissws eceplhssonto legontes kalws panta pepoihken kai tous kwfous poiei akouein kai tous alalous lalein.
mar 8:1 en ekeinais tais hmerais palin pollou oxlou ontos kai mh exontwn ti fagwsin proskalesamenos tous maqhtas legei autois
mar 8:2 splagxnizomai epi ton oxlon oti hdh hmerai treis prosmenousin moi kai ouk exousin ti fagwsin
mar 8:3 kai ean apolusw autous nhsteis eis oikon autwn ekluqhsontai en th odw kai tines autwn apo makroqen hkasin.
mar 8:4 kai apekriqhsan autw oi maqhtai autou oti poqen toutous dunhsetai tis wde xortasai artwn ep erhmias;
mar 8:5 kai hrwta autous posous exete artous; oi de eipan epta.
mar 8:6 kai paraggellei tw oxlw anapesein epi ths ghs kai labwn tous epta artous euxaristhsas eklasen kai edidou tois maqhtais autou ina paratiqwsin kai pareqhkan tw oxlw.
mar 8:7 kai eixon ixqudia oliga kai euloghsas auta eipen kai tauta paratiqenai.
mar 8:8 kai efagon kai exortasqhsan kai hran perisseumata klasmatwn epta spuridas.
mar 8:9 hsan de ws tetrakisxilioi. kai apelusen autous.
mar 8:10 kai euqus embas eis to ploion meta twn maqhtwn autou hlqen eis ta merh dalmanouqa.
mar 8:11 kai echlqon oi farisaioi kai hrcanto suzhtein autw zhtountes par autou shmeion apo tou ouranou peirazontes auton.
mar 8:12 kai anastenacas tw pneumati autou legei ti h genea auth zhtei shmeion; amhn legw umin ei doqhsetai th genea tauth shmeion.
mar 8:13 kai afeis autous palin embas aphlqen eis to peran.
mar 8:14 kai epelaqonto labein artous kai ei mh ena arton ouk eixon meq eautwn en tw ploiw.
mar 8:15 kai diestelleto autois legwn orate blepete apo ths zumhs twn farisaiwn kai ths zumhs hrwdou.
mar 8:16 kai dielogizonto pros allhlous oti artous ouk exousin.
mar 8:17 kai gnous legei autois ti dialogizesqe oti artous ouk exete; oupw noeite oude suniete; pepwrwmenhn exete thn kardian umwn;
mar 8:18 ofqalmous exontes ou blepete kai wta exontes ouk akouete; kai ou mnhmoneuete
mar 8:19 ote tous pente artous eklasa eis tous pentakisxilious posous kofinous klasmatwn plhreis hrate; legousin autw dwdeka.
mar 8:20 ote tous epta eis tous tetrakisxilious poswn spuridwn plhrwmata klasmatwn hrate; kai legousin autw epta.
mar 8:21 kai elegen autois oupw suniete;
mar 8:22 kai erxontai eis bhqsaidan. kai ferousin autw tuflon kai parakalousin auton ina autou ayhtai.
mar 8:23 kai epilabomenos ths xeiros tou tuflou echnegken auton ecw ths kwmhs kai ptusas eis ta ommata autou epiqeis tas xeiras autw ephrwta auton ei ti blepeis;
mar 8:24 kai anableyas elegen blepw tous anqrwpous oti ws dendra orw peripatountas.
mar 8:25 eita palin epeqhken tas xeiras epi tous ofqalmous autou kai diebleyen kai apekatesth kai eneblepen thlaugws apanta.
mar 8:26 kai apesteilen auton eis oikon autou legwn mhde eis thn kwmhn eiselqhs.
mar 8:27 kai echlqen o ihsous kai oi maqhtai autou eis tas kwmas kaisareias ths filippou kai en th odw ephrwta tous maqhtas autou legwn autois tina me legousin oi anqrwpoi einai;
mar 8:28 oi de eipan autw legontes oti iwannhn ton baptisthn kai alloi hlian alloi de oti eis twn profhtwn.
mar 8:29 kai autos ephrwta autous umeis de tina me legete einai; apokriqeis o petros legei autw su ei o xristos.
mar 8:30 kai epetimhsen autois ina mhdeni legwsin peri autou.
mar 8:31 kai hrcato didaskein autous oti dei ton uion tou anqrwpou polla paqein kai apodokimasqhnai upo twn presbuterwn kai twn arxierewn kai twn grammatewn kai apoktanqhnai kai meta treis hmeras anasthnai
mar 8:32 kai parrhsia ton logon elalei. kai proslabomenos o petros auton hrcato epitiman autw.
mar 8:33 o de epistrafeis kai idwn tous maqhtas autou epetimhsen petrw kai legei upage opisw mou satana oti ou froneis ta tou qeou alla ta twn anqrwpwn.
mar 8:34 kai proskalesamenos ton oxlon sun tois maqhtais autou eipen autois ei tis qelei opisw mou akolouqein aparnhsasqw eauton kai aratw ton stauron autou kai akolouqeitw moi.
mar 8:35 os gar ean qelh thn yuxhn autou swsai apolesei authn os d an apolesei thn yuxhn autou eneken emou kai tou euaggeliou swsei authn.
mar 8:36 ti gar wfelei anqrwpon kerdhsai ton kosmon olon kai zhmiwqhnai thn yuxhn autou;
mar 8:37 ti gar doi anqrwpos antallagma ths yuxhs autou;
mar 8:38 os gar ean epaisxunqh me kai tous emous [--] en th genea tauth th moixalidi kai amartwlw kai o uios tou anqrwpou epaisxunqhsetai auton otan elqh en th doch tou patros autou meta twn aggelwn twn agiwn.
mar 9:1 kai elegen autois amhn legw umin oti eisin tines wde twn esthkotwn oitines ou mh geuswntai qanatou ews an idwsin thn basileian tou qeou elhluquian en dunamei.
mar 9:2 kai meta hmeras ec paralambanei o ihsous ton petron kai ton iakwbon kai ton iwannhn kai anaferei autous eis oros uyhlon kat idian monous. kai metemorfwqh emprosqen autwn
mar 9:3 kai ta imatia autou egeneto stilbonta leuka lian oia gnafeus epi ths ghs ou dunatai outws leukanai.
mar 9:4 kai wfqh autois hlias sun mwusei kai hsan sullalountes tw ihsou.
mar 9:5 kai apokriqeis o petros legei tw ihsou rabbi kalon estin hmas wde einai kai poihswmen treis skhnas soi mian kai mwusei mian kai hlia mian.
mar 9:6 ou gar hdei ti apokriqh ekfoboi gar egenonto.
mar 9:7 kai egeneto nefelh episkiazousa autois kai egeneto fwnh ek ths nefelhs outos estin o uios mou o agaphtos akouete autou.
mar 9:8 kai ecapina peribleyamenoi ouketi oudena eidon alla ton ihsoun monon meq eautwn.
mar 9:9 kai katabainontwn autwn ek tou orous diesteilato autois ina mhdeni a eidon dihghswntai ei mh otan o uios tou anqrwpou ek nekrwn anasth.
mar 9:10 kai ton logon ekrathsan pros eautous suzhtountes ti estin to ek nekrwn anasthnai.
mar 9:11 kai ephrwtwn auton legontes oti legousin oi grammateis oti hlian dei elqein prwton;
mar 9:12 o de efh autois hlias men elqwn prwton apokaqistanei panta kai pws gegraptai epi ton uion tou anqrwpou ina polla paqh kai ecoudenhqh;
mar 9:13 alla legw umin oti kai hlias elhluqen kai epoihsan autw osa hqelon kaqws gegraptai ep auton.
mar 9:14 kai elqontes pros tous maqhtas eidon oxlon polun peri autous kai grammateis suzhtountas pros autous.
mar 9:15 kai euqus pas o oxlos idontes auton eceqambhqhsan kai prostrexontes hspazonto auton.
mar 9:16 kai ephrwthsen autous ti suzhteite pros autous;
mar 9:17 kai apekriqh autw eis ek tou oxlou didaskale hnegka ton uion mou pros se exonta pneuma alalon
mar 9:18 kai opou ean auton katalabh rhssei auton kai afrizei kai trizei tous odontas kai chrainetai kai eipa tois maqhtais sou ina auto ekbalwsin kai ouk isxusan.
mar 9:19 o de apokriqeis autois legei w genea apistos ews pote pros umas esomai; ews pote anecomai umwn; ferete auton pros me.
mar 9:20 kai hnegkan auton pros auton. kai idwn auton to pneuma euqus sunesparacen auton kai peswn epi ths ghs ekulieto afrizwn.
mar 9:21 kai ephrwthsen ton patera autou posos xronos estin ws touto gegonen autw; o de eipen ek paidioqen
mar 9:22 kai pollakis kai eis pur auton ebalen kai eis udata ina apolesh auton all ei ti dunh bohqhson hmin splagxnisqeis ef hmas.
mar 9:23 o de ihsous eipen autw to ei dunh panta dunata tw pisteuonti.
mar 9:24 euqus kracas o pathr tou paidiou elegen pisteuw bohqei mou th apistia.
mar 9:25 idwn de o ihsous oti episuntrexei oxlos epetimhsen tw pneumati tw akaqartw legwn autw to alalon kai kwfon pneuma egw epitassw soi ecelqe ec autou kai mhketi eiselqhs eis auton.
mar 9:26 kai kracas kai polla sparacas echlqen kai egeneto wsei nekros wste tous pollous legein oti apeqanen.
mar 9:27 o de ihsous krathsas ths xeiros autou hgeiren auton kai anesth.
mar 9:28 kai eiselqontos autou eis oikon oi maqhtai autou kat idian ephrwtwn auton oti hmeis ouk hdunhqhmen ekbalein auto;
mar 9:29 kai eipen autois touto to genos en oudeni dunatai ecelqein ei mh en proseuxh [kai nhsteia].
mar 9:30 kakeiqen ecelqontes pareporeuonto dia ths galilaias kai ouk hqelen ina tis gnoi
mar 9:31 edidasken gar tous maqhtas autou kai elegen autois oti o uios tou anqrwpou paradidotai eis xeiras anqrwpwn kai apoktenousin auton kai apoktanqeis meta treis hmeras anasthsetai.
mar 9:32 oi de hgnooun to rhma kai efobounto auton eperwthsai.
mar 9:33 kai hlqon eis kafarnaoum. kai en th oikia genomenos ephrwta autous ti en th odw dielogizesqe;
mar 9:34 oi de esiwpwn pros allhlous gar dielexqhsan en th odw tis meizwn.
mar 9:35 kai kaqisas efwnhsen tous dwdeka kai legei autois ei tis qelei prwtos einai estai pantwn esxatos kai pantwn diakonos.
mar 9:36 kai labwn paidion esthsen auto en mesw autwn kai enagkalisamenos auto eipen autois
mar 9:37 os an en twn toioutwn paidiwn dechtai epi tw onomati mou eme dexetai kai os an eme dexhtai ouk eme dexetai alla ton aposteilanta me.
mar 9:38 efh autw o iwannhs didaskale eidomen tina en tw onomati sou ekballonta daimonia kai ekwluomen auton oti ouk hkolouqei hmin.
mar 9:39 o de ihsous eipen mh kwluete auton oudeis gar estin os poihsei dunamin epi tw onomati mou kai dunhsetai taxu kakologhsai me
mar 9:40 os gar ouk estin kaq hmwn uper hmwn estin.
mar 9:41 os gar an potish umas pothrion udatos en onomati [mou] oti xristou este amhn legw umin oti ou mh apolesh ton misqon autou.
mar 9:42 kai os an skandalish ena twn mikrwn toutwn twn pisteuontwn eis eme kalon estin autw mallon ei perikeitai mulos onikos peri ton traxhlon autou kai beblhtai eis thn qalassan.
mar 9:43 kai ean skandalizh se h xeir sou apokoyon authn kalon estin se kullon eiselqein eis thn zwhn h tas duo xeiras exonta apelqein eis thn geennan eis to pur to asbeston.
mar 9:44 [--]
mar 9:45 kai ean o pous sou skandalizh se apokoyon auton kalon estin se eiselqein eis thn zwhn xwlon h tous duo podas exonta blhqhnai eis thn geennan.
mar 9:46 [--]
mar 9:47 kai ean o ofqalmos sou skandalizh se ekbale auton kalon se estin monofqalmon eiselqein eis thn basileian tou qeou h duo ofqalmous exonta blhqhnai eis thn geennan
mar 9:48 opou o skwlhc autwn ou teleuta kai to pur ou sbennutai
mar 9:49 pas gar puri alisqhsetai.
mar 9:50 kalon to alas ean de to alas analon genhtai en tini auto artusete; exete en eautois ala kai eirhneuete en allhlois.
mar 10:1 kai ekeiqen anastas erxetai eis ta oria ths ioudaias kai peran tou iordanou kai sumporeuontai palin oxloi pros auton kai ws eiwqei palin edidasken autous.
mar 10:2 kai proselqontes farisaioi ephrwtwn auton ei ecestin andri gunaika apolusai peirazontes auton.
mar 10:3 o de apokriqeis eipen autois ti umin eneteilato mwushs;
mar 10:4 oi de eipan epetreyen mwushs biblion apostasiou grayai kai apolusai.
mar 10:5 o de ihsous eipen autois pros thn sklhrokardian umwn egrayen umin thn entolhn tauthn.
mar 10:6 apo de arxhs ktisews arsen kai qhlu epoihsen autous
mar 10:7 eneken toutou kataleiyei anqrwpos ton patera autou kai thn mhtera kai proskollhqhsetai pros thn gunaika autou
mar 10:8 kai esontai oi duo eis sarka mian wste ouketi eisin duo alla mia sarc.
mar 10:9 o oun o qeos sunezeucen anqrwpos mh xwrizetw.
mar 10:10 kai eis thn oikian palin oi maqhtai peri toutou ephrwtwn auton.
mar 10:11 kai legei autois os an apolush thn gunaika autou kai gamhsh allhn moixatai ep authn
mar 10:12 kai ean auth apolusasa ton andra auths gamhsh allon moixatai.
mar 10:13 kai proseferon autw paidia ina autwn ayhtai oi de maqhtai epetimhsan autois.
mar 10:14 idwn de o ihsous hganakthsen kai eipen autois afete ta paidia erxesqai pros me mh kwluete auta twn gar toioutwn estin h basileia tou qeou.
mar 10:15 amhn legw umin os an mh dechtai thn basileian tou qeou ws paidion ou mh eiselqh eis authn.
mar 10:16 kai enagkalisamenos auta kateulogei tiqeis tas xeiras ep auta.
mar 10:17 kai ekporeuomenou autou eis odon prosdramwn eis kai gonupethsas auton ephrwta auton didaskale agaqe ti poihsw ina zwhn aiwnion klhronomhsw;
mar 10:18 o de ihsous eipen autw ti me legeis agaqon; oudeis agaqos ei mh eis o qeos.
mar 10:19 tas entolas oidas mh foneushs mh moixeushs mh kleyhs mh yeudomarturhshs mh aposterhshs tima ton patera sou kai thn mhtera.
mar 10:20 o de efh autw didaskale tauta panta efulacamhn ek neothtos mou.
mar 10:21 o de ihsous embleyas autw hgaphsen auton kai eipen autw en se usterei upage osa exeis pwlhson kai dos tois ptwxois kai eceis qhsauron en ouranw kai deuro akolouqei moi.
mar 10:22 o de stugnasas epi tw logw aphlqen lupoumenos hn gar exwn kthmata polla.
mar 10:23 kai peribleyamenos o ihsous legei tois maqhtais autou pws duskolws oi ta xrhmata exontes eis thn basileian tou qeou eiseleusontai.
mar 10:24 oi de maqhtai eqambounto epi tois logois autou. o de ihsous palin apokriqeis legei autois tekna pws duskolon estin eis thn basileian tou qeou eiselqein
mar 10:25 eukopwteron estin kamhlon dia ths trumalias ths rafidos dielqein h plousion eis thn basileian tou qeou eiselqein.
mar 10:26 oi de perissws eceplhssonto legontes pros [allhlous] kai tis dunatai swqhnai;
mar 10:27 embleyas autois o ihsous legei para anqrwpois adunaton all ou para qew panta gar dunata para tw qew.
mar 10:28 hrcato legein o petros autw idou hmeis afhkamen panta kai hkolouqhkamen soi.
mar 10:29 efh o ihsous amhn legw umin oudeis estin os afhken oikian h adelfous h adelfas h mhtera h patera h tekna h agrous eneken emou kai eneken tou euaggeliou
mar 10:30 ean mh labh ekatontaplasiona nun en tw kairw toutw oikias kai adelfous kai adelfas kai mhteras kai tekna kai agrous meta diwgmwn kai en tw aiwni tw erxomenw zwhn aiwnion.
mar 10:31 polloi de esontai prwtoi esxatoi kai oi esxatoi prwtoi.
mar 10:32 hsan de en th odw anabainontes eis ierosoluma kai hn proagwn autous o ihsous kai eqambounto oi de akolouqountes efobounto. kai paralabwn palin tous dwdeka hrcato autois legein ta mellonta autw sumbainein
mar 10:33 oti idou anabainomen eis ierosoluma kai o uios tou anqrwpou paradoqhsetai tois arxiereusin kai tois grammateusin kai katakrinousin auton qanatw kai paradwsousin auton tois eqnesin
mar 10:34 kai empaicousin autw kai emptusousin autw kai mastigwsousin auton kai apoktenousin kai meta treis hmeras anasthsetai.
mar 10:35 kai prosporeuontai autw iakwbos kai iwannhs oi uioi zebedaiou legontes autw didaskale qelomen ina o ean aithswmen se poihshs hmin.
mar 10:36 o de eipen autois ti qelete me poihsw umin;
mar 10:37 oi de eipan autw dos hmin ina eis sou ek deciwn kai eis ec aristerwn kaqiswmen en th doch sou.
mar 10:38 o de ihsous eipen autois ouk oidate ti aiteisqe. dunasqe piein to pothrion o egw pinw h to baptisma o egw baptizomai baptisqhnai;
mar 10:39 oi de eipan autw dunameqa. o de ihsous eipen autois to pothrion o egw pinw piesqe kai to baptisma o egw baptizomai baptisqhsesqe
mar 10:40 to de kaqisai ek deciwn mou h ec euwnumwn ouk estin emon dounai all ois htoimastai.
mar 10:41 kai akousantes oi deka hrcanto aganaktein peri iakwbou kai iwannou.
mar 10:42 kai proskalesamenos autous o ihsous legei autois oidate oti oi dokountes arxein twn eqnwn katakurieuousin autwn kai oi megaloi autwn katecousiazousin autwn.
mar 10:43 oux outws de estin en umin all os an qelh megas genesqai en umin estai umwn diakonos
mar 10:44 kai os an qelh en umin einai prwtos estai pantwn doulos
mar 10:45 kai gar o uios tou anqrwpou ouk hlqen diakonhqhnai alla diakonhsai kai dounai thn yuxhn autou lutron anti pollwn.
mar 10:46 kai erxontai eis ierixw. kai ekporeuomenou autou apo ierixw kai twn maqhtwn autou kai oxlou ikanou o uios timaiou bartimaios tuflos prosaiths ekaqhto para thn odon.
mar 10:47 kai akousas oti ihsous o nazarhnos estin hrcato krazein kai legein uie dauid ihsou elehson me.
mar 10:48 kai epetimwn autw polloi ina siwphsh o de pollw mallon ekrazen uie dauid elehson me.
mar 10:49 kai stas o ihsous eipen fwnhsate auton. kai fwnousin ton tuflon legontes autw qarsei egeire fwnei se.
mar 10:50 o de apobalwn to imation autou anaphdhsas hlqen pros ton ihsoun.
mar 10:51 kai apokriqeis autw o ihsous eipen ti soi qeleis poihsw; o de tuflos eipen autw rabbouni ina anableyw.
mar 10:52 kai o ihsous eipen autw upage h pistis sou seswken se. kai euqus anebleyen kai hkolouqei autw en th odw.
mar 11:1 kai ote eggizousin eis ierosoluma eis bhqfagh kai bhqanian pros to oros twn elaiwn apostellei duo twn maqhtwn autou
mar 11:2 kai legei autois upagete eis thn kwmhn thn katenanti umwn kai euqus eisporeuomenoi eis authn eurhsete pwlon dedemenon ef on oudeis oupw anqrwpwn ekaqisen lusate auton kai ferete.
mar 11:3 kai ean tis umin eiph ti poieite touto; eipate o kurios autou xreian exei kai euqus auton apostellei palin wde.
mar 11:4 kai aphlqon kai euron pwlon dedemenon pros quran ecw epi tou amfodou kai luousin auton.
mar 11:5 kai tines twn ekei esthkotwn elegon autois ti poieite luontes ton pwlon;
mar 11:6 oi de eipan autois kaqws eipen o ihsous kai afhkan autous.
mar 11:7 kai ferousin ton pwlon pros ton ihsoun kai epiballousin autw ta imatia autwn kai ekaqisen ep auton.
mar 11:8 kai polloi ta imatia autwn estrwsan eis thn odon alloi de stibadas koyantes ek twn agrwn.
mar 11:9 kai oi proagontes kai oi akolouqountes ekrazon wsanna euloghmenos o erxomenos en onomati kuriou
mar 11:10 euloghmenh h erxomenh basileia tou patros hmwn dauid wsanna en tois uyistois.
mar 11:11 kai eishlqen eis ierosoluma eis to ieron kai peribleyamenos panta oyias hdh oushs ths wras echlqen eis bhqanian meta twn dwdeka.
mar 11:12 kai th epaurion ecelqontwn autwn apo bhqanias epeinasen.
mar 11:13 kai idwn sukhn apo makroqen exousan fulla hlqen ei ara ti eurhsei en auth kai elqwn ep authn ouden euren ei mh fulla o gar kairos ouk hn sukwn.
mar 11:14 kai apokriqeis eipen auth mhketi eis ton aiwna ek sou mhdeis karpon fagoi. kai hkouon oi maqhtai autou.
mar 11:15 kai erxontai eis ierosoluma. kai eiselqwn eis to ieron hrcato ekballein tous pwlountas kai tous agorazontas en tw ierw kai tas trapezas twn kollubistwn kai tas kaqedras twn pwlountwn tas peristeras katestreyen
mar 11:16 kai ouk hfien ina tis dienegkh skeuos dia tou ierou.
mar 11:17 kai edidasken kai elegen autois ou gegraptai oti o oikos mou oikos proseuxhs klhqhsetai pasin tois eqnesin; umeis de pepoihkate auton sphlaion lhstwn.
mar 11:18 kai hkousan oi arxiereis kai oi grammateis kai ezhtoun pws auton apoleswsin efobounto gar auton pas gar o oxlos eceplhsseto epi th didaxh autou.
mar 11:19 kai otan oye egeneto eceporeuonto ecw ths polews.
mar 11:20 kai paraporeuomenoi prwi eidon thn sukhn echrammenhn ek rizwn.
mar 11:21 kai anamnhsqeis o petros legei autw rabbi ide h sukh hn kathrasw echrantai.
mar 11:22 kai apokriqeis o ihsous legei autois exete pistin qeou
mar 11:23 amhn legw umin oti os an eiph tw orei toutw arqhti kai blhqhti eis thn qalassan kai mh diakriqh en th kardia autou alla pisteuh oti o lalei ginetai estai autw.
mar 11:24 dia touto legw umin panta osa proseuxesqe kai aiteisqe pisteuete oti elabete kai estai umin.
mar 11:25 kai otan sthkete proseuxomenoi afiete ei ti exete kata tinos ina kai o pathr umwn o en tois ouranois afh umin ta paraptwmata umwn.
mar 11:26 [--]
mar 11:27 kai erxontai palin eis ierosoluma. kai en tw ierw peripatountos autou erxontai pros auton oi arxiereis kai oi grammateis kai oi presbuteroi
mar 11:28 kai elegon autw en poia ecousia tauta poieis; h tis soi edwken thn ecousian tauthn ina tauta poihs;
mar 11:29 o de ihsous eipen autois eperwthsw umas ena logon kai apokriqhte moi kai erw umin en poia ecousia tauta poiw
mar 11:30 to baptisma to iwannou ec ouranou hn h ec anqrwpwn; apokriqhte moi.
mar 11:31 kai dielogizonto pros eautous legontes ean eipwmen ec ouranou erei dia ti oun ouk episteusate autw;
mar 11:32 alla eipwmen ec anqrwpwn; efobounto ton oxlon apantes gar eixon ton iwannhn ontws oti profhths hn.
mar 11:33 kai apokriqentes tw ihsou legousin ouk oidamen. kai o ihsous legei autois oude egw legw umin en poia ecousia tauta poiw.
mar 12:1 kai hrcato autois en parabolais lalein ampelwna anqrwpos efuteusen kai perieqhken fragmon kai wrucen upolhnion kai wkodomhsen purgon kai ecedeto auton gewrgois kai apedhmhsen.
mar 12:2 kai apesteilen pros tous gewrgous tw kairw doulon ina para twn gewrgwn labh apo twn karpwn tou ampelwnos
mar 12:3 kai labontes auton edeiran kai apesteilan kenon.
mar 12:4 kai palin apesteilen pros autous allon doulon kakeinon ekefaliwsan kai htimasan.
mar 12:5 kai allon apesteilen kakeinon apekteinan kai pollous allous ous men derontes ous de apoktennontes.
mar 12:6 eti ena eixen uion agaphton apesteilen auton esxaton pros autous legwn oti entraphsontai ton uion mou.
mar 12:7 ekeinoi de oi gewrgoi pros eautous eipan oti outos estin o klhronomos deute apokteinwmen auton kai hmwn estai h klhronomia.
mar 12:8 kai labontes apekteinan auton kai ecebalon auton ecw tou ampelwnos.
mar 12:9 ti oun poihsei o kurios tou ampelwnos; eleusetai kai apolesei tous gewrgous kai dwsei ton ampelwna allois.
mar 12:10 oude thn grafhn tauthn anegnwte liqon on apedokimasan oi oikodomountes outos egenhqh eis kefalhn gwnias
mar 12:11 para kuriou egeneto auth kai estin qaumasth en ofqalmois hmwn;
mar 12:12 kai ezhtoun auton krathsai kai efobhqhsan ton oxlon egnwsan gar oti pros autous thn parabolhn eipen. kai afentes auton aphlqon.
mar 12:13 kai apostellousin pros auton tinas twn farisaiwn kai twn hrwdianwn ina auton agreuswsin logw.
mar 12:14 kai elqontes legousin autw didaskale oidamen oti alhqhs ei kai ou melei soi peri oudenos ou gar blepeis eis proswpon anqrwpwn all ep alhqeias thn odon tou qeou didaskeis ecestin dounai khnson kaisari h ou; dwmen h mh dwmen;
mar 12:15 o de eidws autwn thn upokrisin eipen autois ti me peirazete; ferete moi dhnarion ina idw.
mar 12:16 oi de hnegkan. kai legei autois tinos h eikwn auth kai h epigrafh; oi de eipan autw kaisaros.
mar 12:17 o de ihsous eipen autois ta kaisaros apodote kaisari kai ta tou qeou tw qew. kai eceqaumazon ep autw.
mar 12:18 kai erxontai saddoukaioi pros auton oitines legousin anastasin mh einai kai ephrwtwn auton legontes
mar 12:19 didaskale mwushs egrayen hmin oti ean tinos adelfos apoqanh kai kataliph gunaika kai mh afh teknon ina labh o adelfos autou thn gunaika kai ecanasthsh sperma tw adelfw autou.
mar 12:20 epta adelfoi hsan kai o prwtos elaben gunaika kai apoqnhskwn ouk afhken sperma
mar 12:21 kai o deuteros elaben authn kai apeqanen mh katalipwn sperma kai o tritos wsautws
mar 12:22 kai oi epta ouk afhkan sperma. esxaton pantwn kai h gunh apeqanen.
mar 12:23 en th anastasei otan anastwsin tinos autwn estai gunh; oi gar epta esxon authn gunaika.
mar 12:24 efh autois o ihsous ou dia touto planasqe mh eidotes tas grafas mhde thn dunamin tou qeou;
mar 12:25 otan gar ek nekrwn anastwsin oute gamousin oute gamizontai all eisin ws aggeloi en tois ouranois.
mar 12:26 peri de twn nekrwn oti egeirontai ouk anegnwte en th biblw mwusews epi tou batou pws eipen autw o qeos legwn egw o qeos abraam kai o qeos isaak kai o qeos iakwb;
mar 12:27 ouk estin qeos nekrwn alla zwntwn polu planasqe.
mar 12:28 kai proselqwn eis twn grammatewn akousas autwn suzhtountwn idwn oti kalws apekriqh autois ephrwthsen auton poia estin entolh prwth pantwn;
mar 12:29 apekriqh o ihsous oti prwth estin akoue israhl kurios o qeos hmwn kurios eis estin
mar 12:30 kai agaphseis kurion ton qeon sou ec olhs ths kardias sou kai ec olhs ths yuxhs sou kai ec olhs ths dianoias sou kai ec olhs ths isxuos sou.
mar 12:31 deutera auth agaphseis ton plhsion sou ws seauton. meizwn toutwn allh entolh ouk estin.
mar 12:32 kai eipen autw o grammateus kalws didaskale ep alhqeias eipes oti eis estin kai ouk estin allos plhn autou
mar 12:33 kai to agapan auton ec olhs ths kardias kai ec olhs ths sunesews kai ec olhs ths isxuos kai to agapan ton plhsion ws eauton perissoteron estin pantwn twn olokautwmatwn kai qusiwn.
mar 12:34 kai o ihsous idwn auton oti nounexws apekriqh eipen autw ou makran ei apo ths basileias tou qeou. kai oudeis ouketi etolma auton eperwthsai.
mar 12:35 kai apokriqeis o ihsous elegen didaskwn en tw ierw pws legousin oi grammateis oti o xristos uios dauid estin;
mar 12:36 autos dauid eipen en tw pneumati tw agiw eipen kurios tw kuriw mou kaqou ek deciwn mou ews an qw tous exqrous sou upokatw twn podwn sou.
mar 12:37 autos dauid legei auton kurion kai poqen autou estin uios; kai o polus oxlos hkouen autou hdews.
mar 12:38 kai en th didaxh autou elegen blepete apo twn grammatewn twn qelontwn en stolais peripatein kai aspasmous en tais agorais
mar 12:39 kai prwtokaqedrias en tais sunagwgais kai prwtoklisias en tois deipnois
mar 12:40 oi katesqiontes tas oikias twn xhrwn kai profasei makra proseuxomenoi outoi lhmyontai perissoteron krima.
mar 12:41 kai kaqisas katenanti tou gazofulakiou eqewrei pws o oxlos ballei xalkon eis to gazofulakion kai polloi plousioi eballon polla
mar 12:42 kai elqousa mia xhra ptwxh ebalen lepta duo o estin kodranths.
mar 12:43 kai proskalesamenos tous maqhtas autou eipen autois amhn legw umin oti h xhra auth h ptwxh pleion pantwn ebalen twn ballontwn eis to gazofulakion
mar 12:44 pantes gar ek tou perisseuontos autois ebalon auth de ek ths usterhsews auths panta osa eixen ebalen olon ton bion auths.
mar 13:1 kai ekporeuomenou autou ek tou ierou legei autw eis twn maqhtwn autou didaskale ide potapoi liqoi kai potapai oikodomai.
mar 13:2 kai o ihsous eipen autw blepeis tautas tas megalas oikodomas; ou mh afeqh wde liqos epi liqon os ou mh kataluqh.
mar 13:3 kai kaqhmenou autou eis to oros twn elaiwn katenanti tou ierou ephrwta auton kat idian petros kai iakwbos kai iwannhs kai andreas
mar 13:4 eipon hmin pote tauta estai kai ti to shmeion otan mellh tauta sunteleisqai panta.
mar 13:5 o de ihsous hrcato legein autois blepete mh tis umas planhsh
mar 13:6 polloi eleusontai epi tw onomati mou legontes oti egw eimi kai pollous planhsousin.
mar 13:7 otan de akoushte polemous kai akoas polemwn mh qroeisqe dei genesqai all oupw to telos.
mar 13:8 egerqhsetai gar eqnos ep eqnos kai basileia epi basileian esontai seismoi kata topous esontai limoi arxh wdinwn tauta.
mar 13:9 blepete de umeis eautous paradwsousin umas eis sunedria kai eis sunagwgas darhsesqe kai epi hgemonwn kai basilewn staqhsesqe eneken emou eis marturion autois.
mar 13:10 kai eis panta ta eqnh prwton dei khruxqhnai to euaggelion.
mar 13:11 kai otan agwsin umas paradidontes mh promerimnate ti lalhshte all o ean doqh umin en ekeinh th wra touto laleite ou gar este umeis oi lalountes alla to pneuma to agion.
mar 13:12 kai paradwsei adelfos adelfon eis qanaton kai pathr teknon kai epanasthsontai tekna epi goneis kai qanatwsousin autous
mar 13:13 kai esesqe misoumenoi upo pantwn dia to onoma mou. o de upomeinas eis telos outos swqhsetai.
mar 13:14 otan de idhte to bdelugma ths erhmwsews esthkota opou ou dei o anaginwskwn noeitw tote oi en th ioudaia feugetwsan eis ta orh
mar 13:15 o de epi tou dwmatos mh katabatw mhde eiselqatw arai ti ek ths oikias autou
mar 13:16 kai o eis ton agron mh epistreyatw eis ta opisw arai to imation autou.
mar 13:17 ouai de tais en gastri exousais kai tais qhlazousais en ekeinais tais hmerais.
mar 13:18 proseuxesqe de ina mh genhtai xeimwnos
mar 13:19 esontai gar ai hmerai ekeinai qliyis oia ou gegonen toiauth ap arxhs ktisews hn ektisen o qeos ews tou nun kai ou mh genhtai.
mar 13:20 kai ei mh ekolobwsen kurios tas hmeras ouk an eswqh pasa sarc. alla dia tous eklektous ous ecelecato ekolobwsen tas hmeras.
mar 13:21 kai tote ean tis umin eiph ide wde o xristos ide ekei mh pisteuete
mar 13:22 egerqhsontai gar yeudoxristoi kai yeudoprofhtai kai dwsousin shmeia kai terata pros to apoplanan ei dunaton tous eklektous.
mar 13:23 umeis de blepete proeirhka umin panta.
mar 13:24 alla en ekeinais tais hmerais meta thn qliyin ekeinhn o hlios skotisqhsetai kai h selhnh ou dwsei to feggos auths
mar 13:25 kai oi asteres esontai ek tou ouranou piptontes kai ai dunameis ai en tois ouranois saleuqhsontai.
mar 13:26 kai tote oyontai ton uion tou anqrwpou erxomenon en nefelais meta dunamews pollhs kai dochs.
mar 13:27 kai tote apostelei tous aggelous kai episunacei tous eklektous autou ek twn tessarwn anemwn ap akrou ghs ews akrou ouranou.
mar 13:28 apo de ths sukhs maqete thn parabolhn otan hdh o klados auths apalos genhtai kai ekfuh ta fulla ginwskete oti eggus to qeros estin.
mar 13:29 outws kai umeis otan idhte tauta ginomena ginwskete oti eggus estin epi qurais.
mar 13:30 amhn legw umin oti ou mh parelqh h genea auth mexris ou tauta panta genhtai.
mar 13:31 o ouranos kai h gh pareleusontai oi de logoi mou ou mh pareleusontai.
mar 13:32 peri de ths hmeras ekeinhs h ths wras oudeis oiden oude oi aggeloi en ouranw oude o uios ei mh o pathr.
mar 13:33 blepete agrupneite ouk oidate gar pote o kairos estin.
mar 13:34 ws anqrwpos apodhmos afeis thn oikian autou kai dous tois doulois autou thn ecousian ekastw to ergon autou kai tw qurwrw eneteilato ina grhgorh.
mar 13:35 grhgoreite oun ouk oidate gar pote o kurios ths oikias erxetai h oye h mesonuktion h alektorofwnias h prwi
mar 13:36 mh elqwn ecaifnhs eurh umas kaqeudontas.
mar 13:37 o de umin legw pasin legw grhgoreite.
mar 14:1 hn de to pasxa kai ta azuma meta duo hmeras. kai ezhtoun oi arxiereis kai oi grammateis pws auton en dolw krathsantes apokteinwsin
mar 14:2 elegon gar mh en th eorth mhpote estai qorubos tou laou.
mar 14:3 kai ontos autou en bhqania en th oikia simwnos tou leprou katakeimenou autou hlqen gunh exousa alabastron murou nardou pistikhs polutelous suntriyasa thn alabastron katexeen autou ths kefalhs.
mar 14:4 hsan de tines aganaktountes pros eautous eis ti h apwleia auth tou murou gegonen;
mar 14:5 hdunato gar touto to muron praqhnai epanw dhnariwn triakosiwn kai doqhnai tois ptwxois kai enebrimwnto auth.
mar 14:6 o de ihsous eipen afete authn ti auth kopous parexete; kalon ergon hrgasato en emoi.
mar 14:7 pantote gar tous ptwxous exete meq eautwn kai otan qelhte dunasqe autois eu poihsai eme de ou pantote exete.
mar 14:8 o esxen epoihsen proelaben murisai to swma mou eis ton entafiasmon.
mar 14:9 amhn de legw umin opou ean khruxqh to euaggelion eis olon ton kosmon kai o epoihsen auth lalhqhsetai eis mnhmosunon auths.
mar 14:10 kai ioudas iskariwq o eis twn dwdeka aphlqen pros tous arxiereis ina auton paradoi autois.
mar 14:11 oi de akousantes exarhsan kai ephggeilanto autw argurion dounai. kai ezhtei pws auton eukairws paradoi.
mar 14:12 kai th prwth hmera twn azumwn ote to pasxa equon legousin autw oi maqhtai autou pou qeleis apelqontes etoimaswmen ina faghs to pasxa;
mar 14:13 kai apostellei duo twn maqhtwn autou kai legei autois upagete eis thn polin kai apanthsei umin anqrwpos keramion udatos bastazwn akolouqhsate autw
mar 14:14 kai opou ean eiselqh eipate tw oikodespoth oti o didaskalos legei pou estin to kataluma mou opou to pasxa meta twn maqhtwn mou fagw;
mar 14:15 kai autos umin deicei anagaion mega estrwmenon etoimon kai ekei etoimasate hmin.
mar 14:16 kai echlqon oi maqhtai kai hlqon eis thn polin kai euron kaqws eipen autois kai htoimasan to pasxa.
mar 14:17 kai oyias genomenhs erxetai meta twn dwdeka.
mar 14:18 kai anakeimenwn autwn kai esqiontwn o ihsous eipen amhn legw umin oti eis ec umwn paradwsei me o esqiwn met emou.
mar 14:19 hrcanto lupeisqai kai legein autw eis kata eis mhti egw;
mar 14:20 o de eipen autois eis twn dwdeka o embaptomenos met emou eis to trublion.
mar 14:21 oti o men uios tou anqrwpou upagei kaqws gegraptai peri autou ouai de tw anqrwpw ekeinw di ou o uios tou anqrwpou paradidotai kalon autw ei ouk egennhqh o anqrwpos ekeinos.
mar 14:22 kai esqiontwn autwn labwn arton euloghsas eklasen kai edwken autois kai eipen labete touto estin to swma mou.
mar 14:23 kai labwn pothrion euxaristhsas edwken autois kai epion ec autou pantes.
mar 14:24 kai eipen autois touto estin to aima mou ths diaqhkhs to ekxunnomenon uper pollwn
mar 14:25 amhn legw umin oti ouketi ou mh piw ek tou genhmatos ths ampelou ews ths hmeras ekeinhs otan auto pinw kainon en th basileia tou qeou.
mar 14:26 kai umnhsantes echlqon eis to oros twn elaiwn.
mar 14:27 kai legei autois o ihsous oti pantes skandalisqhsesqe oti gegraptai patacw ton poimena kai ta probata diaskorpisqhsontai
mar 14:28 alla meta to egerqhnai me proacw umas eis thn galilaian.
mar 14:29 o de petros efh autw ei kai pantes skandalisqhsontai all ouk egw.
mar 14:30 kai legei autw o ihsous amhn legw soi oti su shmeron tauth th nukti prin h dis alektora fwnhsai tris me aparnhsh.
mar 14:31 o de ekperissws elalei ean deh me sunapoqanein soi ou mh se aparnhsomai. wsautws de kai pantes elegon.
mar 14:32 kai erxontai eis xwrion ou to onoma geqshmani kai legei tois maqhtais autou kaqisate wde ews proseucwmai.
mar 14:33 kai paralambanei ton petron kai ton iakwbon kai ton iwannhn met autou kai hrcato ekqambeisqai kai adhmonein
mar 14:34 kai legei autois perilupos estin h yuxh mou ews qanatou meinate wde kai grhgoreite.
mar 14:35 kai proelqwn mikron epipten epi ths ghs kai proshuxeto ina ei dunaton estin parelqh ap autou h wra
mar 14:36 kai elegen abba o pathr panta dunata soi parenegke to pothrion touto ap emou all ou ti egw qelw alla ti su.
mar 14:37 kai erxetai kai euriskei autous kaqeudontas kai legei tw petrw simwn kaqeudeis; ouk isxusas mian wran grhgorhsai;
mar 14:38 grhgoreite kai proseuxesqe ina mh elqhte eis peirasmon to men pneuma proqumon h de sarc asqenhs.
mar 14:39 kai palin apelqwn proshucato ton auton logon eipwn.
mar 14:40 kai palin elqwn euren autous kaqeudontas hsan gar autwn oi ofqalmoi katabarunomenoi kai ouk hdeisan ti apokriqwsin autw.
mar 14:41 kai erxetai to triton kai legei autois kaqeudete to loipon kai anapauesqe; apexei hlqen h wra idou paradidotai o uios tou anqrwpou eis tas xeiras twn amartwlwn.
mar 14:42 egeiresqe agwmen idou o paradidous me hggiken.
mar 14:43 kai euqus eti autou lalountos paraginetai ioudas eis twn dwdeka kai met autou oxlos meta maxairwn kai culwn para twn arxierewn kai twn grammatewn kai twn presbuterwn.
mar 14:44 dedwkei de o paradidous auton susshmon autois legwn on an filhsw autos estin krathsate auton kai apagete asfalws.
mar 14:45 kai elqwn euqus proselqwn autw legei rabbi kai katefilhsen auton.
mar 14:46 oi de epebalon tas xeiras autw kai ekrathsan auton.
mar 14:47 eis de tis twn paresthkotwn spasamenos thn maxairan epaisen ton doulon tou arxierews kai afeilen autou to wtarion.
mar 14:48 kai apokriqeis o ihsous eipen autois ws epi lhsthn echlqate meta maxairwn kai culwn sullabein me;
mar 14:49 kaq hmeran hmhn pros umas en tw ierw didaskwn kai ouk ekrathsate me all ina plhrwqwsin ai grafai.
mar 14:50 kai afentes auton efugon pantes.
mar 14:51 kai neaniskos tis sunhkolouqei autw peribeblhmenos sindona epi gumnou kai kratousin auton
mar 14:52 o de katalipwn thn sindona gumnos efugen.
mar 14:53 kai aphgagon ton ihsoun pros ton arxierea kai sunerxontai pantes oi arxiereis kai oi presbuteroi kai oi grammateis.
mar 14:54 kai o petros apo makroqen hkolouqhsen autw ews esw eis thn aulhn tou arxierews kai hn sugkaqhmenos meta twn uphretwn kai qermainomenos pros to fws.
mar 14:55 oi de arxiereis kai olon to sunedrion ezhtoun kata tou ihsou marturian eis to qanatwsai auton kai oux huriskon
mar 14:56 polloi gar eyeudomarturoun kat autou kai isai ai marturiai ouk hsan.
mar 14:57 kai tines anastantes eyeudomarturoun kat autou legontes
mar 14:58 oti hmeis hkousamen autou legontos oti egw katalusw ton naon touton ton xeiropoihton kai dia triwn hmerwn allon axeiropoihton oikodomhsw
mar 14:59 kai oude outws ish hn h marturia autwn.
mar 14:60 kai anastas o arxiereus eis meson ephrwthsen ton ihsoun legwn ouk apokrinh ouden; ti outoi sou katamarturousin;
mar 14:61 o de esiwpa kai ouk apekrinato ouden. palin o arxiereus ephrwta auton kai legei autw su ei o xristos o uios tou euloghtou;
mar 14:62 o de ihsous eipen egw eimi kai oyesqe ton uion tou anqrwpou ek deciwn kaqhmenon ths dunamews kai erxomenon meta twn nefelwn tou ouranou.
mar 14:63 o de arxiereus diarrhcas tous xitwnas autou legei ti eti xreian exomen marturwn;
mar 14:64 hkousate ths blasfhmias ti umin fainetai; oi de pantes katekrinan auton enoxon einai qanatou.
mar 14:65 kai hrcanto tines emptuein autw kai perikaluptein autou to proswpon kai kolafizein auton kai legein autw profhteuson kai oi uphretai rapismasin auton elabon.
mar 14:66 kai ontos tou petrou katw en th aulh erxetai mia twn paidiskwn tou arxierews
mar 14:67 kai idousa ton petron qermainomenon embleyasa autw legei kai su meta tou nazarhnou hsqa tou ihsou.
mar 14:68 o de hrnhsato legwn oute oida oute epistamai su ti legeis. kai echlqen ecw eis to proaulion kai alektwr efwnhsen.
mar 14:69 kai h paidiskh idousa auton hrcato palin legein tois parestwsin oti outos ec autwn estin.
mar 14:70 o de palin hrneito. kai meta mikron palin oi parestwtes elegon tw petrw alhqws ec autwn ei kai gar galilaios ei.
mar 14:71 o de hrcato anaqematizein kai omnunai oti ouk oida ton anqrwpon touton on legete.
mar 14:72 kai euqus ek deuterou alektwr efwnhsen. kai anemnhsqh o petros to rhma ws eipen autw o ihsous oti prin alektora fwnhsai dis tris me aparnhsh kai epibalwn eklaien.
mar 15:1 kai euqus prwi sumboulion poihsantes oi arxiereis meta twn presbuterwn kai grammatewn kai olon to sunedrion dhsantes ton ihsoun aphnegkan kai paredwkan pilatw.
mar 15:2 kai ephrwthsen auton o pilatos su ei o basileus twn ioudaiwn; o de apokriqeis autw legei su legeis.
mar 15:3 kai kathgoroun autou oi arxiereis polla.
mar 15:4 o de pilatos palin ephrwta auton legwn ouk apokrinh ouden; ide posa sou kathgorousin.
mar 15:5 o de ihsous ouketi ouden apekriqh wste qaumazein ton pilaton.
mar 15:6 kata de eorthn apeluen autois ena desmion on parhtounto.
mar 15:7 hn de o legomenos barabbas meta twn stasiastwn dedemenos oitines en th stasei fonon pepoihkeisan.
mar 15:8 kai anabas o oxlos hrcato aiteisqai kaqws epoiei autois.
mar 15:9 o de pilatos apekriqh autois legwn qelete apolusw umin ton basilea twn ioudaiwn;
mar 15:10 eginwsken gar oti dia fqonon paradedwkeisan auton oi arxiereis.
mar 15:11 oi de arxiereis aneseisan ton oxlon ina mallon ton barabban apolush autois.
