mar 15:13 oi de palin ekracan staurwson auton.
mar 15:14 o de pilatos elegen autois ti gar epoihsen kakon; oi de perissws ekracan staurwson auton.
mar 15:15 o de pilatos boulomenos tw oxlw to ikanon poihsai apelusen autois ton barabban kai paredwken ton ihsoun fragellwsas ina staurwqh.
mar 15:16 oi de stratiwtai aphgagon auton esw ths aulhs o estin praitwrion kai sugkalousin olhn thn speiran.
mar 15:17 kai endiduskousin auton porfuran kai peritiqeasin autw plecantes akanqinon stefanon
mar 15:18 kai hrcanto aspazesqai auton xaire basileu twn ioudaiwn
mar 15:19 kai etupton autou thn kefalhn kalamw kai eneptuon autw kai tiqentes ta gonata prosekunoun autw.
mar 15:20 kai ote enepaican autw ecedusan auton thn porfuran kai enedusan auton ta imatia autou. kai ecagousin auton ina staurwswsin auton.
mar 15:21 kai aggareuousin paragonta tina simwna kurhnaion erxomenon ap agrou ton patera alecandrou kai roufou ina arh ton stauron autou.
mar 15:22 kai ferousin auton epi ton golgoqan topon o estin meqermhneuomenon kraniou topos.
mar 15:23 kai edidoun autw esmurnismenon oinon os de ouk elaben.
mar 15:24 kai staurousin auton kai diamerizontai ta imatia autou ballontes klhron ep auta tis ti arh.
mar 15:25 hn de wra trith kai estaurwsan auton.
mar 15:26 kai hn h epigrafh ths aitias autou epigegrammenh o basileus twn ioudaiwn.
mar 15:27 kai sun autw staurousin duo lhstas ena ek deciwn kai ena ec euwnumwn autou.

mar 15:30 swson seauton katabas apo tou staurou.
mar 15:31 omoiws kai oi arxiereis empaizontes pros allhlous meta twn grammatewn elegon allous eswsen eauton ou dunatai swsai
mar 15:32 o xristos o basileus israhl katabatw nun apo tou staurou ina idwmen kai pisteuswmen. kai oi sunestaurwmenoi sun autw wneidizon auton.

mar 15:34 kai th enath wra ebohsen o ihsous fwnh megalh elwi elwi lema sabaxqani; o estin meqermhneuomenon o qeos mou o qeos mou eis ti egkatelipes me;
mar 15:35 kai tines twn paresthkotwn akousantes elegon ide hlian fwnei.

mar 15:39 idwn de o kenturiwn o paresthkws ec enantias autou oti outws ecepneusen eipen alhqws outos o anqrwpos uios qeou hn.
mar 15:40 hsan de kai gunaikes apo makroqen qewrousai en ais kai maria h magdalhnh kai maria h iakwbou tou mikrou kai iwshtos mhthr kai salwmh
mar 15:41 ai ote hn en th galilaia hkolouqoun autw kai dihkonoun autw kai allai pollai ai sunanabasai autw eis ierosoluma.
mar 15:42 kai hdh oyias genomenhs epei hn paraskeuh o estin prosabbaton
mar 15:43 elqwn iwshf o apo arimaqaias eusxhmwn bouleuths os kai autos hn prosdexomenos thn basileian tou qeou tolmhsas eishlqen pros ton pilaton kai hthsato to swma tou ihsou.
mar 15:44 o de pilatos eqaumasen ei hdh teqnhken kai proskalesamenos ton kenturiwna ephrwthsen auton ei palai apeqanen
mar 15:45 kai gnous apo tou kenturiwnos edwrhsato to ptwma tw iwshf.
mar 15:46 kai agorasas sindona kaqelwn auton eneilhsen th sindoni kai eqhken auton en mnhmeiw o hn lelatomhmenon ek petras kai prosekulisen liqon epi thn quran tou mnhmeiou.
mar 15:47 h de maria h magdalhnh kai maria h iwshtos eqewroun pou teqeitai.
mar 16:1 kai diagenomenou tou sabbatou maria h magdalhnh kai maria h tou iakwbou kai salwmh hgorasan arwmata ina elqousai aleiywsin auton.
mar 16:2 kai lian prwi th mia twn sabbatwn erxontai epi to mnhmeion anateilantos tou hliou.
mar 16:3 kai elegon pros eautas tis apokulisei hmin ton liqon ek ths quras tou mnhmeiou;
mar 16:4 kai anableyasai qewrousin oti apokekulistai o liqos hn gar megas sfodra.
mar 16:5 kai eiselqousai eis to mnhmeion eidon neaniskon kaqhmenon en tois deciois peribeblhmenon stolhn leukhn kai eceqambhqhsan.
mar 16:6 o de legei autais mh ekqambeisqe ihsoun zhteite ton nazarhnon ton estaurwmenon hgerqh ouk estin wde ide o topos opou eqhkan auton.
mar 16:7 alla upagete eipate tois maqhtais autou kai tw petrw oti proagei umas eis thn galilaian ekei auton oyesqe kaqws eipen umin.
mar 16:8 kai ecelqousai efugon apo tou mnhmeiou eixen gar autas tromos kai ekstasis kai oudeni ouden eipan efobounto gar.

mar 16:10 ekeinh poreuqeisa aphggeilen tois met autou genomenois penqousi kai klaiousin
mar 16:11 kakeinoi akousantes oti zh kai eqeaqh up auths hpisthsan.
mar 16:12 meta de tauta dusin ec autwn peripatousin efanerwqh en etera morfh poreuomenois eis agron
mar 16:13 kakeinoi apelqontes aphggeilan tois loipois oude ekeinois episteusan.
mar 16:14 usteron de anakeimenois autois tois endeka efanerwqh kai wneidisen thn apistian autwn kai sklhrokardian oti tois qeasamenois auton eghgermenon ouk episteusan.
mar 16:15 kai eipen autois poreuqentes eis ton kosmon apanta khrucate to euaggelion pash th ktisei.
mar 16:16 o pisteusas kai baptisqeis swqhsetai o de apisthsas katakriqhsetai.
mar 16:17 shmeia de tois pisteusasin tauta parakolouqhsei en tw onomati mou daimonia ekbalousin glwssais lalhsousin kainais
mar 16:18 kai en tais xersin ofeis arousin kan qanasimon ti piwsin ou mh autous blayh epi arrwstous xeiras epiqhsousin kai kalws ecousin.
mar 16:19 o men oun kurios ihsous meta to lalhsai autois anelhmfqh eis ton ouranon kai ekaqisen ek deciwn tou qeou.
mar 16:20 ekeinoi de ecelqontes ekhrucan pantaxou tou kuriou sunergountos kai ton logon bebaiountos dia twn epakolouqountwn shmeiwn.]]
luk 1:1 epeidhper polloi epexeirhsan anatacasqai dihghsin peri twn peplhroforhmenwn en hmin pragmatwn
luk 1:2 kaqws paredosan hmin oi ap arxhs autoptai kai uphretai genomenoi tou logou
luk 1:3 edoce kamoi parhkolouqhkoti anwqen pasin akribws kaqechs soi grayai kratiste qeofile
luk 1:4 ina epignws peri wn kathxhqhs logwn thn asfaleian.
luk 1:5 egeneto en tais hmerais hrwdou basilews ths ioudaias iereus tis onomati zaxarias ec efhmerias abia kai gunh autw ek twn qugaterwn aarwn kai to onoma auths elisabet.
luk 1:6 hsan de dikaioi amfoteroi enantion tou qeou poreuomenoi en pasais tais entolais kai dikaiwmasin tou kuriou amemptoi.
luk 1:7 kai ouk hn autois teknon kaqoti hn h elisabet steira kai amfoteroi probebhkotes en tais hmerais autwn hsan.
luk 1:8 egeneto de en tw ierateuein auton en th tacei ths efhmerias autou enanti tou qeou
luk 1:9 kata to eqos ths ierateias elaxe tou qumiasai eiselqwn eis ton naon tou kuriou
luk 1:10 kai pan to plhqos hn tou laou proseuxomenon ecw th wra tou qumiamatos
luk 1:11 wfqh de autw aggelos kuriou estws ek deciwn tou qusiasthriou tou qumiamatos.
luk 1:12 kai etaraxqh zaxarias idwn kai fobos epepesen ep auton.
luk 1:13 eipen de pros auton o aggelos mh fobou zaxaria dioti eishkousqh h dehsis sou kai h gunh sou elisabet gennhsei uion soi kai kaleseis to onoma autou iwannhn.
luk 1:14 kai estai xara soi kai agalliasis kai polloi epi th genesei autou xarhsontai
luk 1:15 estai gar megas enwpion tou kuriou kai oinon kai sikera ou mh pih kai pneumatos agiou plhsqhsetai eti ek koilias mhtros autou
luk 1:16 kai pollous twn uiwn israhl epistreyei epi kurion ton qeon autwn.
luk 1:17 kai autos proeleusetai enwpion autou en pneumati kai dunamei hliou epistreyai kardias paterwn epi tekna kai apeiqeis en fronhsei dikaiwn etoimasai kuriw laon kateskeuasmenon.
luk 1:18 kai eipen zaxarias pros ton aggelon kata ti gnwsomai touto; egw gar eimi presbuths kai h gunh mou probebhkuia en tais hmerais auths.
luk 1:19 kai apokriqeis o aggelos eipen autw egw eimi gabrihl o paresthkws enwpion tou qeou kai apestalhn lalhsai pros se kai euaggelisasqai soi tauta
luk 1:20 kai idou esh siwpwn kai mh dunamenos lalhsai axri hs hmeras genhtai tauta anq wn ouk episteusas tois logois mou oitines plhrwqhsontai eis ton kairon autwn.
luk 1:21 kai hn o laos prosdokwn ton zaxarian kai eqaumazon en tw xronizein en tw naw auton.
luk 1:22 ecelqwn de ouk edunato lalhsai autois kai epegnwsan oti optasian ewraken en tw naw kai autos hn dianeuwn autois kai diemenen kwfos.
luk 1:23 kai egeneto ws eplhsqhsan ai hmerai ths leitourgias autou aphlqen eis ton oikon autou.
luk 1:24 meta de tautas tas hmeras sunelaben elisabet h gunh autou kai periekruben eauthn mhnas pente legousa
luk 1:25 oti outws moi pepoihken kurios en hmerais ais epeiden afelein oneidos mou en anqrwpois.
luk 1:26 en de tw mhni tw ektw apestalh o aggelos gabrihl apo tou qeou eis polin ths galilaias h onoma nazareq
luk 1:27 pros parqenon emnhsteumenhn andri w onoma iwshf ec oikou dauid kai to onoma ths parqenou mariam.
luk 1:28 kai eiselqwn pros authn eipen xaire kexaritwmenh o kurios meta sou.
luk 1:29 h de epi tw logw dietaraxqh kai dielogizeto potapos eih o aspasmos outos.
luk 1:30 kai eipen o aggelos auth mh fobou mariam eures gar xarin para tw qew
luk 1:31 kai idou sullhmyh en gastri kai tech uion kai kaleseis to onoma autou ihsoun.
luk 1:32 outos estai megas kai uios uyistou klhqhsetai kai dwsei autw kurios o qeos ton qronon dauid tou patros autou
luk 1:33 kai basileusei epi ton oikon iakwb eis tous aiwnas kai ths basileias autou ouk estai telos.
luk 1:34 eipen de mariam pros ton aggelon pws estai touto epei andra ou ginwskw;
luk 1:35 kai apokriqeis o aggelos eipen auth pneuma agion epeleusetai epi se kai dunamis uyistou episkiasei soi dio kai to gennwmenon agion klhqhsetai uios qeou.
luk 1:36 kai idou elisabet h suggenis sou kai auth suneilhfen uion en ghrei auths kai outos mhn ektos estin auth th kaloumenh steira
luk 1:37 oti ouk adunathsei para tou qeou pan rhma.
luk 1:38 eipen de mariam idou h doulh kuriou genoito moi kata to rhma sou. kai aphlqen ap auths o aggelos.
luk 1:39 anastasa de mariam en tais hmerais tautais eporeuqh eis thn oreinhn meta spoudhs eis polin iouda
luk 1:40 kai eishlqen eis ton oikon zaxariou kai hspasato thn elisabet.
luk 1:41 kai egeneto ws hkousen ton aspasmon ths marias h elisabet eskirthsen to brefos en th koilia auths kai eplhsqh pneumatos agiou h elisabet
luk 1:42 kai anefwnhsen kraugh megalh kai eipen euloghmenh su en gunaicin kai euloghmenos o karpos ths koilias sou.
luk 1:43 kai poqen moi touto ina elqh h mhthr tou kuriou mou pros eme;
luk 1:44 idou gar ws egeneto h fwnh tou aspasmou sou eis ta wta mou eskirthsen en agalliasei to brefos en th koilia mou.
luk 1:45 kai makaria h pisteusasa oti estai teleiwsis tois lelalhmenois auth para kuriou.
luk 1:46 kai eipen mariam
luk 1:47 megalunei h yuxh mou ton kurion kai hgalliasen to pneuma mou epi tw qew tw swthri mou
luk 1:48 oti epebleyen epi thn tapeinwsin ths doulhs autou. idou gar apo tou nun makariousin me pasai ai geneai
luk 1:49 oti epoihsen moi megala o dunatos kai agion to onoma autou
luk 1:50 kai to eleos autou eis geneas kai geneas tois foboumenois auton.
luk 1:51 epoihsen kratos en braxioni autou dieskorpisen uperhfanous dianoia kardias autwn
luk 1:52 kaqeilen dunastas apo qronwn kai uywsen tapeinous
luk 1:53 peinwntas eneplhsen agaqwn kai ploutountas ecapesteilen kenous.
luk 1:54 antelabeto israhl paidos autou mnhsqhnai eleous
luk 1:55 kaqws elalhsen pros tous pateras hmwn tw abraam kai tw spermati autou eis ton aiwna.
luk 1:56 emeinen de mariam sun auth ws mhnas treis kai upestreyen eis ton oikon auths.
luk 1:57 th de elisabet eplhsqh o xronos tou tekein authn kai egennhsen uion.
luk 1:58 kai hkousan oi perioikoi kai oi suggeneis auths oti emegalunen kurios to eleos autou met auths kai sunexairon auth.
luk 1:59 kai egeneto en th hmera th ogdoh hlqon peritemein to paidion kai ekaloun auto epi tw onomati tou patros autou zaxarian.
luk 1:60 kai apokriqeisa h mhthr autou eipen ouxi alla klhqhsetai iwannhs.
luk 1:61 kai eipan pros authn oti oudeis estin ek ths suggeneias sou os kaleitai tw onomati toutw.
luk 1:62 eneneuon de tw patri autou to ti an qeloi kaleisqai auto.
luk 1:63 kai aithsas pinakidion egrayen legwn iwannhs estin onoma autou. kai eqaumasan pantes.
luk 1:64 anewxqh de to stoma autou paraxrhma kai h glwssa autou kai elalei eulogwn ton qeon.
luk 1:65 kai egeneto epi pantas fobos tous perioikountas autous kai en olh th oreinh ths ioudaias dielaleito panta ta rhmata tauta
luk 1:66 kai eqento pantes oi akousantes en th kardia autwn legontes ti ara to paidion touto estai; kai gar xeir kuriou hn met autou.
luk 1:67 kai zaxarias o pathr autou eplhsqh pneumatos agiou kai eprofhteusen legwn
luk 1:68 euloghtos kurios o qeos tou israhl oti epeskeyato kai epoihsen lutrwsin tw law autou
luk 1:69 kai hgeiren keras swthrias hmin en oikw dauid paidos autou
luk 1:70 kaqws elalhsen dia stomatos twn agiwn ap aiwnos profhtwn autou
luk 1:71 swthrian ec exqrwn hmwn kai ek xeiros pantwn twn misountwn hmas
luk 1:72 poihsai eleos meta twn paterwn hmwn kai mnhsqhnai diaqhkhs agias autou
luk 1:73 orkon on wmosen pros abraam ton patera hmwn tou dounai hmin
luk 1:74 afobws ek xeiros [pantwn twn exqrwn hmwn] rusqentas latreuein autw
luk 1:75 en osiothti kai dikaiosunh enwpion autou pasais tais hmerais hmwn.
luk 1:76 kai su de paidion profhths uyistou klhqhsh proporeush gar enwpion kuriou etoimasai odous autou
luk 1:77 tou dounai gnwsin swthrias tw law autou en afesei amartiwn autwn
luk 1:78 dia splagxna eleous qeou hmwn en ois episkeyetai hmas anatolh ec uyous
luk 1:79 epifanai tois en skotei kai skia qanatou kaqhmenois tou kateuqunai tous podas hmwn eis odon eirhnhs.
luk 1:80 to de paidion hucanen kai ekrataiouto pneumati kai hn en tais erhmois ews hmeras anadeicews autou pros ton israhl.
luk 2:1 egeneto de en tais hmerais ekeinais echlqen dogma para kaisaros augoustou apografesqai pasan thn oikoumenhn.
luk 2:2 auth apografh prwth egeneto hgemoneuontos ths surias kurhniou.
luk 2:3 kai eporeuonto pantes apografesqai ekastos eis thn eautou polin.
luk 2:4 anebh de kai iwshf apo ths galilaias ek polews nazareq eis thn ioudaian eis polin dauid htis kaleitai bhqleem dia to einai auton ec oikou kai patrias dauid
luk 2:5 apograyasqai sun mariam th emnhsteumenh autw oush egkuw.
luk 2:6 egeneto de en tw einai autous ekei eplhsqhsan ai hmerai tou tekein authn
luk 2:7 kai eteken ton uion auths ton prwtotokon kai esparganwsen auton kai aneklinen auton en fatnh dioti ouk hn autois topos en tw katalumati.
luk 2:8 kai poimenes hsan en th xwra th auth agraulountes kai fulassontes fulakas ths nuktos epi thn poimnhn autwn.

luk 4:1 ihsous de plhrhs pneumatos agiou upestreyen apo tou iordanou kai hgeto en tw pneumati en th erhmw
luk 4:2 hmeras tesserakonta peirazomenos upo tou diabolou. kai ouk efagen ouden en tais hmerais ekeinais kai suntelesqeiswn autwn epeinasen.
luk 4:3 eipen de autw o diabolos ei uios ei tou qeou eipe tw liqw toutw ina genhtai artos.
luk 4:4 kai apekriqh pros auton o ihsous gegraptai oti ouk ep artw monw zhsetai o anqrwpos.
luk 4:5 kai anagagwn auton edeicen autw pasas tas basileias ths oikoumenhs en stigmh xronou
luk 4:6 kai eipen autw o diabolos soi dwsw thn ecousian tauthn apasan kai thn docan autwn oti emoi paradedotai kai w ean qelw didwmi authn
luk 4:7 su oun ean proskunhshs enwpion emou estai sou pasa.
luk 4:8 kai apokriqeis o ihsous eipen autw gegraptai kurion ton qeon sou proskunhseis kai autw monw latreuseis.

luk 4:11 kai oti epi xeirwn arousin se mhpote proskoyhs pros liqon ton poda sou.
luk 4:12 kai apokriqeis eipen autw o ihsous oti eirhtai ouk ekpeiraseis kurion ton qeon sou.
luk 4:13 kai suntelesas panta peirasmon o diabolos apesth ap autou axri kairou.
luk 4:14 kai upestreyen o ihsous en th dunamei tou pneumatos eis thn galilaian. kai fhmh echlqen kaq olhs ths perixwrou peri autou.

luk 4:16 kai hlqen eis nazara ou hn teqrammenos kai eishlqen kata to eiwqos autw en th hmera twn sabbatwn eis thn sunagwghn kai anesth anagnwnai.

luk 4:18 pneuma kuriou ep eme ou eineken exrisen me euaggelisasqai ptwxois apestalken me khrucai aixmalwtois afesin kai tuflois anableyin aposteilai teqrausmenous en afesei
luk 4:19 khrucai eniauton kuriou dekton.

luk 4:22 kai pantes emarturoun autw kai eqaumazon epi tois logois ths xaritos tois ekporeuomenois ek tou stomatos autou kai elegon ouxi uios estin iwshf outos;
luk 4:23 kai eipen pros autous pantws ereite moi thn parabolhn tauthn iatre qerapeuson seauton osa hkousamen genomena eis thn kafarnaoum poihson kai wde en th patridi sou.
luk 4:24 eipen de amhn legw umin oti oudeis profhths dektos estin en th patridi autou.
luk 4:25 ep alhqeias de legw umin pollai xhrai hsan en tais hmerais hliou en tw israhl ote ekleisqh o ouranos epi eth tria kai mhnas ec ws egeneto limos megas epi pasan thn ghn
luk 4:26 kai pros oudemian autwn epemfqh hlias ei mh eis sarepta ths sidwnias pros gunaika xhran.
luk 4:27 kai polloi leproi hsan en tw israhl epi elisaiou tou profhtou kai oudeis autwn ekaqarisqh ei mh naiman o suros.
luk 4:28 kai eplhsqhsan pantes qumou en th sunagwgh akouontes tauta
luk 4:29 kai anastantes ecebalon auton ecw ths polews kai hgagon auton ews ofruos tou orous ef ou h polis wkodomhto autwn wste katakrhmnisai auton
luk 4:30 autos de dielqwn dia mesou autwn eporeueto.

luk 4:32 kai eceplhssonto epi th didaxh autou oti en ecousia hn o logos autou.
luk 4:33 kai en th sunagwgh hn anqrwpos exwn pneuma daimoniou akaqartou kai anekracen fwnh megalh

luk 4:36 kai egeneto qambos epi pantas kai sunelaloun pros allhlous legontes tis o logos outos oti en ecousia kai dunamei epitassei tois akaqartois pneumasin kai ecerxontai;
luk 4:37 kai eceporeueto hxos peri autou eis panta topon ths perixwrou.

luk 5:20 kai idwn thn pistin autwn eipen anqrwpe afewntai soi ai amartiai sou.
luk 5:21 kai hrcanto dialogizesqai oi grammateis kai oi farisaioi legontes tis estin outos os lalei blasfhmias; tis dunatai amartias afeinai ei mh monos o qeos;

luk 5:24 ina de eidhte oti o uios tou anqrwpou ecousian exei epi ths ghs afienai amartias eipen tw paralelumenw soi legw egeire kai aras to klinidion sou poreuou eis ton oikon sou.
luk 5:25 kai paraxrhma anastas enwpion autwn aras ef o katekeito aphlqen eis ton oikon autou docazwn ton qeon.

luk 5:32 ouk elhluqa kalesai dikaious alla amartwlous eis metanoian.

luk 6:2 tines de twn farisaiwn eipan ti poieite o ouk ecestin tois sabbasin;
luk 6:3 kai apokriqeis pros autous eipen o ihsous oude touto anegnwte o epoihsen dauid ote epeinasen autos kai oi met autou ontes;
luk 6:4 ws eishlqen eis ton oikon tou qeou kai tous artous ths proqesews labwn efagen kai edwken tois met autou ous ouk ecestin fagein ei mh monous tous iereis;
luk 6:5 kai elegen autois kurios estin tou sabbatou o uios tou anqrwpou.
luk 6:6 egeneto de en eterw sabbatw eiselqein auton eis thn sunagwghn kai didaskein kai hn anqrwpos ekei kai h xeir autou h decia hn chra
luk 6:7 parethrounto de auton oi grammateis kai oi farisaioi ei en tw sabbatw qerapeuei ina eurwsin kathgorein autou.
luk 6:8 autos de hdei tous dialogismous autwn eipen de tw andri tw chran exonti thn xeira egeire kai sthqi eis to meson kai anastas esth.
luk 6:9 eipen de o ihsous pros autous eperwtw umas ei ecestin tw sabbatw agaqopoihsai h kakopoihsai yuxhn swsai h apolesai;
luk 6:10 kai peribleyamenos pantas autous eipen autw ekteinon thn xeira sou. o de epoihsen kai apekatestaqh h xeir autou.
luk 6:11 autoi de eplhsqhsan anoias kai dielaloun pros allhlous ti an poihsaien tw ihsou.
luk 6:12 egeneto de en tais hmerais tautais ecelqein auton eis to oros proseucasqai kai hn dianuktereuwn en th proseuxh tou qeou.
luk 6:13 kai ote egeneto hmera prosefwnhsen tous maqhtas autou kai eklecamenos ap autwn dwdeka ous kai apostolous wnomasen
luk 6:14 simwna on kai wnomasen petron kai andrean ton adelfon autou kai iakwbon kai iwannhn kai filippon kai barqolomaion
luk 6:15 kai maqqaion kai qwman kai iakwbon alfaiou kai simwna ton kaloumenon zhlwthn
luk 6:16 kai ioudan iakwbou kai ioudan iskariwq os egeneto prodoths.
luk 6:17 kai katabas met autwn esth epi topou pedinou kai oxlos polus maqhtwn autou kai plhqos polu tou laou apo pashs ths ioudaias kai ierousalhm kai ths paraliou turou kai sidwnos
luk 6:18 oi hlqon akousai autou kai iaqhnai apo twn noswn autwn kai oi enoxloumenoi apo pneumatwn akaqartwn eqerapeuonto.
luk 6:19 kai pas o oxlos ezhtoun aptesqai autou oti dunamis par autou echrxeto kai iato pantas.
luk 6:20 kai autos eparas tous ofqalmous autou eis tous maqhtas autou elegen makarioi oi ptwxoi oti umetera estin h basileia tou qeou.
luk 6:21 makarioi oi peinwntes nun oti xortasqhsesqe. makarioi oi klaiontes nun oti gelasete.
luk 6:22 makarioi este otan mishswsin umas oi anqrwpoi kai otan aforiswsin umas kai oneidiswsin kai ekbalwsin to onoma umwn ws ponhron eneka tou uiou tou anqrwpou
luk 6:23 xarhte en ekeinh th hmera kai skirthsate idou gar o misqos umwn polus en tw ouranw kata ta auta gar epoioun tois profhtais oi pateres autwn.
luk 6:24 plhn ouai umin tois plousiois oti apexete thn paraklhsin umwn.
luk 6:25 ouai umin oi empeplhsmenoi nun oti peinasete. ouai oi gelwntes nun oti penqhsete kai klausete.
luk 6:26 ouai otan umas kalws eipwsin pantes oi anqrwpoi kata ta auta gar epoioun tois yeudoprofhtais oi pateres autwn.
luk 6:27 alla umin legw tois akouousin agapate tous exqrous umwn kalws poieite tois misousin umas
luk 6:28 eulogeite tous katarwmenous umas proseuxesqe peri twn ephreazontwn umas.
luk 6:29 tw tuptonti se epi thn siagona parexe kai thn allhn kai apo tou airontos sou to imation kai ton xitwna mh kwlushs.
luk 6:30 panti aitounti se didou kai apo tou airontos ta sa mh apaitei.
luk 6:31 kai kaqws qelete ina poiwsin umin oi anqrwpoi poieite autois omoiws.
luk 6:32 kai ei agapate tous agapwntas umas poia umin xaris estin; kai gar oi amartwloi tous agapwntas autous agapwsin.
luk 6:33 kai gar ean agaqopoihte tous agaqopoiountas umas poia umin xaris estin; kai oi amartwloi to auto poiousin.
luk 6:34 kai ean danishte par wn elpizete labein poia umin xaris estin; kai amartwloi amartwlois danizousin ina apolabwsin ta isa.
luk 6:35 plhn agapate tous exqrous umwn kai agaqopoieite kai danizete mhden apelpizontes kai estai o misqos umwn polus kai esesqe uioi uyistou oti autos xrhstos estin epi tous axaristous kai ponhrous.
luk 6:36 ginesqe oiktirmones kaqws kai o pathr umwn oiktirmwn estin.
luk 6:37 kai mh krinete kai ou mh kriqhte kai mh katadikazete kai ou mh katadikasqhte. apoluete kai apoluqhsesqe
luk 6:38 didote kai doqhsetai umin metron kalon pepiesmenon sesaleumenon uperekxunnomenon dwsousin eis ton kolpon umwn w gar metrw metreite antimetrhqhsetai umin.
luk 6:39 eipen de kai parabolhn autois mhti dunatai tuflos tuflon odhgein; ouxi amfoteroi eis boqunon empesountai;
luk 6:40 ouk estin maqhths uper ton didaskalon kathrtismenos de pas estai ws o didaskalos autou.
luk 6:41 ti de blepeis to karfos to en tw ofqalmw tou adelfou sou thn de dokon thn en tw idiw ofqalmw ou katanoeis;
luk 6:42 pws dunasai legein tw adelfw sou adelfe afes ekbalw to karfos to en tw ofqalmw sou autos thn en tw ofqalmw sou dokon ou blepwn; upokrita ekbale prwton thn dokon ek tou ofqalmou sou kai tote diableyeis to karfos to en tw ofqalmw tou adelfou sou ekbalein.
luk 6:43 ou gar estin dendron kalon poioun karpon sapron oude palin dendron sapron poioun karpon kalon.
luk 6:44 ekaston gar dendron ek tou idiou karpou ginwsketai ou gar ec akanqwn sullegousin suka oude ek batou stafulhn trugwsin.
luk 6:45 o agaqos anqrwpos ek tou agaqou qhsaurou ths kardias proferei to agaqon kai o ponhros ek tou ponhrou proferei to ponhron ek gar perisseumatos kardias lalei to stoma autou.
luk 6:46 ti de me kaleite kurie kurie kai ou poieite a legw;
luk 6:47 pas o erxomenos pros me kai akouwn mou twn logwn kai poiwn autous upodeicw umin tini estin omoios
luk 6:48 omoios estin anqrwpw oikodomounti oikian os eskayen kai ebaqunen kai eqhken qemelion epi thn petran plhmmurhs de genomenhs proserhcen o potamos th oikia ekeinh kai ouk isxusen saleusai authn dia to kalws oikodomhsqai authn.
luk 6:49 o de akousas kai mh poihsas omoios estin anqrwpw oikodomhsanti oikian epi thn ghn xwris qemeliou h proserhcen o potamos kai euqus sunepesen kai egeneto to rhgma ths oikias ekeinhs mega.
luk 7:1 epeidh eplhrwsen panta ta rhmata autou eis tas akoas tou laou eishlqen eis kafarnaoum.
luk 7:2 ekatontarxou de tinos doulos kakws exwn hmellen teleutan os hn autw entimos.
luk 7:3 akousas de peri tou ihsou apesteilen pros auton presbuterous twn ioudaiwn erwtwn auton opws elqwn diaswsh ton doulon autou.
luk 7:4 oi de paragenomenoi pros ton ihsoun parekaloun auton spoudaiws legontes oti acios estin w parech touto
luk 7:5 agapa gar to eqnos hmwn kai thn sunagwghn autos wkodomhsen hmin.
luk 7:6 o de ihsous eporeueto sun autois. hdh de autou ou makran apexontos apo ths oikias epemyen filous o ekatontarxhs legwn autw kurie mh skullou ou gar ikanos eimi ina upo thn steghn mou eiselqhs
luk 7:7 dio oude emauton hciwsa pros se elqein alla eipe logw kai iaqhtw o pais mou.
luk 7:8 kai gar egw anqrwpos eimi upo ecousian tassomenos exwn up emauton stratiwtas kai legw toutw poreuqhti kai poreuetai kai allw erxou kai erxetai kai tw doulw mou poihson touto kai poiei.
luk 7:9 akousas de tauta o ihsous eqaumasen auton kai strafeis tw akolouqounti autw oxlw eipen legw umin oude en tw israhl tosauthn pistin euron.
luk 7:10 kai upostreyantes eis ton oikon oi pemfqentes euron ton doulon ugiainonta.
luk 7:11 kai egeneto en tw echs eporeuqh eis polin kaloumenhn nain kai suneporeuonto autw oi maqhtai autou kai oxlos polus.
luk 7:12 ws de hggisen th pulh ths polews kai idou ecekomizeto teqnhkws monogenhs uios th mhtri autou kai auth hn xhra kai oxlos ths polews ikanos hn sun auth.
luk 7:13 kai idwn authn o kurios esplagxnisqh ep auth kai eipen auth mh klaie.
luk 7:14 kai proselqwn hyato ths sorou oi de bastazontes esthsan kai eipen neaniske soi legw egerqhti.
luk 7:15 kai anekaqisen o nekros kai hrcato lalein kai edwken auton th mhtri autou.
luk 7:16 elaben de fobos pantas kai edocazon ton qeon legontes oti profhths megas hgerqh en hmin kai oti epeskeyato o qeos ton laon autou.
luk 7:17 kai echlqen o logos outos en olh th ioudaia peri autou kai pash th perixwrw.
luk 7:18 kai aphggeilan iwannh oi maqhtai autou peri pantwn toutwn. kai proskalesamenos duo tinas twn maqhtwn autou o iwannhs
luk 7:19 epemyen pros ton kurion legwn su ei o erxomenos h allon prosdokwmen;
luk 7:20 paragenomenoi de pros auton oi andres eipan iwannhs o baptisths apesteilen hmas pros se legwn su ei o erxomenos h allon prosdokwmen;
luk 7:21 en ekeinh th wra eqerapeusen pollous apo noswn kai mastigwn kai pneumatwn ponhrwn kai tuflois pollois exarisato blepein.
luk 7:22 kai apokriqeis eipen autois poreuqentes apaggeilate iwannh a eidete kai hkousate tufloi anablepousin xwloi peripatousin leproi kaqarizontai kai kwfoi akouousin nekroi egeirontai ptwxoi euaggelizontai
luk 7:23 kai makarios estin os ean mh skandalisqh en emoi.
luk 7:24 apelqontwn de twn aggelwn iwannou hrcato legein pros tous oxlous peri iwannou ti echlqate eis thn erhmon qeasasqai; kalamon upo anemou saleuomenon;
luk 7:25 alla ti echlqate idein; anqrwpon en malakois imatiois hmfiesmenon; idou oi en imatismw endocw kai trufh uparxontes en tois basileiois eisin.
luk 7:26 alla ti echlqate idein; profhthn; nai legw umin kai perissoteron profhtou.
luk 7:27 outos estin peri ou gegraptai idou apostellw ton aggelon mou pro proswpou sou os kataskeuasei thn odon sou emprosqen sou.
luk 7:28 legw umin meizwn en gennhtois gunaikwn iwannou oudeis estin o de mikroteros en th basileia tou qeou meizwn autou estin.
luk 7:29 kai pas o laos akousas kai oi telwnai edikaiwsan ton qeon baptisqentes to baptisma iwannou
luk 7:30 oi de farisaioi kai oi nomikoi thn boulhn tou qeou hqethsan eis eautous mh baptisqentes up autou.
luk 7:31 tini oun omoiwsw tous anqrwpous ths geneas tauths kai tini eisin omoioi;
luk 7:32 omoioi eisin paidiois tois en agora kaqhmenois kai prosfwnousin allhlois a legei hulhsamen umin kai ouk wrxhsasqe eqrhnhsamen kai ouk eklausate.
luk 7:33 elhluqen gar iwannhs o baptisths mh esqiwn arton mhte pinwn oinon kai legete daimonion exei
luk 7:34 elhluqen o uios tou anqrwpou esqiwn kai pinwn kai legete idou anqrwpos fagos kai oinopoths filos telwnwn kai amartwlwn.
luk 7:35 kai edikaiwqh h sofia apo pantwn twn teknwn auths.
luk 7:36 hrwta de tis auton twn farisaiwn ina fagh met autou kai eiselqwn eis ton oikon tou farisaiou katekliqh.
luk 7:37 kai idou gunh htis hn en th polei amartwlos kai epignousa oti katakeitai en th oikia tou farisaiou komisasa alabastron murou
luk 7:38 kai stasa opisw para tous podas autou klaiousa tois dakrusin hrcato brexein tous podas autou kai tais qricin ths kefalhs auths ecemassen kai katefilei tous podas autou kai hleifen tw murw.
luk 7:39 idwn de o farisaios o kalesas auton eipen en eautw legwn outos ei hn profhths eginwsken an tis kai potaph h gunh htis aptetai autou oti amartwlos estin.
luk 7:40 kai apokriqeis o ihsous eipen pros auton simwn exw soi ti eipein. o de didaskale eipe fhsin.
luk 7:41 duo xreofeiletai hsan danisth tini o eis wfeilen dhnaria pentakosia o de eteros penthkonta.
luk 7:42 mh exontwn autwn apodounai amfoterois exarisato. tis oun autwn pleion agaphsei auton;
luk 7:43 apokriqeis simwn eipen upolambanw oti w to pleion exarisato. o de eipen autw orqws ekrinas.
luk 7:44 kai strafeis pros thn gunaika tw simwni efh blepeis tauthn thn gunaika; eishlqon sou eis thn oikian udwr moi epi podas ouk edwkas auth de tois dakrusin ebrecen mou tous podas kai tais qricin auths ecemacen.
luk 7:45 filhma moi ouk edwkas auth de af hs eishlqon ou dielipen katafilousa mou tous podas.
luk 7:46 elaiw thn kefalhn mou ouk hleiyas auth de murw hleiyen tous podas mou.
luk 7:47 ou xarin legw soi afewntai ai amartiai auths ai pollai oti hgaphsen polu w de oligon afietai oligon agapa.
luk 7:48 eipen de auth afewntai sou ai amartiai.
luk 7:49 kai hrcanto oi sunanakeimenoi legein en eautois tis outos estin os kai amartias afihsin;
luk 7:50 eipen de pros thn gunaika h pistis sou seswken se poreuou eis eirhnhn.
luk 8:1 kai egeneto en tw kaqechs kai autos diwdeuen kata polin kai kwmhn khrusswn kai euaggelizomenos thn basileian tou qeou kai oi dwdeka sun autw
luk 8:2 kai gunaikes tines ai hsan teqerapeumenai apo pneumatwn ponhrwn kai asqeneiwn maria h kaloumenh magdalhnh af hs daimonia epta ecelhluqei
luk 8:3 kai iwanna gunh xouza epitropou hrwdou kai sousanna kai eterai pollai aitines dihkonoun autois ek twn uparxontwn [autw].
luk 8:4 suniontos de oxlou pollou kai twn kata polin epiporeuomenwn pros auton eipen dia parabolhs
luk 8:5 echlqen o speirwn tou speirai ton sporon autou. kai en tw speirein auton o men epesen para thn odon kai katepathqh kai ta peteina tou ouranou katefagen auto.
luk 8:6 kai eteron katepesen epi thn petran kai fuen echranqh dia to mh exein ikmada.
luk 8:7 kai eteron epesen en mesw twn akanqwn kai sumfueisai ai akanqai apepnican auto.
luk 8:8 kai eteron epesen eis thn ghn thn agaqhn kai fuen epoihsen karpon ekatontaplasiona. tauta legwn efwnei o exwn wta akouein akouetw.
luk 8:9 ephrwtwn de auton oi maqhtai autou tis auth eih h parabolh.
luk 8:10 o de eipen umin dedotai gnwnai ta musthria ths basileias tou qeou tois de loipois en parabolais ina blepontes mh blepwsin kai akouontes mh suniwsin.
luk 8:11 estin de auth h parabolh o sporos estin o logos tou qeou.
luk 8:12 oi de para thn odon eisin oi akousantes eita erxetai o diabolos kai airei ton logon apo ths kardias autwn ina mh pisteusantes swqwsin.
luk 8:13 oi de epi ths petras oi otan akouswsin meta xaras dexontai ton logon kai outoi rizan ouk exousin oi pros kairon pisteuousin kai en kairw peirasmou afistantai.
luk 8:14 to de eis tas akanqas peson outoi eisin oi akousantes kai upo merimnwn kai ploutou kai hdonwn tou biou poreuomenoi sumpnigontai kai ou telesforousin.
luk 8:15 to de en th kalh gh outoi eisin oitines en kardia kalh kai agaqh akousantes ton logon katexousin kai karpoforousin en upomonh.
luk 8:16 oudeis de luxnon ayas kaluptei auton skeuei h upokatw klinhs tiqhsin all epi luxnias tiqhsin ina oi eisporeuomenoi blepwsin to fws.
luk 8:17 ou gar estin krupton o ou faneron genhsetai oude apokrufon o ou mh gnwsqh kai eis faneron elqh.
luk 8:18 blepete oun pws akouete os an gar exh doqhsetai autw kai os an mh exh kai o dokei exein arqhsetai ap autou.
luk 8:19 paregeneto de pros auton h mhthr kai oi adelfoi autou kai ouk hdunanto suntuxein autw dia ton oxlon.
luk 8:20 aphggelh de autw h mhthr sou kai oi adelfoi sou esthkasin ecw idein qelontes se.
luk 8:21 o de apokriqeis eipen pros autous mhthr mou kai adelfoi mou outoi eisin oi ton logon tou qeou akouontes kai poiountes.
luk 8:22 egeneto de en mia twn hmerwn kai autos enebh eis ploion kai oi maqhtai autou kai eipen pros autous dielqwmen eis to peran ths limnhs kai anhxqhsan.
luk 8:23 pleontwn de autwn afupnwsen. kai katebh lailay anemou eis thn limnhn kai suneplhrounto kai ekinduneuon.
luk 8:24 proselqontes de dihgeiran auton legontes epistata epistata apollumeqa. o de diegerqeis epetimhsen tw anemw kai tw kludwni tou udatos kai epausanto kai egeneto galhnh.
luk 8:25 eipen de autois pou h pistis umwn; fobhqentes de eqaumasan legontes pros allhlous tis ara outos estin oti kai tois anemois epitassei kai tw udati kai upakouousin autw;
luk 8:26 kai katepleusan eis thn xwran twn gerashnwn htis estin antipera ths galilaias.
luk 8:27 ecelqonti de autw epi thn ghn uphnthsen anhr tis ek ths polews exwn daimonia kai xronw ikanw ouk enedusato imation kai en oikia ouk emenen all en tois mnhmasin.
luk 8:28 idwn de ton ihsoun anakracas prosepesen autw kai fwnh megalh eipen ti emoi kai soi ihsou uie tou qeou tou uyistou; deomai sou mh me basanishs.
luk 8:29 parhggeilen gar tw pneumati tw akaqartw ecelqein apo tou anqrwpou. pollois gar xronois sunhrpakei auton kai edesmeueto alusesin kai pedais fulassomenos kai diarrhsswn ta desma hlauneto upo tou daimoniou eis tas erhmous.
luk 8:30 ephrwthsen de auton o ihsous ti soi onoma estin; o de eipen legiwn oti eishlqen daimonia polla eis auton.
luk 8:31 kai parekaloun auton ina mh epitach autois eis thn abusson apelqein.
luk 8:32 hn de ekei agelh xoirwn ikanwn boskomenh en tw orei kai parekalesan auton ina epitreyh autois eis ekeinous eiselqein kai epetreyen autois.
luk 8:33 ecelqonta de ta daimonia apo tou anqrwpou eishlqon eis tous xoirous kai wrmhsen h agelh kata tou krhmnou eis thn limnhn kai apepnigh.
luk 8:34 idontes de oi boskontes to gegonos efugon kai aphggeilan eis thn polin kai eis tous agrous.
luk 8:35 echlqon de idein to gegonos kai hlqon pros ton ihsoun kai euron kaqhmenon ton anqrwpon af ou ta daimonia echlqen imatismenon kai swfronounta para tous podas tou ihsou kai efobhqhsan.
luk 8:36 aphggeilan de autois oi idontes pws eswqh o daimonisqeis.
luk 8:37 kai hrwthsen auton apan to plhqos ths perixwrou twn gerashnwn apelqein ap autwn oti fobw megalw suneixonto autos de embas eis ploion upestreyen.
luk 8:38 edeito de autou o anhr af ou ecelhluqei ta daimonia einai sun autw apelusen de auton legwn
luk 8:39 upostrefe eis ton oikon sou kai dihgou osa soi epoihsen o qeos. kai aphlqen kaq olhn thn polin khrusswn osa epoihsen autw o ihsous.
luk 8:40 en de tw upostrefein ton ihsoun apedecato auton o oxlos hsan gar pantes prosdokwntes auton.
luk 8:41 kai idou hlqen anhr w onoma iairos kai outos arxwn ths sunagwghs uphrxen kai peswn para tous podas tou ihsou parekalei auton eiselqein eis ton oikon autou
luk 8:42 oti qugathr monogenhs hn autw ws etwn dwdeka kai auth apeqnhsken. en de tw upagein auton oi oxloi sunepnigon auton.
luk 8:43 kai gunh ousa en rusei aimatos apo etwn dwdeka htis [--] ouk isxusen ap oudenos qerapeuqhnai
luk 8:44 proselqousa opisqen hyato tou kraspedou tou imatiou autou kai paraxrhma esth h rusis tou aimatos auths.
luk 8:45 kai eipen o ihsous tis o ayamenos mou; arnoumenwn de pantwn eipen o petros epistata oi oxloi sunexousin se kai apoqlibousin.
luk 8:46 o de ihsous eipen hyato mou tis egw gar egnwn dunamin ecelhluquian ap emou.
luk 8:47 idousa de h gunh oti ouk elaqen tremousa hlqen kai prospesousa autw di hn aitian hyato autou aphggeilen enwpion pantos tou laou kai ws iaqh paraxrhma.
luk 8:48 o de eipen auth qugathr h pistis sou seswken se poreuou eis eirhnhn.
luk 8:49 eti autou lalountos erxetai tis para tou arxisunagwgou legwn oti teqnhken h qugathr sou mhketi skulle ton didaskalon.
luk 8:50 o de ihsous akousas apekriqh autw mh fobou monon pisteuson kai swqhsetai.
luk 8:51 elqwn de eis thn oikian ouk afhken eiselqein tina sun autw ei mh petron kai iwannhn kai iakwbon kai ton patera ths paidos kai thn mhtera.
luk 8:52 eklaion de pantes kai ekoptonto authn. o de eipen mh klaiete ou gar apeqanen alla kaqeudei.
luk 8:53 kai kategelwn autou eidotes oti apeqanen.
luk 8:54 autos de krathsas ths xeiros auths efwnhsen legwn h pais egeire.
luk 8:55 kai epestreyen to pneuma auths kai anesth paraxrhma kai dietacen auth doqhnai fagein.
luk 8:56 kai ecesthsan oi goneis auths o de parhggeilen autois mhdeni eipein to gegonos.
luk 9:1 sugkalesamenos de tous dwdeka edwken autois dunamin kai ecousian epi panta ta daimonia kai nosous qerapeuein
luk 9:2 kai apesteilen autous khrussein thn basileian tou qeou kai iasqai tous asqeneis
luk 9:3 kai eipen pros autous mhden airete eis thn odon mhte rabdon mhte phran mhte arton mhte argurion mhte ana duo xitwnas exein.
luk 9:4 kai eis hn an oikian eiselqhte ekei menete kai ekeiqen ecerxesqe.
luk 9:5 kai osoi an mh dexwntai umas ecerxomenoi apo ths polews ekeinhs ton koniorton apo twn podwn umwn apotinassete eis marturion ep autous.
luk 9:6 ecerxomenoi de dihrxonto kata tas kwmas euaggelizomenoi kai qerapeuontes pantaxou.
luk 9:7 hkousen de hrwdhs o tetraarxhs ta ginomena panta kai dihporei dia to legesqai upo tinwn oti iwannhs hgerqh ek nekrwn
luk 9:8 upo tinwn de oti hlias efanh allwn de oti profhths tis twn arxaiwn anesth.
luk 9:9 eipen de hrwdhs iwannhn egw apekefalisa tis de estin outos peri ou akouw toiauta; kai ezhtei idein auton.
luk 9:10 kai upostreyantes oi apostoloi dihghsanto autw osa epoihsan. kai paralabwn autous upexwrhsen kat idian eis polin kaloumenhn bhqsaida.
luk 9:11 oi de oxloi gnontes hkolouqhsan autw. kai apodecamenos autous elalei autois peri ths basileias tou qeou kai tous xreian exontas qerapeias iato.
luk 9:12 h de hmera hrcato klinein proselqontes de oi dwdeka eipan autw apoluson ton oxlon ina poreuqentes eis tas kuklw kwmas kai agrous kataluswsin kai eurwsin episitismon oti wde en erhmw topw esmen.
luk 9:13 eipen de pros autous dote autois umeis fagein. oi de eipan ouk eisin hmin pleion h artoi pente kai ixques duo ei mhti poreuqentes hmeis agoraswmen eis panta ton laon touton brwmata.
luk 9:14 hsan gar wsei andres pentakisxilioi. eipen de pros tous maqhtas autou kataklinate autous klisias wsei ana penthkonta.
luk 9:15 kai epoihsan outws kai kateklinan apantas.
luk 9:16 labwn de tous pente artous kai tous duo ixquas anableyas eis ton ouranon euloghsen autous kai kateklasen kai edidou tois maqhtais paraqeinai tw oxlw.
luk 9:17 kai efagon kai exortasqhsan pantes kai hrqh to perisseusan autois klasmatwn kofinoi dwdeka.
luk 9:18 kai egeneto en tw einai auton proseuxomenon kata monas sunhsan autw oi maqhtai kai ephrwthsen autous legwn tina me legousin oi oxloi einai;
luk 9:19 oi de apokriqentes eipan iwannhn ton baptisthn alloi de hlian alloi de oti profhths tis twn arxaiwn anesth.
luk 9:20 eipen de autois umeis de tina me legete einai; petros de apokriqeis eipen ton xriston tou qeou.
luk 9:21 o de epitimhsas autois parhggeilen mhdeni legein touto
luk 9:22 eipwn oti dei ton uion tou anqrwpou polla paqein kai apodokimasqhnai apo twn presbuterwn kai arxierewn kai grammatewn kai apoktanqhnai kai th trith hmera egerqhnai.
luk 9:23 elegen de pros pantas ei tis qelei opisw mou erxesqai arnhsasqw eauton kai aratw ton stauron autou kaq hmeran kai akolouqeitw moi.
luk 9:24 os gar an qelh thn yuxhn autou swsai apolesei authn os d an apolesh thn yuxhn autou eneken emou outos swsei authn.
luk 9:25 ti gar wfeleitai anqrwpos kerdhsas ton kosmon olon eauton de apolesas h zhmiwqeis;
luk 9:26 os gar an epaisxunqh me kai tous emous logous touton o uios tou anqrwpou epaisxunqhsetai otan elqh en th doch autou kai tou patros kai twn agiwn aggelwn.
luk 9:27 legw de umin alhqws eisin tines twn autou esthkotwn oi ou mh geuswntai qanatou ews an idwsin thn basileian tou qeou.
luk 9:28 egeneto de meta tous logous toutous wsei hmerai oktw kai paralabwn petron kai iwannhn kai iakwbon anebh eis to oros proseucasqai.
luk 9:29 kai egeneto en tw proseuxesqai auton to eidos tou proswpou autou eteron kai o imatismos autou leukos ecastraptwn.
luk 9:30 kai idou andres duo sunelaloun autw oitines hsan mwushs kai hlias
luk 9:31 oi ofqentes en doch elegon thn ecodon autou hn hmellen plhroun en ierousalhm.
luk 9:32 o de petros kai oi sun autw hsan bebarhmenoi upnw diagrhgorhsantes de eidon thn docan autou kai tous duo andras tous sunestwtas autw.
luk 9:33 kai egeneto en tw diaxwrizesqai autous ap autou eipen o petros pros ton ihsoun epistata kalon estin hmas wde einai kai poihswmen skhnas treis mian soi kai mian mwusei kai mian hlia mh eidws o legei.
luk 9:34 tauta de autou legontos egeneto nefelh kai epeskiazen autous efobhqhsan de en tw eiselqein autous eis thn nefelhn.
luk 9:35 kai fwnh egeneto ek ths nefelhs legousa outos estin o uios mou o eklelegmenos autou akouete.
luk 9:36 kai en tw genesqai thn fwnhn eureqh ihsous monos. kai autoi esighsan kai oudeni aphggeilan en ekeinais tais hmerais ouden wn ewrakan.
luk 9:37 egeneto de th echs hmera katelqontwn autwn apo tou orous sunhnthsen autw oxlos polus.
luk 9:38 kai idou anhr apo tou oxlou ebohsen legwn didaskale deomai sou epibleyai epi ton uion mou oti monogenhs moi estin
luk 9:39 kai idou pneuma lambanei auton kai ecaifnhs krazei kai sparassei auton meta afrou kai mogis apoxwrei ap autou suntribon auton
luk 9:40 kai edehqhn twn maqhtwn sou ina ekbalwsin auto kai ouk hdunhqhsan.
luk 9:41 apokriqeis de o ihsous eipen w genea apistos kai diestrammenh ews pote esomai pros umas kai anecomai umwn; prosagage wde ton uion sou.
luk 9:42 eti de proserxomenou autou errhcen auton to daimonion kai sunesparacen epetimhsen de o ihsous tw pneumati tw akaqartw kai iasato ton paida kai apedwken auton tw patri autou.
luk 9:43 eceplhssonto de pantes epi th megaleiothti tou qeou. pantwn de qaumazontwn epi pasin ois epoiei eipen pros tous maqhtas autou
luk 9:44 qesqe umeis eis ta wta umwn tous logous toutous o gar uios tou anqrwpou mellei paradidosqai eis xeiras anqrwpwn.
luk 9:45 oi de hgnooun to rhma touto kai hn parakekalummenon ap autwn ina mh aisqwntai auto kai efobounto erwthsai auton peri tou rhmatos toutou.
luk 9:46 eishlqen de dialogismos en autois to tis an eih meizwn autwn.
luk 9:47 o de ihsous eidws ton dialogismon ths kardias autwn epilabomenos paidion esthsen auto par eautw
luk 9:48 kai eipen autois os ean dechtai touto to paidion epi tw onomati mou eme dexetai kai os an eme dechtai dexetai ton aposteilanta me o gar mikroteros en pasin umin uparxwn outos estin megas.
luk 9:49 apokriqeis de iwannhs eipen epistata eidomen tina en tw onomati sou ekballonta daimonia kai ekwluomen auton oti ouk akolouqei meq hmwn.
luk 9:50 eipen de pros auton o ihsous mh kwluete os gar ouk estin kaq umwn uper umwn estin.
luk 9:51 egeneto de en tw sumplhrousqai tas hmeras ths analhmyews autou kai autos to proswpon esthrisen tou poreuesqai eis ierousalhm
luk 9:52 kai apesteilen aggelous pro proswpou autou. kai poreuqentes eishlqon eis kwmhn samaritwn ws etoimasai autw
luk 9:53 kai ouk edecanto auton oti to proswpon autou hn poreuomenon eis ierousalhm.
luk 9:54 idontes de oi maqhtai iakwbos kai iwannhs eipan kurie qeleis eipwmen pur katabhnai apo tou ouranou kai analwsai autous;
luk 9:55 strafeis de epetimhsen autois.
luk 9:56 kai eporeuqhsan eis eteran kwmhn.
luk 9:57 kai poreuomenwn autwn en th odw eipen tis pros auton akolouqhsw soi opou ean aperxh.
luk 9:58 kai eipen autw o ihsous ai alwpekes fwleous exousin kai ta peteina tou ouranou kataskhnwseis o de uios tou anqrwpou ouk exei pou thn kefalhn klinh.
luk 9:59 eipen de pros eteron akolouqei moi. o de eipen kurie epitreyon moi apelqonti prwton qayai ton patera mou.
luk 9:60 eipen de autw afes tous nekrous qayai tous eautwn nekrous su de apelqwn diaggelle thn basileian tou qeou.
luk 9:61 eipen de kai eteros akolouqhsw soi kurie prwton de epitreyon moi apotacasqai tois eis ton oikon mou.
luk 9:62 eipen de pros auton o ihsous oudeis epibalwn thn xeira ep arotron kai blepwn eis ta opisw euqetos estin th basileia tou qeou.
luk 10:1 meta de tauta anedeicen o kurios eterous ebdomhkonta duo kai apesteilen autous ana duo duo pro proswpou autou eis pasan polin kai topon ou hmellen autos erxesqai.
luk 10:2 elegen de pros autous o men qerismos polus oi de ergatai oligoi dehqhte oun tou kuriou tou qerismou opws ergatas ekbalh eis ton qerismon autou.
luk 10:3 upagete idou apostellw umas ws arnas en mesw lukwn.
luk 10:4 mh bastazete ballantion mh phran mh upodhmata kai mhdena kata thn odon aspashsqe.
luk 10:5 eis hn d an eiselqhte oikian prwton legete eirhnh tw oikw toutw.
luk 10:6 kai ean ekei h uios eirhnhs epanapahsetai ep auton h eirhnh umwn ei de mh ge ef umas anakamyei.
luk 10:7 en auth de th oikia menete esqiontes kai pinontes ta par autwn acios gar o ergaths tou misqou autou. mh metabainete ec oikias eis oikian.
luk 10:8 kai eis hn an polin eiserxhsqe kai dexwntai umas esqiete ta paratiqemena umin
luk 10:9 kai qerapeuete tous en auth asqeneis kai legete autois hggiken ef umas h basileia tou qeou.
luk 10:10 eis hn d an polin eiselqhte kai mh dexwntai umas ecelqontes eis tas plateias auths eipate
luk 10:11 kai ton koniorton ton kollhqenta hmin ek ths polews umwn eis tous podas apomassomeqa umin plhn touto ginwskete oti hggiken h basileia tou qeou.
luk 10:12 legw umin oti sodomois en th hmera ekeinh anektoteron estai h th polei ekeinh.
luk 10:13 ouai soi xorazin ouai soi bhqsaida oti ei en turw kai sidwni egenhqhsan ai dunameis ai genomenai en umin palai an en sakkw kai spodw kaqhmenoi metenohsan.
luk 10:14 plhn turw kai sidwni anektoteron estai en th krisei h umin.
luk 10:15 kai su kafarnaoum mh ews ouranou uywqhsh; ews tou adou [katabibasqhsh].
luk 10:16 o akouwn umwn emou akouei kai o aqetwn umas eme aqetei o de eme aqetwn aqetei ton aposteilanta me.
luk 10:17 upestreyan de oi ebdomhkonta duo meta xaras legontes kurie kai ta daimonia upotassetai hmin en tw onomati sou.
luk 10:18 eipen de autois eqewroun ton satanan ws astraphn ek tou ouranou pesonta.
luk 10:19 idou dedwka umin thn ecousian tou patein epanw ofewn kai skorpiwn kai epi pasan thn dunamin tou exqrou kai ouden umas ou mh adikhsh.
luk 10:20 plhn en toutw mh xairete oti ta pneumata umin upotassetai xairete de oti ta onomata umwn eggegraptai en tois ouranois.
luk 10:21 en auth th wra hgalliasato en tw pneumati tw agiw kai eipen ecomologoumai soi pater kurie tou ouranou kai ths ghs oti apekruyas tauta apo sofwn kai sunetwn kai apekaluyas auta nhpiois nai o pathr oti outws eudokia egeneto emprosqen sou.
luk 10:22 panta moi paredoqh upo tou patros mou kai oudeis ginwskei tis estin o uios ei mh o pathr kai tis estin o pathr ei mh o uios kai w ean boulhtai o uios apokaluyai.
luk 10:23 kai strafeis pros tous maqhtas kat idian eipen makarioi oi ofqalmoi oi blepontes a blepete.
luk 10:24 legw gar umin oti polloi profhtai kai basileis hqelhsan idein a umeis blepete kai ouk eidan kai akousai a akouete kai ouk hkousan.
luk 10:25 kai idou nomikos tis anesth ekpeirazwn auton legwn didaskale ti poihsas zwhn aiwnion klhronomhsw;
luk 10:26 o de eipen pros auton en tw nomw ti gegraptai; pws anaginwskeis;
luk 10:27 o de apokriqeis eipen agaphseis kurion ton qeon sou ec olhs ths kardias sou kai en olh th yuxh sou kai en olh th isxui sou kai en olh th dianoia sou kai ton plhsion sou ws seauton.
luk 10:28 eipen de autw orqws apekriqhs touto poiei kai zhsh.
luk 10:29 o de qelwn dikaiwsai eauton eipen pros ton ihsoun kai tis estin mou plhsion;
luk 10:30 upolabwn o ihsous eipen anqrwpos tis katebainen apo ierousalhm eis ierixw kai lhstais periepesen oi kai ekdusantes auton kai plhgas epiqentes aphlqon afentes hmiqanh.
luk 10:31 kata sugkurian de iereus tis katebainen en th odw ekeinh kai idwn auton antiparhlqen
luk 10:32 omoiws de kai leuiths genomenos kata ton topon elqwn kai idwn antiparhlqen.
luk 10:33 samariths de tis odeuwn hlqen kat auton kai idwn esplagxnisqh
luk 10:34 kai proselqwn katedhsen ta traumata autou epixewn elaion kai oinon epibibasas de auton epi to idion kthnos hgagen auton eis pandoxeion kai epemelhqh autou.
luk 10:35 kai epi thn aurion ekbalwn edwken duo dhnaria tw pandoxei kai eipen epimelhqhti autou kai o ti an prosdapanhshs egw en tw epanerxesqai me apodwsw soi.
luk 10:36 tis toutwn twn triwn plhsion dokei soi gegonenai tou empesontos eis tous lhstas;
luk 10:37 o de eipen o poihsas to eleos met autou. eipen de autw o ihsous poreuou kai su poiei omoiws.
luk 10:38 en de tw poreuesqai autous autos eishlqen eis kwmhn tina gunh de tis onomati marqa upedecato auton.
luk 10:39 kai thde hn adelfh kaloumenh mariam h kai parakaqesqeisa pros tous podas tou kuriou hkouen ton logon autou.
luk 10:40 h de marqa periespato peri pollhn diakonian epistasa de eipen kurie ou melei soi oti h adelfh mou monhn me katelipen diakonein; eipe oun auth ina moi sunantilabhtai.
luk 10:41 apokriqeis de eipen auth o kurios marqa marqa merimnas kai [tupbazh] peri polla
luk 10:42 enos de estin xreia mariam gar thn agaqhn merida ecelecato htis ouk afaireqhsetai auths.
luk 11:1 kai egeneto en tw einai auton en topw tini proseuxomenon ws epausato eipen tis twn maqhtwn autou pros auton kurie didacon hmas proseuxesqai kaqws kai iwannhs edidacen tous maqhtas autou.
luk 11:2 eipen de autois otan proseuxhsqe legete pater [hmwn o en tois ouranois] agiasqhtw to onoma sou elqetw h basileia sou
luk 11:3 ton arton hmwn ton epiousion didou hmin to kaq hmeran
luk 11:4 kai afes hmin tas amartias hmwn kai gar autoi afiomen panti ofeilonti hmin kai mh eisenegkhs hmas eis peirasmon.
luk 11:5 kai eipen pros autous tis ec umwn ecei filon kai poreusetai pros auton mesonuktiou kai eiph autw file xrhson moi treis artous
luk 11:6 epeidh filos mou paregeneto ec odou pros me kai ouk exw o paraqhsw autw
luk 11:7 kakeinos eswqen apokriqeis eiph mh moi kopous parexe hdh h qura kekleistai kai ta paidia mou met emou eis thn koithn eisin ou dunamai anastas dounai soi.
luk 11:8 legw umin ei kai ou dwsei autw anastas dia to einai filon autou dia ge thn anaideian autou egerqeis dwsei autw oswn xrhzei.
luk 11:9 kagw umin legw aiteite kai doqhsetai umin zhteite kai eurhsete krouete kai anoighsetai umin.
luk 11:10 pas gar o aitwn lambanei kai o zhtwn euriskei kai tw krouonti anoighsetai.
luk 11:11 tina de ec umwn ton patera aithsei o uios ixqun kai anti ixquos ofin autw epidwsei;
luk 11:12 h kai aithsei won epidwsei autw skorpion;
luk 11:13 ei oun umeis ponhroi uparxontes oidate domata agaqa didonai tois teknois umwn posw mallon o pathr [umwn] o ec ouranou dwsei pneuma agion tois aitousin auton.
luk 11:14 kai hn ekballwn daimonion [--] kwfon egeneto de tou daimoniou ecelqontos elalhsen o kwfos. kai eqaumasan oi oxloi
luk 11:15 tines de ec autwn eipon en beelzeboul tw arxonti twn daimoniwn ekballei ta daimonia
luk 11:16 eteroi de peirazontes shmeion ec ouranou ezhtoun par autou.
luk 11:17 autos de eidws autwn ta dianohmata eipen autois pasa basileia ef eauthn diamerisqeisa erhmoutai kai oikos epi oikon piptei.
luk 11:18 ei de kai o satanas ef eauton diemerisqh pws staqhsetai h basileia autou; oti legete en beelzeboul ekballein me ta daimonia.
luk 11:19 ei de egw en beelzeboul ekballw ta daimonia oi uioi umwn en tini ekballousin; dia touto autoi umwn kritai esontai.
luk 11:20 ei de en daktulw qeou egw ekballw ta daimonia ara efqasen ef umas h basileia tou qeou.
luk 11:21 otan o isxuros kaqwplismenos fulassh thn eautou aulhn en eirhnh estin ta uparxonta autou
luk 11:22 epan de isxuroteros autou epelqwn nikhsh auton thn panoplian autou airei ef h epepoiqei kai ta skula autou diadidwsin.
luk 11:23 o mh wn met emou kat emou estin kai o mh sunagwn met emou skorpizei.
luk 11:24 otan to akaqarton pneuma ecelqh apo tou anqrwpou dierxetai di anudrwn topwn zhtoun anapausin kai mh euriskon tote legei upostreyw eis ton oikon mou oqen echlqon
luk 11:25 kai elqon euriskei sesarwmenon kai kekosmhmenon.
luk 11:26 tote poreuetai kai paralambanei etera pneumata ponhrotera eautou epta kai eiselqonta katoikei ekei kai ginetai ta esxata tou anqrwpou ekeinou xeirona twn prwtwn.
luk 11:27 egeneto de en tw legein auton tauta eparasa tis fwnhn gunh ek tou oxlou eipen autw makaria h koilia h bastasasa se kai mastoi ous eqhlasas.
luk 11:28 autos de eipen menoun makarioi oi akouontes ton logon tou qeou kai fulassontes.
luk 11:29 twn de oxlwn epaqroizomenwn hrcato legein h genea auth genea ponhra estin shmeion zhtei kai shmeion ou doqhsetai auth ei mh to shmeion iwna.
luk 11:30 kaqws gar egeneto iwnas tois nineuitais shmeion outws estai kai o uios tou anqrwpou th genea tauth.
luk 11:31 basilissa notou egerqhsetai en th krisei meta twn andrwn ths geneas tauths kai katakrinei autous oti hlqen ek twn peratwn ths ghs akousai thn sofian solomwnos kai idou pleion solomwnos wde.
luk 11:32 andres nineuitai anasthsontai en th krisei meta ths geneas tauths kai katakrinousin authn oti metenohsan eis to khrugma iwna kai idou pleion iwna wde.
luk 11:33 oudeis luxnon ayas eis krupthn tiqhsin [--] all epi thn luxnian ina oi eisporeuomenoi to fws blepwsin.
luk 11:34 o luxnos tou swmatos estin o ofqalmos sou. otan o ofqalmos sou aplous h kai olon to swma sou fwteinon estin epan de ponhros h kai to swma sou skoteinon.
luk 11:35 skopei oun mh to fws to en soi skotos estin.
luk 11:36 ei oun to swma sou olon fwteinon mh exon meros ti skoteinon estai fwteinon olon ws otan o luxnos th astraph fwtizh se.
luk 11:37 en de tw lalhsai erwta auton farisaios opws aristhsh par autw eiselqwn de anepesen.
luk 11:38 o de farisaios idwn eqaumasen oti ou prwton ebaptisqh pro tou aristou.
luk 11:39 eipen de o kurios pros auton nun umeis oi farisaioi to ecwqen tou pothriou kai tou pinakos kaqarizete to de eswqen umwn gemei arpaghs kai ponhrias.
luk 11:40 afrones oux o poihsas to ecwqen kai to eswqen epoihsen;
luk 11:41 plhn ta enonta dote elehmosunhn kai idou panta kaqara umin estin.
luk 11:42 alla ouai umin tois farisaiois oti apodekatoute to hduosmon kai to phganon kai pan laxanon kai parerxesqe thn krisin kai thn agaphn tou qeou tauta de edei poihsai kakeina mh pareinai.
luk 11:43 ouai umin tois farisaiois oti agapate thn prwtokaqedrian en tais sunagwgais kai tous aspasmous en tais agorais.
luk 11:44 ouai umin oti este ws ta mnhmeia ta adhla kai oi anqrwpoi oi peripatountes epanw ouk oidasin.
luk 11:45 apokriqeis de tis twn nomikwn legei autw didaskale tauta legwn kai hmas ubrizeis.
luk 11:46 o de eipen kai umin tois nomikois ouai oti fortizete tous anqrwpous fortia dusbastakta kai autoi eni twn daktulwn umwn ou prosyauete tois fortiois.
luk 11:47 ouai umin oti oikodomeite ta mnhmeia twn profhtwn oi de pateres umwn apekteinan autous.
luk 11:48 ara martures este kai suneudokeite tois ergois twn paterwn umwn oti autoi men apekteinan autous umeis de oikodomeite.
luk 11:49 dia touto kai h sofia tou qeou eipen apostelw eis autous profhtas kai apostolous kai ec autwn apoktenousin kai diwcousin
luk 11:50 ina ekzhthqh to aima pantwn twn profhtwn to ekkexumenon apo katabolhs kosmou apo ths geneas tauths
luk 11:51 apo aimatos abel ews aimatos zaxariou tou apolomenou metacu tou qusiasthriou kai tou oikou nai legw umin ekzhthqhsetai apo ths geneas tauths.
luk 11:52 ouai umin tois nomikois oti hrate thn kleida ths gnwsews autoi ouk eishlqate kai tous eiserxomenous ekwlusate.
luk 11:53 kakeiqen ecelqontos autou hrcanto oi grammateis kai oi farisaioi deinws enexein kai apostomatizein auton peri pleionwn
luk 11:54 enedreuontes auton qhreusai ti ek tou stomatos autou.
luk 12:1 en ois episunaxqeiswn twn muriadwn tou oxlou wste katapatein allhlous hrcato legein pros tous maqhtas autou prwton prosexete eautois apo ths zumhs htis estin upokrisis twn farisaiwn.
luk 12:2 ouden de sugkekalummenon estin o ouk apokalufqhsetai kai krupton o ou gnwsqhsetai.
luk 12:3 anq wn osa en th skotia eipate en tw fwti akousqhsetai kai o pros to ous elalhsate en tois tameiois khruxqhsetai epi twn dwmatwn.
luk 12:4 legw de umin tois filois mou mh fobhqhte apo twn apokteinontwn to swma kai meta tauta mh exontwn perissoteron ti poihsai.
luk 12:5 upodeicw de umin tina fobhqhte fobhqhte ton meta to apokteinai exonta ecousian embalein eis thn geennan nai legw umin touton fobhqhte.
luk 12:6 ouxi pente strouqia pwlountai assariwn duo; kai en ec autwn ouk estin epilelhsmenon enwpion tou qeou.
luk 12:7 alla kai ai trixes ths kefalhs umwn pasai hriqmhntai. mh fobeisqe pollwn strouqiwn diaferete.
luk 12:8 legw de umin pas os an omologhsh en emoi emprosqen twn anqrwpwn kai o uios tou anqrwpou omologhsei en autw emprosqen twn aggelwn tou qeou
luk 12:9 o de arnhsamenos me enwpion twn anqrwpwn aparnhqhsetai enwpion twn aggelwn tou qeou.
luk 12:10 kai pas os erei logon eis ton uion tou anqrwpou afeqhsetai autw tw de eis to agion pneuma blasfhmhsanti ouk afeqhsetai.
luk 12:11 otan de eisferwsin umas epi tas sunagwgas kai tas arxas kai tas ecousias mh merimnhshte pws h ti apologhshsqe h ti eiphte
luk 12:12 to gar agion pneuma didacei umas en auth th wra a dei eipein.
luk 12:13 eipen de tis ek tou oxlou autw didaskale eipe tw adelfw mou merisasqai met emou thn klhronomian.
luk 12:14 o de eipen autw anqrwpe tis me katesthsen krithn h meristhn ef umas;
luk 12:15 eipen de pros autous orate kai fulassesqe apo pashs pleonecias oti ouk en tw perisseuein tini h zwh autou estin ek twn uparxontwn autw.
luk 12:16 eipen de parabolhn pros autous legwn anqrwpou tinos plousiou euforhsen h xwra.
luk 12:17 kai dielogizeto en eautw legwn ti poihsw oti ouk exw pou sunacw tous karpous mou;
luk 12:18 kai eipen touto poihsw kaqelw mou tas apoqhkas kai meizonas oikodomhsw kai sunacw ekei panta ton siton kai ta agaqa mou
luk 12:19 kai erw th yuxh mou yuxh exeis polla agaqa keimena eis eth polla anapauou fage pie eufrainou.
luk 12:20 eipen de autw o qeos afrwn tauth th nukti thn yuxhn sou apaitousin apo sou a de htoimasas tini estai;
luk 12:21 outws o qhsaurizwn eautw kai mh eis qeon ploutwn.
luk 12:22 eipen de pros tous maqhtas autou dia touto legw umin mh merimnate th yuxh ti faghte mhde tw swmati ti endushsqe.
luk 12:23 h gar yuxh pleion estin ths trofhs kai to swma tou endumatos.
luk 12:24 katanohsate tous korakas oti ou speirousin oude qerizousin ois ouk estin tameion oude apoqhkh kai o qeos trefei autous posw mallon umeis diaferete twn peteinwn.
luk 12:25 tis de ec umwn merimnwn dunatai epi thn hlikian autou prosqeinai phxun;
luk 12:26 ei oun oude elaxiston dunasqe ti peri twn loipwn merimnate;
luk 12:27 katanohsate ta krina pws aucanei ou kopia oude nhqei legw de umin oude solomwn en pash th doch autou periebaleto ws en toutwn.
luk 12:28 ei de en agrw ton xorton onta shmeron kai aurion eis klibanon ballomenon o qeos outws amfiezei posw mallon umas oligopistoi.
luk 12:29 kai umeis mh zhteite ti faghte kai ti pihte kai mh metewrizesqe
luk 12:30 tauta gar panta ta eqnh tou kosmou epizhtousin umwn de o pathr oiden oti xrhzete toutwn.
luk 12:31 plhn zhteite thn basileian autou kai tauta prosteqhsetai umin.
luk 12:32 mh fobou to mikron poimnion oti eudokhsen o pathr umwn dounai umin thn basileian.
luk 12:33 pwlhsate ta uparxonta umwn kai dote elehmosunhn poihsate eautois ballantia mh palaioumena qhsauron anekleipton en tois ouranois opou klepths ouk eggizei oude shs diafqeirei
luk 12:34 opou gar estin o qhsauros umwn ekei kai h kardia umwn estai.
luk 12:35 estwsan umwn ai osfues periezwsmenai kai oi luxnoi kaiomenoi
luk 12:36 kai umeis omoioi anqrwpois prosdexomenois ton kurion eautwn pote analush ek twn gamwn ina elqontos kai krousantos euqews anoicwsin autw.
luk 12:37 makarioi oi douloi ekeinoi ous elqwn o kurios eurhsei grhgorountas amhn legw umin oti perizwsetai kai anaklinei autous kai parelqwn diakonhsei autois.
luk 12:38 kan en th deutera kan en th trith fulakh elqh kai eurh outws makarioi eisin ekeinoi.
luk 12:39 touto de ginwskete oti ei hdei o oikodespoths poia wra o klepths erxetai ouk an afhken dioruxqhnai ton oikon autou.
luk 12:40 kai umeis ginesqe etoimoi oti h wra ou dokeite o uios tou anqrwpou erxetai.
luk 12:41 eipen de o petros kurie pros hmas thn parabolhn tauthn legeis h kai pros pantas;
luk 12:42 kai eipen o kurios tis ara estin o pistos oikonomos o fronimos on katasthsei o kurios epi ths qerapeias autou tou didonai en kairw to sitometrion;
luk 12:43 makarios o doulos ekeinos on elqwn o kurios autou eurhsei poiounta outws
luk 12:44 alhqws legw umin oti epi pasin tois uparxousin autou katasthsei auton.
luk 12:45 ean de eiph o doulos ekeinos en th kardia autou xronizei o kurios mou erxesqai kai archtai tuptein tous paidas kai tas paidiskas esqiein te kai pinein kai mequskesqai
luk 12:46 hcei o kurios tou doulou ekeinou en hmera h ou prosdoka kai en wra h ou ginwskei kai dixotomhsei auton kai to meros autou meta twn apistwn qhsei.
luk 12:47 ekeinos de o doulos o gnous to qelhma tou kuriou autou kai mh etoimasas h poihsas pros to qelhma autou darhsetai pollas
luk 12:48 o de mh gnous poihsas de acia plhgwn darhsetai oligas. panti de w edoqh polu polu zhthqhsetai par autou kai w pareqento polu perissoteron aithsousin auton.
luk 12:49 pur hlqon balein epi thn ghn kai ti qelw ei hdh anhfqh.
luk 12:50 baptisma de exw baptisqhnai kai pws sunexomai ews otou telesqh.
luk 12:51 dokeite oti eirhnhn paregenomhn dounai en th gh; ouxi legw umin all h diamerismon.
luk 12:52 esontai gar apo tou nun pente en eni oikw diamemerismenoi treis epi dusin kai duo epi trisin
luk 12:53 diamerisqhsontai pathr epi uiw kai uios epi patri mhthr epi thn qugatera kai qugathr epi thn mhtera penqera epi thn numfhn auths kai numfh epi thn penqeran.
luk 12:54 elegen de kai tois oxlois otan idhte thn nefelhn anatellousan epi dusmwn euqews legete oti ombros erxetai kai ginetai outws
luk 12:55 kai otan noton pneonta legete oti kauswn estai kai ginetai.
luk 12:56 upokritai to proswpon ths ghs kai tou ouranou oidate dokimazein ton kairon de touton pws ouk oidate dokimazein;
luk 12:57 ti de kai af eautwn ou krinete to dikaion;

luk 13:1 parhsan de tines en autw tw kairw apaggellontes autw peri twn galilaiwn wn to aima pilatos emicen meta twn qusiwn autwn.
luk 13:2 kai apokriqeis eipen autois dokeite oti oi galilaioi outoi amartwloi para pantas tous galilaious egenonto oti tauta peponqasin;
luk 13:3 ouxi legw umin all ean mh metanohte pantes omoiws apoleisqe.
luk 13:4 h ekeinoi oi dekaoktw ef ous epesen o purgos en tw silwam kai apekteinen autous dokeite oti autoi ofeiletai egenonto para pantas tous anqrwpous tous katoikountas ierousalhm;
luk 13:5 ouxi legw umin all ean mh metanohte pantes wsautws apoleisqe.
luk 13:6 elegen de tauthn thn parabolhn sukhn eixen tis pefuteumenhn en tw ampelwni autou kai hlqen zhtwn karpon en auth kai oux euren.

luk 13:8 o de apokriqeis legei autw kurie afes authn kai touto to etos ews otou skayw peri authn kai balw kopria
luk 13:9 kan men poihsh karpon eis to mellon ei de mh ge ekkoyeis authn.
luk 13:10 hn de didaskwn en mia twn sunagwgwn en tois sabbasin.
luk 13:11 kai idou gunh pneuma exousa asqeneias eth dekaoktw kai hn sugkuptousa kai mh dunamenh anakuyai eis to panteles.
luk 13:12 idwn de authn o ihsous prosefwnhsen kai eipen auth gunai apolelusai ths asqeneias sou
luk 13:13 kai epeqhken auth tas xeiras kai paraxrhma anwrqwqh kai edocazen ton qeon.
luk 13:14 apokriqeis de o arxisunagwgos aganaktwn oti tw sabbatw eqerapeusen o ihsous elegen tw oxlw oti ec hmerai eisin en ais dei ergazesqai en autais oun erxomenoi qerapeuesqe kai mh th hmera tou sabbatou.
luk 13:15 apekriqh de autw o kurios kai eipen upokritai ekastos umwn tw sabbatw ou luei ton boun autou h ton onon apo ths fatnhs kai apagagwn potizei;
luk 13:16 tauthn de qugatera abraam ousan hn edhsen o satanas idou deka kai oktw eth ouk edei luqhnai apo tou desmou toutou th hmera tou sabbatou;
luk 13:17 kai tauta legontos autou kathsxunonto pantes oi antikeimenoi autw kai pas o oxlos exairen epi pasin tois endocois tois ginomenois up autou.
luk 13:18 elegen oun tini omoia estin h basileia tou qeou kai tini omoiwsw authn;
luk 13:19 omoia estin kokkw sinapews on labwn anqrwpos ebalen eis khpon eautou kai huchsen kai egeneto eis dendron kai ta peteina tou ouranou kateskhnwsen en tois kladois autou.
luk 13:20 kai palin eipen tini omoiwsw thn basileian tou qeou;
luk 13:21 omoia estin zumh hn labousa gunh enekruyen eis aleurou sata tria ews ou ezumwqh olon.
luk 13:22 kai dieporeueto kata poleis kai kwmas didaskwn kai poreian poioumenos eis ierosoluma.
luk 13:23 eipen de tis autw kurie ei oligoi oi swzomenoi; o de eipen pros autous
luk 13:24 agwnizesqe eiselqein dia ths stenhs quras oti polloi legw umin zhthsousin eiselqein kai ouk isxusousin.
luk 13:25 af ou an egerqh o oikodespoths kai apokleish thn quran kai archsqe ecw estanai kai krouein thn quran legontes kurie anoicon hmin kai apokriqeis erei umin ouk oida umas poqen este.
luk 13:26 tote arcesqe legein efagomen enwpion sou kai epiomen kai en tais plateiais hmwn edidacas
luk 13:27 kai erei [--] umin ouk oida umas poqen este aposthte ap emou pantes ergatai adikias.
luk 13:28 ekei estai o klauqmos kai o brugmos twn odontwn otan oyesqe abraam kai isaak kai iakwb kai pantas tous profhtas en th basileia tou qeou umas de ekballomenous ecw.
luk 13:29 kai hcousin apo anatolwn kai dusmwn kai apo borra kai notou kai anakliqhsontai en th basileia tou qeou.
luk 13:30 kai idou eisin esxatoi oi esontai prwtoi kai eisin prwtoi oi esontai esxatoi.
luk 13:31 en auth th wra proshlqan tines farisaioi legontes autw ecelqe kai poreuou enteuqen oti hrwdhs qelei se apokteinai.
luk 13:32 kai eipen autois poreuqentes eipate th alwpeki tauth idou ekballw daimonia kai iaseis apotelw shmeron kai aurion kai th trith teleioumai.
luk 13:33 plhn dei me shmeron kai aurion kai th exomenh poreuesqai oti ouk endexetai profhthn apolesqai ecw ierousalhm.
luk 13:34 ierousalhm ierousalhm h apokteinousa tous profhtas kai liqobolousa tous apestalmenous pros authn posakis hqelhsa episunacai ta tekna sou on tropon ornis thn eauths nossian upo tas pterugas kai ouk hqelhsate.

luk 14:6 kai ouk isxusan antapokriqhnai pros tauta.

luk 14:11 oti pas o uywn eauton tapeinwqhsetai kai o tapeinwn eauton uywqhsetai.
luk 14:12 elegen de kai tw keklhkoti auton otan poihs ariston h deipnon mh fwnei tous filous sou mhde tous adelfous sou mhde tous suggeneis sou mhde geitonas plousious mhpote kai autoi antikaleswsin se kai genhtai antapodoma soi.
luk 14:13 all otan doxhn poihs kalei ptwxous anapeirous xwlous tuflous
luk 14:14 kai makarios esh oti ouk exousin antapodounai soi antapodoqhsetai gar soi en th anastasei twn dikaiwn.
luk 14:15 akousas de tis twn sunanakeimenwn tauta eipen autw makarios ostis fagetai arton en th basileia tou qeou.
luk 14:16 o de eipen autw anqrwpos tis epoiei deipnon mega kai ekalesen pollous
luk 14:17 kai apesteilen ton doulon autou th wra tou deipnou eipein tois keklhmenois erxesqe oti hdh etoima estin.
luk 14:18 kai hrcanto apo mias pantes paraiteisqai. o prwtos eipen autw agron hgorasa kai exw anagkhn ecelqwn idein auton erwtw se exe me parhthmenon.
luk 14:19 kai eteros eipen zeugh bown hgorasa pente kai poreuomai dokimasai auta erwtw se exe me parhthmenon.
luk 14:20 kai eteros eipen gunaika eghma kai dia touto ou dunamai elqein.
luk 14:21 kai paragenomenos o doulos aphggeilen tw kuriw autou tauta. tote orgisqeis o oikodespoths eipen tw doulw autou ecelqe taxews eis tas plateias kai rumas ths polews kai tous ptwxous kai anapeirous kai tuflous kai xwlous eisagage wde.
luk 14:22 kai eipen o doulos kurie gegonen o epetacas kai eti topos estin.
luk 14:23 kai eipen o kurios pros ton doulon ecelqe eis tas odous kai fragmous kai anagkason eiselqein ina gemisqh mou o oikos
luk 14:24 legw gar umin oti oudeis twn andrwn ekeinwn twn keklhmenwn geusetai mou tou deipnou.
luk 14:25 suneporeuonto de autw oxloi polloi kai strafeis eipen pros autous
luk 14:26 ei tis erxetai pros me kai ou misei ton patera eautou kai thn mhtera kai thn gunaika kai ta tekna kai tous adelfous kai tas adelfas eti te kai thn yuxhn eautou ou dunatai einai mou maqhths.
luk 14:27 ostis ou bastazei ton stauron eautou kai erxetai opisw mou ou dunatai einai mou maqhths.
luk 14:28 tis gar ec umwn qelwn purgon oikodomhsai ouxi prwton kaqisas yhfizei thn dapanhn ei exei eis apartismon;
luk 14:29 ina mhpote qentos autou qemelion kai mh isxuontos ektelesai pantes oi qewrountes arcwntai autw empaizein
luk 14:30 legontes oti outos o anqrwpos hrcato oikodomein kai ouk isxusen ektelesai.
luk 14:31 h tis basileus poreuomenos eterw basilei sumbalein eis polemon ouxi kaqisas prwton bouleusetai ei dunatos estin en deka xiliasin upanthsai tw meta eikosi xiliadwn erxomenw ep auton;
luk 14:32 ei de mh ge eti autou porrw ontos presbeian aposteilas erwta ta pros eirhnhn.
luk 14:33 outws oun pas ec umwn os ouk apotassetai pasin tois eautou uparxousin ou dunatai einai mou maqhths.
luk 14:34 kalon oun to alas ean de kai to alas mwranqh en tini artuqhsetai;
luk 14:35 oute eis ghn oute eis koprian euqeton estin ecw ballousin auto. o exwn wta akouein akouetw.
