luk 15:2 kai diegogguzon oi te farisaioi kai oi grammateis legontes oti outos amartwlous prosdexetai kai sunesqiei autois.
luk 15:3 eipen de pros autous thn parabolhn tauthn legwn
luk 15:4 tis anqrwpos ec umwn exwn ekaton probata kai apolesas ec autwn en ou kataleipei ta enenhkonta ennea en th erhmw kai poreuetai epi to apolwlos ews eurh auto;
luk 15:5 kai eurwn epitiqhsin epi tous wmous autou xairwn
luk 15:6 kai elqwn eis ton oikon sugkalei tous filous kai tous geitonas legwn autois sugxarhte moi oti euron to probaton mou to apolwlos.
luk 15:7 legw umin oti outws xara en tw ouranw estai epi eni amartwlw metanoounti h epi enenhkonta ennea dikaiois oitines ou xreian exousin metanoias.
luk 15:8 h tis gunh draxmas exousa deka ean apolesh draxmhn mian ouxi aptei luxnon kai saroi thn oikian kai zhtei epimelws ews ou eurh;
luk 15:9 kai eurousa sugkalei tas filas kai geitonas legousa sugxarhte moi oti euron thn draxmhn hn apwlesa.
luk 15:10 outws legw umin ginetai xara enwpion twn aggelwn tou qeou epi eni amartwlw metanoounti.
luk 15:11 eipen de anqrwpos tis eixen duo uious.
luk 15:12 kai eipen o newteros autwn tw patri pater dos moi to epiballon meros ths ousias. o de dieilen autois ton bion.
luk 15:13 kai met ou pollas hmeras sunagagwn panta o newteros uios apedhmhsen eis xwran makran kai ekei dieskorpisen thn ousian autou zwn aswtws.
luk 15:14 dapanhsantos de autou panta egeneto limos isxura kata thn xwran ekeinhn kai autos hrcato ustereisqai.
luk 15:15 kai poreuqeis ekollhqh eni twn politwn ths xwras ekeinhs kai epemyen auton eis tous agrous autou boskein xoirous
luk 15:16 kai epequmei xortasqhnai ek twn keratiwn wn hsqion oi xoiroi kai oudeis edidou autw.
luk 15:17 eis eauton de elqwn efh posoi misqioi tou patros mou perisseuontai artwn egw de limw wde apollumai.
luk 15:18 anastas poreusomai pros ton patera mou kai erw autw pater hmarton eis ton ouranon kai enwpion sou
luk 15:19 ouketi eimi acios klhqhnai uios sou poihson me ws ena twn misqiwn sou.
luk 15:20 kai anastas hlqen pros ton patera eautou. eti de autou makran apexontos eiden auton o pathr autou kai esplagxnisqh kai dramwn epepesen epi ton traxhlon autou kai katefilhsen auton.
luk 15:21 eipen de o uios autw pater hmarton eis ton ouranon kai enwpion sou ouketi eimi acios klhqhnai uios sou.
luk 15:22 eipen de o pathr pros tous doulous autou taxu ecenegkate stolhn thn prwthn kai endusate auton kai dote daktulion eis thn xeira autou kai upodhmata eis tous podas
luk 15:23 kai ferete ton mosxon ton siteuton qusate kai fagontes eufranqwmen
luk 15:24 oti outos o uios mou nekros hn kai anezhsen hn apolwlws kai eureqh. kai hrcanto eufrainesqai.
luk 15:25 hn de o uios autou o presbuteros en agrw kai ws erxomenos hggisen th oikia hkousen sumfwnias kai xorwn
luk 15:26 kai proskalesamenos ena twn paidwn epunqaneto ti an eih tauta.
luk 15:27 o de eipen autw oti o adelfos sou hkei kai equsen o pathr sou ton mosxon ton siteuton oti ugiainonta auton apelaben.
luk 15:28 wrgisqh de kai ouk hqelen eiselqein. o de pathr autou ecelqwn parekalei auton.
luk 15:29 o de apokriqeis eipen tw patri autou idou tosauta eth douleuw soi kai oudepote entolhn sou parhlqon kai emoi oudepote edwkas erifon ina meta twn filwn mou eufranqw
luk 15:30 ote de o uios sou outos o katafagwn sou ton bion meta pornwn hlqen equsas autw ton siteuton mosxon.
luk 15:31 o de eipen autw teknon su pantote met emou ei kai panta ta ema sa estin
luk 15:32 eufranqhnai de kai xarhnai edei oti o adelfos sou outos nekros hn kai ezhsen kai apolwlws kai eureqh.
luk 16:1 elegen de kai pros tous maqhtas anqrwpos tis hn plousios os eixen oikonomon kai outos dieblhqh autw ws diaskorpizwn ta uparxonta autou.
luk 16:2 kai fwnhsas auton eipen autw ti touto akouw peri sou; apodos ton logon ths oikonomias sou ou gar dunh eti oikonomein.
luk 16:3 eipen de en eautw o oikonomos ti poihsw oti o kurios mou afaireitai thn oikonomian ap emou; skaptein ouk isxuw epaitein aisxunomai.
luk 16:4 egnwn ti poihsw ina otan metastaqw ek ths oikonomias decwntai me eis tous oikous autwn.
luk 16:5 kai proskalesamenos ena ekaston twn xreofeiletwn tou kuriou eautou elegen tw prwtw poson ofeileis tw kuriw mou;
luk 16:6 o de eipen ekaton batous elaiou. o de eipen autw decai sou ta grammata kai kaqisas taxews grayon penthkonta.
luk 16:7 epeita eterw eipen su de poson ofeileis; o de eipen ekaton korous sitou. legei autw decai sou ta grammata kai grayon ogdohkonta.
luk 16:8 kai ephnesen o kurios ton oikonomon ths adikias oti fronimws epoihsen oti oi uioi tou aiwnos toutou fronimwteroi uper tous uious tou fwtos eis thn genean thn eautwn eisin.
luk 16:9 kai egw umin legw eautois poihsate filous ek tou mamwna ths adikias ina otan ekliph decwntai umas eis tas aiwnious skhnas.
luk 16:10 o pistos en elaxistw kai en pollw pistos estin kai o en elaxistw adikos kai en pollw adikos estin.
luk 16:11 ei oun en tw adikw mamwna pistoi ouk egenesqe to alhqinon tis umin pisteusei;
luk 16:12 kai ei en tw allotriw pistoi ouk egenesqe to umeteron tis umin dwsei;
luk 16:13 oudeis oikeths dunatai dusi kuriois douleuein h gar ton ena mishsei kai ton eteron agaphsei h enos anqecetai kai tou eterou katafronhsei. ou dunasqe qew douleuein kai mamwna.
luk 16:14 hkouon de tauta panta oi farisaioi filarguroi uparxontes kai ecemukthrizon auton.
luk 16:15 kai eipen autois umeis este oi dikaiountes eautous enwpion twn anqrwpwn o de qeos ginwskei tas kardias umwn oti to en anqrwpois uyhlon bdelugma enwpion tou qeou.
luk 16:16 o nomos kai oi profhtai mexri iwannou apo tote h basileia tou qeou euaggelizetai kai pas eis authn biazetai.
luk 16:17 eukopwteron de estin ton ouranon kai thn ghn parelqein h tou nomou mian keraian pesein.
luk 16:18 pas o apoluwn thn gunaika autou kai gamwn eteran moixeuei kai o apolelumenhn apo andros gamwn moixeuei.
luk 16:19 anqrwpos de tis hn plousios kai enedidusketo porfuran kai busson eufrainomenos kaq hmeran lamprws.
luk 16:20 ptwxos de tis onomati lazaros ebeblhto pros ton pulwna autou eilkwmenos
luk 16:21 kai epiqumwn xortasqhnai apo twn piptontwn apo ths trapezhs tou plousiou alla kai oi kunes erxomenoi epeleixon ta elkh autou.
luk 16:22 egeneto de apoqanein ton ptwxon kai apenexqhnai auton upo twn aggelwn eis ton kolpon abraam apeqanen de kai o plousios kai etafh.
luk 16:23 kai en tw adh eparas tous ofqalmous autou uparxwn en basanois ora abraam apo makroqen kai lazaron en tois kolpois autou.
luk 16:24 kai autos fwnhsas eipen pater abraam elehson me kai pemyon lazaron ina bayh to akron tou daktulou autou udatos kai katayuch thn glwssan mou oti odunwmai en th flogi tauth.
luk 16:25 eipen de abraam teknon mnhsqhti oti apelabes ta agaqa sou en th zwh sou kai lazaros omoiws ta kaka nun de wde parakaleitai su de odunasai.
luk 16:26 kai en pasi toutois metacu hmwn kai umwn xasma mega esthriktai opws oi qelontes diabhnai enqen pros umas mh dunwntai mhde ekeiqen pros hmas diaperwsin.
luk 16:27 eipen de erwtw se oun pater ina pemyhs auton eis ton oikon tou patros mou
luk 16:28 exw gar pente adelfous opws diamarturhtai autois ina mh kai autoi elqwsin eis ton topon touton ths basanou.
luk 16:29 legei de abraam exousi mwusea kai tous profhtas akousatwsan autwn.
luk 16:30 o de eipen ouxi pater abraam all ean tis apo nekrwn poreuqh pros autous metanohsousin.
luk 16:31 eipen de autw ei mwusews kai twn profhtwn ouk akouousin oud ean tis ek nekrwn anasth peisqhsontai.
luk 17:1 eipen de pros tous maqhtas autou anendekton estin tou ta skandala mh elqein plhn ouai di ou erxetai
luk 17:2 lusitelei autw ei liqos mulikos perikeitai peri ton traxhlon autou kai erriptai eis thn qalassan h ina skandalish twn mikrwn toutwn ena.
luk 17:3 prosexete eautois. ean amarth o adelfos sou epitimhson autw kai ean metanohsh afes autw
luk 17:4 kai ean eptakis ths hmeras amarthsh eis se kai eptakis epistreyh pros se legwn metanow afhseis autw.
luk 17:5 kai eipan oi apostoloi tw kuriw prosqes hmin pistin.
luk 17:6 eipen de o kurios ei exete pistin ws kokkon sinapews elegete an th sukaminw tauth ekrizwqhti kai futeuqhti en th qalassh kai uphkousen an umin.
luk 17:7 tis de ec umwn doulon exwn arotriwnta h poimainonta os eiselqonti ek tou agrou erei autw euqews parelqwn anapese
luk 17:8 all ouxi erei autw etoimason ti deipnhsw kai perizwsamenos diakonei moi ews fagw kai piw kai meta tauta fagesai kai piesai su;
luk 17:9 mh exei xarin tw doulw oti epoihsen ta diataxqenta;
luk 17:10 outws kai umeis otan poihshte panta ta diataxqenta umin legete oti douloi axreioi esmen o wfeilomen poihsai pepoihkamen.
luk 17:11 kai egeneto en tw poreuesqai eis ierousalhm kai autos dihrxeto dia meson samareias kai galilaias.
luk 17:12 kai eiserxomenou autou eis tina kwmhn aphnthsan autw deka leproi andres oi esthsan porrwqen
luk 17:13 kai autoi hran fwnhn legontes ihsou epistata elehson hmas.
luk 17:14 kai idwn eipen autois poreuqentes epideicate eautous tois iereusin. kai egeneto en tw upagein autous ekaqarisqhsan.
luk 17:15 eis de ec autwn idwn oti iaqh upestreyen meta fwnhs megalhs docazwn ton qeon
luk 17:16 kai epesen epi proswpon para tous podas autou euxaristwn autw kai autos hn samariths.
luk 17:17 apokriqeis de o ihsous eipen ouxi oi deka ekaqarisqhsan; oi de ennea pou;
luk 17:18 oux eureqhsan upostreyantes dounai docan tw qew ei mh o allogenhs outos;
luk 17:19 kai eipen autw anastas poreuou h pistis sou seswken se.
luk 17:20 eperwthqeis de upo twn farisaiwn pote erxetai h basileia tou qeou apekriqh autois kai eipen ouk erxetai h basileia tou qeou meta parathrhsews
luk 17:21 oude erousin idou wde h ekei idou gar h basileia tou qeou entos umwn estin.
luk 17:22 eipen de pros tous maqhtas eleusontai hmerai ote epiqumhsete mian twn hmerwn tou uiou tou anqrwpou idein kai ouk oyesqe.
luk 17:23 kai erousin umin idou ekei h idou wde mh apelqhte mhde diwchte.
luk 17:24 wsper gar h astraph astraptousa ek ths upo ton ouranon eis thn up ouranon lampei outws estai o uios tou anqrwpou [--].
luk 17:25 prwton de dei auton polla paqein kai apodokimasqhnai apo ths geneas tauths.
luk 17:26 kai kaqws egeneto en tais hmerais nwe outws estai kai en tais hmerais tou uiou tou anqrwpou
luk 17:27 hsqion epinon egamoun egamizonto axri hs hmeras eishlqen nwe eis thn kibwton kai hlqen o kataklusmos kai apwlesen pantas.
luk 17:28 omoiws kaqws egeneto en tais hmerais lwt hsqion epinon hgorazon epwloun efuteuon wkodomoun
luk 17:29 h de hmera echlqen lwt apo sodomwn ebrecen pur kai qeion ap ouranou kai apwlesen pantas.
luk 17:30 kata ta auta estai h hmera o uios tou anqrwpou apokaluptetai.
luk 17:31 en ekeinh th hmera os estai epi tou dwmatos kai ta skeuh autou en th oikia mh katabatw arai auta kai o en agrw omoiws mh epistreyatw eis ta opisw.
luk 17:32 mnhmoneuete ths gunaikos lwt.
luk 17:33 os [an qelhsh zwougonhsai thn yuxhn autou] apolesei authn os d an apolesh zwogonhsei authn.
luk 17:34 legw umin tauth th nukti esontai duo epi klinhs mias o eis paralhmfqhsetai kai o eteros afeqhsetai
luk 17:35 esontai duo alhqousai epi to auto h mia paralhmfqhsetai h de etera afeqhsetai.

luk 18:1 elegen de parabolhn autois pros to dein pantote proseuxesqai autous kai mh egkakein
luk 18:2 legwn kriths tis hn en tini polei ton qeon mh foboumenos kai anqrwpon mh entrepomenos.
luk 18:3 xhra de hn en th polei ekeinh kai hrxeto pros auton legousa ekdikhson me apo tou antidikou mou.
luk 18:4 kai ouk hqelen epi xronon meta de tauta eipen en eautw ei kai ton qeon ou foboumai oude anqrwpon entrepomai
luk 18:5 dia ge to parexein moi kopon thn xhran tauthn ekdikhsw authn ina mh eis telos erxomenh upwpiazh me.
luk 18:6 eipen de o kurios akousate ti o kriths ths adikias legei
luk 18:7 o de qeos ou mh poihsh thn ekdikhsin twn eklektwn autou twn bowntwn autw hmeras kai nuktos kai makroqumei ep autois;
luk 18:8 legw umin oti poihsei thn ekdikhsin autwn en taxei. plhn o uios tou anqrwpou elqwn ara eurhsei thn pistin epi ths ghs;
luk 18:9 eipen de kai pros tinas tous pepoiqotas ef eautois oti eisin dikaioi kai ecouqenountas tous loipous thn parabolhn tauthn
luk 18:10 anqrwpoi duo anebhsan eis to ieron proseucasqai o eis farisaios kai o eteros telwnhs.
luk 18:11 o farisaios staqeis [--] tauta proshuxeto o qeos euxaristw soi oti ouk eimi wsper oi loipoi twn anqrwpwn arpages adikoi moixoi h kai ws outos o telwnhs
luk 18:12 nhsteuw dis tou sabbatou apodekatw panta osa ktwmai.
luk 18:13 o de telwnhs makroqen estws ouk hqelen oude tous ofqalmous eparai eis ton ouranon all etupten to sthqos autou legwn o qeos ilasqhti moi tw amartwlw.
luk 18:14 legw umin katebh outos dedikaiwmenos eis ton oikon autou par ekeinon oti pas o uywn eauton tapeinwqhsetai o de tapeinwn eauton uywqhsetai.
luk 18:15 proseferon de autw kai ta brefh ina autwn apthtai idontes de oi maqhtai epetimwn autois.
luk 18:16 o de ihsous prosekalesato auta legwn afete ta paidia erxesqai pros me kai mh kwluete auta twn gar toioutwn estin h basileia tou qeou.
luk 18:17 amhn legw umin os an mh dechtai thn basileian tou qeou ws paidion ou mh eiselqh eis authn.
luk 18:18 kai ephrwthsen tis auton arxwn legwn didaskale agaqe ti poihsas zwhn aiwnion klhronomhsw;
luk 18:19 eipen de autw o ihsous ti me legeis agaqon; oudeis agaqos ei mh eis o qeos.
luk 18:20 tas entolas oidas mh moixeushs mh foneushs mh kleyhs mh yeudomarturhshs tima ton patera sou kai thn mhtera.
luk 18:21 o de eipen tauta panta efulaca ek neothtos.
luk 18:22 akousas de o ihsous eipen autw eti en soi leipei panta osa exeis pwlhson kai diados ptwxois kai eceis qhsauron en tois ouranois kai deuro akolouqei moi.
luk 18:23 o de akousas tauta perilupos egenhqh hn gar plousios sfodra.
luk 18:24 idwn de auton o ihsous [--] eipen pws duskolws oi ta xrhmata exontes eis thn basileian tou qeou eisporeuontai
luk 18:25 eukopwteron gar estin kamhlon dia trhmatos belonhs eiselqein h plousion eis thn basileian tou qeou eiselqein.
luk 18:26 eipan de oi akousantes kai tis dunatai swqhnai;
luk 18:27 o de eipen ta adunata para anqrwpois dunata para tw qew estin.
luk 18:28 eipen de o petros idou hmeis afentes ta idia hkolouqhsamen soi.
luk 18:29 o de eipen autois amhn legw umin oti oudeis estin os afhken oikian h gunaika h adelfous h goneis h tekna eneken ths basileias tou qeou
luk 18:30 os ouxi mh apolabh pollaplasiona en tw kairw toutw kai en tw aiwni tw erxomenw zwhn aiwnion.
luk 18:31 paralabwn de tous dwdeka eipen pros autous idou anabainomen eis ierousalhm kai telesqhsetai panta ta gegrammena dia twn profhtwn tw uiw tou anqrwpou
luk 18:32 paradoqhsetai gar tois eqnesin kai empaixqhsetai kai ubrisqhsetai kai emptusqhsetai
luk 18:33 kai mastigwsantes apoktenousin auton kai th hmera th trith anasthsetai.
luk 18:34 kai autoi ouden toutwn sunhkan kai hn to rhma touto kekrummenon ap autwn kai ouk eginwskon ta legomena.
luk 18:35 egeneto de en tw eggizein auton eis ierixw tuflos tis ekaqhto para thn odon epaitwn.
luk 18:36 akousas de oxlou diaporeuomenou epunqaneto ti eih touto
luk 18:37 aphggeilan de autw oti ihsous o nazwraios parerxetai.
luk 18:38 kai ebohsen legwn ihsou uie dauid elehson me.
luk 18:39 kai oi proagontes epetimwn autw ina sighsh autos de pollw mallon ekrazen uie dauid elehson me.
luk 18:40 staqeis de o ihsous ekeleusen auton axqhnai pros auton. eggisantos de autou ephrwthsen auton
luk 18:41 ti soi qeleis poihsw; o de eipen kurie ina anableyw.
luk 18:42 kai o ihsous eipen autw anableyon h pistis sou seswken se.
luk 18:43 kai paraxrhma anebleyen kai hkolouqei autw docazwn ton qeon. kai pas o laos idwn edwken ainon tw qew.
luk 19:1 kai eiselqwn dihrxeto thn ierixw.
luk 19:2 kai idou anhr onomati kaloumenos zakxaios kai autos hn arxitelwnhs kai autos plousios.
luk 19:3 kai ezhtei idein ton ihsoun tis estin kai ouk hdunato apo tou oxlou oti th hlikia mikros hn.
luk 19:4 kai prodramwn eis to emprosqen anebh epi sukomorean ina idh auton oti ekeinhs hmellen dierxesqai.
luk 19:5 kai ws hlqen epi ton topon anableyas o ihsous eipen pros auton zakxaie speusas katabhqi shmeron gar en tw oikw sou dei me meinai.
luk 19:6 kai speusas katebh kai upedecato auton xairwn.
luk 19:7 kai idontes pantes diegogguzon legontes oti para amartwlw andri eishlqen katalusai.
luk 19:8 staqeis de zakxaios eipen pros ton kurion idou ta hmisia mou twn uparxontwn kurie tois ptwxois didwmi kai ei tinos ti esukofanthsa apodidwmi tetraploun.
luk 19:9 eipen de pros auton o ihsous oti shmeron swthria tw oikw toutw egeneto kaqoti kai autos uios abraam estin
luk 19:10 hlqen gar o uios tou anqrwpou zhthsai kai swsai to apolwlos.
luk 19:11 akouontwn de autwn tauta prosqeis eipen parabolhn dia to eggus einai ierousalhm auton kai dokein autous oti paraxrhma mellei h basileia tou qeou anafainesqai.
luk 19:12 eipen oun anqrwpos tis eugenhs eporeuqh eis xwran makran labein eautw basileian kai upostreyai.
luk 19:13 kalesas de deka doulous eautou edwken autois deka mnas kai eipen pros autous pragmateusasqe en w erxomai.
luk 19:14 oi de politai autou emisoun auton kai apesteilan presbeian opisw autou legontes ou qelomen touton basileusai ef hmas.
luk 19:15 kai egeneto en tw epanelqein auton labonta thn basileian kai eipen fwnhqhnai autw tous doulous toutous ois dedwkei to argurion ina gnoi ti diepragmateusanto.
luk 19:16 paregeneto de o prwtos legwn kurie h mna sou deka proshrgasato mnas.
luk 19:17 kai eipen autw euge agaqe doule oti en elaxistw pistos egenou isqi ecousian exwn epanw deka polewn.
luk 19:18 kai hlqen o deuteros legwn h mna sou kurie epoihsen pente mnas.
luk 19:19 eipen de kai toutw kai su epanw ginou pente polewn.
luk 19:20 kai o eteros hlqen legwn kurie idou h mna sou hn eixon apokeimenhn en soudariw
luk 19:21 efoboumhn gar se oti anqrwpos austhros ei aireis o ouk eqhkas kai qerizeis o ouk espeiras.
luk 19:22 legei autw ek tou stomatos sou krinw se ponhre doule. hdeis oti egw anqrwpos austhros eimi airwn o ouk eqhka kai qerizwn o ouk espeira;
luk 19:23 kai dia ti ouk edwkas mou to argurion epi trapezan; kagw elqwn sun tokw an auto epraca.
luk 19:24 kai tois parestwsin eipen arate ap autou thn mnan kai dote tw tas deka mnas exonti
luk 19:25 kai eipan autw kurie exei deka mnas 
luk 19:26 legw umin oti panti tw exonti doqhsetai apo de tou mh exontos kai o exei arqhsetai.
luk 19:27 plhn tous exqrous mou toutous tous mh qelhsantas me basileusai ep autous agagete wde kai katasfacate autous emprosqen mou.
luk 19:28 kai eipwn tauta eporeueto emprosqen anabainwn eis ierosoluma.
luk 19:29 kai egeneto ws hggisen eis bhqfagh kai bhqanian pros to oros to kaloumenon elaiwn apesteilen duo twn maqhtwn
luk 19:30 legwn upagete eis thn katenanti kwmhn en h eisporeuomenoi eurhsete pwlon dedemenon ef on oudeis pwpote anqrwpwn ekaqisen kai lusantes auton agagete.
luk 19:31 kai ean tis umas erwta dia ti luete; outws ereite oti o kurios autou xreian exei.
luk 19:32 apelqontes de oi apestalmenoi euron kaqws eipen autois.
luk 19:33 luontwn de autwn ton pwlon eipan oi kurioi autou pros autous ti luete ton pwlon;
luk 19:34 oi de eipan oti o kurios autou xreian exei.
luk 19:35 kai hgagon auton pros ton ihsoun kai epiriyantes autwn ta imatia epi ton pwlon epebibasan ton ihsoun.
luk 19:36 poreuomenou de autou upestrwnnuon ta imatia autwn en th odw.
luk 19:37 eggizontos de autou hdh pros th katabasei tou orous twn elaiwn hrcanto apan to plhqos twn maqhtwn xairontes ainein ton qeon fwnh megalh peri paswn wn eidon dunamewn
luk 19:38 legontes euloghmenos o erxomenos o basileus en onomati kuriou en ouranw eirhnh kai doca en uyistois.
luk 19:39 kai tines twn farisaiwn apo tou oxlou eipan pros auton didaskale epitimhson tois maqhtais sou.
luk 19:40 kai apokriqeis eipen legw umin ean outoi siwphsousin oi liqoi kracousin.
luk 19:41 kai ws hggisen idwn thn polin eklausen ep authn
luk 19:42 legwn oti ei egnws [kai su] en th hmera tauth ta pros eirhnhn nun de ekrubh apo ofqalmwn sou.
luk 19:43 oti hcousin hmerai epi se kai parembalousin oi exqroi sou xaraka soi kai perikuklwsousin se kai sunecousin se pantoqen
luk 19:44 kai edafiousin se kai ta tekna sou en soi kai ouk afhsousin liqon epi liqon en soi anq wn ouk egnws ton kairon ths episkophs sou.
luk 19:45 kai eiselqwn eis to ieron hrcato ekballein tous pwlountas
luk 19:46 legwn autois gegraptai kai estai o oikos mou oikos proseuxhs umeis de auton epoihsate sphlaion lhstwn.
luk 19:47 kai hn didaskwn to kaq hmeran en tw ierw. oi de arxiereis kai oi grammateis ezhtoun auton apolesai kai oi prwtoi tou laou
luk 19:48 kai oux euriskon to ti poihswsin o laos gar apas ecekremato autou akouwn.
luk 20:1 kai egeneto en mia twn hmerwn didaskontos autou ton laon en tw ierw kai euaggelizomenou epesthsan oi arxiereis kai oi grammateis sun tois presbuterois
luk 20:2 kai eipan legontes pros auton eipon hmin en poia ecousia tauta poieis h tis estin o dous soi thn ecousian tauthn.
luk 20:3 apokriqeis de eipen pros autous erwthsw umas kagw logon kai eipate moi
luk 20:4 to baptisma iwannou ec ouranou hn h ec anqrwpwn;
luk 20:5 oi de sunelogisanto pros eautous legontes oti ean eipwmen ec ouranou erei dia ti ouk episteusate autw;
luk 20:6 ean de eipwmen ec anqrwpwn o laos apas kataliqasei hmas pepeismenos gar estin iwannhn profhthn einai.

luk 23:37 kai legontes ei su ei o basileus twn ioudaiwn swson seauton.
luk 23:38 hn de kai epigrafh ep autw o basileus twn ioudaiwn outos.
luk 23:39 eis de twn kremasqentwn kakourgwn eblasfhmei auton legwn ouxi su ei o xristos; swson seauton kai hmas.
luk 23:40 apokriqeis de o eteros epitimwn autw efh oude fobh su ton qeon oti en tw autw krimati ei;
luk 23:41 kai hmeis men dikaiws acia gar wn epracamen apolambanomen outos de ouden atopon epracen.
luk 23:42 kai elegen ihsou mnhsqhti mou otan elqhs eis thn basileian sou.
luk 23:43 kai eipen autw amhn soi legw shmeron met emou esh en tw paradeisw.
luk 23:44 kai hn hdh wsei wra ekth kai skotos egeneto ef olhn thn ghn ews wras enaths
luk 23:45 tou hliou eklipontos esxisqh de to katapetasma tou naou meson.
luk 23:46 kai fwnhsas fwnh megalh o ihsous eipen pater eis xeiras sou paratiqemai to pneuma mou touto de eipwn ecepneusen.
luk 23:47 idwn de o ekatontarxhs to genomenon edocazen ton qeon legwn ontws o anqrwpos outos dikaios hn.
luk 23:48 kai pantes oi sumparagenomenoi oxloi epi thn qewrian tauthn qewrhsantes ta genomena tuptontes ta sthqh upestrefon.
luk 23:49 eisthkeisan de pantes oi gnwstoi autw apo makroqen kai gunaikes ai sunakolouqousai autw apo ths galilaias orwsai tauta.
luk 23:50 kai idou anhr onomati iwshf bouleuths uparxwn kai anhr agaqos kai dikaios
luk 23:51 outos ouk hn sugkatateqeimenos th boulh kai th pracei autwn apo arimaqaias polews twn ioudaiwn os prosedexeto thn basileian tou qeou
luk 23:52 outos proselqwn tw pilatw hthsato to swma tou ihsou
luk 23:53 kai kaqelwn enetulicen auto sindoni kai eqhken auton en mnhmati laceutw ou ouk hn oudeis oupw keimenos.
luk 23:54 kai hmera hn paraskeuhs kai sabbaton epefwsken.
luk 23:55 katakolouqhsasai de ai gunaikes aitines hsan sunelhluquiai ek ths galilaias autw eqeasanto to mnhmeion kai ws eteqh to swma autou
luk 23:56 upostreyasai de htoimasan arwmata kai mura. kai to men sabbaton hsuxasan kata thn entolhn
luk 24:1 th de mia twn sabbatwn orqrou baqews epi to mnhma hlqon ferousai a htoimasan arwmata.
luk 24:2 euron de ton liqon apokekulismenon apo tou mnhmeiou
luk 24:3 eiselqousai de oux euron to swma tou kuriou ihsou.
luk 24:4 kai egeneto en tw aporeisqai autas peri toutou kai idou andres duo epesthsan autais en esqhti astraptoush.
luk 24:5 emfobwn de genomenwn autwn kai klinouswn ta proswpa eis thn ghn eipan pros autas ti zhteite ton zwnta meta twn nekrwn;
luk 24:6 ouk estin wde alla hgerqh. mnhsqhte ws elalhsen umin eti wn en th galilaia
luk 24:7 legwn ton uion tou anqrwpou oti dei paradoqhnai eis xeiras anqrwpwn amartwlwn kai staurwqhnai kai th trith hmera anasthnai.
luk 24:8 kai emnhsqhsan twn rhmatwn autou
luk 24:9 kai upostreyasai apo tou mnhmeiou aphggeilan tauta panta tois endeka kai pasin tois loipois.
luk 24:10 hsan de h magdalhnh maria kai iwanna kai maria h iakwbou kai ai loipai sun autais elegon pros tous apostolous tauta.
luk 24:11 kai efanhsan enwpion autwn wsei lhros ta rhmata tauta kai hpistoun autais.
luk 24:12 o de petros anastas edramen epi to mnhmeion kai parakuyas blepei ta oqonia mona kai aphlqen pros eauton qaumazwn to gegonos.
luk 24:13 kai idou duo ec autwn en auth th hmera hsan poreuomenoi eis kwmhn apexousan stadious echkonta apo ierousalhm h onoma emmaous
luk 24:14 kai autoi wmiloun pros allhlous peri pantwn twn sumbebhkotwn toutwn.
luk 24:15 kai egeneto en tw omilein autous kai suzhtein kai autos ihsous eggisas suneporeueto autois
luk 24:16 oi de ofqalmoi autwn ekratounto tou mh epignwnai auton.
luk 24:17 eipen de pros autous tines oi logoi outoi ous antiballete pros allhlous peripatountes; kai estaqhsan skuqrwpoi.
luk 24:18 apokriqeis de eis onomati kleopas eipen pros auton su monos paroikeis ierousalhm kai ouk egnws ta genomena en auth en tais hmerais tautais;
luk 24:19 kai eipen autois poia; oi de eipan autw ta peri ihsou tou [nazwraiou] os egeneto anhr profhths dunatos en ergw kai logw enantion tou qeou kai pantos tou laou
luk 24:20 opws te paredwkan auton oi arxiereis kai oi arxontes hmwn eis krima qanatou kai estaurwsan auton.
luk 24:21 hmeis de hlpizomen oti autos estin o mellwn lutrousqai ton israhl alla ge kai sun pasin toutois trithn tauthn hmeran agei af ou tauta egeneto.
luk 24:22 alla kai gunaikes tines ec hmwn ecesthsan hmas genomenai orqrinai epi to mnhmeion
luk 24:23 kai mh eurousai to swma autou hlqon legousai kai optasian aggelwn ewrakenai oi legousin auton zhn.
luk 24:24 kai aphlqon tines twn sun hmin epi to mnhmeion kai euron outws kaqws kai ai gunaikes eipon auton de ouk eidon.
luk 24:25 kai autos eipen pros autous w anohtoi kai bradeis th kardia tou pisteuein epi pasin ois elalhsan oi profhtai
luk 24:26 ouxi tauta edei paqein ton xriston kai eiselqein eis thn docan autou;
luk 24:27 kai arcamenos apo mwusews kai apo pantwn twn profhtwn diermhneusen autois en pasais tais grafais ta peri eautou.
luk 24:28 kai hggisan eis thn kwmhn ou eporeuonto kai autos prosepoihsato porrwteron poreuesqai.
luk 24:29 kai parebiasanto auton legontes meinon meq hmwn oti pros esperan estin kai kekliken hdh h hmera. kai eishlqen tou meinai sun autois.
luk 24:30 kai egeneto en tw katakliqhnai auton met autwn labwn ton arton euloghsen kai klasas epedidou autois
luk 24:31 autwn de dihnoixqhsan oi ofqalmoi kai epegnwsan auton kai autos afantos egeneto ap autwn.
luk 24:32 kai eipan pros allhlous ouxi h kardia hmwn kaiomenh hn en hmin ws elalei hmin en th odw ws dihnoigen hmin tas grafas;
luk 24:33 kai anastantes auth th wra upestreyan eis ierousalhm kai euron hqroismenous tous endeka kai tous sun autois
luk 24:34 legontas oti ontws hgerqh o kurios kai wfqh simwni.
luk 24:35 kai autoi echgounto ta en th odw kai ws egnwsqh autois en th klasei tou artou.
luk 24:36 tauta de autwn lalountwn autos esth en mesw autwn kai legei autois eirhnh umin.
luk 24:37 ptohqentes de kai emfoboi genomenoi edokoun pneuma qewrein.
luk 24:38 kai eipen autois ti tetaragmenoi este kai dia ti dialogismoi anabainousin en th kardia umwn;
luk 24:39 idete tas xeiras mou kai tous podas mou oti egw eimi autos yhlafhsate me kai idete oti pneuma sarka kai ostea ouk exei kaqws eme qewreite exonta.
luk 24:40 kai touto eipwn edeicen autois tas xeiras kai tous podas.
luk 24:41 eti de apistountwn autwn apo ths xaras kai qaumazontwn eipen autois exete ti brwsimon enqade;
luk 24:42 oi de epedwkan autw ixquos optou meros
luk 24:43 kai labwn enwpion autwn efagen.
luk 24:44 eipen de pros autous outoi oi logoi mou ous elalhsa pros umas eti wn sun umin oti dei plhrwqhnai panta ta gegrammena en tw nomw mwusews kai tois profhtais kai yalmois peri emou.
luk 24:45 tote dihnoicen autwn ton noun tou sunienai tas grafas.
luk 24:46 kai eipen autois oti outws gegraptai paqein ton xriston kai anasthnai ek nekrwn th trith hmera
luk 24:47 kai khruxqhnai epi tw onomati autou metanoian eis afesin amartiwn eis panta ta eqnh arcamenoi apo ierousalhm
luk 24:48 umeis martures toutwn.
luk 24:49 kai [--] egw apostellw thn epaggelian tou patros mou ef umas umeis de kaqisate en th polei ews ou endushsqe ec uyous dunamin.
luk 24:50 echgagen de autous ecw ews pros bhqanian kai eparas tas xeiras autou euloghsen autous.
luk 24:51 kai egeneto en tw eulogein auton autous diesth ap autwn kai anefereto eis ton ouranon.
luk 24:52 kai autoi proskunhsantes auton upestreyan eis ierousalhm meta xaras megalhs
luk 24:53 kai hsan dia pantos en tw ierw eulogountes ton qeon.
joh 1:1 en arxh hn o logos kai o logos hn pros ton qeon kai qeos hn o logos.
joh 1:2 outos hn en arxh pros ton qeon.
joh 1:3 panta di autou egeneto kai xwris autou egeneto oude en. o gegonen
joh 1:4 en autw zwh [estin] kai h zwh hn to fws twn anqrwpwn
joh 1:5 kai to fws en th skotia fainei kai h skotia auto ou katelaben.
joh 1:6 egeneto anqrwpos apestalmenos para qeou onoma autw iwannhs
joh 1:7 outos hlqen eis marturian ina marturhsh peri tou fwtos ina pantes pisteuswsin di autou.
joh 1:8 ouk hn ekeinos to fws all ina marturhsh peri tou fwtos.
joh 1:9 hn to fws to alhqinon o fwtizei panta anqrwpon erxomenon eis ton kosmon.
joh 1:10 en tw kosmw hn kai o kosmos di autou egeneto kai o kosmos auton ouk egnw.
joh 1:11 eis ta idia hlqen kai oi idioi auton ou parelabon.
joh 1:12 osoi de elabon auton edwken autois ecousian tekna qeou genesqai tois pisteuousin eis to onoma autou
joh 1:13 oi ouk ec aimatwn oude ek qelhmatos sarkos oude ek qelhmatos andros all ek qeou egennhqhsan.
joh 1:14 kai o logos sarc egeneto kai eskhnwsen en hmin kai eqeasameqa thn docan autou docan ws monogenous para patros plhrhs xaritos kai alhqeias.
joh 1:15 iwannhs marturei peri autou kai kekragen legwn outos hn on eipon o opisw mou erxomenos emprosqen mou gegonen oti prwtos mou hn.
joh 1:16 oti ek tou plhrwmatos autou hmeis pantes elabomen kai xarin anti xaritos
joh 1:17 oti o nomos dia mwusews edoqh h xaris kai h alhqeia dia ihsou xristou egeneto.
joh 1:18 qeon oudeis ewraken pwpote monogenhs qeos o wn eis ton kolpon tou patros ekeinos echghsato.
joh 1:19 kai auth estin h marturia tou iwannou ote apesteilan pros auton oi ioudaioi ec ierosolumwn iereis kai leuitas ina erwthswsin auton su tis ei;
joh 1:20 kai wmologhsen kai ouk hrnhsato kai wmologhsen oti egw ouk eimi o xristos.
joh 1:21 kai hrwthsan auton ti oun; su hlias ei; kai legei ouk eimi. o profhths ei su; kai apekriqh ou.
joh 1:22 eipan oun autw tis ei; ina apokrisin dwmen tois pemyasin hmas ti legeis peri seautou;
joh 1:23 efh egw fwnh bowntos en th erhmw euqunate thn odon kuriou kaqws eipen hsaias o profhths.
joh 1:24 kai apestalmenoi hsan ek twn farisaiwn.
joh 1:25 kai hrwthsan auton kai eipan autw ti oun baptizeis ei su ouk ei o xristos oude hlias oude o profhths;
joh 1:26 apekriqh autois o iwannhs legwn egw baptizw en udati mesos umwn [eisthkei] on umeis ouk oidate
joh 1:27 o opisw mou erxomenos ou ouk eimi egw acios ina lusw autou ton imanta tou upodhmatos.
joh 1:28 tauta en [bhqabara] egeneto peran tou iordanou opou hn o iwannhs baptizwn.
joh 1:29 th epaurion blepei ton ihsoun erxomenon pros auton kai legei ide o amnos tou qeou o airwn thn amartian tou kosmou.
joh 1:30 outos estin uper ou egw eipon opisw mou erxetai anhr os emprosqen mou gegonen oti prwtos mou hn.
joh 1:31 kagw ouk hdein auton all ina fanerwqh tw israhl dia touto hlqon egw en udati baptizwn.
joh 1:32 kai emarturhsen iwannhs legwn oti teqeamai to pneuma katabainon ws peristeran ec ouranou kai emeinen ep auton
joh 1:33 kagw ouk hdein auton all o pemyas me baptizein en udati ekeinos moi eipen ef on an idhs to pneuma katabainon kai menon ep auton outos estin o baptizwn en pneumati agiw.
joh 1:34 kagw ewraka kai memarturhka oti outos estin o [eklektos] uios tou qeou.
joh 1:35 th epaurion palin eisthkei o iwannhs kai ek twn maqhtwn autou duo
joh 1:36 kai embleyas tw ihsou peripatounti legei ide o amnos tou qeou.
joh 1:37 kai hkousan oi duo maqhtai autou lalountos kai hkolouqhsan tw ihsou.
joh 1:38 strafeis de o ihsous kai qeasamenos autous akolouqountas legei autois ti zhteite; oi de eipan autw rabbi o legetai meqermhneuomenon didaskale pou meneis;
joh 1:39 legei autois erxesqe kai oyesqe. hlqan oun kai eidan pou menei kai par autw emeinan thn hmeran ekeinhn wra hn ws dekath.
joh 1:40 hn andreas o adelfos simwnos petrou eis ek twn duo twn akousantwn para iwannou kai akolouqhsantwn autw
joh 1:41 euriskei outos prwton ton adelfon ton idion simwna kai legei autw eurhkamen ton messian o estin meqermhneuomenon xristos
joh 1:42 hgagen auton pros ton ihsoun. embleyas autw o ihsous eipen su ei simwn o uios iwannou su klhqhsh khfas o ermhneuetai petros.
joh 1:43 th epaurion hqelhsen ecelqein eis thn galilaian kai euriskei filippon. kai legei autw o ihsous akolouqei moi.
joh 1:44 hn de o filippos apo bhqsaida ek ths polews andreou kai petrou.
joh 1:45 euriskei filippos ton naqanahl kai legei autw on egrayen mwushs en tw nomw kai oi profhtai eurhkamen ihsoun uion tou iwshf ton apo nazaret.
joh 1:46 kai eipen autw naqanahl ek nazaret dunatai ti agaqon einai; legei autw o filippos erxou kai ide.
joh 1:47 eiden o ihsous ton naqanahl erxomenon pros auton kai legei peri autou ide alhqws israhliths en w dolos ouk estin.
joh 1:48 legei autw naqanahl poqen me ginwskeis; apekriqh ihsous kai eipen autw pro tou se filippon fwnhsai onta upo thn sukhn eidon se.
joh 1:49 apekriqh autw naqanahl rabbi su ei o uios tou qeou su basileus ei tou israhl.
joh 1:50 apekriqh ihsous kai eipen autw oti eipon soi oti eidon se upokatw ths sukhs pisteueis; meizw toutwn oyh.
joh 1:51 kai legei autw amhn amhn legw umin oyesqe ton ouranon anewgota kai tous aggelous tou qeou anabainontas kai katabainontas epi ton uion tou anqrwpou.
joh 2:1 kai th hmera th trith gamos egeneto en kana ths galilaias kai hn h mhthr tou ihsou ekei
joh 2:2 eklhqh de kai o ihsous kai oi maqhtai autou eis ton gamon.
joh 2:3 kai usterhsantos oinou legei h mhthr tou ihsou pros auton oinon ouk exousin.
joh 2:4 kai legei auth o ihsous ti emoi kai soi gunai; oupw hkei h wra mou.
joh 2:5 legei h mhthr autou tois diakonois o ti an legh umin poihsate.
joh 2:6 hsan de ekei liqinai udriai ec kata ton kaqarismon twn ioudaiwn keimenai xwrousai ana metrhtas duo h treis.
joh 2:7 legei autois o ihsous gemisate tas udrias udatos. kai egemisan autas ews anw.
joh 2:8 kai legei autois antlhsate nun kai ferete tw arxitriklinw oi de hnegkan.
joh 2:9 ws de egeusato o arxitriklinos to udwr oinon gegenhmenon kai ouk hdei poqen estin oi de diakonoi hdeisan oi hntlhkotes to udwr fwnei ton numfion o arxitriklinos
joh 2:10 kai legei autw pas anqrwpos prwton ton kalon oinon tiqhsin kai otan mequsqwsin ton elassw su tethrhkas ton kalon oinon ews arti.
joh 2:11 tauthn epoihsen arxhn twn shmeiwn o ihsous en kana ths galilaias kai efanerwsen thn docan autou kai episteusan eis auton oi maqhtai autou.
joh 2:12 meta touto katebh eis kafarnaoum autos kai h mhthr autou kai oi adelfoi autou kai oi maqhtai autou kai ekei emeinan ou pollas hmeras.
joh 2:13 kai eggus hn to pasxa twn ioudaiwn kai anebh eis ierosoluma o ihsous.
joh 2:14 kai euren en tw ierw tous pwlountas boas kai probata kai peristeras kai tous kermatistas kaqhmenous
joh 2:15 kai poihsas fragellion ek sxoiniwn pantas ecebalen ek tou ierou ta te probata kai tous boas kai twn kollubistwn ecexeen to kerma kai tas trapezas anetreyen
joh 2:16 kai tois tas peristeras pwlousin eipen arate tauta enteuqen mh poieite ton oikon tou patros mou oikon emporiou.
joh 2:17 emnhsqhsan oi maqhtai autou oti gegrammenon estin o zhlos tou oikou sou katafagetai me.
joh 2:18 apekriqhsan oun oi ioudaioi kai eipan autw ti shmeion deiknueis hmin oti tauta poieis;
joh 2:19 apekriqh ihsous kai eipen autois lusate ton naon touton kai en trisin hmerais egerw auton.
joh 2:20 eipan oun oi ioudaioi tesserakonta kai ec etesin oikodomhqh o naos outos kai su en trisin hmerais egereis auton;
joh 2:21 ekeinos de elegen peri tou naou tou swmatos autou.
joh 2:22 ote oun hgerqh ek nekrwn emnhsqhsan oi maqhtai autou oti touto elegen kai episteusan th grafh kai tw logw on eipen o ihsous.
joh 2:23 ws de hn en tois ierosolumois en tw pasxa en th eorth polloi episteusan eis to onoma autou qewrountes autou ta shmeia a epoiei
joh 2:24 autos de ihsous ouk episteuen auton autois dia to auton ginwskein pantas
joh 2:25 kai oti ou xreian eixen ina tis marturhsh peri tou anqrwpou autos gar eginwsken ti hn en tw anqrwpw.
joh 3:1 hn de anqrwpos ek twn farisaiwn nikodhmos onoma autw arxwn twn ioudaiwn
joh 3:2 outos hlqen pros auton nuktos kai eipen autw rabbi oidamen oti apo qeou elhluqas didaskalos oudeis gar dunatai tauta ta shmeia poiein a su poieis ean mh h o qeos met autou.
joh 3:3 apekriqh ihsous kai eipen autw amhn amhn legw soi ean mh tis gennhqh anwqen ou dunatai idein thn basileian tou qeou.
joh 3:4 legei pros auton o nikodhmos pws dunatai anqrwpos gennhqhnai gerwn wn; mh dunatai eis thn koilian ths mhtros autou deuteron eiselqein kai gennhqhnai;
joh 3:5 apekriqh ihsous amhn amhn legw soi ean mh tis gennhqh ec udatos kai pneumatos ou dunatai eiselqein eis thn basileian tou qeou.
joh 3:6 to gegennhmenon ek ths sarkos sarc estin kai to gegennhmenon ek tou pneumatos pneuma estin.
joh 3:7 mh qaumashs oti eipon soi dei umas gennhqhnai anwqen.
joh 3:8 to pneuma opou qelei pnei kai thn fwnhn autou akoueis all ouk oidas poqen erxetai kai pou upagei outws estin pas o gegennhmenos ek tou pneumatos.
joh 3:9 apekriqh nikodhmos kai eipen autw pws dunatai tauta genesqai;
joh 3:10 apekriqh ihsous kai eipen autw su ei o didaskalos tou israhl kai tauta ou ginwskeis;
joh 3:11 amhn amhn legw soi oti o oidamen laloumen kai o ewrakamen marturoumen kai thn marturian hmwn ou lambanete.
joh 3:12 ei ta epigeia eipon umin kai ou pisteuete pws ean eipw umin ta epourania pisteusete;
joh 3:13 kai oudeis anabebhken eis ton ouranon ei mh o ek tou ouranou katabas o uios tou anqrwpou.
joh 3:14 kai kaqws mwushs uywsen ton ofin en th erhmw outws uywqhnai dei ton uion tou anqrwpou
joh 3:15 ina pas o pisteuwn en autw exh zwhn aiwnion.
joh 3:16 outws gar hgaphsen o qeos ton kosmon wste ton uion ton monogenh edwken ina pas o pisteuwn eis auton mh apolhtai all exh zwhn aiwnion.
joh 3:17 ou gar apesteilen o qeos ton uion eis ton kosmon ina krinh ton kosmon all ina swqh o kosmos di autou.
joh 3:18 o pisteuwn eis auton ou krinetai o de mh pisteuwn hdh kekritai oti mh pepisteuken eis to onoma tou monogenous uiou tou qeou.
joh 3:19 auth de estin h krisis oti to fws elhluqen eis ton kosmon kai hgaphsan oi anqrwpoi mallon to skotos h to fws hn gar autwn ponhra ta erga.
joh 3:20 pas gar o faula prasswn misei to fws kai ouk erxetai pros to fws ina mh elegxqh ta erga autou
joh 3:21 o de poiwn thn alhqeian erxetai pros to fws ina fanerwqh autou ta erga oti en qew estin eirgasmena.
joh 3:22 meta tauta hlqen o ihsous kai oi maqhtai autou eis thn ioudaian ghn kai ekei dietriben met autwn kai ebaptizen.
joh 3:23 hn de kai o iwannhs baptizwn en ainwn eggus tou saleim oti udata polla hn ekei kai pareginonto kai ebaptizonto
joh 3:24 oupw gar hn beblhmenos eis thn fulakhn o iwannhs.
joh 3:25 egeneto oun zhthsis ek twn maqhtwn iwannou meta ioudaiou peri kaqarismou.
joh 3:26 kai hlqon pros ton iwannhn kai eipan autw rabbi os hn meta sou peran tou iordanou w su memarturhkas ide outos baptizei kai pantes erxontai pros auton.

joh 6:58 outos estin o artos o ec ouranou katabas ou kaqws efagon oi pateres kai apeqanon o trwgwn touton ton arton zhsei eis ton aiwna.

joh 6:60 polloi oun akousantes ek twn maqhtwn autou eipan sklhros estin o logos outos tis dunatai autou akouein;
joh 6:61 eidws de o ihsous en eautw oti gogguzousin peri toutou oi maqhtai autou eipen autois touto umas skandalizei;
joh 6:62 ean oun qewrhte ton uion tou anqrwpou anabainonta opou hn to proteron;
joh 6:63 to pneuma estin to zwopoioun h sarc ouk wfelei ouden ta rhmata a egw lelalhka umin pneuma estin kai zwh estin.
joh 6:64 all eisin ec umwn tines oi ou pisteuousin. hdei gar ec arxhs o ihsous tines eisin oi mh pisteuontes kai tis estin o paradwswn auton.
joh 6:65 kai elegen dia touto eirhka umin oti oudeis dunatai elqein pros me ean mh h dedomenon autw ek tou patros.
joh 6:66 ek toutou polloi ek twn maqhtwn autou aphlqon eis ta opisw kai ouketi met autou periepatoun.
joh 6:67 eipen oun o ihsous tois dwdeka mh kai umeis qelete upagein;

joh 6:71 elegen de ton ioudan simwnos iskariwtou outos gar emellen paradidonai auton eis ek twn dwdeka.
joh 7:1 kai meta tauta periepatei o ihsous en th galilaia ou gar hqelen en th ioudaia peripatein oti ezhtoun auton oi ioudaioi apokteinai.
joh 7:2 hn de eggus h eorth twn ioudaiwn h skhnophgia.
joh 7:3 eipon oun pros auton oi adelfoi autou metabhqi enteuqen kai upage eis thn ioudaian ina kai oi maqhtai sou qewrhsousin sou ta erga a poieis
joh 7:4 oudeis gar ti en kruptw poiei kai zhtei autos en parrhsia einai. ei tauta poieis fanerwson seauton tw kosmw.
joh 7:5 oude gar oi adelfoi autou episteuon eis auton.
joh 7:6 legei oun autois o ihsous o kairos o emos oupw parestin o de kairos o umeteros pantote estin etoimos.
joh 7:7 ou dunatai o kosmos misein umas eme de misei oti egw marturw peri autou oti ta erga autou ponhra estin.

joh 7:9 tauta de eipwn autos emeinen en th galilaia.
joh 7:10 ws de anebhsan oi adelfoi autou eis thn eorthn tote kai autos anebh ou fanerws alla [--] en kruptw.

joh 7:13 oudeis mentoi parrhsia elalei peri autou dia ton fobon twn ioudaiwn.
joh 7:14 hdh de ths eorths mesoushs anebh ihsous eis to ieron kai edidasken.
joh 7:15 eqaumazon oun oi ioudaioi legontes pws outos grammata oiden mh memaqhkws;

joh 7:17 ean tis qelh to qelhma autou poiein gnwsetai peri ths didaxhs poteron ek tou qeou estin h egw ap emautou lalw.
joh 7:18 o af eautou lalwn thn docan thn idian zhtei o de zhtwn thn docan tou pemyantos auton outos alhqhs estin kai adikia en autw ouk estin.
joh 7:19 ou mwushs dedwken umin ton nomon; kai oudeis ec umwn poiei ton nomon. ti me zhteite apokteinai;
joh 7:20 apekriqh o oxlos daimonion exeis tis se zhtei apokteinai;
joh 7:21 apekriqh ihsous kai eipen autois en ergon epoihsa kai pantes qaumazete.

joh 7:23 ei peritomhn lambanei anqrwpos en sabbatw ina mh luqh o nomos mwusews emoi xolate oti olon anqrwpon ugih epoihsa en sabbatw;
joh 7:24 mh krinete kat oyin alla thn dikaian krisin krinete.
joh 7:25 elegon oun tines ek twn ierosolumitwn oux outos estin on zhtousin apokteinai;
joh 7:26 kai ide parrhsia lalei kai ouden autw legousin. mhpote alhqws egnwsan oi arxontes oti outos estin o xristos;
joh 7:27 alla touton oidamen poqen estin o de xristos otan erxhtai oudeis ginwskei poqen estin.
joh 7:28 ekracen oun en tw ierw didaskwn o ihsous kai legwn kame oidate kai oidate poqen eimi kai ap emautou ouk elhluqa all estin alhqinos o pemyas me on umeis ouk oidate
joh 7:29 egw oida auton oti par autou eimi kakeinos me apesteilen.
joh 7:30 ezhtoun oun auton piasai kai oudeis epebalen ep auton thn xeira oti oupw elhluqei h wra autou.
joh 7:31 ek tou oxlou de polloi episteusan eis auton kai elegon o xristos otan elqh mh pleiona shmeia poihsei wn outos epoihsen;
joh 7:32 hkousan oi farisaioi tou oxlou gogguzontos peri autou tauta kai apesteilan oi arxiereis kai oi farisaioi uphretas ina piaswsin auton.
joh 7:33 eipen oun o ihsous eti xronon mikron meq umwn eimi kai upagw pros ton pemyanta me.
joh 7:34 zhthsete me kai oux eurhsete me kai opou eimi egw umeis ou dunasqe elqein.
joh 7:35 eipon oun oi ioudaioi pros eautous pou outos mellei poreuesqai oti hmeis oux eurhsomen auton; mh eis thn diasporan twn ellhnwn mellei poreuesqai kai didaskein tous ellhnas;
joh 7:36 tis estin o logos outos on eipen zhthsete me kai oux eurhsete me kai opou eimi egw umeis ou dunasqe elqein;
joh 7:37 en de th esxath hmera th megalh ths eorths eisthkei o ihsous kai ekracen legwn ean tis diya erxesqw pros me kai pinetw.

joh 7:39 touto de eipen peri tou pneumatos o emellon lambanein oi pisteusantes eis auton oupw gar hn pneuma oti ihsous oudepw edocasqh.
joh 7:40 ek tou oxlou oun akousantes twn logwn toutwn elegon outos estin alhqws o profhths
joh 7:41 alloi elegon outos estin o xristos oi de elegon mh gar ek ths galilaias o xristos erxetai;
joh 7:42 oux h grafh eipen oti ek tou spermatos dauid kai apo bhqleem ths kwmhs opou hn dauid erxetai o xristos;

joh 7:46 apekriqhsan oi uphretai oudepote outws elalhsen anqrwpos [ws outos o anqrwpos].
joh 7:47 apekriqhsan oun autois oi farisaioi mh kai umeis peplanhsqe;
joh 7:48 mh tis ek twn arxontwn episteusen eis auton h ek twn farisaiwn;
joh 7:49 alla o oxlos outos o mh ginwskwn ton nomon eparatoi eisin.

joh 8:12 palin oun autois elalhsen o ihsous legwn egw eimi to fws tou kosmou o akolouqwn emoi ou mh peripathsh en th skotia all ecei to fws ths zwhs.
joh 8:13 eipon oun autw oi farisaioi su peri seautou martureis h marturia sou ouk estin alhqhs.
joh 8:14 apekriqh ihsous kai eipen autois kan egw marturw peri emautou alhqhs estin h marturia mou oti oida poqen hlqon kai pou upagw umeis de ouk oidate poqen erxomai h pou upagw.
joh 8:15 umeis kata thn sarka krinete egw ou krinw oudena.
joh 8:16 kai ean krinw de egw h krisis h emh alhqinh estin oti monos ouk eimi all egw kai o pemyas me pathr.
joh 8:17 kai en tw nomw de tw umeterw gegraptai oti duo anqrwpwn h marturia alhqhs estin.
joh 8:18 egw eimi o marturwn peri emautou kai marturei peri emou o pemyas me pathr.
joh 8:19 elegon oun autw pou estin o pathr sou; apekriqh ihsous oute eme oidate oute ton patera mou ei eme hdeite kai ton patera mou an hdeite.
joh 8:20 tauta ta rhmata elalhsen en tw gazofulakiw didaskwn en tw ierw kai oudeis epiasen auton oti oupw elhluqei h wra autou.

joh 8:22 elegon oun oi ioudaioi mhti apoktenei eauton oti legei opou egw upagw umeis ou dunasqe elqein;
joh 8:23 kai elegen autois umeis ek twn katw este egw ek twn anw eimi umeis ek toutou tou kosmou este egw ouk eimi ek tou kosmou toutou.
joh 8:24 eipon oun umin oti apoqaneisqe en tais amartiais umwn ean gar mh pisteushte oti egw eimi apoqaneisqe en tais amartiais umwn.
joh 8:25 elegon oun autw su tis ei; eipen autois o ihsous thn arxhn o ti kai lalw umin;
joh 8:26 polla exw peri umwn lalein kai krinein all o pemyas me alhqhs estin kagw a hkousa par autou tauta lalw eis ton kosmon.
joh 8:27 ouk egnwsan oti ton patera autois elegen.
joh 8:28 eipen oun autois o ihsous otan uywshte ton uion tou anqrwpou tote gnwsesqe oti egw eimi kai ap emautou poiw ouden alla kaqws edidacen me o pathr tauta lalw.
joh 8:29 kai o pemyas me met emou estin ouk afhken me monon oti egw ta aresta autw poiw pantote.
joh 8:30 tauta autou lalountos polloi episteusan eis auton.
joh 8:31 elegen oun o ihsous pros tous pepisteukotas autw ioudaious ean umeis meinhte en tw logw tw emw alhqws maqhtai mou este
joh 8:32 kai gnwsesqe thn alhqeian kai h alhqeia eleuqerwsei umas.
joh 8:33 apekriqhsan pros auton sperma abraam esmen kai oudeni dedouleukamen pwpote pws su legeis oti eleuqeroi genhsesqe;
joh 8:34 apekriqh autois o ihsous amhn amhn legw umin oti pas o poiwn thn amartian doulos estin ths amartias.
joh 8:35 o de doulos ou menei en th oikia eis ton aiwna o uios menei eis ton aiwna.
joh 8:36 ean oun o uios umas eleuqerwsh ontws eleuqeroi esesqe.
joh 8:37 oida oti sperma abraam este alla zhteite me apokteinai oti o logos o emos ou xwrei en umin.
joh 8:38 a egw ewraka para tw patri lalw kai umeis oun a [ewrakate] para tou patros poieite.
joh 8:39 apekriqhsan kai eipan autw o pathr hmwn abraam estin. legei autois o ihsous ei tekna tou abraam este ta erga tou abraam epoieite
joh 8:40 nun de zhteite me apokteinai anqrwpon os thn alhqeian umin lelalhka hn hkousa para tou qeou touto abraam ouk epoihsen.
joh 8:41 umeis poieite ta erga tou patros umwn. eipan oun autw hmeis ek porneias ou gegennhmeqa ena patera exomen ton qeon.
joh 8:42 eipen autois o ihsous ei o qeos pathr umwn hn hgapate an eme egw gar ek tou qeou echlqon kai hkw oude gar ap emautou elhluqa all ekeinos me apesteilen.
joh 8:43 dia ti thn lalian thn emhn ou ginwskete; oti ou dunasqe akouein ton logon ton emon.
joh 8:44 umeis ek tou patros tou diabolou este kai tas epiqumias tou patros umwn qelete poiein. ekeinos anqrwpoktonos hn ap arxhs kai en th alhqeia ouk esthken oti ouk estin alhqeia en autw. otan lalh to yeudos ek twn idiwn lalei oti yeusths estin kai o pathr autou.
joh 8:45 egw de oti thn alhqeian legw ou pisteuete moi.
joh 8:46 tis ec umwn elegxei me peri amartias; ei alhqeian legw dia ti umeis ou pisteuete moi;
joh 8:47 o wn ek tou qeou ta rhmata tou qeou akouei dia touto umeis ouk akouete oti ek tou qeou ouk este.
joh 8:48 apekriqhsan oi ioudaioi kai eipan autw ou kalws legomen hmeis oti samariths ei su kai daimonion exeis;
joh 8:49 apekriqh ihsous egw daimonion ouk exw alla timw ton patera mou kai umeis atimazete me.
joh 8:50 egw de ou zhtw thn docan mou estin o zhtwn kai krinwn.
joh 8:51 amhn amhn legw umin ean tis ton emon logon thrhsh qanaton ou mh qewrhsh eis ton aiwna.
joh 8:52 eipon oun autw oi ioudaioi nun egnwkamen oti daimonion exeis. abraam apeqanen kai oi profhtai kai su legeis ean tis ton logon mou thrhsh ou mh geushtai qanatou eis ton aiwna.
joh 8:53 mh su meizwn ei tou patros hmwn abraam ostis apeqanen; kai oi profhtai apeqanon tina seauton poieis;
joh 8:54 apekriqh ihsous ean egw docasw emauton h doca mou ouden estin estin o pathr mou o docazwn me on umeis legete oti qeos hmwn estin
joh 8:55 kai ouk egnwkate auton egw de oida auton. kan eipw oti ouk oida auton esomai omoios umin yeusths alla oida auton kai ton logon autou thrw.
joh 8:56 abraam o pathr umwn hgalliasato ina idh thn hmeran thn emhn kai eiden kai exarh.
joh 8:57 eipon oun oi ioudaioi pros auton penthkonta eth oupw exeis kai abraam ewrakas [se];
joh 8:58 eipen autois ihsous amhn amhn legw umin prin abraam genesqai egw eimi.
joh 8:59 hran oun liqous ina balwsin ep auton ihsous de ekrubh kai echlqen ek tou ierou.
joh 9:1 kai paragwn eiden anqrwpon tuflon ek geneths.

joh 9:22 tauta eipan oi goneis autou oti efobounto tous ioudaious hdh gar suneteqeinto oi ioudaioi ina ean tis auton omologhsh xriston aposunagwgos genhtai.

joh 9:28 kai eloidorhsan auton kai eipon su maqhths ei ekeinou hmeis de tou mwusews esmen maqhtai
joh 9:29 hmeis oidamen oti mwusei lelalhken o qeos touton de ouk oidamen poqen estin.

joh 10:1 amhn amhn legw umin o mh eiserxomenos dia ths quras eis thn aulhn twn probatwn alla anabainwn allaxoqen ekeinos klepths estin kai lhsths
joh 10:2 o de eiserxomenos dia ths quras poimhn estin twn probatwn.
joh 10:3 toutw o qurwros anoigei kai ta probata ths fwnhs autou akouei kai ta idia probata fwnei kat onoma kai ecagei auta.
joh 10:4 otan ta idia panta ekbalh emprosqen autwn poreuetai kai ta probata autw akolouqei oti oidasin thn fwnhn autou
joh 10:5 allotriw de ou mh akolouqhsousin alla feucontai ap autou oti ouk oidasin twn allotriwn thn fwnhn.
joh 10:6 tauthn thn paroimian eipen autois o ihsous ekeinoi de ouk egnwsan tina hn a elalei autois.
joh 10:7 eipen oun palin o ihsous amhn amhn legw umin oti egw eimi h qura twn probatwn.
joh 10:8 pantes osoi hlqon [--] kleptai eisin kai lhstai all ouk hkousan autwn ta probata.
joh 10:9 egw eimi h qura di emou ean tis eiselqh swqhsetai kai eiseleusetai kai eceleusetai kai nomhn eurhsei.
joh 10:10 o klepths ouk erxetai ei mh ina kleyh kai qush kai apolesh egw hlqon ina zwhn exwsin kai perisson exwsin.
joh 10:11 egw eimi o poimhn o kalos o poimhn o kalos thn yuxhn autou tiqhsin uper twn probatwn
joh 10:12 o misqwtos kai ouk wn poimhn ou ouk estin ta probata idia qewrei ton lukon erxomenon kai afihsin ta probata kai feugei kai o lukos arpazei auta kai skorpizei 
joh 10:13 oti misqwtos estin kai ou melei autw peri twn probatwn.
joh 10:14 egw eimi o poimhn o kalos kai ginwskw ta ema kai ginwskousi me ta ema
joh 10:15 kaqws ginwskei me o pathr kagw ginwskw ton patera kai thn yuxhn mou tiqhmi uper twn probatwn.
joh 10:16 kai alla probata exw a ouk estin ek ths aulhs tauths kakeina dei me agagein kai ths fwnhs mou akousousin kai genhsontai mia poimnh eis poimhn.
joh 10:17 dia touto me o pathr agapa oti egw tiqhmi thn yuxhn mou ina palin labw authn.
joh 10:18 oudeis airei authn ap emou all egw tiqhmi authn ap emautou. ecousian exw qeinai authn kai ecousian exw palin labein authn tauthn thn entolhn elabon para tou patros mou.
joh 10:19 sxisma palin egeneto en tois ioudaiois dia tous logous toutous.
joh 10:20 elegon de polloi ec autwn daimonion exei kai mainetai ti autou akouete;
joh 10:21 alloi elegon tauta ta rhmata ouk estin daimonizomenou mh daimonion dunatai tuflwn ofqalmous anoicai;
joh 10:22 egeneto tote ta egkainia en tois ierosolumois xeimwn hn
joh 10:23 kai periepatei o ihsous en tw ierw en th stoa tou solomwnos.
joh 10:24 ekuklwsan oun auton oi ioudaioi kai elegon autw ews pote thn yuxhn hmwn aireis; ei su ei o xristos eipe hmin parrhsia.
joh 10:25 apekriqh autois o ihsous eipon umin kai ou pisteuete ta erga a egw poiw en tw onomati tou patros mou tauta marturei peri emou
joh 10:26 alla umeis ou pisteuete oti ouk este ek twn probatwn twn emwn.
joh 10:27 ta probata ta ema ths fwnhs mou akouousin kagw ginwskw auta kai akolouqousin moi
joh 10:28 kagw didwmi autois zwhn aiwnion kai ou mh apolwntai eis ton aiwna kai oux arpasei tis auta ek ths xeiros mou.
joh 10:29 o pathr mou o dedwken moi pantwn meizon estin kai oudeis dunatai arpazein ek ths xeiros tou patros.
joh 10:30 egw kai o pathr en esmen.
joh 10:31 ebastasan palin liqous oi ioudaioi ina liqaswsin auton.
joh 10:32 apekriqh autois o ihsous polla erga kala edeica umin ek tou patros dia poion autwn ergon eme liqazete;
joh 10:33 apekriqhsan autw oi ioudaioi peri kalou ergou ou liqazomen se alla peri blasfhmias kai oti su anqrwpos wn poieis seauton qeon.
joh 10:34 apekriqh autois o ihsous ouk estin gegrammenon en tw nomw umwn oti egw eipa qeoi este;
joh 10:35 ei ekeinous eipen qeous pros ous o logos tou qeou egeneto kai ou dunatai luqhnai h grafh
joh 10:36 on o pathr hgiasen kai apesteilen eis ton kosmon umeis legete oti blasfhmeis oti eipon uios tou qeou eimi;
joh 10:37 ei ou poiw ta erga tou patros mou mh pisteuete moi
joh 10:38 ei de poiw kan emoi mh pisteuhte tois ergois pisteuete ina gnwte kai ginwskhte oti en emoi o pathr kagw en tw patri.
joh 10:39 ezhtoun oun auton palin piasai kai echlqen ek ths xeiros autwn.
joh 10:40 kai aphlqen palin peran tou iordanou eis ton topon opou hn iwannhs to prwton baptizwn kai emeinen ekei.
joh 10:41 kai polloi hlqon pros auton kai elegon oti iwannhs men shmeion epoihsen ouden panta de osa eipen iwannhs peri toutou alhqh hn.
joh 10:42 kai polloi episteusan eis auton ekei.
joh 11:1 hn de tis asqenwn lazaros apo bhqanias ek ths kwmhs marias kai marqas ths adelfhs auths.
joh 11:2 hn de mariam h aleiyasa ton kurion murw kai ekmacasa tous podas autou tais qricin auths hs o adelfos lazaros hsqenei.
joh 11:3 apesteilan oun ai adelfai pros auton legousai kurie ide on fileis asqenei.
joh 11:4 akousas de o ihsous eipen auth h asqeneia ouk estin pros qanaton all uper ths dochs tou qeou ina docasqh o uios tou qeou di auths.
joh 11:5 hgapa de o ihsous thn marqan kai thn adelfhn auths kai ton lazaron.
joh 11:6 ws oun hkousen oti asqenei tote men emeinen en w hn topw duo hmeras
joh 11:7 epeita meta touto legei tois maqhtais agwmen eis thn ioudaian palin.
joh 11:8 legousin autw oi maqhtai rabbi nun ezhtoun se liqasai oi ioudaioi kai palin upageis ekei;
joh 11:9 apekriqh ihsous ouxi dwdeka wrai eisin ths hmeras; ean tis peripath en th hmera ou proskoptei oti to fws tou kosmou toutou blepei
joh 11:10 ean de tis peripath en th nukti proskoptei oti to fws ouk estin en autw.
joh 11:11 tauta eipen kai meta touto legei autois lazaros o filos hmwn kekoimhtai alla poreuomai ina ecupnisw auton.
joh 11:12 eipan oun oi maqhtai autw kurie ei kekoimhtai swqhsetai.
joh 11:13 eirhkei de o ihsous peri tou qanatou autou. ekeinoi de edocan oti peri ths koimhsews tou upnou legei.
joh 11:14 tote oun eipen autois o ihsous parrhsia lazaros apeqanen
joh 11:15 kai xairw di umas ina pisteushte oti ouk hmhn ekei alla agwmen pros auton.
joh 11:16 eipen oun qwmas o legomenos didumos tois summaqhtais agwmen kai hmeis ina apoqanwmen met autou.
joh 11:17 elqwn oun o ihsous euren auton tessaras hdh hmeras exonta en tw mnhmeiw.
joh 11:18 hn de h bhqania eggus twn ierosolumwn ws apo stadiwn dekapente.
joh 11:19 polloi de ek twn ioudaiwn elhluqeisan pros thn marqan kai mariam ina paramuqhswntai autas peri tou adelfou.
joh 11:20 h oun marqa ws hkousen oti ihsous erxetai uphnthsen autw mariam de en tw oikw ekaqezeto.
joh 11:21 eipen oun h marqa pros ton ihsoun kurie ei hs wde ouk an apeqanen o adelfos mou
joh 11:22 alla kai nun oida oti osa an aithsh ton qeon dwsei soi o qeos.
joh 11:23 legei auth o ihsous anasthsetai o adelfos sou.
joh 11:24 legei autw h marqa oida oti anasthsetai en th anastasei en th esxath hmera.
joh 11:25 eipen auth o ihsous egw eimi h anastasis kai h zwh o pisteuwn eis eme kan apoqanh zhsetai
joh 11:26 kai pas o zwn kai pisteuwn eis eme ou mh apoqanh eis ton aiwna pisteueis touto;
joh 11:27 legei autw nai kurie egw pepisteuka oti su ei o xristos o uios tou qeou o eis ton kosmon erxomenos.
joh 11:28 kai touto eipousa aphlqen kai efwnhsen mariam thn adelfhn auths laqra eipousa o didaskalos parestin kai fwnei se.
joh 11:29 ekeinh de ws hkousen hgerqh taxu kai hrxeto pros auton
joh 11:30 oupw de elhluqei o ihsous eis thn kwmhn all hn eti en tw topw opou uphnthsen autw h marqa.
joh 11:31 oi oun ioudaioi oi ontes met auths en th oikia kai paramuqoumenoi authn idontes thn mariam oti taxews anesth kai echlqen hkolouqhsan auth [docazontes] oti upagei eis to mnhmeion ina klaush ekei.
joh 11:32 h oun mariam ws hlqen opou hn ihsous idousa auton epesen autou pros tous podas legousa autw kurie ei hs wde ouk an mou apeqanen o adelfos.
joh 11:33 ihsous oun ws eiden authn klaiousan kai tous sunelqontas auth ioudaious klaiontas enebrimhsato tw pneumati kai etaracen eauton
joh 11:34 kai eipen pou teqeikate auton; legousin autw kurie erxou kai ide.
joh 11:35 edakrusen o ihsous.
joh 11:36 elegon oun oi ioudaioi ide pws efilei auton.
joh 11:37 tines de ec autwn eipan ouk edunato outos o anoicas tous ofqalmous tou tuflou poihsai ina kai outos mh apoqanh;
joh 11:38 ihsous oun palin embrimwmenos en eautw erxetai eis to mnhmeion hn de sphlaion kai liqos epekeito ep autw.
joh 11:39 legei o ihsous arate ton liqon. legei autw h adelfh tou teteleuthkotos marqa kurie hdh ozei tetartaios gar estin.
joh 11:40 legei auth o ihsous ouk eipon soi oti ean pisteushs oyh thn docan tou qeou;
joh 11:41 hran oun ton liqon. o de ihsous hren tous ofqalmous anw kai eipen pater euxaristw soi oti hkousas mou.
joh 11:42 egw de hdein oti pantote mou akoueis alla dia ton oxlon ton periestwta eipon ina pisteuswsin oti su me apesteilas.
joh 11:43 kai tauta eipwn fwnh megalh ekraugasen lazare deuro ecw.
joh 11:44 echlqen o teqnhkws dedemenos tous podas kai tas xeiras keiriais kai h oyis autou soudariw periededeto. legei autois o ihsous lusate auton kai afete auton upagein.
joh 11:45 polloi oun ek twn ioudaiwn oi elqontes pros thn mariam kai qeasamenoi a epoihsen episteusan eis auton
joh 11:46 tines de ec autwn aphlqon pros tous farisaious kai eipan autois a epoihsen ihsous.
joh 11:47 sunhgagon oun oi arxiereis kai oi farisaioi sunedrion kai elegon ti poioumen oti outos o anqrwpos polla poiei shmeia;
joh 11:48 ean afwmen auton outws pantes pisteusousin eis auton kai eleusontai oi rwmaioi kai arousin hmwn kai ton topon kai to eqnos.
joh 11:49 eis de tis ec autwn kaiafas arxiereus wn tou eniautou ekeinou eipen autois umeis ouk oidate ouden
joh 11:50 oude logizesqe oti sumferei [--] ina eis anqrwpos apoqanh uper tou laou kai mh olon to eqnos apolhtai.
joh 11:51 touto de af eautou ouk eipen alla arxiereus wn tou eniautou ekeinou eprofhteusen oti emellen ihsous apoqnhskein uper tou eqnous
joh 11:52 kai oux uper tou eqnous monon all ina kai ta tekna tou qeou ta dieskorpismena sunagagh eis en.
joh 11:53 ap ekeinhs oun ths hmeras ebouleusanto ina apokteinwsin auton.
joh 11:54 o oun ihsous ouketi parrhsia periepatei en tois ioudaiois alla aphlqen ekeiqen eis thn xwran eggus ths erhmou eis efraim legomenhn polin kakei emeinen meta twn maqhtwn.
joh 11:55 hn de eggus to pasxa twn ioudaiwn kai anebhsan polloi eis ierosoluma ek ths xwras pro tou pasxa ina agniswsin eautous.
joh 11:56 ezhtoun oun ton ihsoun kai elegon met allhlwn en tw ierw esthkotes ti dokei umin; oti ou mh elqh eis thn eorthn;
joh 11:57 dedwkeisan de oi arxiereis kai oi farisaioi entolas ina ean tis gnw pou estin mhnush opws piaswsin auton.
joh 12:1 o oun ihsous pro ec hmerwn tou pasxa hlqen eis bhqanian opou hn lazaros on hgeiren ek nekrwn ihsous.
joh 12:2 epoihsan oun autw deipnon ekei kai h marqa dihkonei o de lazaros eis hn ek twn anakeimenwn sun autw.
joh 12:3 h oun mariam labousa litran murou nardou pistikhs polutimou hleiyen tous podas tou ihsou kai ecemacen tais qricin auths tous podas autou h de oikia eplhrwqh ek ths osmhs tou murou.
joh 12:4 legei de ioudas o iskariwths eis ek twn maqhtwn autou o mellwn auton paradidonai
joh 12:5 dia ti touto to muron ouk epraqh triakosiwn dhnariwn kai edoqh ptwxois;
joh 12:6 eipen de touto oux oti peri twn ptwxwn emelen autw all oti klepths hn kai to glwssokomon exwn ta ballomena ebastazen.

joh 12:9 [--] oxlos [de] polus ek twn ioudaiwn [hkousan] oti ekei estin kai hlqon ou dia ton ihsoun monon all ina kai ton lazaron idwsin on hgeiren ek nekrwn.

joh 12:13 elabon ta baia twn foinikwn kai echlqon eis upanthsin autw kai ekraugazon wsanna euloghmenos o erxomenos en onomati kuriou kai o basileus tou israhl.

joh 12:16 tauta ouk egnwsan autou oi maqhtai to prwton all ote edocasqh ihsous tote emnhsqhsan oti tauta hn ep autw gegrammena kai tauta epoihsan autw.
joh 12:17 emarturei oun o oxlos o wn met autou [oti] ton lazaron efwnhsen ek tou mnhmeiou kai hgeiren auton ek nekrwn.
joh 12:18 dia touto kai uphnthsen autw o oxlos oti hkousan touto auton pepoihkenai to shmeion.

joh 12:20 hsan de ellhnes tines ek twn anabainontwn ina proskunhswsin en th eorth
joh 12:21 outoi oun proshlqon filippw tw apo bhqsaida ths galilaias kai hrwtwn auton legontes kurie qelomen ton ihsoun idein.
joh 12:22 erxetai o filippos kai legei tw andrea erxetai andreas kai filippos kai legousin tw ihsou.
joh 12:23 o de ihsous apokrinetai autois legwn elhluqen h wra ina docasqh o uios tou anqrwpou.
joh 12:24 amhn amhn legw umin ean mh o kokkos tou sitou peswn eis thn ghn apoqanh autos monos menei ean de apoqanh polun karpon ferei.
joh 12:25 o filwn thn yuxhn autou apolluei authn kai o miswn thn yuxhn autou en tw kosmw toutw eis zwhn aiwnion fulacei authn.
joh 12:26 ean emoi tis diakonh emoi akolouqeitw kai opou eimi egw ekei kai o diakonos o emos estai ean tis emoi diakonh timhsei auton o pathr.
joh 12:27 nun h yuxh mou tetaraktai. kai ti eipw; pater swson me ek ths wras tauths; alla dia touto hlqon eis thn wran tauthn.
joh 12:28 pater docason sou to onoma. hlqen oun fwnh ek tou ouranou kai edocasa kai palin docasw.
joh 12:29 o oun oxlos o estws kai akousas elegen bronthn gegonenai alloi elegon aggelos autw lelalhken.
joh 12:30 apekriqh ihsous kai eipen ou di eme h fwnh auth gegonen alla di umas.

joh 12:32 kagw ean uywqw ek ths ghs pantas elkusw pros emauton.
joh 12:33 touto de elegen shmainwn poiw qanatw hmellen apoqnhskein.

joh 12:35 eipen oun autois o ihsous eti mikron xronon to fws en umin estin. peripateite ws to fws exete ina mh skotia umas katalabh kai o peripatwn en th skotia ouk oiden pou upagei.
joh 12:36 ws to fws exete pisteuete eis to fws ina uioi fwtos genhsqe. tauta elalhsen ihsous kai apelqwn ekrubh ap autwn.
joh 12:37 tosauta de autou shmeia pepoihkotos emprosqen autwn ouk episteuon eis auton
joh 12:38 ina o logos hsaiou tou profhtou plhrwqh on eipen kurie tis episteusen th akoh hmwn; kai o braxiwn kuriou tini apekalufqh;
joh 12:39 dia touto ouk hdunanto pisteuein oti palin eipen hsaias
joh 12:40 tetuflwken autwn tous ofqalmous kai [pepwrwken] autwn thn kardian ina mh idwsin tois ofqalmois kai nohswsin th kardia kai strafwsin kai iasomai autous.
joh 12:41 tauta eipen hsaias oti eiden thn docan autou kai elalhsen peri autou.
joh 12:42 omws mentoi kai ek twn arxontwn polloi episteusan eis auton alla dia tous farisaious oux wmologoun ina mh aposunagwgoi genwntai
joh 12:43 hgaphsan gar thn docan twn anqrwpwn mallon hper thn docan tou qeou.
joh 12:44 ihsous de ekracen kai eipen o pisteuwn eis eme ou pisteuei eis eme alla eis ton pemyanta me
joh 12:45 kai o qewrwn eme qewrei ton pemyanta me.
joh 12:46 egw fws eis ton kosmon elhluqa ina pas o pisteuwn eis eme en th skotia mh meinh.
joh 12:47 kai ean tis mou akoush twn rhmatwn kai mh fulach egw ou krinw auton ou gar hlqon ina krinw ton kosmon all ina swsw ton kosmon.
joh 12:48 o aqetwn eme kai mh lambanwn ta rhmata mou exei ton krinonta auton o logos on elalhsa ekeinos krinei auton en th esxath hmera
joh 12:49 oti egw ec emautou ouk elalhsa all o pemyas me pathr autos moi entolhn dedwken ti eipw kai ti lalhsw.
joh 12:50 kai oida oti h entolh autou zwh aiwnios estin. a oun egw lalw kaqws eirhken moi o pathr outws lalw.
joh 13:1 pro de ths eorths tou pasxa eidws o ihsous oti hlqen autou h wra ina metabh ek tou kosmou toutou pros ton patera agaphsas tous idious tous en tw kosmw eis telos hgaphsen autous.
joh 13:2 kai deipnou ginomenou tou diabolou hdh beblhkotos eis thn kardian ina paradoi auton [iouda] simwnos iskariwtou
joh 13:3 eidws oti panta edwken autw o pathr eis tas xeiras kai oti apo qeou echlqen kai pros ton qeon upagei
joh 13:4 egeiretai ek tou deipnou kai tiqhsin ta imatia kai labwn lention diezwsen eauton.
joh 13:5 eita ballei udwr eis ton nipthra kai hrcato niptein tous podas twn maqhtwn kai ekmassein tw lentiw w hn diezwsmenos.
joh 13:6 erxetai oun pros simwna petron. legei autw kurie su mou nipteis tous podas;
joh 13:7 apekriqh ihsous kai eipen autw o egw poiw su ouk oidas arti gnwsh de meta tauta.
joh 13:8 legei autw petros ou mh niyhs mou tous podas eis ton aiwna. apekriqh ihsous autw ean mh niyw se ouk exeis meros met emou.
joh 13:9 legei autw simwn petros kurie mh tous podas mou monon alla kai tas xeiras kai thn kefalhn.
joh 13:10 legei autw o ihsous o leloumenos ouk exei xreian ei mh tous podas niyasqai all estin kaqaros olos kai umeis kaqaroi este all ouxi pantes.
joh 13:11 hdei gar ton paradidonta auton dia touto eipen oti ouxi pantes kaqaroi este.
joh 13:12 ote oun eniyen tous podas autwn kai elaben ta imatia autou kai anepesen palin eipen autois ginwskete ti pepoihka umin;
joh 13:13 umeis fwneite me o didaskalos kai o kurios kai kalws legete eimi gar.
joh 13:14 ei oun egw eniya umwn tous podas o kurios kai o didaskalos kai umeis ofeilete allhlwn niptein tous podas
joh 13:15 upodeigma gar edwka umin ina kaqws egw epoihsa umin kai umeis poihte.
joh 13:16 amhn amhn legw umin ouk estin doulos meizwn tou kuriou autou oude apostolos meizwn tou pemyantos auton.
joh 13:17 ei tauta oidate makarioi este ean poihte auta.
joh 13:18 ou peri pantwn umwn legw egw oida tinas ecelecamhn all ina h grafh plhrwqh o trwgwn mou ton arton ephren ep eme thn pternan autou.
joh 13:19 ap arti legw umin pro tou genesqai ina pisteushte otan genhtai oti egw eimi.
joh 13:20 amhn amhn legw umin o lambanwn an tina pemyw eme lambanei o de eme lambanwn lambanei ton pemyanta me.
joh 13:21 tauta eipwn o ihsous etaraxqh tw pneumati kai emarturhsen kai eipen amhn amhn legw umin oti eis ec umwn paradwsei me.
joh 13:22 eblepon eis allhlous oi maqhtai aporoumenoi peri tinos legei.
joh 13:23 hn anakeimenos eis ek twn maqhtwn autou en tw kolpw tou ihsou on hgapa o ihsous
joh 13:24 neuei oun toutw simwn petros puqesqai tis an eih peri ou legei.
joh 13:25 anapeswn oun ekeinos outws epi to sthqos tou ihsou legei autw kurie tis estin;
joh 13:26 apokrinetai o ihsous ekeinos estin w egw bayw to ywmion kai dwsw autw. bayas oun to ywmion lambanei kai didwsin iouda simwnos iskariwtou.
joh 13:27 kai meta to ywmion tote eishlqen eis ekeinon o satanas. legei oun autw o ihsous o poieis poihson taxion.
joh 13:28 touto de oudeis egnw twn anakeimenwn pros ti eipen autw
joh 13:29 tines gar edokoun epei to glwssokomon eixen ioudas oti legei autw o ihsous agorason wn xreian exomen eis thn eorthn h tois ptwxois ina ti dw.
joh 13:30 labwn oun to ywmion ekeinos echlqen euqus hn de nuc.
joh 13:31 ote oun echlqen legei ihsous nun edocasqh o uios tou anqrwpou kai o qeos edocasqh en autw
joh 13:32 ei o qeos edocasqh en autw kai o qeos docasei auton en autw kai euqus docasei auton.
joh 13:33 teknia eti mikron meq umwn eimi zhthsete me kai kaqws eipon tois ioudaiois oti opou egw upagw umeis ou dunasqe elqein kai umin legw arti.
joh 13:34 entolhn kainhn didwmi umin ina agapate allhlous kaqws hgaphsa umas ina kai umeis agapate allhlous.
joh 13:35 en toutw gnwsontai pantes oti emoi maqhtai este ean agaphn exhte en allhlois.

joh 19:16 tote oun paredwken auton autois ina staurwqh. parelabon oun ton ihsoun

joh 19:22 apekriqh o pilatos o gegrafa gegrafa.

joh 21:2 hsan omou simwn petros kai qwmas o legomenos didumos kai naqanahl o apo kana ths galilaias kai oi tou zebedaiou kai alloi ek twn maqhtwn autou duo.
joh 21:3 legei autois simwn petros upagw alieuein. legousin autw erxomeqa kai hmeis sun soi. echlqon kai enebhsan eis to ploion kai en ekeinh th nukti epiasan ouden.
joh 21:4 prwias de hdh genomenhs esth ihsous eis ton aigialon ou mentoi hdeisan oi maqhtai oti ihsous estin.
joh 21:5 legei oun autois o ihsous paidia mh ti prosfagion exete; apekriqhsan autw ou.
joh 21:6 o de eipen autois balete eis ta decia merh tou ploiou to diktuon kai eurhsete. ebalon oun kai ouketi auto elkusai isxuon apo tou plhqous twn ixquwn.
joh 21:7 legei oun o maqhths ekeinos on hgapa o ihsous tw petrw o kurios estin. simwn oun petros akousas oti o kurios estin ton ependuthn diezwsato hn gar gumnos kai ebalen eauton eis thn qalassan
joh 21:8 oi de alloi maqhtai tw ploiariw hlqon ou gar hsan makran apo ths ghs alla ws apo phxwn diakosiwn surontes to diktuon twn ixquwn.
joh 21:9 ws oun apebhsan eis thn ghn blepousin anqrakian keimenhn kai oyarion epikeimenon kai arton.
joh 21:10 legei autois o ihsous enegkate apo twn oyariwn wn epiasate nun.
joh 21:11 anebh oun simwn petros kai eilkusen to diktuon eis thn ghn meston ixquwn megalwn ekaton penthkonta triwn kai tosoutwn ontwn ouk esxisqh to diktuon.
joh 21:12 legei autois o ihsous deute aristhsate. oudeis de etolma twn maqhtwn ecetasai auton su tis ei; eidotes oti o kurios estin.
joh 21:13 erxetai ihsous kai lambanei ton arton kai didwsin autois kai to oyarion omoiws.
joh 21:14 touto hdh triton efanerwqh ihsous tois maqhtais egerqeis ek nekrwn.
joh 21:15 ote oun hristhsan legei tw simwni petrw o ihsous simwn iwannou agapas me pleon toutwn; legei autw nai kurie su oidas oti filw se. legei autw boske ta arnia mou.
joh 21:16 legei autw palin deuteron simwn iwannou agapas me; legei autw nai kurie su oidas oti filw se. legei autw poimaine ta probata mou.
joh 21:17 legei autw to triton simwn iwannou fileis me; eluphqh o petros oti eipen autw to triton fileis me; kai legei autw kurie panta su oidas su ginwskeis oti filw se. legei autw o ihsous boske ta probata mou.
joh 21:18 amhn amhn legw soi ote hs newteros ezwnnues seauton kai periepateis opou hqeles otan de ghrashs ekteneis tas xeiras sou kai allos se zwsei kai oisei opou ou qeleis.
joh 21:19 touto de eipen shmainwn poiw qanatw docasei ton qeon. kai touto eipwn legei autw akolouqei moi.
joh 21:20 epistrafeis o petros blepei ton maqhthn on hgapa o ihsous akolouqounta os kai anepesen en tw deipnw epi to sthqos autou kai eipen kurie tis estin o paradidous se;
joh 21:21 touton oun idwn o petros legei tw ihsou kurie outos de ti;
joh 21:22 legei autw o ihsous ean auton qelw menein ews erxomai ti pros se; su moi akolouqei.
joh 21:23 echlqen oun outos o logos eis tous adelfous oti o maqhths ekeinos ouk apoqnhskei. ouk eipen de autw o ihsous oti ouk apoqnhskei all ean auton qelw menein ews erxomai ti pros se;
joh 21:24 outos estin o maqhths o marturwn peri toutwn kai o grayas tauta kai oidamen oti alhqhs autou h marturia estin.

act 7:16 kai meteteqhsan eis suxem kai eteqhsan en tw mnhmati w wnhsato abraam timhs arguriou para twn uiwn emmwr en suxem.

act 7:35 touton ton mwushn on hrnhsanto eipontes tis se katesthsen arxonta kai dikasthn; touton o qeos kai arxonta kai lutrwthn apestalken sun xeiri aggelou tou ofqentos autw en th batw.
act 7:36 outos echgagen autous poihsas terata kai shmeia en gh aiguptw kai en eruqra qalassh kai en th erhmw eth tesserakonta.

act 7:41 kai emosxopoihsan en tais hmerais ekeinais kai anhgagon qusian tw eidwlw kai eufrainonto en tois ergois twn xeirwn autwn.
act 7:42 estreyen de o qeos kai paredwken autous latreuein th stratia tou ouranou kaqws gegraptai en biblw twn profhtwn mh sfagia kai qusias proshnegkate moi eth tesserakonta en th erhmw oikos israhl;
act 7:43 kai anelabete thn skhnhn tou molox kai to astron tou qeou umwn raifan tous tupous ous epoihsate proskunein autois kai metoikiw umas epekeina babulwnos.

act 7:45 hn kai eishgagon diadecamenoi oi pateres hmwn meta ihsou en th katasxesei twn eqnwn wn ecwsen o qeos apo proswpou twn paterwn hmwn ews twn hmerwn dauid
act 7:46 os euren xarin enwpion tou qeou kai hthsato eurein skhnwma tw oikw iakwb.
act 7:47 solomwn de oikodomhsen autw oikon.
act 7:48 all oux o uyistos en xeiropoihtois katoikei kaqws o profhths legei

act 7:50 ouxi h xeir mou epoihsen tauta panta;
act 7:51 sklhrotraxhloi kai aperitmhtoi kardiais kai tois wsin umeis aei tw pneumati tw agiw antipiptete ws oi pateres umwn kai umeis.

act 7:53 oitines elabete ton nomon eis diatagas aggelwn kai ouk efulacate.

act 7:56 kai eipen idou qewrw tous ouranous dihnoigmenous kai ton uion tou anqrwpou ek deciwn estwta tou qeou.

act 8:1 saulos de hn suneudokwn th anairesei autou. egeneto de en ekeinh th hmera diwgmos megas epi thn ekklhsian thn en ierosolumois pantes de diesparhsan kata tas xwras ths ioudaias kai samareias plhn twn apostolwn.
act 8:2 sunekomisan de ton stefanon andres eulabeis kai epoihsan kopeton megan ep autw.
act 8:3 saulos de elumaineto thn ekklhsian kata tous oikous eisporeuomenos surwn te andras kai gunaikas paredidou eis fulakhn.
act 8:4 oi men oun diasparentes dihlqon euaggelizomenoi ton logon.
act 8:5 filippos de katelqwn eis [--] polin ths samareias ekhrussen autois ton xriston.

act 8:12 ote de episteusan tw filippw euaggelizomenw peri ths basileias tou qeou kai tou onomatos ihsou xristou ebaptizonto andres te kai gunaikes.
act 8:13 o de simwn kai autos episteusen kai baptisqeis hn proskarterwn tw filippw qewrwn te shmeia kai dunameis megalas ginomenas ecistato.
act 8:14 akousantes de oi en ierosolumois apostoloi oti dedektai h samareia ton logon tou qeou apesteilan pros autous petron kai iwannhn
act 8:15 oitines katabantes proshucanto peri autwn opws labwsin pneuma agion
act 8:16 oudepw gar hn ep oudeni autwn epipeptwkos monon de bebaptismenoi uphrxon eis to onoma tou kuriou ihsou.
act 8:17 tote epetiqesan tas xeiras ep autous kai elambanon pneuma agion.

act 8:19 legwn dote kamoi thn ecousian tauthn ina w ean epiqw tas xeiras lambanh pneuma agion.

act 8:21 ouk estin soi meris oude klhros en tw logw toutw h gar kardia sou ouk estin euqeia enanti tou qeou.
act 8:22 metanohson oun apo ths kakias sou tauths kai dehqhti tou kuriou ei ara afeqhsetai soi h epinoia ths kardias sou
act 8:23 eis gar xolhn pikrias kai sundesmon adikias orw se onta.
act 8:24 apokriqeis de o simwn eipen dehqhte umeis uper emou pros ton kurion opws mhden epelqh ep eme wn eirhkate.
act 8:25 oi men oun diamarturamenoi kai lalhsantes ton logon tou kuriou upestrefon eis ierosoluma pollas te kwmas twn samaritwn euhggelizonto.
act 8:26 aggelos de kuriou elalhsen pros filippon legwn anasthqi kai poreuou kata meshmbrian epi thn odon thn katabainousan apo ierousalhm eis gazan auth estin erhmos.
act 8:27 kai anastas eporeuqh kai idou anhr aiqioy eunouxos dunasths kandakhs basilisshs aiqiopwn os hn epi pashs ths gazhs auths os elhluqei proskunhswn eis ierousalhm
act 8:28 hn te upostrefwn kai kaqhmenos epi tou armatos autou kai aneginwsken ton profhthn hsaian.
act 8:29 eipen de to pneuma tw filippw proselqe kai kollhqhti tw armati toutw.
act 8:30 prosdramwn de o filippos hkousen autou anaginwskontos hsaian ton profhthn kai eipen ara ge ginwskeis a anaginwskeis;
act 8:31 o de eipen pws gar an dunaimhn ean mh tis odhghsei me; parekalesen te ton filippon anabanta kaqisai sun autw.
act 8:32 h de perioxh ths grafhs hn aneginwsken hn auth ws probaton epi sfaghn hxqh kai ws amnos enantion tou keirantos auton afwnos outws ouk anoigei to stoma autou.
act 8:33 en th tapeinwsei autou h krisis autou hrqh thn genean autou tis dihghsetai; oti airetai apo ths ghs h zwh autou.
act 8:34 apokriqeis de o eunouxos tw filippw eipen deomai sou peri tinos o profhths legei touto; peri eautou h peri eterou tinos;
act 8:35 anoicas de o filippos to stoma autou kai arcamenos apo ths grafhs tauths euhggelisato autw ton ihsoun.
act 8:36 ws de eporeuonto kata thn odon hlqon epi ti udwr kai fhsin o eunouxos idou udwr ti kwluei me baptisqhnai;
