act 9:1 o de saulos eti empnewn apeilhs kai fonou eis tous maqhtas tou kuriou proselqwn tw arxierei
act 9:2 hthsato par autou epistolas eis damaskon pros tas sunagwgas opws ean tinas eurh ths odou ontas andras te kai gunaikas dedemenous agagh eis ierousalhm.
act 9:3 en de tw poreuesqai egeneto auton eggizein th damaskw ecaifnhs te auton perihstrayen fws ek tou ouranou
act 9:4 kai peswn epi thn ghn hkousen fwnhn legousan autw saoul saoul ti me diwkeis;
act 9:5 eipen de tis ei kurie; o de egw eimi ihsous on su diwkeis
act 9:6 alla anasthqi kai eiselqe eis thn polin kai lalhqhsetai soi o ti se dei poiein.
act 9:7 oi de andres oi sunodeuontes autw eisthkeisan eneoi akouontes men ths fwnhs mhdena de qewrountes.
act 9:8 hgerqh de saulos apo ths ghs anewgmenwn de twn ofqalmwn autou ouden eblepen xeiragwgountes de auton eishgagon eis damaskon.
act 9:9 kai hn hmeras treis mh blepwn kai ouk efagen oude epien.
act 9:10 hn de tis maqhths en damaskw onomati ananias kai eipen pros auton en oramati o kurios anania. o de eipen idou egw kurie.
act 9:11 o de kurios pros auton anastas poreuqhti epi thn rumhn thn kaloumenhn euqeian kai zhthson en oikia iouda saulon onomati tarsea idou gar proseuxetai
act 9:12 kai eiden [oramati andra en] ananian onomati eiselqonta kai epiqenta autw tas xeiras opws anableyh.
act 9:13 apekriqh de ananias kurie hkousa apo pollwn peri tou andros toutou osa kaka tois agiois sou epoihsen en ierousalhm
act 9:14 kai wde exei ecousian para twn arxierewn dhsai pantas tous epikaloumenous to onoma sou.
act 9:15 eipen de pros auton o kurios poreuou oti skeuos ekloghs estin moi outos tou bastasai to onoma mou enwpion eqnwn te kai basilewn uiwn te israhl
act 9:16 egw gar upodeicw autw osa dei auton uper tou onomatos mou paqein.
act 9:17 aphlqen de ananias kai eishlqen eis thn oikian kai epiqeis ep auton tas xeiras eipen saoul adelfe o kurios apestalken me ihsous o ofqeis soi en th odw h hrxou opws anableyhs kai plhsqhs pneumatos agiou.
act 9:18 kai euqews apepesan autou apo twn ofqalmwn ws lepides anebleyen te kai anastas ebaptisqh
act 9:19 kai labwn trofhn enisxusen. egeneto de meta twn en damaskw maqhtwn hmeras tinas
act 9:20 kai euqews en tais sunagwgais ekhrussen ton ihsoun oti outos estin o uios tou qeou.
act 9:21 ecistanto de pantes oi akouontes kai elegon oux outos estin o porqhsas eis ierousalhm tous epikaloumenous to onoma touto kai wde eis touto elhluqei ina dedemenous autous agagh epi tous arxiereis;
act 9:22 saulos de mallon enedunamouto kai sunexunnen tous ioudaious tous katoikountas en damaskw sumbibazwn oti outos estin o xristos.
act 9:23 ws de eplhrounto hmerai ikanai sunebouleusanto oi ioudaioi anelein auton
act 9:24 egnwsqh de tw saulw h epiboulh autwn. parethrounto de kai tas pulas hmeras te kai nuktos opws auton anelwsin
act 9:25 labontes de oi maqhtai autou nuktos dia tou teixous kaqhkan auton xalasantes en spuridi.
act 9:26 paragenomenos de eis ierousalhm epeirazen kollasqai tois maqhtais kai pantes efobounto auton mh pisteuontes oti estin maqhths.
act 9:27 barnabas de epilabomenos auton hgagen pros tous apostolous kai dihghsato autois pws en th odw eiden ton kurion kai oti elalhsen autw kai pws en damaskw eparrhsiasato en tw onomati tou ihsou.
act 9:28 kai hn met autwn eisporeuomenos kai ekporeuomenos eis ierousalhm parrhsiazomenos en tw onomati tou kuriou
act 9:29 elalei te kai sunezhtei pros tous ellhnistas oi de epexeiroun anelein auton.
act 9:30 epignontes de oi adelfoi kathgagon auton eis kaisareian kai ecapesteilan auton eis tarson.
act 9:31 h men oun ekklhsia kaq olhs ths ioudaias kai galilaias kai samareias eixen eirhnhn oikodomoumenh kai poreuomenh tw fobw tou kuriou kai th paraklhsei tou agiou pneumatos eplhquneto.
act 9:32 egeneto de petron dierxomenon dia pantwn katelqein kai pros tous agious tous katoikountas ludda.
act 9:33 euren de ekei anqrwpon tina onomati ainean ec etwn oktw katakeimenon epi krabattou os hn paralelumenos.
act 9:34 kai eipen autw o petros ainea iatai se ihsous xristos anasthqi kai strwson seautw. kai euqews anesth.
act 9:35 kai eidan auton pantes oi katoikountes ludda kai ton sarwna oitines epestreyan epi ton kurion.
act 9:36 en iopph de tis hn maqhtria onomati tabiqa h diermhneuomenh legetai dorkas auth hn plhrhs ergwn agaqwn kai elehmosunwn wn epoiei.
act 9:37 egeneto de en tais hmerais ekeinais asqenhsasan authn apoqanein lousantes de eqhkan authn en uperww.
act 9:38 eggus de oushs luddas th iopph oi maqhtai akousantes oti petros estin en auth apesteilan duo andras pros auton parakalountes mh oknhshs dielqein ews hmwn.
act 9:39 anastas de petros sunhlqen autois on paragenomenon anhgagon eis to uperwon kai paresthsan autw pasai ai xhrai klaiousai kai epideiknumenai xitwnas kai imatia osa epoiei met autwn ousa h dorkas.
act 9:40 ekbalwn de ecw pantas o petros kai qeis ta gonata proshucato kai epistreyas pros to swma eipen tabiqa anasthqi. h de hnoicen tous ofqalmous auths kai idousa ton petron anekaqisen.
act 9:41 dous de auth xeira anesthsen authn fwnhsas de tous agious kai tas xhras paresthsen authn zwsan.
act 9:42 gnwston de egeneto kaq olhs ths iopphs kai episteusan polloi epi ton kurion.
act 9:43 egeneto de hmeras ikanas meinai en iopph para tini simwni bursei.
act 10:1 anhr de tis en kaisareia onomati kornhlios ekatontarxhs ek speirhs ths kaloumenhs italikhs

act 10:3 eiden en oramati fanerws wsei peri wran enathn ths hmeras aggelon tou qeou eiselqonta pros auton kai eiponta autw kornhlie.
act 10:4 o de atenisas autw kai emfobos genomenos eipen ti estin kurie; eipen de autw ai proseuxai sou kai ai elehmosunai sou anebhsan eis mnhmosunon emprosqen tou qeou.
act 10:5 kai nun pemyon andras eis iopphn kai metapemyai simwna [--] os epikaleitai petros
act 10:6 outos cenizetai para tini simwni bursei w estin oikia para qalassan.

act 10:8 kai echghsamenos apanta autois apesteilen autous eis thn iopphn.
act 10:9 th de epaurion odoiporountwn ekeinwn kai th polei eggizontwn anebh petros epi to dwma proseucasqai peri wran ekthn.
act 10:10 egeneto de prospeinos kai hqelen geusasqai paraskeuazontwn de autwn egeneto ep auton ekstasis
act 10:11 kai qewrei ton ouranon anewgmenon kai katabainon skeuos ti ws oqonhn megalhn tessarsin arxais kaqiemenon epi ths ghs
act 10:12 en w uphrxen panta ta tetrapoda kai erpeta ths ghs kai peteina tou ouranou.
act 10:13 kai egeneto fwnh pros auton anastas petre quson kai fage.
act 10:14 o de petros eipen mhdamws kurie oti oudepote efagon pan koinon kai akaqarton.
act 10:15 kai fwnh palin ek deuterou pros auton a o qeos ekaqarisen su mh koinou.
act 10:16 touto de egeneto epi tris kai [palin] anelhmfqh to skeuos eis ton ouranon.
act 10:17 ws de en eautw dihporei o petros ti an eih to orama o eiden idou oi andres oi apestalmenoi upo tou kornhliou dierwthsantes thn oikian tou simwnos epesthsan epi ton pulwna
act 10:18 kai fwnhsantes epunqanonto ei simwn o epikaloumenos petros enqade cenizetai.
act 10:19 tou de petrou dienqumoumenou peri tou oramatos eipen autw to pneuma idou andres treis zhtountes se
act 10:20 alla anastas katabhqi kai poreuou sun autois mhden diakrinomenos oti egw apestalka autous.
act 10:21 katabas de petros pros tous andras eipen idou egw eimi on zhteite tis h aitia di hn pareste;
act 10:22 oi de eipan kornhlios ekatontarxhs anhr dikaios kai foboumenos ton qeon marturoumenos te upo olou tou eqnous twn ioudaiwn exrhmatisqh upo aggelou agiou metapemyasqai se eis ton oikon autou kai akousai rhmata para sou.
act 10:23 eiskalesamenos oun autous ecenisen. th de epaurion anastas echlqen sun autois kai tines twn adelfwn twn apo iopphs sunhlqon autw.
act 10:24 th de epaurion eishlqen eis thn kaisareian o de kornhlios hn prosdokwn autous sugkalesamenos tous suggeneis autou kai tous anagkaious filous.
act 10:25 ws de egeneto tou eiselqein ton petron sunanthsas autw o kornhlios peswn epi tous podas prosekunhsen.
act 10:26 o de petros hgeiren auton legwn anasthqi kai egw autos anqrwpos eimi.
act 10:27 kai sunomilwn autw eishlqen kai euriskei sunelhluqotas pollous
act 10:28 efh te pros autous umeis epistasqe ws aqemiton estin andri ioudaiw kollasqai h proserxesqai allofulw kamoi o qeos edeicen mhdena koinon h akaqarton legein anqrwpon
act 10:29 dio kai anantirrhtws hlqon metapemfqeis. punqanomai oun tini logw metepemyasqe me;
act 10:30 kai o kornhlios efh apo tetarths hmeras mexri tauths ths wras hmhn [nhsteuwn kai] thn enathn proseuxomenos en tw oikw mou kai idou anhr esth enwpion mou en esqhti lampra
act 10:31 kai fhsin kornhlie eishkousqh sou h proseuxh kai ai elehmosunai sou emnhsqhsan enwpion tou qeou.
act 10:32 pemyon oun eis iopphn kai metakalesai simwna os epikaleitai petros outos cenizetai en oikia simwnos bursews para qalassan [os paragenoumenos lalhsei soi].
act 10:33 ecauths oun epemya pros se su te kalws epoihsas paragenomenos. nun oun pantes hmeis enwpion tou qeou paresmen akousai panta ta prostetagmena soi upo tou [qeou].

act 15:2 genomenhs de stasews kai zhthsews ouk olighs tw paulw kai tw barnaba pros autous etacan anabainein paulon kai barnaban kai tinas allous ec autwn pros tous apostolous kai presbuterous eis ierousalhm peri tou zhthmatos toutou.
act 15:3 oi men oun propemfqentes upo ths ekklhsias dihrxonto thn te foinikhn kai samareian ekdihgoumenoi thn epistrofhn twn eqnwn kai epoioun xaran megalhn pasin tois adelfois.

act 15:5 ecanesthsan de tines twn apo ths airesews twn farisaiwn pepisteukotes legontes oti dei peritemnein autous paraggellein te threin ton nomon mwusews.
act 15:6 sunhxqhsan te oi apostoloi kai oi presbuteroi idein peri tou logou toutou.

act 19:19 ikanoi de twn ta perierga pracantwn sunenegkantes tas biblous katekaion enwpion pantwn kai suneyhfisan tas timas autwn kai euron arguriou muriadas pente.
act 19:20 outws kata kratos [o logos tou kuriou] hucanen kai isxuen.
act 19:21 ws de eplhrwqh tauta eqeto o paulos en tw pneumati dielqwn thn makedonian kai axaian poreuesqai eis ierosoluma eipwn oti meta to genesqai me ekei dei me kai rwmhn idein.
act 19:22 aposteilas de eis thn makedonian duo twn diakonountwn autw timoqeon kai eraston autos epesxen xronon eis thn asian.
act 19:23 egeneto de kata ton kairon ekeinon taraxos ouk oligos peri ths odou.
act 19:24 dhmhtrios gar tis onomati argurokopos poiwn naous argurous artemidos pareixeto tois texnitais ouk olighn ergasian
act 19:25 ous sunaqroisas kai tous peri ta toiauta ergatas eipen andres epistasqe oti ek tauths ths ergasias h euporia hmin estin
act 19:26 kai qewreite kai akouete oti ou monon efesou alla sxedon pashs ths asias o paulos outos peisas metesthsen ikanon oxlon legwn oti ouk eisin qeoi oi dia xeirwn ginomenoi.
act 19:27 ou monon de touto kinduneuei hmin to meros eis apelegmon elqein alla kai to ths megalhs qeas artemidos ieron eis ouqen logisqhnai mellein te kai kaqaireisqai ths megaleiothtos auths hn olh h asia kai h oikoumenh sebetai.
act 19:28 akousantes de kai genomenoi plhreis qumou ekrazon legontes megalh h artemis efesiwn.
act 19:29 kai eplhsqh h polis ths sugxusews wrmhsan te omoqumadon eis to qeatron sunarpasantes gaion kai aristarxon makedonas sunekdhmous paulou.
act 19:30 paulou de boulomenou eiselqein eis ton dhmon ouk eiwn auton oi maqhtai
act 19:31 tines de kai twn asiarxwn ontes autw filoi pemyantes pros auton parekaloun mh dounai eauton eis to qeatron.
act 19:32 alloi men oun allo ti ekrazon hn gar h ekklhsia sugkexumenh kai oi pleious ouk hdeisan tinos eneka sunelhluqeisan.
act 19:33 ek de tou oxlou sunebibasan alecandron probalontwn auton twn ioudaiwn o de alecandros kataseisas thn xeira hqelen apologeisqai tw dhmw.
act 19:34 epignontes de oti ioudaios estin fwnh egeneto mia ek pantwn ws epi wras duo krazontwn megalh h artemis efesiwn.
act 19:35 katasteilas de o grammateus ton oxlon fhsin andres efesioi tis gar estin anqrwpwn os ou ginwskei thn efesiwn polin newkoron ousan ths megalhs artemidos kai tou diopetous;
act 19:36 anantirrhtwn oun ontwn toutwn deon estin umas katestalmenous uparxein kai mhden propetes prassein.
act 19:37 hgagete gar tous andras toutous oute ierosulous oute blasfhmountas thn qeon hmwn.
act 19:38 ei men oun dhmhtrios kai oi sun autw texnitai exousi pros tina logon agoraioi agontai kai anqupatoi eisin egkaleitwsan allhlois.
act 19:39 ei de ti [peri eterwn] epizhteite en th ennomw ekklhsia epiluqhsetai.
act 19:40 kai gar kinduneuomen egkaleisqai stasews peri ths shmeron mhdenos aitiou uparxontos peri ou [--] dunhsomeqa apodounai logon peri ths sustrofhs tauths. kai tauta eipwn apelusen thn ekklhsian.
act 20:1 meta de to pausasqai ton qorubon metapemyamenos o paulos tous maqhtas kai parakalesas aspasamenos echlqen poreuesqai eis makedonian.
act 20:2 dielqwn de ta merh ekeina kai parakalesas autous logw pollw hlqen eis thn ellada
act 20:3 poihsas te mhnas treis genomenhs epiboulhs autw upo twn ioudaiwn mellonti anagesqai eis thn surian egeneto gnwmhs tou upostrefein dia makedonias.
act 20:4 suneipeto de autw swpatros purrou beroiaios qessalonikewn de aristarxos kai sekoundos kai gaios derbaios kai timoqeos asianoi de tuxikos kai trofimos.
act 20:5 outoi de proelqontes emenon hmas en trwadi
act 20:6 hmeis de ecepleusamen meta tas hmeras twn azumwn apo filippwn kai hlqomen pros autous eis thn trwada axri hmerwn pente opou dietriyamen hmeras epta.
act 20:7 en de th mia twn sabbatwn sunhgmenwn hmwn klasai arton o paulos dielegeto autois mellwn ecienai th epaurion pareteinen te ton logon mexri mesonuktiou.
act 20:8 hsan de lampades ikanai en tw uperww ou hmen sunhgmenoi
act 20:9 kaqezomenos de tis neanias onomati eutuxos epi ths quridos kataferomenos upnw baqei dialegomenou tou paulou epi pleion katenexqeis apo tou upnou epesen apo tou tristegou katw kai hrqh nekros.
act 20:10 katabas de o paulos epepesen autw kai sumperilabwn eipen mh qorubeisqe h gar yuxh autou en autw estin.
act 20:11 anabas de kai klasas ton arton kai geusamenos ef ikanon te omilhsas axri aughs outws echlqen.
act 20:12 hgagon de ton paida zwnta kai pareklhqhsan ou metriws.
act 20:13 hmeis de proelqontes epi to ploion anhxqhmen epi thn asson ekeiqen mellontes analambanein ton paulon outws gar diatetagmenos hn mellwn autos pezeuein.
act 20:14 ws de suneballen hmin eis thn asson analabontes auton hlqomen eis mitulhnhn
act 20:15 kakeiqen apopleusantes th epioush kathnthsamen antikrus xiou th de etera parebalomen eis samon [kai meinantes en trwgulliw th] exomenh hlqomen eis milhton
act 20:16 kekrikei gar o paulos parapleusai thn efeson opws mh genhtai autw xronotribhsai en th asia espeuden gar ei dunaton eih autw thn hmeran ths penthkosths genesqai eis ierosoluma.
act 20:17 apo de ths milhtou pemyas eis efeson metekalesato tous presbuterous ths ekklhsias.
act 20:18 ws de paregenonto pros auton eipen autois umeis epistasqe apo prwths hmeras af hs epebhn eis thn asian pws meq umwn ton panta xronon egenomhn
act 20:19 douleuwn tw kuriw meta pashs tapeinofrosunhs kai dakruwn kai peirasmwn twn sumbantwn moi en tais epiboulais twn ioudaiwn
act 20:20 ws ouden upesteilamhn twn sumferontwn tou mh anaggeilai umin kai didacai umas dhmosia kai kat oikous
act 20:21 diamarturomenos ioudaiois te kai ellhsin thn eis qeon metanoian kai pistin eis ton kurion hmwn ihsoun.
act 20:22 kai nun idou dedemenos egw tw pneumati poreuomai eis ierousalhm ta en auth sunanthsonta moi mh eidws
act 20:23 plhn oti to pneuma to agion kata polin diamarturetai moi legon oti desma kai qliyeis me menousin.
act 20:24 all oudenos logou poioumai thn yuxhn timian emautw ws teleiwsai ton dromon mou kai thn diakonian hn elabon para tou kuriou ihsou diamarturasqai to euaggelion ths xaritos tou qeou.
act 20:25 kai nun idou egw oida oti ouketi oyesqe to proswpon mou umeis pantes en ois dihlqon khrusswn thn basileian
act 20:26 dioti marturomai umin en th shmeron hmera oti kaqaros eimi apo tou aimatos pantwn
act 20:27 ou gar upesteilamhn tou mh anaggeilai pasan thn boulhn tou qeou umin.
act 20:28 prosexete eautois kai panti tw poimniw en w umas to pneuma to agion eqeto episkopous poimainein thn ekklhsian tou [kuriou] hn periepoihsato dia tou aimatos tou idiou.
act 20:29 egw oida oti eiseleusontai meta thn aficin mou lukoi bareis eis umas mh feidomenoi tou poimniou
act 20:30 kai ec umwn autwn anasthsontai andres lalountes diestrammena tou apospan tous maqhtas opisw autwn.
act 20:31 dio grhgoreite mnhmoneuontes oti trietian nukta kai hmeran ouk epausamhn meta dakruwn nouqetwn ena ekaston.
act 20:32 kai ta nun paratiqemai umas tw qew kai tw logw ths xaritos autou tw dunamenw oikodomhsai kai dounai thn klhronomian en tois hgiasmenois pasin.
act 20:33 arguriou h xrusiou h imatismou oudenos epequmhsa
act 20:34 autoi ginwskete oti tais xreiais mou kai tois ousin met emou uphrethsan ai xeires autai.
act 20:35 panta upedeica umin oti outws kopiwntas dei antilambanesqai twn asqenountwn mnhmoneuein te twn logwn tou kuriou ihsou oti autos eipen makarion estin mallon didonai h lambanein.
act 20:36 kai tauta eipwn qeis ta gonata autou sun pasin autois proshucato.
act 20:37 ikanos de klauqmos egeneto pantwn kai epipesontes epi ton traxhlon tou paulou katefiloun auton
act 20:38 odunwmenoi malista epi tw logw w eirhkei oti ouketi mellousin to proswpon autou qewrein. proepempon de auton eis to ploion.
act 21:1 ws de egeneto anaxqhnai hmas apospasqentas ap autwn euqudromhsantes hlqomen eis thn kw th de echs eis thn rodon kakeiqen eis patara [kai mura]
act 21:2 kai eurontes ploion diaperwn eis foinikhn epibantes anhxqhmen.
act 21:3 anafanantes de thn kupron kai katalipontes authn euwnumon epleomen eis surian kai kathlqomen eis turon ekeise gar to ploion hn apofortizomenon ton gomon.
act 21:4 aneurontes de tous maqhtas epemeinamen autou hmeras epta oitines tw paulw elegon dia tou pneumatos mh epibainein eis ierosoluma.
act 21:5 ote de egeneto hmas ecartisai tas hmeras ecelqontes eporeuomeqa propempontwn hmas pantwn sun gunaici kai teknois ews ecw ths polews kai qentes ta gonata epi ton aigialon proseucamenoi
act 21:6 aphspasameqa allhlous kai anebhmen eis to ploion ekeinoi de upestreyan eis ta idia.
act 21:7 hmeis de ton ploun dianusantes apo turou kathnthsamen eis ptolemaida kai aspasamenoi tous adelfous emeinamen hmeran mian par autois.
act 21:8 th de epaurion ecelqontes hlqomen eis kaisareian kai eiselqontes eis ton oikon filippou tou euaggelistou ontos ek twn epta emeinamen par autw.
act 21:9 toutw de hsan qugateres tessares parqenoi profhteuousai.
act 21:10 epimenontwn de hmeras pleious kathlqen tis apo ths ioudaias profhths onomati agabos
act 21:11 kai elqwn pros hmas kai aras thn zwnhn tou paulou dhsas eautou tous podas kai tas xeiras eipen tade legei to pneuma to agion ton andra ou estin h zwnh auth outws dhsousin en ierousalhm oi ioudaioi kai paradwsousin eis xeiras eqnwn.
act 21:12 ws de hkousamen tauta parekaloumen hmeis te kai oi entopioi tou mh anabainein auton eis ierousalhm.
act 21:13 tote apekriqh o paulos ti poieite klaiontes kai sunqruptontes mou thn kardian; egw gar ou monon deqhnai alla kai apoqanein eis ierousalhm etoimws exw uper tou onomatos tou kuriou ihsou.
act 21:14 mh peiqomenou de autou hsuxasamen eipontes tou kuriou to qelhma ginesqw.
act 21:15 meta de tas hmeras tautas episkeuasamenoi anebainomen eis ierosoluma
act 21:16 sunhlqon de kai twn maqhtwn apo kaisareias sun hmin agontes par w cenisqwmen mnaswni tini kupriw arxaiw maqhth.
act 21:17 genomenwn de hmwn eis ierosoluma asmenws apedecanto hmas oi adelfoi.
act 21:18 th de epioush eishei o paulos sun hmin pros iakwbon pantes te paregenonto oi presbuteroi.
act 21:19 kai aspasamenos autous echgeito kaq en ekaston wn epoihsen o qeos en tois eqnesin dia ths diakonias autou.
act 21:20 oi de akousantes edocazon ton qeon eipon te autw qewreis adelfe posai muriades eisin en tois ioudaiois twn pepisteukotwn kai pantes zhlwtai tou nomou uparxousin
act 21:21 kathxhqhsan de peri sou oti apostasian didaskeis apo mwusews tous kata ta eqnh pantas ioudaious legwn mh peritemnein autous ta tekna mhde tois eqesin peripatein.
act 21:22 ti oun estin; pantws akousontai oti elhluqas.
act 21:23 touto oun poihson o soi legomen eisin hmin andres tessares euxhn exontes ef eautwn.
act 21:24 toutous paralabwn agnisqhti sun autois kai dapanhson ep autois ina curhsontai thn kefalhn kai gnwsontai pantes oti wn kathxhntai peri sou ouden estin alla stoixeis kai autos fulasswn ton nomon.
act 21:25 peri de twn pepisteukotwn eqnwn [ouden ecousin legein pros se hmais gar apesteilamen] krinantes fulassesqai autous to te eidwloquton kai aima kai pnikton kai porneian.
act 21:26 tote o paulos paralabwn tous andras th exomenh hmera sun autois agnisqeis eishei eis to ieron diaggellwn thn ekplhrwsin twn hmerwn tou agnismou ews ou proshnexqh uper enos ekastou autwn h prosfora.
act 21:27 ws de emellon ai epta hmerai sunteleisqai oi apo ths asias ioudaioi qeasamenoi auton en tw ierw sunexeon panta ton oxlon kai epebalon ep auton tas xeiras
act 21:28 krazontes andres israhlitai bohqeite outos estin o anqrwpos o kata tou laou kai tou nomou kai tou topou toutou pantas pantaxh didaskwn eti te kai ellhnas eishgagen eis to ieron kai kekoinwken ton agion topon touton.
act 21:29 hsan gar proewrakotes trofimon ton efesion en th polei sun autw on enomizon oti eis to ieron eishgagen o paulos.
act 21:30 ekinhqh te h polis olh kai egeneto sundromh tou laou kai epilabomenoi tou paulou eilkon auton ecw tou ierou kai euqews ekleisqhsan ai qurai.
act 21:31 zhtountwn te auton apokteinai anebh fasis tw xiliarxw ths speirhs oti olh sugxunnetai ierousalhm
act 21:32 os ecauths paralabwn stratiwtas kai ekatontarxas katedramen ep autous oi de idontes ton xiliarxon kai tous stratiwtas epausanto tuptontes ton paulon.
act 21:33 tote eggisas o xiliarxos epelabeto autou kai ekeleusen deqhnai alusesi dusi kai epunqaneto tis eih kai ti estin pepoihkws.
act 21:34 alloi de allo ti epefwnoun en tw oxlw mh dunamenou de autou gnwnai to asfales dia ton qorubon ekeleusen agesqai auton eis thn parembolhn.
act 21:35 ote de egeneto epi tous anabaqmous sunebh bastazesqai auton upo twn stratiwtwn dia thn bian tou oxlou
act 21:36 hkolouqei gar to plhqos tou laou krazontes aire auton.
act 21:37 mellwn te eisagesqai eis thn parembolhn o paulos legei tw xiliarxw ei ecestin moi eipein ti pros se; o de efh ellhnisti ginwskeis;
act 21:38 ouk ara su ei o aiguptios o pro toutwn twn hmerwn anastatwsas kai ecagagwn eis thn erhmon tous tetrakisxilious andras twn sikariwn;
act 21:39 eipen de o paulos egw anqrwpos men eimi ioudaios tarseus ths kilikias ouk ashmou polews poliths deomai de sou epitreyon moi lalhsai pros ton laon.
act 21:40 epitreyantos de autou o paulos estws epi twn anabaqmwn kateseisen th xeiri tw law pollhs de sighs genomenhs prosefwnhsen th ebraidi dialektw legwn
act 22:1 andres adelfoi kai pateres akousate mou ths pros umas nuni apologias 
act 22:2 akousantes de oti th ebraidi dialektw prosefwnei autois mallon paresxon hsuxian. kai fhsin 
act 22:3 egw eimi anhr ioudaios gegennhmenos en tarsw ths kilikias anateqrammenos de en th polei tauth para tous podas gamalihl pepaideumenos kata akribeian tou patrwou nomou zhlwths uparxwn tou qeou kaqws pantes umeis este shmeron
act 22:4 os tauthn thn odon ediwca axri qanatou desmeuwn kai paradidous eis fulakas andras te kai gunaikas
act 22:5 ws kai o arxiereus marturei moi kai pan to presbuterion par wn kai epistolas decamenos pros tous adelfous eis damaskon eporeuomhn acwn kai tous ekeise ontas dedemenous eis ierousalhm ina timwrhqwsin.
act 22:6 egeneto de moi poreuomenw kai eggizonti th damaskw peri meshmbrian ecaifnhs ek tou ouranou periastrayai fws ikanon peri eme
act 22:7 epesa te eis to edafos kai hkousa fwnhs legoushs moi saoul saoul ti me diwkeis;
act 22:8 egw de apekriqhn tis ei kurie; eipen te pros me egw eimi ihsous o nazwraios on su diwkeis.
act 22:9 oi de sun emoi ontes to men fws eqeasanto [kai emfoboi egenonto] thn de fwnhn ouk hkousan tou lalountos moi.
act 22:10 eipon de ti poihsw kurie; o de kurios eipen pros me anastas poreuou eis damaskon kakei soi lalhqhsetai peri pantwn wn tetaktai soi poihsai.
act 22:11 ws de ouk eneblepon apo ths dochs tou fwtos ekeinou xeiragwgoumenos upo twn sunontwn moi hlqon eis damaskon.
act 22:12 ananias de tis anhr eulabhs kata ton nomon marturoumenos upo pantwn twn katoikountwn [en damaskw] ioudaiwn
act 22:13 elqwn pros me kai epistas eipen moi saoul adelfe anableyon kagw auth th wra anebleya eis auton.
act 22:14 o de eipen o qeos twn paterwn hmwn proexeirisato se gnwnai to qelhma autou kai idein ton dikaion kai akousai fwnhn ek tou stomatos autou
act 22:15 oti esh martus autw pros pantas anqrwpous wn ewrakas kai hkousas.
act 22:16 kai nun ti melleis; anastas baptisai kai apolousai tas amartias sou epikalesamenos to onoma autou.
act 22:17 egeneto de moi upostreyanti eis ierousalhm kai proseuxomenou mou en tw ierw genesqai me en ekstasei
act 22:18 kai idein auton legonta moi speuson kai ecelqe en taxei ec ierousalhm dioti ou paradecontai sou marturian peri emou.
act 22:19 kagw eipon kurie autoi epistantai oti egw hmhn fulakizwn kai derwn kata tas sunagwgas tous pisteuontas epi se
act 22:20 kai ote ecexunneto to aima stefanou tou marturos sou kai autos hmhn efestws kai suneudokwn kai fulasswn ta imatia twn anairountwn auton.
act 22:21 kai eipen pros me poreuou oti egw eis eqnh makran ecapostelw se.
act 22:22 hkouon de autou axri toutou tou logou kai ephran thn fwnhn autwn legontes aire apo ths ghs ton toiouton ou gar kaqhken auton zhn.
act 22:23 kraugazontwn te autwn kai riptountwn ta imatia kai koniorton ballontwn eis ton aera
act 22:24 ekeleusen o xiliarxos eisagesqai auton eis thn parembolhn eipas masticin anetazesqai auton ina epignw di hn aitian outws epefwnoun autw.
act 22:25 ws de proeteinan auton tois imasin eipen pros ton estwta ekatontarxon o paulos ei anqrwpon rwmaion kai akatakriton ecestin umin mastizein;
act 22:26 akousas de o ekatontarxhs proselqwn tw xiliarxw aphggeilen legwn [ora] ti melleis poiein; o gar anqrwpos outos rwmaios estin.
act 22:27 proselqwn de o xiliarxos eipen autw lege moi su rwmaios ei; o de efh nai.
act 22:28 apekriqh de o xiliarxos egw pollou kefalaiou thn politeian tauthn ekthsamhn. o de paulos efh egw de kai gegennhmai.
act 22:29 euqews oun apesthsan ap autou oi mellontes auton anetazein kai o xiliarxos de efobhqh epignous oti rwmaios estin kai oti auton hn dedekws.
act 22:30 th de epaurion boulomenos gnwnai to asfales to ti kathgoreitai upo twn ioudaiwn elusen auton kai ekeleusen sunelqein tous arxiereis kai pan to sunedrion kai katagagwn ton paulon esthsen eis autous.
act 23:1 atenisas de o paulos tw sunedriw eipen andres adelfoi egw pash suneidhsei agaqh pepoliteumai tw qew axri tauths ths hmeras.
act 23:2 o de arxiereus ananias epetacen tois parestwsin autw tuptein autou to stoma.
act 23:3 tote o paulos pros auton eipen tuptein se mellei o qeos toixe kekoniamene kai su kaqh krinwn me kata ton nomon kai paranomwn keleueis me tuptesqai;
act 23:4 oi de parestwtes eipan ton arxierea tou qeou loidoreis;
act 23:5 efh te o paulos ouk hdein adelfoi oti estin arxiereus gegraptai gar oti arxonta tou laou sou ouk ereis kakws.
act 23:6 gnous de o paulos oti to en meros estin saddoukaiwn to de eteron farisaiwn ekrazen en tw sunedriw andres adelfoi egw farisaios eimi uios farisaiwn peri elpidos kai anastasews nekrwn egw krinomai.
act 23:7 touto de autou eipontos egeneto stasis twn farisaiwn kai saddoukaiwn kai esxisqh to plhqos.
act 23:8 saddoukaioi men gar legousin mh einai anastasin mhte aggelon mhte pneuma farisaioi de omologousin ta amfotera.
act 23:9 egeneto de kraugh megalh kai anastantes tines twn grammatewn tou merous twn farisaiwn diemaxonto legontes ouden kakon euriskomen en tw anqrwpw toutw ei de pneuma elalhsen autw h aggelos 
act 23:10 pollhs de ginomenhs stasews fobhqeis o xiliarxos mh diaspasqh o paulos up autwn ekeleusen to strateuma kataban arpasai auton ek mesou autwn agein te eis thn parembolhn.
act 23:11 th de epioush nukti epistas autw o kurios eipen qarsei ws gar diemarturw ta peri emou eis ierousalhm outw se dei kai eis rwmhn marturhsai.
act 23:12 genomenhs de hmeras poihsantes [tines twn ioudaiwn sustrofhn] aneqematisan eautous legontes mhte fagein mhte piein ews ou apokteinwsin ton paulon.
act 23:13 hsan de pleious tesserakonta oi tauthn thn sunwmosian poihsamenoi
act 23:14 oitines proselqontes tois arxiereusin kai tois presbuterois eipan anaqemati aneqematisamen eautous mhdenos geusasqai ews ou apokteinwmen ton paulon.
act 23:15 nun oun umeis emfanisate tw xiliarxw sun tw sunedriw opws katagagh auton eis umas ws mellontas diaginwskein akribesteron ta peri autou hmeis de pro tou eggisai auton etoimoi esmen tou anelein auton.
act 23:16 akousas de o uios ths adelfhs paulou thn enedran paragenomenos kai eiselqwn eis thn parembolhn aphggeilen tw paulw.
act 23:17 proskalesamenos de o paulos ena twn ekatontarxwn efh ton neanian touton apagage pros ton xiliarxon exei gar apaggeilai ti autw.
act 23:18 o men oun paralabwn auton hgagen pros ton xiliarxon kai fhsin o desmios paulos proskalesamenos me hrwthsen touton ton neaniskon agagein pros se exonta ti lalhsai soi.
act 23:19 epilabomenos de ths xeiros autou o xiliarxos kai anaxwrhsas kat idian epunqaneto ti estin o exeis apaggeilai moi;
act 23:20 eipen de oti oi ioudaioi suneqento tou erwthsai se opws aurion ton paulon katagaghs eis to sunedrion ws mellon ti akribesteron punqanesqai peri autou.

act 27:32 tote apekoyan oi stratiwtai ta sxoinia ths skafhs kai eiasan authn ekpesein.

act 28:1 kai diaswqentes tote epegnwmen oti melith h nhsos kaleitai.
act 28:2 oi te barbaroi pareixon ou thn tuxousan filanqrwpian hmin ayantes gar puran proselabonto pantas hmas dia ton ueton ton efestwta kai dia to yuxos.
act 28:3 sustreyantos de tou paulou fruganwn ti plhqos kai epiqentos epi thn puran exidna apo ths qermhs ecelqousa kaqhyen ths xeiros autou.
act 28:4 ws de eidon oi barbaroi kremamenon to qhrion ek ths xeiros autou pros allhlous elegon pantws foneus estin o anqrwpos outos on diaswqenta ek ths qalasshs h dikh zhn ouk eiasen.
act 28:5 o men oun apotinacas to qhrion eis to pur epaqen ouden kakon
act 28:6 oi de prosedokwn auton mellein pimprasqai h katapiptein afnw nekron. epi polu de autwn prosdokwntwn kai qewrountwn mhden atopon eis auton ginomenon metabalomenoi elegon auton einai qeon.
act 28:7 en de tois peri ton topon ekeinon uphrxen xwria tw prwtw ths nhsou onomati popliw os anadecamenos hmas treis hmeras filofronws ecenisen.
act 28:8 egeneto de ton patera tou popliou puretois kai dusenteriw sunexomenon katakeisqai pros on o paulos eiselqwn kai proseucamenos epiqeis tas xeiras autw iasato auton.
act 28:9 toutou de genomenou kai oi loipoi oi en th nhsw exontes asqeneias proshrxonto kai eqerapeuonto
act 28:10 oi kai pollais timais etimhsan hmas kai anagomenois epeqento ta pros tas xreias.
act 28:11 meta de treis mhnas anhxqhmen en ploiw parakexeimakoti en th nhsw alecandrinw parashmw dioskourois.

1co 4:5 wste mh pro kairou ti krinete ews an elqh o kurios os kai fwtisei ta krupta tou skotous kai fanerwsei tas boulas twn kardiwn kai tote o epainos genhsetai ekastw apo tou qeou.
1co 4:6 tauta de adelfoi metesxhmatisa eis emauton kai apollwn di umas ina en hmin maqhte to mh uper a gegraptai ina mh eis uper tou enos fusiousqe kata tou eterou.
1co 4:7 tis gar se diakrinei; ti de exeis o ouk elabes; ei de kai elabes ti kauxasai ws mh labwn;
1co 4:8 hdh kekoresmenoi este hdh eplouthsate xwris hmwn ebasileusate kai ofelon ge ebasileusate ina kai hmeis umin sumbasileuswmen.

1co 11:2 epainw de umas oti panta mou memnhsqe kai kaqws paredwka umin tas paradoseis katexete.
1co 11:3 qelw de umas eidenai oti pantos andros h kefalh o xristos estin kefalh de gunaikos o anhr kefalh de tou xristou o qeos.
1co 11:4 pas anhr proseuxomenos h profhteuwn kata kefalhs exwn kataisxunei thn kefalhn autou
1co 11:5 pasa de gunh proseuxomenh h profhteuousa akatakaluptw th kefalh kataisxunei thn kefalhn auths en gar estin kai to auto th ecurhmenh.
1co 11:6 ei gar ou katakaluptetai gunh kai keirasqw ei de aisxron gunaiki to keirasqai h curasqai katakaluptesqw.
1co 11:7 anhr men gar ouk ofeilei katakaluptesqai thn kefalhn eikwn kai doca qeou uparxwn h gunh de doca andros estin.
1co 11:8 ou gar estin anhr ek gunaikos alla gunh ec andros
1co 11:9 kai gar ouk ektisqh anhr dia thn gunaika alla gunh dia ton andra.

1co 11:25 wsautws kai to pothrion meta to deipnhsai legwn touto to pothrion h kainh diaqhkh estin en tw emw aimati touto poieite osakis ean pinhte eis thn emhn anamnhsin.

1co 11:27 wste os an esqih ton arton h pinh to pothrion tou kuriou anaciws enoxos estai tou swmatos kai tou aimatos tou kuriou.

1co 12:1 peri de twn pneumatikwn adelfoi ou qelw umas agnoein.

1co 16:23 h xaris tou kuriou ihsou meq umwn.
1co 16:24 h agaph mou meta pantwn umwn en xristw ihsou.
2co 1:1 paulos apostolos xristou ihsou dia qelhmatos qeou kai timoqeos o adelfos th ekklhsia tou qeou th oush en korinqw sun tois agiois pasin tois ousin en olh th axaia
2co 1:2 xaris umin kai eirhnh apo qeou patros hmwn kai kuriou ihsou xristou.
2co 1:3 euloghtos o qeos kai pathr tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou o pathr twn oiktirmwn kai qeos pashs paraklhsews
2co 1:4 o parakalwn hmas epi pash th qliyei hmwn eis to dunasqai hmas parakalein tous en pash qliyei dia ths paraklhsews hs parakaloumeqa autoi upo tou qeou
2co 1:5 oti kaqws perisseuei ta paqhmata tou xristou eis hmas outws dia tou xristou perisseuei kai h paraklhsis hmwn.
2co 1:6 eite de qlibomeqa uper ths umwn paraklhsews kai swthrias eite parakaloumeqa uper ths umwn paraklhsews ths energoumenhs en upomonh twn autwn paqhmatwn wn kai hmeis pasxomen.
2co 1:7 kai h elpis hmwn bebaia uper umwn eidotes oti ws koinwnoi este twn paqhmatwn outws kai ths paraklhsews.
2co 1:8 ou gar qelomen umas agnoein adelfoi uper ths qliyews hmwn ths genomenhs en th asia oti kaq uperbolhn uper dunamin ebarhqhmen wste ecaporhqhnai hmas kai tou zhn
2co 1:9 alla autoi en eautois to apokrima tou qanatou esxhkamen ina mh pepoiqotes wmen ef eautois all epi tw qew tw egeironti tous nekrous
2co 1:10 os ek thlikoutou qanatou errusato hmas kai rusetai eis on hlpikamen oti kai eti rusetai
2co 1:11 sunupourgountwn kai umwn uper hmwn th dehsei ina ek pollwn proswpwn to eis hmas xarisma dia pollwn euxaristhqh uper hmwn.
2co 1:12 h gar kauxhsis hmwn auth estin to marturion ths suneidhsews hmwn oti en [agiothti] kai eilikrineia tou qeou kai ouk en sofia sarkikh all en xariti qeou anestrafhmen en tw kosmw perissoterws de pros umas.
2co 1:13 ou gar alla grafomen umin all h a anaginwskete h kai epiginwskete elpizw de oti ews telous epignwsesqe
2co 1:14 kaqws kai epegnwte hmas apo merous oti kauxhma umwn esmen kaqaper kai umeis hmwn en th hmera tou kuriou hmwn ihsou.
2co 1:15 kai tauth th pepoiqhsei eboulomhn proteron pros umas elqein ina deuteran xarin sxhte
2co 1:16 kai di umwn dielqein eis makedonian kai palin apo makedonias elqein pros umas kai uf umwn propemfqhnai eis thn ioudaian.
2co 1:17 touto oun boulomenos mhti ara th elafria exrhsamhn; h a bouleuomai kata sarka bouleuomai ina h par emoi to nai nai kai to ou ou;
2co 1:18 pistos de o qeos oti o logos hmwn o pros umas ouk estin nai kai ou.
2co 1:19 o tou qeou gar uios ihsous xristos o en umin di hmwn khruxqeis di emou kai silouanou kai timoqeou ouk egeneto nai kai ou alla nai en autw gegonen.
2co 1:20 osai gar epaggeliai qeou en autw to nai dio kai di autou to amhn tw qew pros docan di hmwn.
2co 1:21 o de bebaiwn hmas sun umin eis xriston kai xrisas hmas qeos
2co 1:22 o kai sfragisamenos hmas kai dous ton arrabwna tou pneumatos en tais kardiais hmwn.
2co 1:23 egw de martura ton qeon epikaloumai epi thn emhn yuxhn oti feidomenos umwn ouketi hlqon eis korinqon.
2co 1:24 oux oti kurieuomen umwn ths pistews alla sunergoi esmen ths xaras umwn th gar pistei esthkate.
2co 2:1 ekrina gar emautw touto to mh palin en luph pros umas elqein
2co 2:2 ei gar egw lupw umas kai tis o eufrainwn me ei mh o lupoumenos ec emou;
2co 2:3 kai egraya touto auto ina mh elqwn luphn sxw af wn edei me xairein pepoiqws epi pantas umas oti h emh xara pantwn umwn estin.
2co 2:4 ek gar pollhs qliyews kai sunoxhs kardias egraya umin dia pollwn dakruwn oux ina luphqhte alla thn agaphn ina gnwte hn exw perissoterws eis umas.
2co 2:5 ei de tis leluphken ouk eme leluphken alla apo merous ina mh epibarw pantas umas.
2co 2:6 ikanon tw toioutw h epitimia auth h upo twn pleionwn
2co 2:7 wste tounantion mallon umas xarisasqai kai parakalesai mh pws th perissotera luph katapoqh o toioutos.
2co 2:8 dio parakalw umas kurwsai eis auton agaphn
2co 2:9 eis touto gar kai egraya ina gnw thn dokimhn umwn ei eis panta uphkooi este.
2co 2:10 w de ti xarizesqe kagw kai gar egw o kexarismai ei ti kexarismai di umas en proswpw xristou
2co 2:11 ina mh pleonekthqwmen upo tou satana ou gar autou ta nohmata agnooumen.
2co 2:12 elqwn de eis thn trwada eis to euaggelion tou xristou kai quras moi anewgmenhs en kuriw
2co 2:13 ouk esxhka anesin tw pneumati mou tw mh eurein me titon ton adelfon mou alla apotacamenos autois echlqon eis makedonian.
2co 2:14 tw de qew xaris tw pantote qriambeuonti hmas en tw xristw kai thn osmhn ths gnwsews autou fanerounti di hmwn en panti topw
2co 2:15 oti xristou euwdia esmen tw qew en tois swzomenois kai en tois apollumenois
2co 2:16 ois men osmh ek qanatou eis qanaton ois de osmh ek zwhs eis zwhn. kai pros tauta tis ikanos;
2co 2:17 ou gar esmen ws oi polloi kaphleuontes ton logon tou qeou all ws ec eilikrineias all ws ek qeou katenanti qeou en xristw laloumen.
2co 3:1 arxomeqa palin eautous sunistanein; h mh xrhzomen ws tines sustatikwn epistolwn pros umas h ec umwn;
2co 3:2 h epistolh hmwn umeis este eggegrammenh en tais kardiais hmwn ginwskomenh kai anaginwskomenh upo pantwn anqrwpwn
2co 3:3 faneroumenoi oti este epistolh xristou diakonhqeisa uf hmwn eggegrammenh ou melani alla pneumati qeou zwntos ouk en placin liqinais all en placin [kardias] sarkinais.
2co 3:4 pepoiqhsin de toiauthn exomen dia tou xristou pros ton qeon.
2co 3:5 oux oti af eautwn ikanoi esmen logisasqai ti ws ec eautwn all h ikanoths hmwn ek tou qeou
2co 3:6 os kai ikanwsen hmas diakonous kainhs diaqhkhs ou grammatos alla pneumatos to gar gramma apoktennei to de pneuma zwopoiei.
2co 3:7 ei de h diakonia tou qanatou en grammasin entetupwmenh liqois egenhqh en doch wste mh dunasqai atenisai tous uious israhl eis to proswpon mwusews dia thn docan tou proswpou autou thn katargoumenhn
2co 3:8 pws ouxi mallon h diakonia tou pneumatos estai en doch;
2co 3:9 ei gar th diakonia ths katakrisews doca pollw mallon perisseuei h diakonia ths dikaiosunhs doch.
2co 3:10 kai gar ou dedocastai to dedocasmenon en toutw tw merei eineken ths uperballoushs dochs
2co 3:11 ei gar to katargoumenon dia dochs pollw mallon to menon en doch.
2co 3:12 exontes oun toiauthn elpida pollh parrhsia xrwmeqa
2co 3:13 kai ou kaqaper mwushs etiqei kalumma epi to proswpon autou pros to mh atenisai tous uious israhl eis to telos tou katargoumenou.
2co 3:14 alla epwrwqh ta nohmata autwn. axri gar ths shmeron hmeras to auto kalumma epi th anagnwsei ths palaias diaqhkhs menei mh anakaluptomenon oti en xristw katargeitai
2co 3:15 all ews shmeron hnika an anaginwskhtai mwushs kalumma epi thn kardian autwn keitai
2co 3:16 hnika de ean epistreyh pros kurion periaireitai to kalumma.
2co 3:17 o de kurios to pneuma estin ou de to pneuma kuriou eleuqeria.
2co 3:18 hmeis de pantes anakekalummenw proswpw thn docan kuriou katoptrizomenoi thn authn eikona metamorfoumeqa apo dochs eis docan kaqaper apo kuriou pneumatos.
2co 4:1 dia touto exontes thn diakonian tauthn kaqws hlehqhmen ouk egkakoumen
2co 4:2 alla apeipameqa ta krupta ths aisxunhs mh peripatountes en panourgia mhde dolountes ton logon tou qeou alla th fanerwsei ths alhqeias sunistanontes eautous pros pasan suneidhsin anqrwpwn enwpion tou qeou.
2co 4:3 ei de kai estin kekalummenon to euaggelion hmwn en tois apollumenois estin kekalummenon
2co 4:4 en ois o qeos tou aiwnos toutou etuflwsen ta nohmata twn apistwn eis to mh augasai ton fwtismon tou euaggeliou ths dochs tou xristou os estin eikwn tou qeou.
2co 4:5 ou gar eautous khrussomen alla ihsoun xriston kurion eautous de doulous umwn dia [ihsou].
2co 4:6 oti o qeos o eipwn ek skotous fws lamyei os elamyen en tais kardiais hmwn pros fwtismon ths gnwsews ths dochs tou qeou en proswpw ihsou xristou.
2co 4:7 exomen de ton qhsauron touton en ostrakinois skeuesin ina h uperbolh ths dunamews h tou qeou kai mh ec hmwn
2co 4:8 en panti qlibomenoi all ou stenoxwroumenoi aporoumenoi all ouk ecaporoumenoi
2co 4:9 diwkomenoi all ouk egkataleipomenoi kataballomenoi all ouk apollumenoi
2co 4:10 pantote thn nekrwsin tou ihsou en tw swmati periferontes ina kai h zwh tou ihsou en tw swmati hmwn fanerwqh.
2co 4:11 aei gar hmeis oi zwntes eis qanaton paradidomeqa dia ihsoun ina kai h zwh tou ihsou fanerwqh en th qnhth sarki hmwn.
2co 4:12 wste o qanatos en hmin energeitai h de zwh en umin.
2co 4:13 exontes de to auto pneuma ths pistews kata to gegrammenon episteusa dio elalhsa kai hmeis pisteuomen dio kai laloumen
2co 4:14 eidotes oti o egeiras ton [--] ihsoun kai hmas sun ihsou egerei kai parasthsei sun umin.
2co 4:15 ta gar panta di umas ina h xaris pleonasasa dia twn pleionwn thn euxaristian perisseush eis thn docan tou qeou.
2co 4:16 dio ouk egkakoumen all ei kai o ecw hmwn anqrwpos diafqeiretai all o esw hmwn anakainoutai hmera kai hmera.
2co 4:17 to gar parautika elafron ths qliyews hmwn kaq uperbolhn eis uperbolhn aiwnion baros dochs katergazetai hmin
2co 4:18 mh skopountwn hmwn ta blepomena alla ta mh blepomena ta gar blepomena proskaira ta de mh blepomena aiwnia.
2co 5:1 oidamen gar oti ean h epigeios hmwn oikia tou skhnous kataluqh oikodomhn ek qeou exomen oikian axeiropoihton aiwnion en tois ouranois.
2co 5:2 kai gar en toutw stenazomen to oikhthrion hmwn to ec ouranou ependusasqai epipoqountes
2co 5:3 ei ge kai [endusamenoi] ou gumnoi eureqhsomeqa.
2co 5:4 kai gar oi ontes en tw skhnei stenazomen baroumenoi ef w ou qelomen ekdusasqai all ependusasqai ina katapoqh to qnhton upo ths zwhs.
2co 5:5 o de katergasamenos hmas eis auto touto qeos o dous hmin ton arrabwna tou pneumatos.
2co 5:6 qarrountes oun pantote kai eidotes oti endhmountes en tw swmati ekdhmoumen apo tou kuriou
2co 5:7 dia pistews gar peripatoumen ou dia eidous 
2co 5:8 qarroumen de kai eudokoumen mallon ekdhmhsai ek tou swmatos kai endhmhsai pros ton kurion.
2co 5:9 dio kai filotimoumeqa eite endhmountes eite ekdhmountes euarestoi autw einai.
2co 5:10 tous gar pantas hmas fanerwqhnai dei emprosqen tou bhmatos tou xristou ina komishtai ekastos ta dia tou swmatos pros a epracen eite agaqon eite faulon.
2co 5:11 eidotes oun ton fobon tou kuriou anqrwpous peiqomen qew de pefanerwmeqa elpizw de kai en tais suneidhsesin umwn pefanerwsqai.
2co 5:12 ou palin eautous sunistanomen umin alla aformhn didontes umin kauxhmatos uper hmwn ina exhte pros tous en proswpw kauxwmenous kai mh en kardia.
2co 5:13 eite gar ecesthmen qew eite swfronoumen umin.
2co 5:14 h gar agaph tou xristou sunexei hmas krinantas touto oti eis uper pantwn apeqanen ara oi pantes apeqanon
2co 5:15 kai uper pantwn apeqanen ina oi zwntes mhketi eautois zwsin alla tw uper autwn apoqanonti kai egerqenti.
2co 5:16 wste hmeis apo tou nun oudena oidamen kata sarka ei kai egnwkamen kata sarka xriston alla nun ouketi ginwskomen.
2co 5:17 wste ei tis en xristw kainh ktisis ta arxaia parhlqen idou gegonen kaina
2co 5:18 ta de panta ek tou qeou tou katallacantos hmas eautw dia xristou kai dontos hmin thn diakonian ths katallaghs
2co 5:19 ws oti qeos hn en xristw kosmon katallasswn eautw mh logizomenos autois ta paraptwmata autwn kai qemenos en hmin ton logon ths katallaghs.
2co 5:20 uper xristou oun presbeuomen ws tou qeou parakalountos di hmwn deomeqa uper xristou katallaghte tw qew.
2co 5:21 ton mh gnonta amartian uper hmwn amartian epoihsen ina hmeis genwmeqa dikaiosunh qeou en autw.
2co 6:1 sunergountes de kai parakaloumen mh eis kenon thn xarin tou qeou decasqai umas 
2co 6:2 legei gar kairw dektw ephkousa sou kai en hmera swthrias ebohqhsa soi idou nun kairos euprosdektos idou nun hmera swthrias 
2co 6:3 mhdemian en mhdeni didontes proskophn ina mh mwmhqh h diakonia
2co 6:4 all en panti sunistantes eautous ws qeou diakonoi en upomonh pollh en qliyesin en anagkais en stenoxwriais
2co 6:5 en plhgais en fulakais en akatastasiais en kopois en agrupniais en nhsteiais
2co 6:6 en agnothti en gnwsei en makroqumia en xrhstothti en pneumati agiw en agaph anupokritw
2co 6:7 en logw alhqeias en dunamei qeou dia twn oplwn ths dikaiosunhs twn deciwn kai aristerwn
2co 6:8 dia dochs kai atimias dia dusfhmias kai eufhmias ws planoi kai alhqeis
2co 6:9 ws agnooumenoi kai epiginwskomenoi ws apoqnhskontes kai idou zwmen ws paideuomenoi kai mh qanatoumenoi
2co 6:10 ws lupoumenoi aei de xairontes ws ptwxoi pollous de ploutizontes ws mhden exontes kai panta katexontes.
2co 6:11 to stoma hmwn anewgen pros umas korinqioi h kardia hmwn peplatuntai
2co 6:12 ou stenoxwreisqe en hmin stenoxwreisqe de en tois splagxnois umwn
2co 6:13 thn de authn antimisqian ws teknois legw platunqhte kai umeis.
2co 6:14 mh ginesqe eterozugountes apistois tis gar metoxh dikaiosunh kai anomia; h tis koinwnia fwti pros skotos;
2co 6:15 tis de sumfwnhsis xristou pros beliar h tis meris pistw meta apistou;
2co 6:16 tis de sugkataqesis naw qeou meta eidwlwn; hmeis gar naos qeou esmen zwntos kaqws eipen o qeos oti enoikhsw en autois kai emperipathsw kai esomai autwn qeos kai autoi esontai mou laos.
2co 6:17 dio ecelqate ek mesou autwn kai aforisqhte legei kurios kai akaqartou mh aptesqe kagw eisdecomai umas
2co 6:18 kai esomai umin eis patera kai umeis esesqe moi eis uious kai qugateras legei kurios pantokratwr.
2co 7:1 tautas oun exontes tas epaggelias agaphtoi kaqariswmen eautous apo pantos molusmou sarkos kai pneumatos epitelountes agiwsunhn en fobw qeou.
2co 7:2 xwrhsate hmas oudena hdikhsamen oudena efqeiramen oudena epleonekthsamen.
2co 7:3 pros katakrisin ou legw proeirhka gar oti en tais kardiais hmwn este eis to sunapoqanein kai suzhn.
2co 7:4 pollh moi parrhsia pros umas pollh moi kauxhsis uper umwn peplhrwmai th paraklhsei uperperisseuomai th xara epi pash th qliyei hmwn.
2co 7:5 kai gar elqontwn hmwn eis makedonian oudemian esxhken anesin h sarc hmwn all en panti qlibomenoi ecwqen maxai eswqen foboi.
2co 7:6 all o parakalwn tous tapeinous parekalesen hmas o qeos en th parousia titou
2co 7:7 ou monon de en th parousia autou alla kai en th paraklhsei h pareklhqh ef umin anaggellwn hmin thn umwn epipoqhsin ton umwn odurmon ton umwn zhlon uper emou wste me mallon xarhnai.
2co 7:8 oti ei kai eluphsa umas en th epistolh ou metamelomai ei kai metemelomhn blepw gar oti h epistolh ekeinh ei kai pros wran eluphsen umas
2co 7:9 nun xairw oux oti eluphqhte all oti eluphqhte eis metanoian eluphqhte gar kata qeon ina en mhdeni zhmiwqhte ec hmwn.
2co 7:10 h gar kata qeon luph metanoian eis swthrian ametamelhton ergazetai h de tou kosmou luph qanaton katergazetai.
2co 7:11 idou gar auto touto to kata qeon luphqhnai poshn kateirgasato umin spoudhn alla apologian alla aganakthsin alla fobon alla epipoqhsin alla zhlon alla ekdikhsin en panti sunesthsate eautous agnous einai tw pragmati.
2co 7:12 ara ei kai egraya umin oux eneken tou adikhsantos oude eneken tou adikhqentos all eneken tou fanerwqhnai thn spoudhn umwn thn uper hmwn pros umas enwpion tou qeou.
2co 7:13 dia touto parakeklhmeqa. epi de th paraklhsei hmwn perissoterws mallon exarhmen epi th xara titou oti anapepautai to pneuma autou apo pantwn umwn
2co 7:14 oti ei ti autw uper umwn kekauxhmai ou kathsxunqhn all ws panta en alhqeia elalhsamen umin outws kai h kauxhsis hmwn h epi titou alhqeia egenhqh.
2co 7:15 kai ta splagxna autou perissoterws eis umas estin anamimnhskomenou thn pantwn umwn upakohn ws meta fobou kai tromou edecasqe auton.
2co 7:16 xairw oti en panti qarrw en umin.
2co 8:1 gnwrizomen de umin adelfoi thn xarin tou qeou thn dedomenhn en tais ekklhsiais ths makedonias
2co 8:2 oti en pollh dokimh qliyews h perisseia ths xaras autwn kai h kata baqous ptwxeia autwn eperisseusen eis to ploutos ths aplothtos autwn
2co 8:3 oti kata dunamin marturw kai para dunamin auqairetoi
2co 8:4 meta pollhs paraklhsews deomenoi hmwn thn xarin kai thn koinwnian ths diakonias ths eis tous agious 
2co 8:5 kai ou kaqws hlpisamen all eautous edwkan prwton tw kuriw kai hmin dia qelhmatos qeou
2co 8:6 eis to parakalesai hmas titon ina kaqws proenhrcato outws kai epitelesh eis umas kai thn xarin tauthn.
2co 8:7 all wsper en panti perisseuete pistei kai logw kai gnwsei kai pash spoudh kai th ec hmwn en umin agaph ina kai en tauth th xariti perisseuhte.
2co 8:8 ou kat epitaghn legw alla dia ths eterwn spoudhs kai to ths umeteras agaphs gnhsion dokimazwn
2co 8:9 ginwskete gar thn xarin tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou oti di umas eptwxeusen plousios wn ina umeis th ekeinou ptwxeia plouthshte.
2co 8:10 kai gnwmhn en toutw didwmi touto gar umin sumferei oitines ou monon to poihsai alla kai to qelein proenhrcasqe apo perusi
2co 8:11 nuni de kai to poihsai epitelesate opws kaqaper h proqumia tou qelein outws kai to epitelesai ek tou exein.
2co 8:12 ei gar h proqumia prokeitai kaqo ean exh euprosdektos ou kaqo ouk exei.
2co 8:13 ou gar ina allois anesis umin qliyis all ec isothtos
2co 8:14 en tw nun kairw to umwn perisseuma eis to ekeinwn usterhma ina kai to ekeinwn perisseuma genhtai eis to umwn usterhma opws genhtai isoths
2co 8:15 kaqws gegraptai o to polu ouk epleonasen kai o to oligon ouk hlattonhsen.
2co 8:16 xaris de tw qew tw donti thn authn spoudhn uper umwn en th kardia titou
2co 8:17 oti thn men paraklhsin edecato spoudaioteros de uparxwn auqairetos echlqen pros umas.
2co 8:18 sunepemyamen de met autou ton adelfon ou o epainos en tw euaggeliw dia paswn twn ekklhsiwn
2co 8:19 ou monon de alla kai xeirotonhqeis upo twn ekklhsiwn sunekdhmos hmwn sun th xariti tauth th diakonoumenh uf hmwn pros thn [authn] tou kuriou docan kai proqumian hmwn 
2co 8:20 stellomenoi touto mh tis hmas mwmhshtai en th adrothti tauth th diakonoumenh uf hmwn
2co 8:21 pronooumen gar kala ou monon enwpion kuriou alla kai enwpion anqrwpwn.
2co 8:22 sunepemyamen de autois ton adelfon hmwn on edokimasamen en pollois pollakis spoudaion onta nuni de polu spoudaioteron pepoiqhsei pollh th eis umas.
2co 8:23 eite uper titou koinwnos emos kai eis umas sunergos eite adelfoi hmwn apostoloi ekklhsiwn doca xristou.
2co 8:24 thn oun endeicin ths agaphs umwn kai hmwn kauxhsews uper umwn eis autous endeiknumenoi eis proswpon twn ekklhsiwn.
2co 9:1 peri men gar ths diakonias ths eis tous agious perisson moi estin to grafein umin
2co 9:2 oida gar thn proqumian umwn hn uper umwn kauxwmai makedosin oti axaia pareskeuastai apo perusi kai to umwn zhlos hreqisen tous pleionas.
2co 9:3 epemya de tous adelfous ina mh to kauxhma hmwn to uper umwn kenwqh en tw merei toutw ina kaqws elegon pareskeuasmenoi hte
2co 9:4 mh pws ean elqwsin sun emoi makedones kai eurwsin umas aparaskeuastous kataisxunqwmen hmeis ina mh legw umeis en th upostasei tauth.
2co 9:5 anagkaion oun hghsamhn parakalesai tous adelfous ina proelqwsin eis umas kai prokatartiswsin thn proephggelmenhn eulogian umwn tauthn etoimhn einai outws ws eulogian kai mh ws pleonecian.
2co 9:6 touto de o speirwn feidomenws feidomenws kai qerisei kai o speirwn ep eulogiais ep eulogiais kai qerisei.
2co 9:7 ekastos kaqws prohrhtai th kardia mh ek luphs h ec anagkhs ilaron gar dothn agapa o qeos.
2co 9:8 dunatei de o qeos pasan xarin perisseusai eis umas ina en panti pantote pasan autarkeian exontes perisseuhte eis pan ergon agaqon
2co 9:9 kaqws gegraptai eskorpisen edwken tois penhsin h dikaiosunh autou menei eis ton aiwna.
2co 9:10 o de epixorhgwn sporon tw speironti kai arton eis brwsin xorhghsei kai plhqunei ton sporon umwn kai auchsei ta genhmata ths dikaiosunhs umwn
2co 9:11 en panti ploutizomenoi eis pasan aplothta htis katergazetai di hmwn euxaristian tw qew 
2co 9:12 oti h diakonia ths leitourgias tauths ou monon estin prosanaplhrousa ta usterhmata twn agiwn alla kai perisseuousa dia pollwn euxaristiwn tw qew 
2co 9:13 dia ths dokimhs ths diakonias tauths docazontes ton qeon epi th upotagh ths omologias umwn eis to euaggelion tou xristou kai aplothti ths koinwnias eis autous kai eis pantas
2co 9:14 kai autwn dehsei uper umwn epipoqountwn umas dia thn uperballousan xarin tou qeou ef umin.
2co 9:15 xaris tw qew epi th anekdihghtw autou dwrea.

2co 10:3 en sarki gar peripatountes ou kata sarka strateuomeqa

2co 10:5 kai pan uywma epairomenon kata ths gnwsews tou qeou kai aixmalwtizontes pan nohma eis thn upakohn tou xristou
2co 10:6 kai en etoimw exontes ekdikhsai pasan parakohn otan plhrwqh umwn h upakoh.
2co 10:7 ta kata proswpon blepete. ei tis pepoiqen eautw xristou einai touto logizesqw palin ef eautou oti kaqws autos xristou outws kai hmeis.
2co 10:8 ean te gar perissoteron ti kauxhswmai peri ths ecousias hmwn hs edwken o kurios eis oikodomhn kai ouk eis kaqairesin umwn ouk aisxunqhsomai

2co 10:12 ou gar tolmwmen egkrinai h sugkrinai eautous tisin twn eautous sunistanontwn alla autoi en eautois eautous metrountes kai sugkrinontes eautous eautois ou [suniousin].

2co 10:14 ou gar ws mh efiknoumenoi eis umas uperekteinomen eautous axri gar kai umwn efqasamen en tw euaggeliw tou xristou
2co 10:15 ouk eis ta ametra kauxwmenoi en allotriois kopois elpida de exontes aucanomenhs ths pistews umwn en umin megalunqhnai kata ton kanona hmwn eis perisseian
2co 10:16 eis ta uperekeina umwn euaggelisasqai ouk en allotriw kanoni eis ta etoima kauxhsasqai.
2co 10:17 o de kauxwmenos en kuriw kauxasqw
2co 10:18 ou gar o eauton sunistanwn ekeinos estin dokimos alla on o kurios sunisthsin.

2co 12:1 kauxasqai [de] ou sumferon men eleusomai de eis optasias kai apokaluyeis kuriou.
2co 12:2 oida anqrwpon en xristw pro etwn dekatessarwn eite en swmati ouk oida eite ektos tou swmatos ouk oida o qeos oiden arpagenta ton toiouton ews tritou ouranou.

2co 12:4 oti hrpagh eis ton paradeison kai hkousen arrhta rhmata a ouk econ anqrwpw lalhsai.
2co 12:5 uper tou toioutou kauxhsomai uper de emautou ou kauxhsomai ei mh en tais asqeneiais.
2co 12:6 ean gar qelhsw kauxhsasqai ouk esomai afrwn alhqeian gar erw feidomai de mh tis eis eme logishtai uper o blepei me h akouei ti ec emou

2co 12:8 uper toutou tris ton kurion parekalesa ina aposth ap emou
2co 12:9 kai eirhken moi arkei soi h xaris mou h gar dunamis en asqeneia teleitai. hdista oun mallon kauxhsomai en tais asqeneiais mou ina episkhnwsh ep eme h dunamis tou xristou.
2co 12:10 dio eudokw en asqeneiais en ubresin en anagkais en diwgmois kai stenoxwriais uper xristou otan gar asqenw tote dunatos eimi.
2co 12:11 gegona afrwn umeis me hnagkasate egw gar wfeilon uf umwn sunistasqai. ouden gar usterhsa twn uperlian apostolwn ei kai ouden eimi
2co 12:12 ta men shmeia tou apostolou kateirgasqh en umin en pash upomonh shmeiois te kai terasin kai dunamesin.

2co 12:14 idou triton touto etoimws exw elqein pros umas kai ou katanarkhsw ou gar zhtw ta umwn alla umas ou gar ofeilei ta tekna tois goneusin qhsaurizein alla oi goneis tois teknois.
2co 12:15 egw de hdista dapanhsw kai ekdapanhqhsomai uper twn yuxwn umwn. ei perissoterws umas agapwn hsson agapwmai;
2co 12:16 estw de egw ou katebarhsa umas alla uparxwn panourgos dolw umas elabon.

gal 1:1 paulos apostolos ouk ap anqrwpwn oude di anqrwpou alla dia ihsou xristou kai qeou patros tou egeirantos auton ek nekrwn
gal 1:2 kai oi sun emoi pantes adelfoi tais ekklhsiais ths galatias
gal 1:3 xaris umin kai eirhnh apo qeou patros [kai kuriou hmwn] ihsou xristou
gal 1:4 tou dontos eauton uper twn amartiwn hmwn opws ecelhtai hmas ek tou aiwnos tou enestwtos ponhrou kata to qelhma tou qeou kai patros hmwn
gal 1:5 w h doca eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn amhn.
gal 1:6 qaumazw oti outws taxews metatiqesqe apo tou kalesantos umas en xariti xristou eis eteron euaggelion
gal 1:7 o ouk estin allo ei mh tines eisin oi tarassontes umas kai qelontes metastreyai to euaggelion tou xristou.
gal 1:8 alla kai ean hmeis h aggelos ec ouranou euaggelizhtai umin par o euhggelisameqa umin anaqema estw.
gal 1:9 ws proeirhkamen kai arti palin legw ei tis umas euaggelizetai par o parelabete anaqema estw.
gal 1:10 arti gar anqrwpous peiqw h ton qeon; h zhtw anqrwpois areskein; ei eti anqrwpois hreskon xristou doulos ouk an hmhn.
gal 1:11 gnwrizw gar umin adelfoi to euaggelion to euaggelisqen up emou oti ouk estin kata anqrwpon
gal 1:12 oude gar egw para anqrwpou parelabon auto oute edidaxqhn alla di apokaluyews ihsou xristou.
gal 1:13 hkousate gar thn emhn anastrofhn pote en tw ioudaismw oti kaq uperbolhn ediwkon thn ekklhsian tou qeou kai eporqoun authn
gal 1:14 kai proekopton en tw ioudaismw uper pollous sunhlikiwtas en tw genei mou perissoterws zhlwths uparxwn twn patrikwn mou paradosewn.
gal 1:15 ote de eudokhsen o qeos o aforisas me ek koilias mhtros mou kai kalesas dia ths xaritos autou
gal 1:16 apokaluyai ton uion autou en emoi ina euaggelizwmai auton en tois eqnesin euqews ou prosaneqemhn sarki kai aimati
gal 1:17 oude anhlqon eis ierosoluma pros tous pro emou apostolous alla aphlqon eis arabian kai palin upestreya eis damaskon.
gal 1:18 epeita meta eth tria anhlqon eis ierosoluma istorhsai khfan kai epemeina pros auton hmeras dekapente
gal 1:19 eteron de twn apostolwn ouk eidon ei mh iakwbon ton adelfon tou kuriou.
gal 1:20 a de grafw umin idou enwpion tou qeou oti ou yeudomai.
gal 1:21 epeita hlqon eis ta klimata ths surias kai ths kilikias.
gal 1:22 hmhn de agnooumenos tw proswpw tais ekklhsiais ths ioudaias tais en xristw
gal 1:23 monon de akouontes hsan oti o diwkwn hmas pote nun euaggelizetai thn pistin hn pote eporqei
gal 1:24 kai edocazon en emoi ton qeon.

gal 2:3 all oude titos o sun emoi ellhn wn hnagkasqh peritmhqhnai
gal 2:4 dia de tous pareisaktous yeudadelfous oitines pareishlqon kataskophsai thn eleuqerian hmwn hn exomen en xristw ihsou ina hmas katadoulwsousin
gal 2:5 ois oude pros wran eicamen th upotagh ina h alhqeia tou euaggeliou diameinh pros umas.
gal 2:6 apo de twn dokountwn einai ti opoioi pote hsan ouden moi diaferei proswpon o qeos anqrwpou ou lambanei emoi gar oi dokountes ouden prosaneqento
gal 2:7 alla tounantion idontes oti pepisteumai to euaggelion ths akrobustias kaqws petros ths peritomhs

gal 2:9 kai gnontes thn xarin thn doqeisan moi iakwbos kai khfas kai iwannhs oi dokountes stuloi einai decias edwkan emoi kai barnaba koinwnias ina hmeis eis ta eqnh autoi de eis thn peritomhn
gal 2:10 monon twn ptwxwn ina mnhmoneuwmen o kai espoudasa auto touto poihsai.
gal 2:11 ote de hlqen khfas eis antioxeian kata proswpon autw antesthn oti kategnwsmenos hn.
gal 2:12 pro tou gar elqein tinas apo iakwbou meta twn eqnwn sunhsqien ote de hlqon upestellen kai afwrizen eauton foboumenos tous ek peritomhs.
gal 2:13 kai sunupekriqhsan autw kai oi loipoi ioudaioi wste kai barnabas sunaphxqh autwn th upokrisei.
gal 2:14 all ote eidon oti ouk orqopodousin pros thn alhqeian tou euaggeliou eipon tw khfa emprosqen pantwn ei su ioudaios uparxwn eqnikws kai ouxi ioudaikws zhs pws ta eqnh anagkazeis ioudaizein;
gal 2:15 hmeis fusei ioudaioi kai ouk ec eqnwn amartwloi
gal 2:16 eidotes de oti ou dikaioutai anqrwpos ec ergwn nomou ean mh dia pistews ihsou xristou kai hmeis eis xriston ihsoun episteusamen ina dikaiwqwmen ek pistews xristou kai ouk ec ergwn nomou oti ec ergwn nomou ou dikaiwqhsetai pasa sarc.
gal 2:17 ei de zhtountes dikaiwqhnai en xristw eureqhmen kai autoi amartwloi ara xristos amartias diakonos; mh genoito.
gal 2:18 ei gar a katelusa tauta palin oikodomw parabathn emauton sunistanw.
gal 2:19 egw gar dia nomou nomw apeqanon ina qew zhsw. xristw sunestaurwmai
gal 2:20 zw de ouketi egw zh de en emoi xristos o de nun zw en sarki en pistei zw th tou uiou tou qeou tou agaphsantos me kai paradontos eauton uper emou.
gal 2:21 ouk aqetw thn xarin tou qeou ei gar dia nomou dikaiosunh ara xristos dwrean apeqanen.
gal 3:1 w anohtoi galatai tis umas ebaskanen ois kat ofqalmous ihsous xristos proegrafh estaurwmenos;
gal 3:2 touto monon qelw maqein af umwn ec ergwn nomou to pneuma elabete h ec akohs pistews;
gal 3:3 outws anohtoi este; enarcamenoi pneumati nun sarki epiteleisqe;
gal 3:4 tosauta epaqete eikh; ei ge kai eikh.
gal 3:5 o oun epixorhgwn umin to pneuma kai energwn dunameis en umin ec ergwn nomou h ec akohs pistews;
gal 3:6 kaqws abraam episteusen tw qew kai elogisqh autw eis dikaiosunhn.
gal 3:7 ginwskete ara oti oi ek pistews outoi uioi eisin abraam.
gal 3:8 proidousa de h grafh oti ek pistews dikaioi ta eqnh o qeos proeuhggelisato tw abraam oti eneuloghqhsontai en soi panta ta eqnh.
gal 3:9 wste oi ek pistews eulogountai sun tw pistw abraam.
gal 3:10 osoi gar ec ergwn nomou eisin upo kataran eisin gegraptai gar oti epikataratos pas os ouk emmenei pasin tois gegrammenois en tw bibliw tou nomou tou poihsai auta.
gal 3:11 oti de en nomw oudeis dikaioutai para tw qew dhlon oti o dikaios ek pistews zhsetai
gal 3:12 o de nomos ouk estin ek pistews all o poihsas auta zhsetai en autois.
gal 3:13 xristos hmas echgorasen ek ths kataras tou nomou genomenos uper hmwn katara oti gegraptai epikataratos pas o kremamenos epi culou
gal 3:14 ina eis ta eqnh h eulogia tou abraam genhtai en xristw ihsou ina thn epaggelian tou pneumatos labwmen dia ths pistews.
gal 3:15 adelfoi kata anqrwpon legw omws anqrwpou kekurwmenhn diaqhkhn oudeis aqetei h epidiatassetai.
gal 3:16 tw de abraam erreqhsan ai epaggeliai kai tw spermati autou. ou legei kai tois spermasin ws epi pollwn all ws ef enos kai tw spermati sou os estin xristos.
gal 3:17 touto de legw diaqhkhn prokekurwmenhn upo tou qeou o meta tetrakosia kai triakonta eth gegonws nomos ouk akuroi eis to katarghsai thn epaggelian.
gal 3:18 ei gar ek nomou h klhronomia ouketi ec epaggelias tw de abraam di epaggelias kexaristai o qeos.
gal 3:19 ti oun o nomos; twn parabasewn xarin proseteqh axris ou elqh to sperma w ephggeltai diatageis di aggelwn en xeiri mesitou.
gal 3:20 o de mesiths enos ouk estin o de qeos eis estin.
gal 3:21 o oun nomos kata twn epaggeliwn tou qeou; mh genoito ei gar edoqh nomos o dunamenos zwopoihsai ontws ek nomou an hn h dikaiosunh.
gal 3:22 alla sunekleisen h grafh ta panta upo amartian ina h epaggelia ek pistews ihsou xristou doqh tois pisteuousin.
gal 3:23 pro tou de elqein thn pistin upo nomon efrouroumeqa sugkleiomenoi eis thn mellousan pistin apokalufqhnai.
gal 3:24 wste o nomos paidagwgos hmwn gegonen eis xriston ina ek pistews dikaiwqwmen
gal 3:25 elqoushs de ths pistews ouketi upo paidagwgon esmen.
gal 3:26 pantes gar uioi qeou este dia ths pistews en xristw ihsou.

gal 5:1 th eleuqeria hmas xristos hleuqerwsen sthkete oun kai mh palin zugw douleias enexesqe.

eph 5:14 pan gar to faneroumenon fws estin. dio legei egeire o kaqeudwn kai anasta ek twn nekrwn kai epifausei soi o xristos.
eph 5:15 blepete oun akribws pws peripateite mh ws asofoi all ws sofoi
eph 5:16 ecagorazomenoi ton kairon oti ai hmerai ponhrai eisin.
eph 5:17 dia touto mh ginesqe afrones alla suniete ti to qelhma tou kuriou.
eph 5:18 kai mh mequskesqe oinw en w estin aswtia alla plhrousqe en pneumati
eph 5:19 lalountes eautois en yalmois kai umnois kai wdais pneumatikais adontes kai yallontes th kardia umwn tw kuriw
eph 5:20 euxaristountes pantote uper pantwn en onomati tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou tw qew kai patri
eph 5:21 upotassomenoi allhlois en fobw xristou.
eph 5:22 ai gunaikes tois idiois andrasin [upotassesqwsan] ws tw kuriw
eph 5:23 oti anhr estin kefalh ths gunaikos ws kai o xristos kefalh ths ekklhsias autos swthr tou swmatos.
eph 5:24 alla ws h ekklhsia upotassetai tw xristw outws kai ai gunaikes tois andrasin en panti.
eph 5:25 oi andres agapate tas gunaikas kaqws kai o xristos hgaphsen thn ekklhsian kai eauton paredwken uper auths
eph 5:26 ina authn agiash kaqarisas tw loutrw tou udatos en rhmati
eph 5:27 ina parasthsh autos eautw endocon thn ekklhsian mh exousan spilon h rutida h ti twn toioutwn all ina h agia kai amwmos.
eph 5:28 outws ofeilousin kai oi andres agapan tas eautwn gunaikas ws ta eautwn swmata. o agapwn thn eautou gunaika eauton agapa
eph 5:29 oudeis gar pote thn eautou sarka emishsen alla ektrefei kai qalpei authn kaqws kai o xristos thn ekklhsian
eph 5:30 oti melh esmen tou swmatos autou.
eph 5:31 anti toutou kataleiyei anqrwpos ton patera kai thn mhtera kai proskollhqhsetai pros thn gunaika autou kai esontai oi duo eis sarka mian.
eph 5:32 to musthrion touto mega estin egw de legw eis xriston kai eis thn ekklhsian.
eph 5:33 plhn kai umeis oi kaq ena ekastos thn eautou gunaika outws agapatw ws eauton h de gunh ina fobhtai ton andra.
eph 6:1 ta tekna upakouete tois goneusin umwn en kuriw touto gar estin dikaion.
eph 6:2 tima ton patera sou kai thn mhtera htis estin entolh prwth en epaggelia
eph 6:3 ina eu soi genhtai kai esh makroxronios epi ths ghs.
eph 6:4 kai oi pateres mh parorgizete ta tekna umwn alla ektrefete auta en paideia kai nouqesia kuriou.
eph 6:5 oi douloi upakouete tois kata sarka kuriois meta fobou kai tromou en aplothti ths kardias umwn ws tw xristw
eph 6:6 mh kat ofqalmodoulian ws anqrwpareskoi all ws douloi xristou poiountes to qelhma tou qeou ek yuxhs
eph 6:7 met eunoias douleuontes ws tw kuriw kai ouk anqrwpois
eph 6:8 eidotes oti ekastos ean ti poihsh agaqon touto komisetai para kuriou eite doulos eite eleuqeros.
eph 6:9 kai oi kurioi ta auta poieite pros autous anientes thn apeilhn eidotes oti kai autwn kai umwn o kurios estin en ouranois kai proswpolhmyia ouk estin par autw.
eph 6:10 tou loipou endunamousqe en kuriw kai en tw kratei ths isxuos autou.
eph 6:11 endusasqe thn panoplian tou qeou pros to dunasqai umas sthnai pros tas meqodeias tou diabolou
eph 6:12 oti ouk estin hmin h palh pros aima kai sarka alla pros tas arxas pros tas ecousias pros tous kosmokratoras tou skotous toutou pros ta pneumatika ths ponhrias en tois epouraniois.
eph 6:13 dia touto analabete thn panoplian tou qeou ina dunhqhte antisthnai en th hmera th ponhra kai apanta katergasamenoi sthnai.
eph 6:14 sthte oun perizwsamenoi thn osfun umwn en alhqeia kai endusamenoi ton qwraka ths dikaiosunhs
eph 6:15 kai upodhsamenoi tous podas en etoimasia tou euaggeliou ths eirhnhs
eph 6:16 en pasin analabontes ton qureon ths pistews en w dunhsesqe panta ta belh tou ponhrou ta pepurwmena sbesai
eph 6:17 kai thn perikefalaian tou swthriou decasqe kai thn maxairan tou pneumatos o estin rhma qeou
eph 6:18 dia pashs proseuxhs kai dehsews proseuxomenoi en panti kairw en pneumati kai eis auto agrupnountes en pash proskarterhsei kai dehsei peri pantwn twn agiwn
eph 6:19 kai uper emou ina moi doqh logos en anoicei tou stomatos mou en parrhsia gnwrisai to musthrion tou euaggeliou
eph 6:20 uper ou presbeuw en alusei ina parrhsiaswmai [en autw] ws dei me lalhsai.
eph 6:21 ina de eidhte kai umeis ta kat eme ti prassw panta gnwrisei umin tuxikos o agaphtos adelfos kai pistos diakonos en kuriw
eph 6:22 on epemya pros umas eis auto touto ina gnwte ta peri hmwn kai parakalesh tas kardias umwn.
eph 6:23 eirhnh tois adelfois kai agaph meta pistews apo qeou patros kai kuriou ihsou xristou.
eph 6:24 h xaris meta pantwn twn agapwntwn ton kurion hmwn ihsoun xriston en afqarsia.
phi 1:1 paulos kai timoqeos douloi xristou ihsou pasin tois agiois en xristw ihsou tois ousin en filippois sun episkopois kai diakonois
phi 1:2 xaris umin kai eirhnh apo qeou patros hmwn kai kuriou ihsou xristou.
phi 1:3 euxaristw tw qew mou epi pash th mneia umwn
phi 1:4 pantote en pash dehsei mou uper pantwn umwn meta xaras thn dehsin poioumenos
phi 1:5 epi th koinwnia umwn eis to euaggelion apo ths prwths hmeras axri tou nun
phi 1:6 pepoiqws auto touto oti o enarcamenos en umin ergon agaqon epitelesei axri hmeras xristou ihsou
phi 1:7 kaqws estin dikaion emoi touto fronein uper pantwn umwn dia to exein me en th kardia umas en te tois desmois mou kai en th apologia kai bebaiwsei tou euaggeliou sugkoinwnous mou ths xaritos pantas umas ontas.
phi 1:8 martus gar mou o qeos ws epipoqw pantas umas en splagxnois xristou ihsou.
phi 1:9 kai touto proseuxomai ina h agaph umwn eti mallon kai mallon perisseuh en epignwsei kai pash aisqhsei
phi 1:10 eis to dokimazein umas ta diaferonta ina hte eilikrineis kai aproskopoi eis hmeran xristou
phi 1:11 peplhrwmenoi karpon dikaiosunhs ton dia ihsou xristou eis docan kai epainon qeou.
phi 1:12 ginwskein de umas boulomai adelfoi oti ta kat eme mallon eis prokophn tou euaggeliou elhluqen
phi 1:13 wste tous desmous mou fanerous en xristw genesqai en olw tw praitwriw kai tois loipois pasin
phi 1:14 kai tous pleionas twn adelfwn en kuriw pepoiqotas tois desmois mou perissoterws tolman afobws ton logon [tou qeou] lalein.
phi 1:15 tines men kai dia fqonon kai erin tines de kai di eudokian ton xriston khrussousin
phi 1:16 oi men ec agaphs eidotes oti eis apologian tou euaggeliou keimai
phi 1:17 oi de ec eriqeias ton xriston kataggellousin oux agnws oiomenoi qliyin egeirein tois desmois mou.
phi 1:18 ti gar; plhn oti panti tropw eite profasei eite alhqeia xristos kataggelletai kai en toutw xairw alla kai xarhsomai
phi 1:19 oida gar oti touto moi apobhsetai eis swthrian dia ths umwn dehsews kai epixorhgias tou pneumatos ihsou xristou
phi 1:20 kata thn apokaradokian kai elpida mou oti en oudeni aisxunqhsomai all en pash parrhsia ws pantote kai nun megalunqhsetai xristos en tw swmati mou eite dia zwhs eite dia qanatou.
phi 1:21 emoi gar to zhn xristos kai to apoqanein kerdos.
phi 1:22 ei de to zhn en sarki touto moi karpos ergou kai ti airhsomai ou gnwrizw.
phi 1:23 sunexomai de ek twn duo thn epiqumian exwn eis to analusai kai sun xristw einai pollw gar mallon kreisson
phi 1:24 to de epimenein en th sarki anagkaioteron di umas.
phi 1:25 kai touto pepoiqws oida oti menw kai paramenw pasin umin eis thn umwn prokophn kai xaran ths pistews
phi 1:26 ina to kauxhma umwn perisseuh en xristw ihsou en emoi dia ths emhs parousias palin pros umas.
phi 1:27 monon aciws tou euaggeliou tou xristou politeuesqe ina eite elqwn kai idwn umas eite apwn akouw ta peri umwn oti sthkete en eni pneumati mia yuxh sunaqlountes th pistei tou euaggeliou
phi 1:28 kai mh pturomenoi en mhdeni upo twn antikeimenwn htis estin autois endeicis apwleias umwn de swthrias kai touto apo qeou
phi 1:29 oti umin exarisqh to uper xristou ou monon to eis auton pisteuein alla kai to uper autou pasxein
phi 1:30 ton auton agwna exontes oion eidete en emoi kai nun akouete en emoi.
phi 2:1 ei tis oun paraklhsis en xristw ei ti paramuqion agaphs ei tis koinwnia pneumatos ei tis splagxna kai oiktirmoi
phi 2:2 plhrwsate mou thn xaran ina to auto fronhte thn authn agaphn exontes sumyuxoi to en fronountes
phi 2:3 mhden kat eriqeian mhde kata kenodocian alla th tapeinofrosunh allhlous hgoumenoi uperexontas eautwn
phi 2:4 mh ta eautwn ekastos skopountes alla kai ta eterwn ekastoi.
phi 2:5 touto froneite en umin o kai en xristw ihsou
phi 2:6 os en morfh qeou uparxwn oux arpagmon hghsato to einai isa qew
