phi 2:11 kai pasa glwssa ecomologhshtai oti kurios ihsous xristos eis docan qeou patros.
phi 2:12 wste agaphtoi mou kaqws pantote uphkousate mh [--] en th parousia mou monon alla nun pollw mallon en th apousia mou meta fobou kai tromou thn eautwn swthrian katergazesqe
phi 2:13 qeos gar estin o energwn en umin kai to qelein kai to energein uper ths eudokias.
phi 2:14 panta poieite xwris goggusmwn kai dialogismwn
phi 2:15 ina genhsqe amemptoi kai akeraioi tekna qeou amwma meson geneas skolias kai diestrammenhs en ois fainesqe ws fwsthres en kosmw
phi 2:16 logon zwhs epexontes eis kauxhma emoi eis hmeran xristou oti ouk eis kenon edramon oude eis kenon ekopiasa.
phi 2:17 alla ei kai spendomai epi th qusia kai leitourgia ths pistews umwn xairw kai sugxairw pasin umin
phi 2:18 to de auto kai umeis xairete kai sugxairete moi.
phi 2:19 elpizw de en kuriw ihsou timoqeon taxews pemyai umin ina kagw euyuxw gnous ta peri umwn.
phi 2:20 oudena gar exw isoyuxon ostis gnhsiws ta peri umwn merimnhsei
phi 2:21 oi pantes gar ta eautwn zhtousin ou ta ihsou xristou.
phi 2:22 thn de dokimhn autou ginwskete oti ws patri teknon sun emoi edouleusen eis to euaggelion.
phi 2:23 touton men oun elpizw pemyai ws an afidw ta peri eme ecauths
phi 2:24 pepoiqa de en kuriw oti kai autos taxews eleusomai.
phi 2:25 anagkaion de hghsamhn epafroditon ton adelfon kai sunergon kai sustratiwthn mou umwn de apostolon kai leitourgon ths xreias mou pemyai pros umas
phi 2:26 epeidh epipoqwn hn pantas umas kai adhmonwn dioti hkousate oti hsqenhsen.
phi 2:27 kai gar hsqenhsen paraplhsion qanatw alla o qeos hlehsen auton ouk auton de monon alla kai eme ina mh luphn epi luphn sxw.
phi 2:28 spoudaioterws oun epemya auton ina idontes auton palin xarhte kagw alupoteros w.
phi 2:29 prosdexesqe oun auton en kuriw meta pashs xaras kai tous toioutous entimous exete
phi 2:30 oti dia to ergon xristou mexri qanatou hggisen paraboleusamenos th yuxh ina anaplhrwsh to umwn usterhma ths pros me leitourgias.
phi 3:1 to loipon adelfoi mou xairete en kuriw. ta auta grafein umin emoi men ouk oknhron umin de asfales.
phi 3:2 blepete tous kunas blepete tous kakous ergatas blepete thn katatomhn.
phi 3:3 hmeis gar esmen h peritomh oi pneumati qeou latreuontes kai kauxwmenoi en xristw ihsou kai ouk en sarki pepoiqotes
phi 3:4 kaiper egw exwn pepoiqhsin kai en sarki. ei tis dokei allos pepoiqenai en sarki egw mallon
phi 3:5 peritomh oktahmeros ek genous israhl fulhs beniamin ebraios ec ebraiwn kata nomon farisaios
phi 3:6 kata zhlos diwkwn thn ekklhsian kata dikaiosunhn thn en nomw genomenos amemptos.
phi 3:7 alla atina hn moi kerdh tauta hghmai dia ton xriston zhmian.
phi 3:8 alla menounge kai hgoumai panta zhmian einai dia to uperexon ths gnwsews xristou ihsou tou kuriou mou di on ta panta ezhmiwqhn kai hgoumai skubala ina xriston kerdhsw
phi 3:9 kai eureqw en autw mh exwn emhn dikaiosunhn thn ek nomou alla thn dia pistews xristou thn ek qeou dikaiosunhn epi th pistei
phi 3:10 tou gnwnai auton kai thn dunamin ths anastasews autou kai thn koinwnian twn paqhmatwn autou summorfizomenos tw qanatw autou
phi 3:11 ei pws katanthsw eis thn ecanastasin thn ek nekrwn.
phi 3:12 oux oti hdh elabon h hdh teteleiwmai diwkw de ei kai katalabw ef w kai katelhmfqhn upo xristou [--].
phi 3:13 adelfoi egw emauton ou logizomai kateilhfenai en de ta men opisw epilanqanomenos tois de emprosqen epekteinomenos
phi 3:14 kata skopon diwkw eis to brabeion ths anw klhsews tou qeou en xristw ihsou.
phi 3:15 osoi oun teleioi touto fronwmen kai ei ti eterws froneite kai touto o qeos umin apokaluyei
phi 3:16 plhn eis o efqasamen tw autw stoixein.
phi 3:17 summimhtai mou ginesqe adelfoi kai skopeite tous outw peripatountas kaqws exete tupon hmas.
phi 3:18 polloi gar peripatousin ous pollakis elegon umin nun de kai klaiwn legw tous exqrous tou staurou tou xristou
phi 3:19 wn to telos apwleia wn o qeos h koilia kai h doca en th aisxunh autwn oi ta epigeia fronountes.
phi 3:20 hmwn gar to politeuma en ouranois uparxei ec ou kai swthra apekdexomeqa kurion ihsoun xriston
phi 3:21 os metasxhmatisei to swma ths tapeinwsews hmwn summorfon tw swmati ths dochs autou kata thn energeian tou dunasqai auton kai upotacai autw ta panta.
phi 4:1 wste adelfoi mou agaphtoi kai epipoqhtoi xara kai stefanos mou outws sthkete en kuriw agaphtoi.
phi 4:2 euodian parakalw kai suntuxhn parakalw to auto fronein en kuriw.
phi 4:3 nai erwtw kai se gnhsie suzuge sullambanou autais aitines en tw euaggeliw sunhqlhsan moi meta kai klhmentos kai twn loipwn sunergwn mou wn ta onomata en biblw zwhs.
phi 4:4 xairete en kuriw pantote palin erw xairete.
phi 4:5 to epieikes umwn gnwsqhtw pasin anqrwpois. o kurios eggus.
phi 4:6 mhden merimnate all en panti th proseuxh kai th dehsei meta euxaristias ta aithmata umwn gnwrizesqw pros ton qeon.
phi 4:7 kai h eirhnh tou qeou h uperexousa panta noun frourhsei tas kardias umwn kai ta nohmata umwn en xristw ihsou.
phi 4:8 to loipon adelfoi osa estin alhqh osa semna osa dikaia osa agna osa prosfilh osa eufhma ei tis areth kai ei tis epainos tauta logizesqe
phi 4:9 a kai emaqete kai parelabete kai hkousate kai eidete en emoi tauta prassete kai o qeos ths eirhnhs estai meq umwn.
phi 4:10 exarhn de en kuriw megalws oti hdh pote aneqalete to uper emou fronein ef w kai efroneite hkaireisqe de.
phi 4:11 oux oti kaq usterhsin legw egw gar emaqon en ois eimi autarkhs einai.
phi 4:12 oida kai tapeinousqai oida kai perisseuein en panti kai en pasin memuhmai kai xortazesqai kai peinan kai perisseuein kai ustereisqai.
phi 4:13 panta isxuw en tw endunamounti me.
phi 4:14 plhn kalws epoihsate sugkoinwnhsantes mou th qliyei.
phi 4:15 oidate de kai umeis filipphsioi oti en arxh tou euaggeliou ote echlqon apo makedonias oudemia moi ekklhsia ekoinwnhsen eis logon dosews kai lhmyews ei mh umeis monoi
phi 4:16 oti kai en qessalonikh kai apac kai dis eis thn xreian moi epemyate.
phi 4:17 oux oti epizhtw to doma alla epizhtw ton karpon ton pleonazonta eis logon umwn.
phi 4:18 apexw de panta kai perisseuw peplhrwmai decamenos para epafroditou ta par umwn osmhn euwdias qusian dekthn euareston tw qew.
phi 4:19 o de qeos mou plhrwsei pasan xreian umwn kata to ploutos autou en doch en xristw ihsou.
phi 4:20 tw de qew kai patri hmwn h doca eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn amhn.
phi 4:21 aspasasqe panta agion en xristw ihsou. aspazontai umas oi sun emoi adelfoi.
phi 4:22 aspazontai umas pantes oi agioi malista de oi ek ths kaisaros oikias.
phi 4:23 h xaris tou kuriou ihsou xristou meta tou pneumatos umwn.
col 1:1 paulos apostolos xristou ihsou dia qelhmatos qeou kai timoqeos o adelfos
col 1:2 tois en kolossais agiois kai pistois adelfois en xristw xaris umin kai eirhnh apo qeou patros hmwn.
col 1:3 euxaristoumen tw qew patri tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou pantote peri umwn proseuxomenoi
col 1:4 akousantes thn pistin umwn en xristw ihsou kai thn agaphn hn exete eis pantas tous agious
col 1:5 dia thn elpida thn apokeimenhn umin en tois ouranois hn prohkousate en tw logw ths alhqeias tou euaggeliou
col 1:6 tou parontos eis umas kaqws kai en panti tw kosmw estin karpoforoumenon kai aucanomenon kaqws kai en umin af hs hmeras hkousate kai epegnwte thn xarin tou qeou en alhqeia
col 1:7 kaqws emaqete apo epafra tou agaphtou sundoulou hmwn os estin pistos uper umwn diakonos tou xristou
col 1:8 o kai dhlwsas hmin thn umwn agaphn en pneumati.
col 1:9 dia touto kai hmeis af hs hmeras hkousamen ou pauomeqa uper umwn proseuxomenoi kai aitoumenoi ina plhrwqhte thn epignwsin tou qelhmatos autou en pash sofia kai sunesei pneumatikh
col 1:10 peripathsai aciws tou kuriou eis pasan areskeian en panti ergw agaqw karpoforountes kai aucanomenoi th epignwsei tou qeou
col 1:11 en pash dunamei dunamoumenoi kata to kratos ths dochs autou eis pasan upomonhn kai makroqumian meta xaras
col 1:12 euxaristountes tw patri tw [kalesanti] umas eis thn merida tou klhrou twn agiwn en tw fwti
col 1:13 os errusato hmas ek ths ecousias tou skotous kai metesthsen eis thn basileian tou uiou ths agaphs autou
col 1:14 en w exomen thn apolutrwsin thn afesin twn amartiwn
col 1:15 os estin eikwn tou qeou tou aoratou prwtotokos pashs ktisews
col 1:16 oti en autw ektisqh ta panta en tois ouranois kai epi ths ghs ta orata kai ta aorata eite qronoi eite kuriothtes eite arxai eite ecousiai ta panta di autou kai eis auton ektistai
col 1:17 kai autos estin pro pantwn kai ta panta en autw sunesthken.
col 1:18 kai autos estin h kefalh tou swmatos ths ekklhsias os estin arxh prwtotokos ek twn nekrwn ina genhtai en pasin autos prwteuwn
col 1:19 oti en autw eudokhsen pan to plhrwma katoikhsai
col 1:20 kai di autou apokatallacai ta panta eis auton eirhnopoihsas dia tou aimatos tou staurou autou [--] eite ta epi ths ghs eite ta en tois ouranois.
col 1:21 kai umas pote ontas aphllotriwmenous kai exqrous th dianoia en tois ergois tois ponhrois
col 1:22 nuni de apokathllacen en tw swmati ths sarkos autou dia tou qanatou parasthsai umas agious kai amwmous kai anegklhtous katenwpion autou
col 1:23 ei ge epimenete th pistei teqemeliwmenoi kai edraioi kai mh metakinoumenoi apo ths elpidos tou euaggeliou ou hkousate tou khruxqentos en pash ktisei th upo ton ouranon ou egenomhn egw paulos diakonos.
col 1:24 nun xairw en tois paqhmasin uper umwn kai antanaplhrw ta usterhmata twn qliyewn tou xristou en th sarki mou uper tou swmatos autou o estin h ekklhsia
col 1:25 hs egenomhn egw diakonos kata thn oikonomian tou qeou thn doqeisan moi eis umas plhrwsai ton logon tou qeou
col 1:26 to musthrion to apokekrummenon apo twn aiwnwn kai apo twn genewn nun de efanerwqh tois agiois autou
col 1:27 ois hqelhsen o qeos gnwrisai ti to ploutos ths dochs tou musthriou toutou en tois eqnesin o estin xristos en umin h elpis ths dochs
col 1:28 on hmeis kataggellomen nouqetountes panta anqrwpon kai didaskontes panta anqrwpon en pash sofia ina parasthswmen panta anqrwpon teleion en xristw
col 1:29 eis o kai kopiw agwnizomenos kata thn energeian autou thn energoumenhn en emoi en dunamei.
col 2:1 qelw gar umas eidenai hlikon agwna exw uper umwn kai twn en laodikeia kai osoi oux eorakan to proswpon mou en sarki
col 2:2 ina paraklhqwsin ai kardiai autwn sumbibasqentes en agaph kai eis pan ploutos ths plhroforias ths sunesews eis epignwsin tou musthriou tou qeou [patros tou] xristou
col 2:3 en w eisin pantes oi qhsauroi ths sofias kai gnwsews apokrufoi.
col 2:4 touto legw ina mhdeis umas paralogizhtai en piqanologia.
col 2:5 ei gar kai th sarki apeimi alla tw pneumati sun umin eimi xairwn kai blepwn umwn thn tacin kai to sterewma ths eis xriston pistews umwn.
col 2:6 ws oun parelabete ton xriston ihsoun ton kurion en autw peripateite
col 2:7 errizwmenoi kai epoikodomoumenoi en autw kai bebaioumenoi [en autw] th pistei kaqws edidaxqhte perisseuontes en euxaristia.
col 2:8 blepete mh tis umas estai o sulagwgwn dia ths filosofias kai kenhs apaths kata thn paradosin twn anqrwpwn kata ta stoixeia tou kosmou kai ou kata xriston
col 2:9 oti en autw katoikei pan to plhrwma ths qeothtos swmatikws
col 2:10 kai este en autw peplhrwmenoi os estin h kefalh pashs arxhs kai ecousias
col 2:11 en w kai perietmhqhte peritomh axeiropoihtw en th apekdusei tou swmatos ths sarkos en th peritomh tou xristou
col 2:12 suntafentes autw en tw baptismw en w kai sunhgerqhte dia ths pistews ths energeias tou qeou tou egeirantos auton ek nekrwn
col 2:13 kai umas nekrous ontas en tois paraptwmasin kai th akrobustia ths sarkos umwn sunezwopoihsen umas sun autw xarisamenos hmin panta ta paraptwmata
col 2:14 ecaleiyas to kaq hmwn xeirografon tois dogmasin o hn upenantion hmin kai auto hrken ek tou mesou proshlwsas auto tw staurw
col 2:15 apekdusamenos tas arxas kai tas ecousias edeigmatisen en parrhsia qriambeusas autous en autw.
col 2:16 mh oun tis umas krinetw en brwsei kai en posei h en merei eorths h neomhnias h sabbatwn
col 2:17 a estin skia twn mellontwn to de swma tou xristou.
col 2:18 mhdeis umas katabrabeuetw qelwn en tapeinofrosunh kai qrhskeia twn aggelwn a eoraken embateuwn eikh fusioumenos upo tou noos ths sarkos autou
col 2:19 kai ou kratwn thn kefalhn ec ou pan to swma dia twn afwn kai sundesmwn epixorhgoumenon kai sumbibazomenon aucei thn auchsin tou qeou.
col 2:20 ei apeqanete sun xristw apo twn stoixeiwn tou kosmou ti ws zwntes en kosmw dogmatizesqe
col 2:21 mh ayh mhde geush mhde qighs
col 2:22 a estin panta eis fqoran th apoxrhsei kata ta entalmata kai didaskalias twn anqrwpwn;
col 2:23 atina estin logon men exonta sofias en eqeloqrhskia kai tapeinofrosunh kai afeidia swmatos ouk en timh tini pros plhsmonhn ths sarkos.
col 3:1 ei oun sunhgerqhte tw xristw ta anw zhteite ou o xristos estin en decia tou qeou kaqhmenos
col 3:2 ta anw froneite mh ta epi ths ghs
col 3:3 apeqanete gar kai h zwh umwn kekruptai sun tw xristw en tw qew.
col 3:4 otan o xristos fanerwqh h zwh [hmwn] tote kai umeis sun autw fanerwqhsesqe en doch.
col 3:5 nekrwsate oun ta melh ta epi ths ghs porneian akaqarsian paqos epiqumian kakhn kai thn pleonecian htis estin eidwlolatria
col 3:6 di a erxetai h orgh tou qeou [--].
col 3:7 en ois kai umeis periepathsate pote ote ezhte en toutois.
col 3:8 nuni de apoqesqe kai umeis ta panta orghn qumon kakian blasfhmian aisxrologian ek tou stomatos umwn
col 3:9 mh yeudesqe eis allhlous apekdusamenoi ton palaion anqrwpon sun tais pracesin autou
col 3:10 kai endusamenoi ton neon ton anakainoumenon eis epignwsin kat eikona tou ktisantos auton
col 3:11 opou ouk eni ellhn kai ioudaios peritomh kai akrobustia barbaros skuqhs doulos eleuqeros alla ta panta kai en pasin xristos.
col 3:12 endusasqe oun ws eklektoi tou qeou agioi kai hgaphmenoi splagxna oiktirmou xrhstothta tapeinofrosunhn prauthta makroqumian
col 3:13 anexomenoi allhlwn kai xarizomenoi eautois ean tis pros tina exh momfhn kaqws kai o [xristos] exarisato umin outws kai umeis
col 3:14 epi pasin de toutois thn agaphn o estin sundesmos ths teleiothtos.
col 3:15 kai h eirhnh tou xristou brabeuetw en tais kardiais umwn eis hn kai eklhqhte en eni swmati kai euxaristoi ginesqe.
col 3:16 o logos tou xristou enoikeitw en umin plousiws en pash sofia didaskontes kai nouqetountes eautous yalmois umnois wdais pneumatikais en th xariti adontes en tais kardiais umwn tw qew
col 3:17 kai pan o ti ean poihte en logw h en ergw panta en onomati kuriou ihsou euxaristountes tw qew patri di autou.
col 3:18 ai gunaikes upotassesqe tois andrasin ws anhken en kuriw.
col 3:19 oi andres agapate tas gunaikas kai mh pikrainesqe pros autas.
col 3:20 ta tekna upakouete tois goneusin kata panta touto gar euareston estin en kuriw.
col 3:21 oi pateres mh ereqizete ta tekna umwn ina mh aqumwsin.
col 3:22 oi douloi upakouete kata panta tois kata sarka kuriois mh en ofqalmodoulia ws anqrwpareskoi all en aplothti kardias foboumenoi ton kurion.
col 3:23 o ean poihte ek yuxhs ergazesqe ws tw kuriw kai ouk anqrwpois
col 3:24 eidotes oti apo kuriou apolhmyesqe thn antapodosin ths klhronomias. tw kuriw xristw douleuete
col 3:25 o gar adikwn komisetai o hdikhsen kai ouk estin proswpolhmyia.
col 4:1 oi kurioi to dikaion kai thn isothta tois doulois parexesqe eidotes oti kai umeis exete kurion en ouranw.
col 4:2 th proseuxh proskartereite grhgorountes en auth en euxaristia
col 4:3 proseuxomenoi ama kai peri hmwn ina o qeos anoich hmin quran tou logou lalhsai to musthrion tou xristou di o kai dedemai
col 4:4 ina fanerwsw auto ws dei me lalhsai.
col 4:5 en sofia peripateite pros tous ecw ton kairon ecagorazomenoi.
col 4:6 o logos umwn pantote en xariti alati hrtumenos eidenai pws dei umas eni ekastw apokrinesqai.
col 4:7 ta kat eme panta gnwrisei umin tuxikos o agaphtos adelfos kai pistos diakonos kai sundoulos en kuriw
col 4:8 on epemya pros umas eis auto touto ina gnwte ta peri hmwn kai parakalesh tas kardias umwn
col 4:9 sun onhsimw tw pistw kai agaphtw adelfw os estin ec umwn panta umin gnwrisousin ta wde.
col 4:10 aspazetai umas aristarxos o sunaixmalwtos mou kai markos o aneyios barnaba peri ou elabete entolas ean elqh pros umas decasqe auton
col 4:11 kai ihsous o legomenos ioustos oi ontes ek peritomhs outoi monoi sunergoi eis thn basileian tou qeou oitines egenhqhsan moi parhgoria.
col 4:12 aspazetai umas epafras o ec umwn doulos xristou ihsou pantote agwnizomenos uper umwn en tais proseuxais ina staqhte teleioi kai peplhroforhmenoi en panti qelhmati tou qeou.
col 4:13 marturw gar autw oti exei polun ponon uper umwn kai twn en laodikeia kai twn en ierapolei.
col 4:14 aspazetai umas loukas o iatros o agaphtos kai dhmas.
col 4:15 aspasasqe tous en laodikeia adelfous kai numfan kai thn kat oikon auths ekklhsian.
col 4:16 kai otan anagnwsqh par umin h epistolh poihsate ina kai en th laodikewn ekklhsia anagnwsqh kai thn ek laodikeias ina kai umeis anagnwte.
col 4:17 kai eipate arxippw blepe thn diakonian hn parelabes en kuriw ina authn plhrois.
col 4:18 o aspasmos th emh xeiri paulou. mnhmoneuete mou twn desmwn. h xaris meq umwn.
1th 1:1 paulos kai silouanos kai timoqeos th ekklhsia qessalonikewn en qew patri kai kuriw ihsou xristw xaris umin kai eirhnh.
1th 1:2 euxaristoumen tw qew pantote peri pantwn umwn mneian poioumenoi epi twn proseuxwn hmwn adialeiptws
1th 1:3 mnhmoneuontes umwn tou ergou ths pistews kai tou kopou ths agaphs kai ths upomonhs ths elpidos tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou emprosqen tou qeou kai patros hmwn
1th 1:4 eidotes adelfoi hgaphmenoi upo tou qeou thn ekloghn umwn
1th 1:5 oti to euaggelion hmwn ouk egenhqh eis umas en logw monon alla kai en dunamei kai en pneumati agiw kai en plhroforia pollh kaqws oidate oioi egenhqhmen en umin di umas.
1th 1:6 kai umeis mimhtai hmwn egenhqhte kai tou kuriou decamenoi ton logon en qliyei pollh meta xaras pneumatos agiou
1th 1:7 wste genesqai umas tupon pasin tois pisteuousin en th makedonia kai en th axaia.
1th 1:8 af umwn gar echxhtai o logos tou kuriou ou monon en th makedonia kai en th axaia all en panti topw h pistis umwn h pros ton qeon ecelhluqen wste mh xreian exein hmas lalein ti
1th 1:9 autoi gar peri hmwn apaggellousin opoian eisodon esxomen pros umas kai pws epestreyate pros ton qeon apo twn eidwlwn douleuein qew zwnti kai alhqinw
1th 1:10 kai anamenein ton uion autou ek twn ouranwn on hgeiren ek twn nekrwn ihsoun ton ruomenon hmas ek ths orghs ths erxomenhs.
1th 2:1 autoi gar oidate adelfoi thn eisodon hmwn thn pros umas oti ou kenh gegonen
1th 2:2 alla propaqontes kai ubrisqentes kaqws oidate en filippois eparrhsiasameqa en tw qew hmwn lalhsai pros umas to euaggelion tou qeou en pollw agwni.
1th 2:3 h gar paraklhsis hmwn ouk ek planhs oude ec akaqarsias oude en dolw
1th 2:4 alla kaqws dedokimasmeqa upo tou qeou pisteuqhnai to euaggelion outws laloumen oux ws anqrwpois areskontes alla qew tw dokimazonti tas kardias hmwn.
1th 2:5 oute gar pote en logw kolakeias egenhqhmen kaqws oidate oute en profasei pleonecias qeos martus
1th 2:6 oute zhtountes ec anqrwpwn docan oute af umwn oute ap allwn
1th 2:7 dunamenoi en barei einai ws xristou apostoloi alla egenhqhmen [hpioi] en mesw umwn. ws ean trofos qalph ta eauths tekna
1th 2:8 outws omeiromenoi umwn eudokoumen metadounai umin ou monon to euaggelion tou qeou alla kai tas eautwn yuxas dioti agaphtoi hmin egenhqhte.
1th 2:9 mnhmoneuete gar adelfoi ton kopon hmwn kai ton moxqon nuktos kai hmeras ergazomenoi pros to mh epibarhsai tina umwn ekhrucamen eis umas to euaggelion tou qeou.
1th 2:10 umeis martures kai o qeos ws osiws kai dikaiws kai amemptws umin tois pisteuousin egenhqhmen
1th 2:11 kaqaper oidate ws ena ekaston umwn ws pathr tekna eautou
1th 2:12 parakalountes umas kai paramuqoumenoi kai marturomenoi eis to peripatein umas aciws tou qeou tou [kalesantos] umas eis thn eautou basileian kai docan.
1th 2:13 kai dia touto kai hmeis euxaristoumen tw qew adialeiptws oti paralabontes logon akohs par hmwn tou qeou edecasqe ou logon anqrwpwn alla kaqws estin alhqws logon qeou os kai energeitai en umin tois pisteuousin.
1th 2:14 umeis gar mimhtai egenhqhte adelfoi twn ekklhsiwn tou qeou twn ouswn en th ioudaia en xristw ihsou oti ta auta epaqete kai umeis upo twn idiwn sumfuletwn kaqws kai autoi upo twn ioudaiwn
1th 2:15 twn kai ton kurion apokteinantwn ihsoun kai tous profhtas kai hmas ekdiwcantwn kai qew mh areskontwn kai pasin anqrwpois enantiwn
1th 2:16 kwluontwn hmas tois eqnesin lalhsai ina swqwsin eis to anaplhrwsai autwn tas amartias pantote. efqasen de ep autous h orgh eis telos.
1th 2:17 hmeis de adelfoi aporfanisqentes af umwn pros kairon wras proswpw ou kardia perissoterws espoudasamen to proswpon umwn idein en pollh epiqumia.
1th 2:18 dioti hqelhsamen elqein pros umas egw men paulos kai apac kai dis kai enekoyen hmas o satanas.
1th 2:19 tis gar hmwn elpis h xara h stefanos kauxhsews h ouxi kai umeis emprosqen tou kuriou hmwn ihsou en th autou parousia;
1th 2:20 umeis gar este h doca hmwn kai h xara.
1th 3:1 dio mhketi stegontes eudokhsamen kataleifqhnai en aqhnais monoi
1th 3:2 kai epemyamen timoqeon ton adelfon hmwn kai [diakonon] tou qeou en tw euaggeliw tou xristou eis to sthricai umas kai parakalesai uper ths pistews umwn
1th 3:3 to mhdena sainesqai en tais qliyesin tautais. autoi gar oidate oti eis touto keimeqa
1th 3:4 kai gar ote pros umas hmen proelegomen umin oti mellomen qlibesqai kaqws kai egeneto kai oidate.
1th 3:5 dia touto kagw mhketi stegwn epemya eis to gnwnai thn pistin umwn mh pws epeirasen umas o peirazwn kai eis kenon genhtai o kopos hmwn.
1th 3:6 arti de elqontos timoqeou pros hmas af umwn kai euaggelisamenou hmin thn pistin kai thn agaphn umwn kai oti exete mneian hmwn agaqhn pantote epipoqountes hmas idein kaqaper kai hmeis umas
1th 3:7 dia touto pareklhqhmen adelfoi ef umin epi pash th anagkh kai qliyei hmwn dia ths umwn pistews
1th 3:8 oti nun zwmen ean umeis sthkete en kuriw.
1th 3:9 tina gar euxaristian dunameqa tw qew antapodounai peri umwn epi pash th xara h xairomen di umas emprosqen tou qeou hmwn
1th 3:10 nuktos kai hmeras uperekperissou deomenoi eis to idein umwn to proswpon kai katartisai ta usterhmata ths pistews umwn;
1th 3:11 autos de o qeos kai pathr hmwn kai o kurios hmwn ihsous kateuqunai thn odon hmwn pros umas
1th 3:12 umas de o kurios pleonasai kai perisseusai th agaph eis allhlous kai eis pantas kaqaper kai hmeis eis umas
1th 3:13 eis to sthricai umwn tas kardias amemptous en agiwsunh emprosqen tou qeou kai patros hmwn en th parousia tou kuriou hmwn ihsou meta pantwn twn agiwn autou [--]. 
1th 4:1 loipon oun adelfoi erwtwmen umas kai parakaloumen en kuriw ihsou ina kaqws parelabete par hmwn to pws dei umas peripatein kai areskein qew kaqws kai peripateite ina perisseuhte mallon.
1th 4:2 oidate gar tinas paraggelias edwkamen umin dia tou kuriou ihsou.
1th 4:3 touto gar estin qelhma tou qeou o agiasmos umwn apexesqai umas apo ths porneias
1th 4:4 eidenai ekaston umwn to eautou skeuos ktasqai en agiasmw kai timh
1th 4:5 mh en paqei epiqumias kaqaper kai ta eqnh ta mh eidota ton qeon
1th 4:6 to mh uperbainein kai pleonektein en tw pragmati ton adelfon autou dioti ekdikos kurios peri pantwn toutwn kaqws kai proeipamen umin kai diemarturameqa.
1th 4:7 ou gar ekalesen hmas o qeos epi akaqarsia all en agiasmw.
1th 4:8 toigaroun o aqetwn ouk anqrwpon aqetei alla ton qeon ton kai didonta to pneuma autou to agion eis umas.
1th 4:9 peri de ths filadelfias ou xreian exete grafein umin autoi gar umeis qeodidaktoi este eis to agapan allhlous
1th 4:10 kai gar poieite auto eis pantas tous adelfous tous en olh th makedonia. parakaloumen de umas adelfoi perisseuein mallon
1th 4:11 kai filotimeisqai hsuxazein kai prassein ta idia kai ergazesqai tais [--] xersin umwn kaqws umin parhggeilamen
1th 4:12 ina peripathte eusxhmonws pros tous ecw kai mhdenos xreian exhte.
1th 4:13 ou qelomen de umas agnoein adelfoi peri twn koimwmenwn ina mh luphsqe kaqws kai oi loipoi oi mh exontes elpida.
1th 4:14 ei gar pisteuomen oti ihsous apeqanen kai anesth outws kai o qeos tous koimhqentas dia tou ihsou acei sun autw.
1th 4:15 touto gar umin legomen en logw kuriou oti hmeis oi zwntes oi perileipomenoi eis thn parousian tou kuriou ou mh fqaswmen tous koimhqentas
1th 4:16 oti autos o kurios en keleusmati en fwnh arxaggelou kai en salpiggi qeou katabhsetai ap ouranou kai oi nekroi en xristw anasthsontai prwton
1th 4:17 epeita hmeis oi zwntes oi perileipomenoi ama sun autois arpaghsomeqa en nefelais eis apanthsin tou kuriou eis aera kai outws pantote sun kuriw esomeqa.
1th 4:18 wste parakaleite allhlous en tois logois toutois.
1th 5:1 peri de twn xronwn kai twn kairwn adelfoi ou xreian exete umin grafesqai
1th 5:2 autoi gar akribws oidate oti hmera kuriou ws klepths en nukti outws erxetai.
1th 5:3 otan legwsin eirhnh kai asfaleia tote aifnidios autois efistatai oleqros wsper h wdin th en gastri exoush kai ou mh ekfugwsin.
1th 5:4 umeis de adelfoi ouk este en skotei ina h hmera umas ws klepths katalabh
1th 5:5 pantes gar umeis uioi fwtos este kai uioi hmeras. ouk esmen nuktos oude skotous
1th 5:6 ara oun mh kaqeudwmen ws oi loipoi alla grhgorwmen kai nhfwmen.
1th 5:7 oi gar kaqeudontes nuktos kaqeudousin kai oi mequskomenoi nuktos mequousin
1th 5:8 hmeis de hmeras ontes nhfwmen endusamenoi qwraka pistews kai agaphs kai perikefalaian elpida swthrias
1th 5:9 oti ouk eqeto hmas o qeos eis orghn alla eis peripoihsin swthrias dia tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou
1th 5:10 tou apoqanontos uper hmwn ina eite grhgorwmen eite kaqeudwmen ama sun autw zhswmen.
1th 5:11 dio parakaleite allhlous kai oikodomeite eis ton ena kaqws kai poieite.
1th 5:12 erwtwmen de umas adelfoi eidenai tous kopiwntas en umin kai proistamenous umwn en kuriw kai nouqetountas umas
1th 5:13 kai hgeisqai autous uperekperissou en agaph dia to ergon autwn. eirhneuete en eautois.
1th 5:14 parakaloumen de umas adelfoi nouqeteite tous ataktous paramuqeisqe tous oligoyuxous antexesqe twn asqenwn makroqumeite pros pantas.
1th 5:15 orate mh tis kakon anti kakou tini apodw alla pantote to agaqon diwkete kai eis allhlous kai eis pantas.
1th 5:16 pantote xairete
1th 5:17 adialeiptws proseuxesqe
1th 5:18 en panti euxaristeite touto gar qelhma qeou en xristw ihsou eis umas.
1th 5:19 to pneuma mh sbennute
1th 5:20 profhteias mh ecouqeneite
1th 5:21 panta de dokimazete to kalon katexete
1th 5:22 apo pantos eidous ponhrou apexesqe.
1th 5:23 autos de o qeos ths eirhnhs agiasai umas oloteleis kai oloklhron umwn to pneuma kai h yuxh kai to swma amemptws en th parousia tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou thrhqeih.
1th 5:24 pistos o kalwn umas os kai poihsei.
1th 5:25 adelfoi proseuxesqe kai peri hmwn.
1th 5:26 aspasasqe tous adelfous pantas en filhmati agiw.
1th 5:27 enorkizw umas ton kurion anagnwsqhnai thn epistolhn pasin tois adelfois.
1th 5:28 h xaris tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou meq umwn.
2th 1:1 paulos kai silouanos kai timoqeos th ekklhsia qessalonikewn en qew patri hmwn kai kuriw ihsou xristw
2th 1:2 xaris umin kai eirhnh apo qeou patros hmwn kai kuriou ihsou xristou.
2th 1:3 euxaristein ofeilomen tw qew pantote peri umwn adelfoi kaqws acion estin oti uperaucanei h pistis umwn kai pleonazei h agaph enos ekastou pantwn umwn eis allhlous
2th 1:4 wste autous hmas en umin egkauxasqai en tais ekklhsiais tou qeou uper ths upomonhs umwn kai pistews en pasin tois diwgmois umwn kai tais qliyesin ais anexesqe
2th 1:5 endeigma ths dikaias krisews tou qeou eis to kataciwqhnai umas ths basileias tou qeou uper hs kai pasxete
2th 1:6 eiper dikaion para qew antapodounai tois qlibousin umas qliyin
2th 1:7 kai umin tois qlibomenois anesin meq hmwn en th apokaluyei tou kuriou ihsou ap ouranou met aggelwn dunamews autou
2th 1:8 en puri flogos didontos ekdikhsin tois mh eidosin qeon kai tois mh upakouousin tw euaggeliw tou kuriou hmwn ihsou
2th 1:9 oitines dikhn tisousin oleqron aiwnion apo proswpou tou kuriou kai apo ths dochs ths isxuos autou
2th 1:10 otan elqh endocasqhnai en tois agiois autou kai qaumasqhnai en pasin tois pisteusasin oti episteuqh to marturion hmwn ef umas en th hmera ekeinh.
2th 1:11 eis o kai proseuxomeqa pantote peri umwn ina umas aciwsh ths klhsews o qeos hmwn kai plhrwsh pasan eudokian agaqwsunhs kai ergon pistews en dunamei
2th 1:12 opws endocasqh to onoma tou kuriou hmwn ihsou en umin kai umeis en autw kata thn xarin tou qeou hmwn kai kuriou ihsou xristou.
2th 2:1 erwtwmen de umas adelfoi uper ths parousias tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou kai hmwn episunagwghs ep auton
2th 2:2 eis to mh taxews saleuqhnai umas apo tou noos mhde qroeisqai mhte dia pneumatos mhte dia logou mhte di epistolhs ws di hmwn ws oti enesthken h hmera tou kuriou.
2th 2:3 mh tis umas ecapathsh kata mhdena tropon oti ean mh elqh h apostasia prwton kai apokalufqh o anqrwpos ths anomias o uios ths apwleias
2th 2:4 o antikeimenos kai uperairomenos epi panta legomenon qeon h sebasma wste auton eis ton naon tou qeou kaqisai apodeiknunta eauton oti estin qeos.
2th 2:5 ou mnhmoneuete oti eti wn pros umas tauta elegon umin;
2th 2:6 kai nun to katexon oidate eis to apokalufqhnai auton en tw eautou kairw.
2th 2:7 to gar musthrion hdh energeitai ths anomias monon o katexwn arti ews ek mesou genhtai.
2th 2:8 kai tote apokalufqhsetai o anomos on o kurios ihsous anelei tw pneumati tou stomatos autou kai katarghsei th epifaneia ths parousias autou
2th 2:9 ou estin h parousia kat energeian tou satana en pash dunamei kai shmeiois kai terasin yeudous
2th 2:10 kai en pash apath adikias tois apollumenois anq wn thn agaphn ths alhqeias ouk edecanto eis to swqhnai autous.
2th 2:11 kai dia touto pempei autois o qeos energeian planhs eis to pisteusai autous tw yeudei
2th 2:12 ina kriqwsin pantes oi mh pisteusantes th alhqeia alla eudokhsantes th adikia.
2th 2:13 hmeis de ofeilomen euxaristein tw qew pantote peri umwn adelfoi hgaphmenoi upo kuriou oti eilato umas o qeos [ap arxhs] eis swthrian en agiasmw pneumatos kai pistei alhqeias
2th 2:14 eis o kai ekalesen umas dia tou euaggeliou hmwn eis peripoihsin dochs tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou.
2th 2:15 ara oun adelfoi sthkete kai krateite tas paradoseis as edidaxqhte eite dia logou eite di epistolhs hmwn.
2th 2:16 autos de o kurios hmwn ihsous xristos kai o qeos o pathr hmwn o agaphsas hmas kai dous paraklhsin aiwnian kai elpida agaqhn en xariti
2th 2:17 parakalesai umwn tas kardias kai sthricai en panti ergw kai logw agaqw.
2th 3:1 to loipon proseuxesqe adelfoi peri hmwn ina o logos tou kuriou trexh kai docazhtai kaqws kai pros umas
2th 3:2 kai ina rusqwmen apo twn atopwn kai ponhrwn anqrwpwn ou gar pantwn h pistis.
2th 3:3 pistos de estin o kurios os sthricei umas kai fulacei apo tou ponhrou.
2th 3:4 pepoiqamen de en kuriw ef umas oti a paraggellomen kai poieite kai poihsete.
2th 3:5 o de kurios kateuqunai umwn tas kardias eis thn agaphn tou qeou kai eis thn upomonhn tou xristou.
2th 3:6 paraggellomen de umin adelfoi en onomati tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou stellesqai umas apo pantos adelfou ataktws peripatountos kai mh kata thn paradosin hn [parelaben] par hmwn.
2th 3:7 autoi gar oidate pws dei mimeisqai hmas oti ouk htakthsamen en umin
2th 3:8 oude dwrean arton efagomen para tinos all en kopw kai moxqw nuktos kai hmeras ergazomenoi pros to mh epibarhsai tina umwn
2th 3:9 oux oti ouk exomen ecousian all ina eautous tupon dwmen umin eis to mimeisqai hmas.
2th 3:10 kai gar ote hmen pros umas touto parhggellomen umin oti ei tis ou qelei ergazesqai mhde esqietw.
2th 3:11 akouomen gar tinas peripatountas en umin ataktws mhden ergazomenous alla periergazomenous
2th 3:12 tois de toioutois paraggellomen kai parakaloumen en kuriw ihsou xristw ina meta hsuxias ergazomenoi ton eautwn arton esqiwsin.
2th 3:13 umeis de adelfoi mh egkakhshte kalopoiountes.
2th 3:14 ei de tis oux upakouei tw logw hmwn dia ths epistolhs touton shmeiousqe mh sunanamignusqai autw ina entraph
2th 3:15 kai mh ws exqron hgeisqe alla nouqeteite ws adelfon.
2th 3:16 autos de o kurios ths eirhnhs dwh umin thn eirhnhn dia pantos en panti tropw. o kurios meta pantwn umwn.
2th 3:17 o aspasmos th emh xeiri paulou o estin shmeion en pash epistolh outws grafw.
2th 3:18 h xaris tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou meta pantwn umwn.
1ti 1:1 paulos apostolos xristou ihsou kat epitaghn qeou swthros hmwn kai xristou ihsou ths elpidos hmwn
1ti 1:2 timoqew gnhsiw teknw en pistei xaris eleos eirhnh apo qeou patros kai xristou ihsou tou kuriou hmwn.
1ti 1:3 kaqws parekalesa se prosmeinai en efesw poreuomenos eis makedonian ina paraggeilhs tisin mh eterodidaskalein
1ti 1:4 mhde prosexein muqois kai genealogiais aperantois aitines ekzhthseis parexousin mallon h oikonomian qeou thn en pistei
1ti 1:5 to de telos ths paraggelias estin agaph ek kaqaras kardias kai suneidhsews agaqhs kai pistews anupokritou
1ti 1:6 wn tines astoxhsantes ecetraphsan eis mataiologian
1ti 1:7 qelontes einai nomodidaskaloi mh noountes mhte a legousin mhte peri tinwn diabebaiountai.
1ti 1:8 oidamen de oti kalos o nomos ean tis autw nomimws xrhtai
1ti 1:9 eidws touto oti dikaiw nomos ou keitai anomois de kai anupotaktois asebesi kai amartwlois anosiois kai bebhlois patrolwais kai mhtrolwais androfonois
1ti 1:10 pornois arsenokoitais andrapodistais yeustais epiorkois kai ei ti eteron th ugiainoush didaskalia antikeitai
1ti 1:11 kata to euaggelion ths dochs tou makariou qeou o episteuqhn egw.
1ti 1:12 xarin exw tw endunamwsanti me xristw ihsou tw kuriw hmwn oti piston me hghsato qemenos eis diakonian
1ti 1:13 to proteron onta blasfhmon kai diwkthn kai ubristhn alla hlehqhn oti agnown epoihsa en apistia
1ti 1:14 uperepleonasen de h xaris tou kuriou hmwn meta pistews kai agaphs ths en xristw ihsou.
1ti 1:15 pistos o logos kai pashs apodoxhs acios oti xristos ihsous hlqen eis ton kosmon amartwlous swsai wn prwtos eimi egw
1ti 1:16 alla dia touto hlehqhn ina en emoi prwtw endeichtai xristos ihsous thn apasan makroqumian pros upotupwsin twn mellontwn pisteuein ep autw eis zwhn aiwnion.
1ti 1:17 tw de basilei twn aiwnwn afqartw aoratw monw qew timh kai doca eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn amhn.
1ti 1:18 tauthn thn paraggelian paratiqemai soi teknon timoqee kata tas proagousas epi se profhteias ina strateuh en autais thn kalhn strateian
1ti 1:19 exwn pistin kai agaqhn suneidhsin hn tines apwsamenoi peri thn pistin enauaghsan
1ti 1:20 wn estin umenaios kai alecandros ous paredwka tw satana ina paideuqwsin mh blasfhmein.
1ti 2:1 parakalw oun prwton pantwn poieisqai dehseis proseuxas enteuceis euxaristias uper pantwn anqrwpwn
1ti 2:2 uper basilewn kai pantwn twn en uperoxh ontwn ina hremon kai hsuxion bion diagwmen en pash eusebeia kai semnothti.
1ti 2:3 touto kalon kai apodekton enwpion tou swthros hmwn qeou
1ti 2:4 os pantas anqrwpous qelei swqhnai kai eis epignwsin alhqeias elqein.
1ti 2:5 eis gar qeos eis kai mesiths qeou kai anqrwpwn anqrwpos xristos ihsous
1ti 2:6 o dous eauton antilutron uper pantwn to marturion kairois idiois
1ti 2:7 eis o eteqhn egw khruc kai apostolos alhqeian legw ou yeudomai didaskalos eqnwn en pistei kai alhqeia.
1ti 2:8 boulomai oun proseuxesqai tous andras en panti topw epairontas osious xeiras xwris orghs kai dialogismou
1ti 2:9 wsautws kai gunaikas en katastolh kosmiw meta aidous kai swfrosunhs kosmein eautas mh en plegmasin kai xrusiw h margaritais h imatismw polutelei
1ti 2:10 all o prepei gunaicin epaggellomenais qeosebeian di ergwn agaqwn.
1ti 2:11 gunh en hsuxia manqanetw en pash upotagh
1ti 2:12 didaskein de gunaiki ouk epitrepw oude auqentein andros all einai en hsuxia.
1ti 2:13 adam gar prwtos eplasqh eita eua
1ti 2:14 kai adam ouk hpathqh h de gunh ecapathqeisa en parabasei gegonen.
1ti 2:15 swqhsetai de dia ths teknogonias ean meinwsin en pistei kai agaph kai agiasmw meta swfrosunhs.
1ti 3:1 pistos o logos ei tis episkophs oregetai kalou ergou epiqumei.
1ti 3:2 dei oun ton episkopon anepilhmpton einai mias gunaikos andra nhfalion swfrona kosmion filocenon didaktikon
1ti 3:3 mh paroinon mh plhkthn alla epieikh amaxon afilarguron
1ti 3:4 tou idiou oikou kalws proistamenon tekna exonta en upotagh meta pashs semnothtos
1ti 3:5 ei de tis tou idiou oikou prosthnai ouk oiden pws ekklhsias qeou epimelhsetai;
1ti 3:6 mh neofuton ina mh tufwqeis eis krima empesh tou diabolou.
1ti 3:7 dei de kai marturian kalhn exein apo twn ecwqen ina mh eis oneidismon empesh kai pagida tou diabolou.
1ti 3:8 diakonous wsautws semnous mh dilogous mh oinw pollw prosexontas mh aisxrokerdeis
1ti 3:9 exontas to musthrion ths pistews en kaqara suneidhsei.
1ti 3:10 kai outoi de dokimazesqwsan prwton eita diakoneitwsan anegklhtoi ontes.
1ti 3:11 gunaikas wsautws semnas mh diabolous nhfalious pistas en pasin.
1ti 3:12 diakonoi estwsan mias gunaikos andres teknwn kalws proistamenoi kai twn idiwn oikwn
1ti 3:13 oi gar kalws diakonhsantes baqmon eautois kalon peripoiountai kai pollhn parrhsian en pistei th en xristw ihsou.
1ti 3:14 tauta soi grafw elpizwn elqein pros se en taxei
1ti 3:15 ean de bradunw ina eidhs pws dei en oikw qeou anastrefesqai htis estin ekklhsia qeou zwntos stulos kai edraiwma ths alhqeias.
1ti 3:16 kai omologoumenws mega estin to ths eusebeias musthrion os efanerwqh en sarki edikaiwqh en pneumati wfqh aggelois ekhruxqh en eqnesin episteuqh en kosmw anelhmfqh en doch.
1ti 4:1 to de pneuma rhtws legei oti en usterois kairois aposthsontai tines ths pistews prosexontes pneumasin planois kai didaskaliais daimoniwn
1ti 4:2 en upokrisei yeudologwn kekausthriasmenwn thn idian suneidhsin
1ti 4:3 kwluontwn gamein apexesqai brwmatwn a o qeos ektisen eis metalhmyin meta euxaristias tois pistois kai epegnwkosi thn alhqeian.
1ti 4:4 oti pan ktisma qeou kalon kai ouden apoblhton meta euxaristias lambanomenon
1ti 4:5 agiazetai gar dia logou qeou kai enteucews.
1ti 4:6 tauta upotiqemenos tois adelfois kalos esh diakonos xristou ihsou entrefomenos tois logois ths pistews kai ths kalhs didaskalias h parhkolouqhkas
1ti 4:7 tous de bebhlous kai grawdeis muqous paraitou. gumnaze de seauton pros eusebeian
1ti 4:8 h gar swmatikh gumnasia pros oligon estin wfelimos h de eusebeia pros panta wfelimos estin epaggelian exousa zwhs ths nun kai ths melloushs.
1ti 4:9 pistos o logos kai pashs apodoxhs acios
1ti 4:10 eis touto gar kopiwmen kai [oneidizomeqa] oti hlpikamen epi qew zwnti os estin swthr pantwn anqrwpwn malista pistwn.
1ti 4:11 paraggelle tauta kai didaske.
1ti 4:12 mhdeis sou ths neothtos katafroneitw alla tupos ginou twn pistwn en logw en anastrofh en agaph en pistei en agneia.
1ti 4:13 ews erxomai prosexe th anagnwsei th paraklhsei th didaskalia.
1ti 4:14 mh amelei tou en soi xarismatos o edoqh soi dia profhteias meta epiqesews twn xeirwn tou presbuteriou.
1ti 4:15 tauta meleta en toutois isqi ina sou h prokoph fanera h pasin.
1ti 4:16 epexe seautw kai th didaskalia epimene autois touto gar poiwn kai seauton swseis kai tous akouontas sou.
1ti 5:1 presbuterw mh epiplhchs alla parakalei ws patera newterous ws adelfous
1ti 5:2 presbuteras ws mhteras newteras ws adelfas en pash agneia.
1ti 5:3 xhras tima tas ontws xhras.
1ti 5:4 ei de tis xhra tekna h ekgona exei manqanetwsan prwton ton idion oikon eusebein kai amoibas apodidonai tois progonois touto gar estin apodekton enwpion tou qeou.
1ti 5:5 h de ontws xhra kai memonwmenh hlpiken epi qeon kai prosmenei tais dehsesin kai tais proseuxais nuktos kai hmeras
1ti 5:6 h de spatalwsa zwsa teqnhken.
1ti 5:7 kai tauta paraggelle ina anepilhmptoi wsin.
1ti 5:8 ei de tis twn idiwn kai malista oikeiwn ou pronoei thn pistin hrnhtai kai estin apistou xeirwn.
1ti 5:9 xhra katalegesqw mh elatton etwn echkonta gegonuia enos andros gunh
1ti 5:10 en ergois kalois marturoumenh ei eteknotrofhsen ei ecenodoxhsen ei agiwn podas eniyen ei qlibomenois ephrkesen ei panti ergw agaqw ephkolouqhsen.
1ti 5:11 newteras de xhras paraitou otan gar katastrhniaswsin tou xristou gamein qelousin
1ti 5:12 exousai krima oti thn prwthn pistin hqethsan
1ti 5:13 ama de kai argai manqanousin perierxomenai tas oikias ou monon de argai alla kai fluaroi kai periergoi lalousai ta mh deonta.
1ti 5:14 boulomai oun newteras gamein teknogonein oikodespotein mhdemian aformhn didonai tw antikeimenw loidorias xarin
1ti 5:15 hdh gar tines ecetraphsan opisw tou satana.
1ti 5:16 ei tis pisth exei xhras eparkeitw autais kai mh bareisqw h ekklhsia ina tais ontws xhrais eparkesh.
1ti 5:17 oi kalws proestwtes presbuteroi diplhs timhs aciousqwsan malista oi kopiwntes en logw kai didaskalia
1ti 5:18 legei gar h grafh boun alownta ou fimwseis kai acios o ergaths tou misqou autou.
1ti 5:19 kata presbuterou kathgorian mh paradexou ektos ei mh epi duo h triwn marturwn.
1ti 5:20 tous amartanontas enwpion pantwn elegxe ina kai oi loipoi fobon exwsin.
1ti 5:21 diamarturomai enwpion tou qeou kai xristou ihsou kai twn eklektwn aggelwn ina tauta fulachs xwris prokrimatos mhden poiwn kata prosklisin.
1ti 5:22 xeiras taxews mhdeni epitiqei mhde koinwnei amartiais allotriais seauton agnon threi.
1ti 5:23 mhketi udropotei alla oinw oligw xrw dia ton stomaxon kai tas puknas sou asqeneias.
1ti 5:24 tinwn anqrwpwn ai amartiai prodhloi eisin proagousai eis krisin tisin de kai epakolouqousin
1ti 5:25 wsautws kai ta erga ta kala prodhla kai ta allws exonta krubhnai ou dunantai.
1ti 6:1 osoi eisin upo zugon douloi tous idious despotas pashs timhs acious hgeisqwsan ina mh to onoma tou qeou kai h didaskalia blasfhmhtai.
1ti 6:2 oi de pistous exontes despotas mh katafroneitwsan oti adelfoi eisin alla mallon douleuetwsan oti pistoi eisin kai agaphtoi oi ths euergesias antilambanomenoi. tauta didaske kai parakalei.
1ti 6:3 ei tis eterodidaskalei kai mh proserxetai ugiainousin logois tois tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou kai th kat eusebeian didaskalia
1ti 6:4 tetufwtai mhden epistamenos alla noswn peri zhthseis kai logomaxias ec wn ginetai fqonos eris blasfhmiai uponoiai ponhrai
1ti 6:5 diaparatribai diefqarmenwn anqrwpwn ton noun kai apesterhmenwn ths alhqeias nomizontwn porismon einai thn eusebeian.
1ti 6:6 estin de porismos megas h eusebeia meta autarkeias
1ti 6:7 ouden gar eishnegkamen eis ton kosmon oti oude ecenegkein ti dunameqa
1ti 6:8 exontes de diatrofas kai skepasmata toutois arkesqhsomeqa.
1ti 6:9 oi de boulomenoi ploutein empiptousin eis peirasmon kai pagida kai epiqumias pollas anohtous kai blaberas aitines buqizousin tous anqrwpous eis oleqron kai apwleian
1ti 6:10 riza gar pantwn twn kakwn estin h filarguria hs tines oregomenoi apeplanhqhsan apo ths pistews kai eautous periepeiran odunais pollais.
1ti 6:11 su de w anqrwpe qeou tauta feuge diwke de dikaiosunhn eusebeian pistin agaphn upomonhn praupaqian.
1ti 6:12 agwnizou ton kalon agwna ths pistews epilabou ths aiwniou zwhs eis hn eklhqhs kai wmologhsas thn kalhn omologian enwpion pollwn marturwn.
1ti 6:13 paraggellw [soi] enwpion tou qeou tou zwogonountos ta panta kai xristou ihsou tou marturhsantos epi pontiou pilatou thn kalhn omologian
1ti 6:14 thrhsai se thn entolhn aspilon anepilhmpton mexri ths epifaneias tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou
1ti 6:15 hn kairois idiois deicei o makarios kai monos dunasths o basileus twn basileuontwn kai kurios twn kurieuontwn
1ti 6:16 o monos exwn aqanasian fws oikwn aprositon on eiden oudeis anqrwpwn oude idein dunatai w timh kai kratos aiwnion amhn.
1ti 6:17 tois plousiois en tw nun aiwni paraggelle mh uyhlofronein mhde hlpikenai epi ploutou adhlothti all epi qew tw parexonti hmin panta plousiws eis apolausin
1ti 6:18 agaqoergein ploutein en ergois kalois eumetadotous einai koinwnikous
1ti 6:19 apoqhsaurizontas eautois qemelion kalon eis to mellon ina epilabwntai ths ontws zwhs.
1ti 6:20 w timoqee thn paraqhkhn fulacon ektrepomenos tas bebhlous kenofwnias kai antiqeseis ths yeudwnumou gnwsews
1ti 6:21 hn tines epaggellomenoi peri thn pistin hstoxhsan [--].
2ti 1:1 paulos apostolos xristou ihsou dia qelhmatos qeou kat epaggelian zwhs ths en xristw ihsou
2ti 1:2 timoqew agaphtw teknw xaris eleos eirhnh apo qeou patros kai xristou ihsou tou kuriou hmwn.
2ti 1:3 xarin exw tw qew w latreuw apo progonwn en kaqara suneidhsei ws adialeipton exw thn peri sou mneian en tais dehsesin mou nuktos kai hmeras
2ti 1:4 epipoqwn se idein memnhmenos sou twn dakruwn ina xaras plhrwqw
2ti 1:5 upomnhsin labwn ths en soi anupokritou pistews htis enwkhsen prwton en th mammh sou lwidi kai th mhtri sou eunikh pepeismai de oti kai en soi.
2ti 1:6 di hn aitian anamimnhskw se anazwpurein to xarisma tou qeou o estin en soi dia ths epiqesews twn xeirwn mou
2ti 1:7 ou gar edwken hmin o qeos pneuma deilias alla dunamews kai agaphs kai swfronismou.
2ti 1:8 mh oun epaisxunqhs to marturion tou kuriou hmwn mhde eme ton desmion autou alla sugkakopaqhson tw euaggeliw kata dunamin qeou
2ti 1:9 tou swsantos hmas kai kalesantos klhsei agia ou kata ta erga hmwn alla kata idian proqesin kai xarin thn doqeisan hmin en xristw ihsou pro xronwn aiwniwn
2ti 1:10 fanerwqeisan de nun dia ths epifaneias tou swthros hmwn xristou ihsou katarghsantos men ton qanaton fwtisantos de zwhn kai afqarsian dia tou euaggeliou
2ti 1:11 eis o eteqhn egw khruc kai apostolos kai didaskalos [eqvwv].
2ti 1:12 di hn aitian kai tauta pasxw all ouk epaisxunomai oida gar w pepisteuka kai pepeismai oti dunatos estin thn paraqhkhn mou fulacai eis ekeinhn thn hmeran.
2ti 1:13 upotupwsin exe ugiainontwn logwn wn par emou hkousas en pistei kai agaph th en xristw ihsou
2ti 1:14 thn kalhn paraqhkhn fulacon dia pneumatos agiou tou enoikountos en hmin.
2ti 1:15 oidas touto oti apestrafhsan me pantes oi en th asia wn estin fugelos kai ermogenhs.
2ti 1:16 dwh eleos o kurios tw onhsiforou oikw oti pollakis me aneyucen kai thn alusin mou ouk epaisxunqh
2ti 1:17 alla genomenos en rwmh spoudaiws ezhthsen me kai euren
2ti 1:18 dwh autw o kurios eurein eleos para kuriou en ekeinh th hmera kai osa en efesw dihkonhsen beltion su ginwskeis.
2ti 2:1 su oun teknon mou endunamou en th xariti th en xristw ihsou
2ti 2:2 kai a hkousas par emou dia pollwn marturwn tauta paraqou pistois anqrwpois oitines ikanoi esontai kai eterous didacai.
2ti 2:3 sugkakopaqhson ws kalos stratiwths xristou ihsou.
2ti 2:4 oudeis strateuomenos empleketai tais tou biou pragmateiais ina tw stratologhsanti aresh
2ti 2:5 ean de kai aqlh tis ou stefanoutai ean mh nomimws aqlhsh.
2ti 2:6 ton kopiwnta gewrgon dei prwton twn karpwn metalambanein.
2ti 2:7 noei o legw dwsei gar soi o kurios sunesin en pasin.
2ti 2:8 mnhmoneue ihsoun xriston eghgermenon ek nekrwn ek spermatos dauid kata to euaggelion mou
2ti 2:9 en w kakopaqw mexri desmwn ws kakourgos alla o logos tou qeou ou dedetai.
2ti 2:10 dia touto panta upomenw dia tous eklektous ina kai autoi swthrias tuxwsin ths en xristw ihsou meta dochs aiwniou.
2ti 2:11 pistos o logos ei gar sunapeqanomen kai suzhsomen
2ti 2:12 ei upomenomen kai sumbasileusomen ei arnhsomeqa kakeinos arnhsetai hmas
2ti 2:13 ei apistoumen ekeinos pistos menei arnhsasqai gar eauton ou dunatai.
2ti 2:14 tauta upomimnhske diamarturomenos enwpion tou [kuriou] mh logomaxein ep ouden xrhsimon epi katastrofh twn akouontwn.
2ti 2:15 spoudason seauton dokimon parasthsai tw qew ergathn anepaisxunton orqotomounta ton logon ths alhqeias.
2ti 2:16 tas de bebhlous kenofwnias periistaso epi pleion gar prokoyousin asebeias
2ti 2:17 kai o logos autwn ws gaggraina nomhn ecei wn estin umenaios kai filhtos

heb 4:10 o gar eiselqwn eis thn katapausin autou kai autos katepausen apo twn ergwn autou wsper apo twn idiwn o qeos.
heb 4:11 spoudaswmen oun eiselqein eis ekeinhn thn katapausin ina mh en tw autw tis upodeigmati pesh ths apeiqeias.
heb 4:12 zwn gar o logos tou qeou kai energhs kai tomwteros uper pasan maxairan distomon kai diiknoumenos axri merismou yuxhs kai pneumatos armwn te kai muelwn kai kritikos enqumhsewn kai ennoiwn kardias
heb 4:13 kai ouk estin ktisis afanhs enwpion autou panta de gumna kai tetraxhlismena tois ofqalmois autou pros on hmin o logos.
heb 4:14 exontes oun arxierea megan dielhluqota tous ouranous ihsoun ton uion tou qeou kratwmen ths omologias
heb 4:15 ou gar exomen arxierea mh dunamenon sumpaqhsai tais asqeneiais hmwn pepeirasmenon de kata panta kaq omoiothta xwris amartias.
heb 4:16 proserxwmeqa oun meta parrhsias tw qronw ths xaritos ina labwmen eleos kai xarin eurwmen eis eukairon bohqeian.
heb 5:1 pas gar arxiereus ec anqrwpwn lambanomenos uper anqrwpwn kaqistatai ta pros ton qeon ina prosferh dwra te kai qusias uper amartiwn
heb 5:2 metriopaqein dunamenos tois agnoousin kai planwmenois epei kai autos perikeitai asqeneian
heb 5:3 kai di authn ofeilei kaqws peri tou laou outws kai peri autou prosferein peri amartiwn.
heb 5:4 kai oux eautw tis lambanei thn timhn alla kaloumenos upo tou qeou kaqwsper kai aarwn.
heb 5:5 outws kai o xristos oux eauton edocasen genhqhnai arxierea all o lalhsas pros auton uios mou ei su egw shmeron gegennhka se
heb 5:6 kaqws kai en eterw legei su iereus eis ton aiwna kata thn tacin melxisedek.
heb 5:7 os en tais hmerais ths sarkos autou dehseis te kai ikethrias pros ton dunamenon swzein auton ek qanatou meta kraughs isxuras kai dakruwn prosenegkas kai eisakousqeis apo ths eulabeias

heb 5:11 peri ou polus hmin o logos kai dusermhneutos legein epei nwqroi gegonate tais akoais.
heb 5:12 kai gar ofeilontes einai didaskaloi dia ton xronon palin xreian exete tou didaskein umas tina ta stoixeia ths arxhs twn logiwn tou qeou kai gegonate xreian exontes galaktos kai ou stereas trofhs.
heb 5:13 pas gar o metexwn galaktos apeiros logou dikaiosunhs nhpios gar estin
heb 5:14 teleiwn de estin h sterea trofh twn dia thn ecin ta aisqhthria gegumnasmena exontwn pros diakrisin kalou te kai kakou.
heb 6:1 dio afentes ton ths arxhs tou xristou logon epi thn teleiothta ferwmeqa mh palin qemelion kataballomenoi metanoias apo nekrwn ergwn kai pistews epi qeon

heb 6:3 kai touto poihsomen eanper epitreph o qeos.
heb 6:4 adunaton gar tous apac fwtisqentas geusamenous te ths dwreas ths epouraniou kai metoxous genhqentas pneumatos agiou

heb 6:10 ou gar adikos o qeos epilaqesqai tou ergou umwn kai ths agaphs hs enedeicasqe eis to onoma autou diakonhsantes tois agiois kai diakonountes.

heb 7:1 outos gar o melxisedek basileus salhm iereus tou qeou tou uyistou o sunanthsas abraam upostrefonti apo ths kophs twn basilewn kai euloghsas auton

heb 7:3 apatwr amhtwr agenealoghtos mhte arxhn hmerwn mhte zwhs telos exwn afwmoiwmenos de tw uiw tou qeou menei iereus eis to dihnekes.
heb 7:4 qewreite de phlikos outos w kai dekathn abraam edwken ek twn akroqiniwn o patriarxhs.
heb 7:5 kai oi men ek twn uiwn leui thn ierateian lambanontes entolhn exousin apodekatoun ton laon kata ton nomon tout estin tous adelfous autwn kaiper ecelhluqotas ek ths osfuos abraam

heb 7:9 kai ws epos eipein di abraam kai leui o dekatas lambanwn dedekatwtai
heb 7:10 eti gar en th osfui tou patros hn ote sunhnthsen autw melxisedek.
heb 7:11 ei men oun teleiwsis dia ths leuitikhs ierwsunhs hn o laos gar ep auths nenomoqethtai tis eti xreia kata thn tacin melxisedek eteron anistasqai ierea kai ou kata thn tacin aarwn legesqai;
heb 7:12 metatiqemenhs gar ths ierwsunhs ec anagkhs kai nomou metaqesis ginetai.
heb 7:13 ef on gar legetai tauta fulhs eteras metesxhken af hs oudeis prosesxhken tw qusiasthriw
heb 7:14 prodhlon gar oti ec iouda anatetalken o kurios hmwn eis hn fulhn peri ierewn ouden mwushs elalhsen.
heb 7:15 kai perissoteron eti katadhlon estin ei kata thn omoiothta melxisedek anistatai iereus eteros
heb 7:16 os ou kata nomon entolhs sarkinhs gegonen alla kata dunamin zwhs akatalutou
heb 7:17 martureitai gar oti su iereus eis ton aiwna kata thn tacin melxisedek.
heb 7:18 aqethsis men gar ginetai proagoushs entolhs dia to auths asqenes kai anwfeles
heb 7:19 ouden gar eteleiwsen o nomos epeisagwgh de kreittonos elpidos di hs eggizomen tw qew.
heb 7:20 kai kaq oson ou xwris orkwmosias oi men gar xwris orkwmosias eisin iereis gegonotes
heb 7:21 o de meta orkwmosias dia tou legontos pros auton wmosen kurios kai ou metamelhqhsetai su iereus eis ton aiwna
heb 7:22 kata tosouto kai kreittonos diaqhkhs gegonen egguos ihsous.

heb 7:24 o de dia to menein auton eis ton aiwna aparabaton exei thn ierwsunhn
heb 7:25 oqen kai swzein eis to panteles dunatai tous proserxomenous di autou tw qew pantote zwn eis to entugxanein uper autwn.
heb 7:26 toioutos gar hmin kai eprepen arxiereus osios akakos amiantos kexwrismenos apo twn amartwlwn kai uyhloteros twn ouranwn genomenos
heb 7:27 os ouk exei kaq hmeran anagkhn wsper oi arxiereis proteron uper twn idiwn amartiwn qusias anaferein epeita twn tou laou touto gar epoihsen efapac eauton anenegkas.

heb 9:1 eixe men oun [--] h prwth dikaiwmata latreias to te agion kosmikon.

heb 9:3 meta de to deuteron katapetasma skhnh h legomenh agia agiwn
heb 9:4 xrusoun exousa qumiathrion kai thn kibwton ths diaqhkhs perikekalummenhn pantoqen xrusiw en h stamnos xrush exousa to manna kai h rabdos aarwn h blasthsasa kai ai plakes ths diaqhkhs
heb 9:5 uperanw de auths xeroubin dochs kataskiazonta to ilasthrion peri wn ouk estin nun legein kata meros.
heb 9:6 toutwn de outws kateskeuasmenwn eis men thn prwthn skhnhn dia pantos eisiasin oi iereis tas latreias epitelountes
heb 9:7 eis de thn deuteran apac tou eniautou monos o arxiereus ou xwris aimatos o prosferei uper eautou kai twn tou laou agnohmatwn
heb 9:8 touto dhlountos tou pneumatos tou agiou mhpw pefanerwsqai thn twn agiwn odon eti ths prwths skhnhs exoushs stasin
heb 9:9 htis parabolh eis ton kairon ton enesthkota kaq hn dwra te kai qusiai prosferontai mh dunamenai kata suneidhsin teleiwsai ton latreuonta
heb 9:10 monon epi brwmasin kai pomasin kai diaforois baptismois dikaiwmata sarkos mexri kairou diorqwsews epikeimena.

heb 9:12 oude di aimatos tragwn kai mosxwn dia de tou idiou aimatos eishlqen efapac eis ta agia aiwnian lutrwsin euramenos.
heb 9:13 ei gar to aima tragwn kai taurwn kai spodos damalews rantizousa tous kekoinwmenous agiazei pros thn ths sarkos kaqarothta
heb 9:14 posw mallon to aima tou xristou os dia pneumatos [agiou] eauton proshnegken amwmon tw qew kaqariei thn suneidhsin [umwn] apo nekrwn ergwn eis to latreuein qew zwnti.
heb 9:15 kai dia touto diaqhkhs kainhs mesiths estin opws qanatou genomenou eis apolutrwsin twn epi th prwth diaqhkh parabasewn thn epaggelian labwsin oi keklhmenoi ths aiwniou klhronomias.
heb 9:16 opou gar diaqhkh qanaton anagkh feresqai tou diaqemenou
heb 9:17 diaqhkh gar epi nekrois bebaia epei mhpote isxuei ote zh o diaqemenos.
heb 9:18 oqen oude h prwth xwris aimatos egkekainistai
heb 9:19 lalhqeishs gar pashs entolhs kata ton nomon upo mwusews panti tw law labwn to aima twn mosxwn kai twn tragwn meta udatos kai eriou kokkinou kai usswpou auto te to biblion kai panta ton laon erantisen
heb 9:20 legwn touto to aima ths diaqhkhs hs eneteilato pros umas o qeos
heb 9:21 kai thn skhnhn de kai panta ta skeuh ths leitourgias tw aimati omoiws erantisen.
heb 9:22 kai sxedon en aimati panta kaqarizetai kata ton nomon kai xwris aimatekxusias ou ginetai afesis.
heb 9:23 anagkh oun ta men upodeigmata twn en tois ouranois toutois kaqarizesqai auta de ta epourania kreittosin qusiais para tautas.
heb 9:24 ou gar eis xeiropoihta eishlqen agia xristos antitupa twn alhqinwn all eis auton ton ouranon nun emfanisqhnai tw proswpw tou qeou uper hmwn

heb 9:26 epei edei auton pollakis paqein apo katabolhs kosmou nuni de apac epi sunteleia twn aiwnwn eis aqethsin ths amartias dia ths qusias autou pefanerwtai.

heb 10:1 skian gar exwn o nomos twn mellontwn agaqwn ouk authn thn eikona twn pragmatwn kat eniauton tais autais qusiais as prosferousin eis to dihnekes oudepote [dunantai] tous proserxomenous teleiwsai
heb 10:2 epei ouk an epausanto prosferomenai dia to mhdemian exein eti suneidhsin amartiwn tous latreuontas apac kekaqarismenous;
heb 10:3 all en autais anamnhsis amartiwn kat eniauton
heb 10:4 adunaton gar aima taurwn kai tragwn afairein amartias.
heb 10:5 dio eiserxomenos eis ton kosmon legei qusian kai prosforan ouk hqelhsas swma de kathrtisw moi
heb 10:6 olokautwmata kai peri amartias ouk eudokhsas.
heb 10:7 tote eipon idou hkw en kefalidi bibliou gegraptai peri emou tou poihsai o qeos to qelhma sou.

heb 10:13 to loipon ekdexomenos ews teqwsin oi exqroi autou upopodion twn podwn autou

heb 10:16 auth h diaqhkh hn diaqhsomai pros autous meta tas hmeras ekeinas legei kurios didous nomous mou epi kardias autwn kai epi thn dianoian autwn epigrayw autous
heb 10:17 kai twn amartiwn autwn kai twn anomiwn autwn ou mh mnhsqhsomai eti.

heb 10:21 kai ierea megan epi ton oikon tou qeou
heb 10:22 proserxwmeqa meta alhqinhs kardias en plhroforia pistews rerantismenoi tas kardias apo suneidhsews ponhras kai lelousmenoi to swma udati kaqarw
heb 10:23 katexwmen thn omologian ths elpidos aklinh pistos gar o epaggeilamenos
heb 10:24 kai katanowmen allhlous eis parocusmon agaphs kai kalwn ergwn
heb 10:25 mh egkataleipontes thn episunagwghn eautwn kaqws eqos tisin alla parakalountes kai tosoutw mallon osw blepete eggizousan thn hmeran.
heb 10:26 ekousiws gar amartanontwn hmwn meta to labein thn epignwsin ths alhqeias ouketi peri amartiwn apoleipetai qusia
heb 10:27 fobera de tis ekdoxh krisews kai puros zhlos esqiein mellontos tous upenantious.
heb 10:28 aqethsas tis nomon mwusews xwris oiktirmwn epi dusin h trisin martusin apoqnhskei
heb 10:29 posw dokeite xeironos aciwqhsetai timwrias o ton uion tou qeou katapathsas kai to aima ths diaqhkhs koinon hghsamenos en w hgiasqh kai to pneuma ths xaritos enubrisas;
heb 10:30 oidamen gar ton eiponta emoi ekdikhsis egw antapodwsw kai palin krinei kurios ton laon autou.
heb 10:31 foberon to empesein eis xeiras qeou zwntos.
heb 10:32 anamimnhskesqe de tas proteron hmeras en ais fwtisqentes pollhn aqlhsin upemeinate paqhmatwn
heb 10:33 touto men oneidismois te kai qliyesin qeatrizomenoi touto de koinwnoi twn outws anastrefomenwn genhqentes
heb 10:34 kai gar tois desmiois sunepaqhsate kai thn arpaghn twn uparxontwn umwn meta xaras prosedecasqe ginwskontes exein eautous kreittona uparcin kai menousan.
heb 10:35 mh apobalhte oun thn parrhsian umwn htis exei megalhn misqapodosian
heb 10:36 upomonhs gar exete xreian ina to qelhma tou qeou poihsantes komishsqe thn epaggelian.
heb 10:37 eti gar mikron oson oson o erxomenos hcei kai ou xronisei

heb 11:1 estin de pistis elpizomenwn upostasis pragmatwn elegxos ou blepomenwn.
heb 11:2 en tauth gar emarturhqhsan oi presbuteroi.
heb 11:3 pistei nooumen kathrtisqai tous aiwnas rhmati qeou eis to mh ek fainomenwn to blepomenon gegonenai.
heb 11:4 pistei pleiona qusian abel para kain proshnegken tw qew di hs emarturhqh einai dikaios marturountos epi tois dwrois autou tou qeou kai di auths apoqanwn eti lalei.
heb 11:5 pistei enwx meteteqh tou mh idein qanaton kai oux hurisketo dioti meteqhken auton o qeos pro gar ths metaqesews memarturhtai euaresthkenai tw qew
heb 11:6 xwris de pistews adunaton euaresthsai pisteusai gar dei ton proserxomenon tw qew oti estin kai tois ekzhtousin auton misqapodoths ginetai.
heb 11:7 pistei xrhmatisqeis nwe peri twn mhdepw blepomenwn eulabhqeis kateskeuasen kibwton eis swthrian tou oikou autou di hs katekrinen ton kosmon kai ths kata pistin dikaiosunhs egeneto klhronomos.
heb 11:8 pistei kaloumenos abraam uphkousen ecelqein eis topon on hmellen lambanein eis klhronomian kai echlqen mh epistamenos pou erxetai.
heb 11:9 pistei parwkhsen eis ghn ths epaggelias ws allotrian en skhnais katoikhsas meta isaak kai iakwb twn sugklhronomwn ths epaggelias ths auths
heb 11:10 ecedexeto gar thn tous qemelious exousan polin hs texniths kai dhmiourgos o qeos.
heb 11:11 pistei kai auth sarra steira dunamin eis katabolhn spermatos elaben kai para kairon hlikias epei piston hghsato ton epaggeilamenon
heb 11:12 dio kai af enos egennhqhsan kai tauta nenekrwmenou kaqws ta astra tou ouranou tw plhqei kai ws h ammos h para to xeilos ths qalasshs h anariqmhtos.
heb 11:13 kata pistin apeqanon outoi pantes mh labontes tas epaggelias alla porrwqen autas idontes kai aspasamenoi kai omologhsantes oti cenoi kai parepidhmoi eisin epi ths ghs
heb 11:14 oi gar toiauta legontes emfanizousin oti patrida epizhtousin.
heb 11:15 kai ei men ekeinhs emnhmoneuon af hs ecebhsan eixon an kairon anakamyai
heb 11:16 nun de kreittonos oregontai tout estin epouraniou. dio ouk epaisxunetai autous o qeos qeos epikaleisqai autwn htoimasen gar autois polin.
heb 11:17 pistei prosenhnoxen abraam ton isaak peirazomenos kai ton monogenh proseferen o tas epaggelias anadecamenos
heb 11:18 pros on elalhqh oti en isaak klhqhsetai soi sperma
heb 11:19 logisamenos oti kai ek nekrwn egeirein dunatos o qeos oqen auton kai en parabolh ekomisato.
heb 11:20 pistei kai peri mellontwn euloghsen isaak ton iakwb kai ton hsau.
heb 11:21 pistei iakwb apoqnhskwn ekaston twn uiwn iwshf euloghsen kai prosekunhsen epi to akron ths rabdou autou.
heb 11:22 pistei iwshf teleutwn peri ths ecodou twn uiwn israhl emnhmoneusen kai peri twn ostewn autou eneteilato.
heb 11:23 pistei mwushs gennhqeis ekrubh trimhnon upo twn paterwn autou dioti eidon asteion to paidion kai ouk efobhqhsan to diatagma tou basilews.
heb 11:24 pistei mwushs megas genomenos hrnhsato legesqai uios qugatros faraw
heb 11:25 mallon elomenos sugkakouxeisqai tw law tou qeou h proskairon exein amartias apolausin
heb 11:26 meizona plouton hghsamenos twn aiguptou qhsaurwn ton oneidismon tou xristou apeblepen gar eis thn misqapodosian.
heb 11:27 pistei katelipen aigupton mh fobhqeis ton qumon tou basilews ton gar aoraton ws orwn ekarterhsen.
heb 11:28 pistei pepoihken to pasxa kai thn prosxusin tou aimatos ina mh o oloqreuwn ta prwtotoka qigh autwn.
heb 11:29 pistei diebhsan thn eruqran qalassan ws dia chras ghs hs peiran labontes oi aiguptioi katepoqhsan.
heb 11:30 pistei ta teixh ierixw epesan kuklwqenta epi epta hmeras.
heb 11:31 pistei raab h pornh ou sunapwleto tois apeiqhsasin decamenh tous kataskopous met eirhnhs.
heb 11:32 kai ti eti legw; epileiyei me gar dihgoumenon o xronos peri gedewn barak samywn iefqae dauid te kai samouhl kai twn profhtwn
heb 11:33 oi dia pistews kathgwnisanto basileias eirgasanto dikaiosunhn epetuxon epaggeliwn efracan stomata leontwn
heb 11:34 esbesan dunamin puros efugon stomata maxairhs edunamwqhsan apo asqeneias egenhqhsan isxuroi en polemw parembolas eklinan allotriwn
heb 11:35 elabon gunaikes ec anastasews tous nekrous autwn alloi de etumpanisqhsan ou prosdecamenoi thn apolutrwsin ina kreittonos anastasews tuxwsin
heb 11:36 eteroi de empaigmwn kai mastigwn peiran elabon eti de desmwn kai fulakhs
heb 11:37 eliqasqhsan eprisqhsan en fonw maxairhs apeqanon perihlqon en mhlwtais en aigeiois dermasin usteroumenoi qlibomenoi kakouxoumenoi
heb 11:38 wn ouk hn acios o kosmos epi erhmiais planwmenoi kai oresin kai sphlaiois kai tais opais ths ghs.
heb 11:39 kai outoi pantes marturhqentes dia ths pistews ouk ekomisanto thn epaggelian
heb 11:40 tou qeou peri hmwn kreitton ti probleyamenou ina mh xwris hmwn teleiwqwsin.
heb 12:1 toigaroun kai hmeis tosouton exontes perikeimenon hmin nefos marturwn ogkon apoqemenoi panta kai thn euperistaton amartian di upomonhs trexwmen ton prokeimenon hmin agwna
heb 12:2 aforwntes eis ton ths pistews arxhgon kai teleiwthn ihsoun os anti ths prokeimenhs autw xaras upemeinen stauron aisxunhs katafronhsas en decia te tou qronou tou qeou kekaqiken.
heb 12:3 analogisasqe gar ton toiauthn upomemenhkota upo twn amartwlwn [--] antilogian ina mh kamhte tais yuxais umwn ekluomenoi.
heb 12:4 oupw mexris aimatos antikatesthte pros thn amartian antagwnizomenoi
heb 12:5 kai eklelhsqe ths paraklhsews htis umin ws uiois dialegetai uie mou mh oligwrei paideias kuriou mhde ekluou up autou elegxomenos
heb 12:6 on gar agapa kurios paideuei mastigoi de panta uion on paradexetai.
heb 12:7 eis paideian upomenete ws uiois umin prosferetai o qeos tis gar uios on ou paideuei pathr;
heb 12:8 ei de xwris este paideias hs metoxoi gegonasin pantes ara noqoi kai oux uioi este.
heb 12:9 eita tous men ths sarkos hmwn pateras eixomen paideutas kai enetrepomeqa ou polu de mallon upotaghsomeqa tw patri twn pneumatwn kai zhsomen;
heb 12:10 oi men gar pros oligas hmeras kata to dokoun autois epaideuon o de epi to sumferon eis to metalabein ths agiothtos autou.
heb 12:11 pasa de paideia pros men to paron ou dokei xaras einai alla luphs usteron de karpon eirhnikon tois di auths gegumnasmenois apodidwsin dikaiosunhs.
heb 12:12 dio tas pareimenas xeiras kai ta paralelumena gonata anorqwsate
heb 12:13 kai troxias orqas poieite tois posin umwn ina mh to xwlon ektraph iaqh de mallon.
heb 12:14 eirhnhn diwkete meta pantwn kai ton agiasmon ou xwris oudeis oyetai ton kurion
heb 12:15 episkopountes mh tis usterwn apo ths xaritos tou qeou mh tis riza pikrias anw fuousa enoxlh kai di auths mianqwsin polloi
heb 12:16 mh tis pornos h bebhlos ws hsau os anti brwsews mias apedeto ta prwtotokia eautou.
heb 12:17 iste gar oti kai metepeita qelwn klhronomhsai thn eulogian apedokimasqh metanoias gar topon oux euren kaiper meta dakruwn ekzhthsas authn.
heb 12:18 ou gar proselhluqate yhlafwmenw kai kekaumenw puri kai gnofw kai zofw kai quellh
heb 12:19 kai salpiggos hxw kai fwnh rhmatwn hs oi akousantes parhthsanto mh prosteqhnai autois logon
heb 12:20 ouk eferon gar to diastellomenon kan qhrion qigh tou orous liqobolhqhsetai
heb 12:21 kai outw foberon hn to fantazomenon mwushs eipen ekfobos eimi kai entromos.
heb 12:22 alla proselhluqate siwn orei kai polei qeou zwntos ierousalhm epouraniw kai muriasin aggelwn panhgurei
heb 12:23 kai ekklhsia prwtotokwn apogegrammenwn en ouranois kai krith qew pantwn kai pneumasi dikaiwn teteleiwmenwn
heb 12:24 kai diaqhkhs neas mesith ihsou kai aimati rantismou kreitton lalounti para ton abel.
heb 12:25 blepete mh paraithshsqe ton lalounta ei gar ekeinoi ouk ecefugon epi ghs paraithsamenoi ton xrhmatizonta polu mallon hmeis oi ton ap ouranwn apostrefomenoi
heb 12:26 ou h fwnh thn ghn esaleusen tote nun de ephggeltai legwn eti apac egw seisw ou monon thn ghn alla kai ton ouranon.
heb 12:27 to de eti apac dhloi thn twn saleuomenwn metaqesin ws pepoihmenwn ina meinh ta mh saleuomena.
heb 12:28 dio basileian asaleuton paralambanontes exwmen xarin di hs latreuwmen euarestws tw qew meta eulabeias kai deous
heb 12:29 kai gar o qeos hmwn pur katanaliskon.
heb 13:1 h filadelfia menetw.
heb 13:2 ths filocenias mh epilanqanesqe dia tauths gar elaqon tines cenisantes aggelous.
heb 13:3 mimnhskesqe twn desmiwn ws sundedemenoi twn kakouxoumenwn ws kai autoi ontes en swmati.
heb 13:4 timios o gamos en pasin kai h koith amiantos pornous gar kai moixous krinei o qeos.
heb 13:5 afilarguros o tropos arkoumenoi tois parousin autos gar eirhken ou mh se anw oud ou mh se egkatalipw
heb 13:6 wste qarrountas hmas legein kurios emoi bohqos kai ou fobhqhsomai ti poihsei moi anqrwpos;
heb 13:7 mnhmoneuete twn hgoumenwn umwn oitines elalhsan umin ton logon tou qeou wn anaqewrountes thn ekbasin ths anastrofhs mimeisqe thn pistin.
heb 13:8 ihsous xristos exqes kai shmeron o autos kai eis tous aiwnas.
heb 13:9 didaxais poikilais kai cenais mh paraferesqe kalon gar xariti bebaiousqai thn kardian ou brwmasin en ois ouk wfelhqhsan oi peripatountes.
heb 13:10 exomen qusiasthrion ec ou fagein ouk exousin ecousian oi th skhnh latreuontes.
heb 13:11 wn gar eisferetai zwwn to aima peri amartias eis ta agia dia tou arxierews toutwn ta swmata katakaietai ecw ths parembolhs.
heb 13:12 dio kai ihsous ina agiash dia tou idiou aimatos ton laon ecw ths pulhs epaqen.
heb 13:13 toinun ecerxwmeqa pros auton ecw ths parembolhs ton oneidismon autou ferontes
heb 13:14 ou gar exomen wde menousan polin alla thn mellousan epizhtoumen.
heb 13:15 di autou oun anaferwmen qusian ainesews dia pantos tw qew tout estin karpon xeilewn omologountwn tw onomati autou.
heb 13:16 ths de eupoiias kai koinwnias mh epilanqanesqe toiautais gar qusiais euaresteitai o qeos.
heb 13:17 peiqesqe tois hgoumenois umwn kai upeikete autoi gar agrupnousin uper twn yuxwn umwn ws logon apodwsontes ina meta xaras touto poiwsin kai mh stenazontes alusiteles gar umin touto.
heb 13:18 proseuxesqe peri hmwn peiqomeqa gar oti kalhn suneidhsin exomen en pasin kalws qelontes anastrefesqai.
heb 13:19 perissoterws de parakalw touto poihsai ina taxion apokatastaqw umin.
heb 13:20 o de qeos ths eirhnhs o anagagwn ek nekrwn ton poimena twn probatwn ton megan en aimati diaqhkhs aiwniou ton kurion hmwn ihsoun
heb 13:21 katartisai umas en panti [ergw] agaqw eis to poihsai to qelhma autou poiwn en hmin to euareston enwpion autou dia ihsou xristou w h doca eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn amhn.
heb 13:22 parakalw de umas adelfoi anexesqe tou logou ths paraklhsews kai gar dia braxewn epesteila umin.
heb 13:23 ginwskete ton adelfon hmwn timoqeon apolelumenon meq ou ean taxion erxhtai oyomai umas.
heb 13:24 aspasasqe pantas tous hgoumenous umwn kai pantas tous agious. aspazontai umas oi apo ths italias.
heb 13:25 h xaris meta pantwn umwn.
jam 1:1 iakwbos qeou kai kuriou ihsou xristou doulos tais dwdeka fulais tais en th diaspora xairein.
jam 1:2 pasan xaran hghsasqe adelfoi mou otan peirasmois peripeshte poikilois
jam 1:3 ginwskontes oti to dokimion umwn ths pistews katergazetai upomonhn
jam 1:4 h de upomonh ergon teleion exetw ina hte teleioi kai oloklhroi en mhdeni leipomenoi.
jam 1:5 ei de tis umwn leipetai sofias aiteitw para tou didontos qeou pasin aplws kai mh oneidizontos kai doqhsetai autw.
jam 1:6 aiteitw de en pistei mhden diakrinomenos o gar diakrinomenos eoiken kludwni qalasshs anemizomenw kai ripizomenw
jam 1:7 mh gar oiesqw o anqrwpos ekeinos oti lhmyetai ti para tou kuriou
jam 1:8 anhr diyuxos akatastatos en pasais tais odois autou.
jam 1:9 kauxasqw de o adelfos o tapeinos en tw uyei autou
jam 1:10 o de plousios en th tapeinwsei autou oti ws anqos xortou pareleusetai.
jam 1:11 aneteilen gar o hlios sun tw kauswni kai echranen ton xorton kai to anqos autou ecepesen kai h euprepeia tou proswpou autou apwleto outws kai o plousios en tais poreiais autou maranqhsetai.
jam 1:12 makarios anhr os upomenei peirasmon oti dokimos genomenos lhmyetai ton stefanon ths zwhs on ephggeilato tois agapwsin auton.
jam 1:13 mhdeis peirazomenos legetw oti apo qeou peirazomai o gar qeos apeirastos estin kakwn peirazei de autos oudena.
jam 1:14 ekastos de peirazetai upo ths idias epiqumias ecelkomenos kai deleazomenos
jam 1:15 eita h epiqumia sullabousa tiktei amartian h de amartia apotelesqeisa apokuei qanaton.
jam 1:16 mh planasqe adelfoi mou agaphtoi.
jam 1:17 pasa dosis agaqh kai pan dwrhma teleion anwqen estin katabainon apo tou patros twn fwtwn par w ouk eni parallagh h trophs aposkiasma.
jam 1:18 boulhqeis apekuhsen hmas logw alhqeias eis to einai hmas aparxhn tina twn autou ktismatwn.
jam 1:19 iste [de] adelfoi mou agaphtoi. estw de pas anqrwpos taxus eis to akousai bradus eis to lalhsai bradus eis orghn
jam 1:20 orgh gar andros dikaiosunhn qeou ouk ergazetai.
jam 1:21 dio apoqemenoi pasan ruparian kai perisseian kakias en prauthti decasqe ton emfuton logon ton dunamenon swsai tas yuxas umwn.
jam 1:22 ginesqe de poihtai logou kai mh monon akroatai paralogizomenoi eautous.
jam 1:23 oti ei tis akroaths logou estin kai ou poihths outos eoiken andri katanoounti to proswpon ths genesews autou en esoptrw
jam 1:24 katenohsen gar eauton kai apelhluqen kai euqews epelaqeto opoios hn.
jam 1:25 o de parakuyas eis nomon teleion ton ths eleuqerias kai parameinas ouk akroaths epilhsmonhs genomenos alla poihths ergou outos makarios en th poihsei autou estai.
jam 1:26 ei tis dokei qrhskos einai mh xalinagwgwn glwssan autou alla apatwn kardian autou toutou mataios h qrhskeia.
jam 1:27 qrhskeia kaqara kai amiantos para tw qew kai patri auth estin episkeptesqai orfanous kai xhras en th qliyei autwn aspilon eauton threin apo tou kosmou.
jam 2:1 adelfoi mou mh en proswpolhmyiais exete thn pistin tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou ths dochs.
jam 2:2 ean gar eiselqh eis sunagwghn umwn anhr xrusodaktulios en esqhti lampra eiselqh de kai ptwxos en rupara esqhti
jam 2:3 epibleyhte de epi ton forounta thn esqhta thn lampran kai eiphte su kaqou wde kalws kai tw ptwxw eiphte su sthqi ekei h kaqou [wde] upo to upopodion mou
jam 2:4 ou diekriqhte en eautois kai egenesqe kritai dialogismwn ponhrwn;
jam 2:5 akousate adelfoi mou agaphtoi. oux o qeos ecelecato tous ptwxous tw kosmw plousious en pistei kai klhronomous ths basileias hs ephggeilato tois agapwsin auton;
jam 2:6 umeis de htimasate ton ptwxon. oux oi plousioi katadunasteuousin umwn kai autoi elkousin umas eis krithria;
jam 2:7 ouk autoi blasfhmousin to kalon onoma to epiklhqen ef umas;
jam 2:8 ei mentoi nomon teleite basilikon kata thn grafhn agaphseis ton plhsion sou ws seauton kalws poieite
jam 2:9 ei de proswpolhmpteite amartian ergazesqe elegxomenoi upo tou nomou ws parabatai.
jam 2:10 ostis gar olon ton nomon thrhsh ptaish de en eni gegonen pantwn enoxos.
jam 2:11 o gar eipwn mh moixeushs eipen kai mh foneushs ei de ou moixeueis foneueis de gegonas parabaths nomou.
jam 2:12 outws laleite kai outws poieite ws dia nomou eleuqerias mellontes krinesqai.
jam 2:13 h gar krisis aneleos tw mh poihsanti eleos katakauxatai eleos krisews.
jam 2:14 ti to ofelos adelfoi mou ean pistin legh tis exein erga de mh exh; mh dunatai h pistis swsai auton;
jam 2:15 ean adelfos h adelfh gumnoi uparxwsin kai leipomenoi ths efhmerou trofhs
jam 2:16 eiph de tis autois ec umwn upagete en eirhnh qermainesqe kai xortazesqe mh dwte de autois ta epithdeia tou swmatos ti to ofelos;
jam 2:17 outws kai h pistis ean mh exh erga nekra estin kaq eauthn.
jam 2:18 all erei tis su pistin exeis kagw erga exw. deicon moi thn pistin sou xwris twn ergwn kagw soi deicw ek twn ergwn mou thn pistin.
jam 2:19 su pisteueis oti eis estin o qeos; kalws poieis kai ta daimonia pisteuousin kai frissousin.
jam 2:20 qeleis de gnwnai w anqrwpe kene oti h pistis xwris twn ergwn argh estin;
jam 2:21 abraam o pathr hmwn ouk ec ergwn edikaiwqh anenegkas isaak ton uion autou epi to qusiasthrion;
jam 2:22 blepeis oti h pistis sunhrgei tois ergois autou kai ek twn ergwn h pistis eteleiwqh
jam 2:23 kai eplhrwqh h grafh h legousa episteusen de abraam tw qew kai elogisqh autw eis dikaiosunhn kai filos qeou eklhqh.
jam 2:24 orate oti ec ergwn dikaioutai anqrwpos kai ouk ek pistews monon.
jam 2:25 omoiws de kai raab h pornh ouk ec ergwn edikaiwqh upodecamenh tous [kataskopous] kai etera odw ekbalousa;
jam 2:26 wsper gar to swma xwris pneumatos nekron estin outws kai h pistis xwris ergwn nekra estin.

jam 3:3 [ide] twn ippwn tous xalinous eis ta stomata ballomen eis to peiqesqai autous hmin kai olon to swma autwn metagomen.
jam 3:4 idou kai ta ploia thlikauta onta kai upo anemwn sklhrwn elaunomena metagetai upo elaxistou phdaliou opou h ormh tou euqunontos bouletai
jam 3:5 outws kai h glwssa mikron melos estin kai megala auxei. idou hlikon pur hlikhn ulhn anaptei
jam 3:6 kai h glwssa pur o kosmos ths adikias h glwssa kaqistatai en tois melesin hmwn h spilousa olon to swma kai flogizousa ton troxon ths genesews kai flogizomenh upo ths geennhs.

jam 3:11 mhti h phgh ek ths auths ophs bruei to gluku kai to pikron;

jam 4:1 poqen polemoi kai poqen maxai en umin; ouk enteuqen ek twn hdonwn umwn twn strateuomenwn en tois melesin umwn;
jam 4:2 epiqumeite kai ouk exete foneuete kai zhloute kai ou dunasqe epituxein maxesqe kai polemeite. ouk exete dia to mh aiteisqai umas
jam 4:3 aiteite kai ou lambanete dioti kakws aiteisqe ina en tais hdonais umwn dapanhshte.
jam 4:4 moixalides ouk oidate oti h filia tou kosmou exqra tou qeou estin; os ean oun boulhqh filos einai tou kosmou exqros tou qeou kaqistatai.
jam 4:5 h dokeite oti kenws h grafh legei pros fqonon epipoqei to pneuma o katwkisen en hmin;
jam 4:6 meizona de didwsin xarin dio legei o qeos uperhfanois antitassetai tapeinois de didwsin xarin.
jam 4:7 upotaghte oun tw qew antisthte de tw diabolw kai feucetai af umwn
jam 4:8 eggisate tw qew kai eggiei umin. kaqarisate xeiras amartwloi kai agnisate kardias diyuxoi.
jam 4:9 talaipwrhsate kai penqhsate kai klausate o gelws umwn eis penqos metatraphtw kai h xara eis kathfeian.
