jam 4:11 mh katalaleite allhlwn adelfoi o katalalwn adelfou h krinwn ton adelfon autou katalalei nomou kai krinei nomon ei de nomon krineis ouk ei poihths nomou alla kriths.
jam 4:12 eis estin o nomoqeths kai kriths o dunamenos swsai kai apolesai su de tis ei o krinwn ton plhsion;
jam 4:13 age nun oi legontes shmeron h aurion poreusomeqa eis thnde thn polin kai poihsomen ekei eniauton kai emporeusomeqa kai kerdhsomen
jam 4:14 oitines ouk epistasqe to ths aurion poia [gar] h zwh umwn. atmis gar [estin h] h pros oligon fainomenh epeita kai afanizomenh
jam 4:15 anti tou legein umas ean o kurios qelhsh kai zhsomen kai poihsomen touto h ekeino.
jam 4:16 nun de kauxasqe en tais alazoneiais umwn pasa kauxhsis toiauth ponhra estin.
jam 4:17 eidoti oun kalon poiein kai mh poiounti amartia autw estin.
jam 5:1 age nun oi plousioi klausate ololuzontes epi tais talaipwriais umwn tais eperxomenais.
jam 5:2 o ploutos umwn seshpen kai ta imatia umwn shtobrwta gegonen
jam 5:3 o xrusos umwn kai o arguros katiwtai kai o ios autwn eis marturion umin estai kai fagetai tas sarkas umwn ws pur eqhsaurisate en esxatais hmerais.
jam 5:4 idou o misqos twn ergatwn twn amhsantwn tas xwras umwn o apesterhmenos af umwn krazei kai ai boai twn qerisantwn eis ta wta kuriou sabawq eiselhluqasin.
jam 5:5 etrufhsate epi ths ghs kai espatalhsate eqreyate tas kardias umwn en hmera sfaghs.
jam 5:6 katedikasate efoneusate ton dikaion. ouk antitassetai umin.
jam 5:7 makroqumhsate oun adelfoi ews ths parousias tou kuriou. idou o gewrgos ekdexetai ton timion karpon ths ghs makroqumwn ep autw ews labh proimon kai oyimon.
jam 5:8 makroqumhsate kai umeis sthricate tas kardias umwn oti h parousia tou kuriou hggiken.
jam 5:9 mh stenazete adelfoi kat allhlwn ina mh kriqhte idou o kriths pro twn qurwn esthken.
jam 5:10 upodeigma labete adelfoi ths kakopaqeias kai ths makroqumias tous profhtas oi elalhsan en tw onomati kuriou.
jam 5:11 idou makarizomen tous upomeinantas thn upomonhn iwb hkousate kai to telos kuriou eidete oti polusplagxnos estin o kurios kai oiktirmwn.
jam 5:12 pro pantwn de adelfoi mou mh omnuete mhte ton ouranon mhte thn ghn mhte allon tina orkon htw de umwn to nai nai kai to ou ou ina mh upo krisin peshte.
jam 5:13 kakopaqei tis en umin; proseuxesqw euqumei tis; yalletw.
jam 5:14 asqenei tis en umin; proskalesasqw tous presbuterous ths ekklhsias kai proseucasqwsan ep auton aleiyantes auton elaiw en tw onomati tou kuriou
jam 5:15 kai h euxh ths pistews swsei ton kamnonta kai egerei auton o kurios kan amartias h pepoihkws afeqhsetai autw.
jam 5:16 ecomologeisqe oun allhlois tas amartias kai euxesqe uper allhlwn opws iaqhte. polu isxuei dehsis dikaiou energoumenh.
jam 5:17 hlias anqrwpos hn omoiopaqhs hmin kai proseuxh proshucato tou mh brecai kai ouk ebrecen epi ths ghs eniautous treis kai mhnas ec
jam 5:18 kai palin proshucato kai o ouranos ueton edwken kai h gh eblasthsen ton karpon auths.
jam 5:19 adelfoi mou ean tis en umin planhqh apo ths alhqeias kai epistreyh tis auton
jam 5:20 [--] o epistreyas amartwlon ek planhs odou autou swsei yuxhn [--] ek qanatou kai kaluyei plhqos amartiwn.
1pe 1:1 petros apostolos ihsou xristou eklektois parepidhmois diasporas pontou galatias kappadokias asias kai biqunias
1pe 1:2 kata prognwsin qeou patros en agiasmw pneumatos eis upakohn kai rantismon aimatos ihsou xristou xaris umin kai eirhnh plhqunqeih.
1pe 1:3 euloghtos o qeos kai pathr tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou o kata to polu autou eleos anagennhsas hmas eis elpida zwsan di anastasews ihsou xristou ek nekrwn
1pe 1:4 eis klhronomian afqarton kai amianton kai amaranton tethrhmenhn en ouranois eis umas
1pe 1:5 tous en dunamei qeou frouroumenous dia pistews eis swthrian etoimhn apokalufqhnai en kairw esxatw.
1pe 1:6 en w agalliasqe oligon arti ei deon estin luphqentes en poikilois peirasmois
1pe 1:7 ina to dokimion umwn ths pistews polutimoteron xrusiou tou apollumenou dia puros de dokimazomenou eureqh eis epainon kai docan kai timhn en apokaluyei ihsou xristou.
1pe 1:8 on ouk idontes agapate eis on arti mh orwntes pisteuontes de agalliasqe xara aneklalhtw kai dedocasmenh
1pe 1:9 komizomenoi to telos ths pistews [--] swthrian yuxwn.
1pe 1:10 peri hs swthrias ecezhthsan kai echraunhsan profhtai oi peri ths eis umas xaritos profhteusantes
1pe 1:11 eraunwntes eis tina h poion kairon edhlou to en autois pneuma xristou promarturomenon ta eis xriston paqhmata kai tas meta tauta docas
1pe 1:12 ois apekalufqh oti oux eautois umin de dihkonoun auta a nun anhggelh umin dia twn euaggelisamenwn umas en pneumati agiw apostalenti ap ouranou eis a epiqumousin aggeloi parakuyai.
1pe 1:13 dio anazwsamenoi tas osfuas ths dianoias umwn nhfontes teleiws elpisate epi thn feromenhn umin xarin en apokaluyei ihsou xristou.
1pe 1:14 ws tekna upakohs mh susxhmatizomenoi tais proteron en th agnoia umwn epiqumiais
1pe 1:15 alla kata ton kalesanta umas agion kai autoi agioi en pash anastrofh genhqhte
1pe 1:16 dioti gegraptai oti agioi esesqe oti egw agios eimi.
1pe 1:17 kai ei patera epikaleisqe ton aproswpolhmptws krinonta kata to ekastou ergon en fobw ton ths paroikias umwn xronon anastrafhte
1pe 1:18 eidotes oti ou fqartois arguriw h xrusiw elutrwqhte ek ths mataias umwn anastrofhs patroparadotou
1pe 1:19 alla timiw aimati ws amnou amwmou kai aspilou xristou
1pe 1:20 proegnwsmenou men pro katabolhs kosmou fanerwqentos de ep esxatou twn xronwn di umas
1pe 1:21 tous di autou pistous eis qeon ton egeiranta auton ek nekrwn kai docan autw donta wste thn pistin umwn kai elpida einai eis qeon.
1pe 1:22 tas yuxas umwn hgnikotes en th upakoh ths alhqeias eis filadelfian anupokriton ek kaqaras kardias allhlous agaphsate ektenws
1pe 1:23 anagegennhmenoi ouk ek sporas fqarths alla afqartou dia logou zwntos qeou kai menontos
1pe 1:24 dioti pasa sarc ws xortos kai pasa doca auths ws anqos xortou echranqh o xortos kai to anqos ecepesen
1pe 1:25 to de rhma kuriou menei eis ton aiwna. touto de estin to rhma to euaggelisqen eis umas.
1pe 2:1 apoqemenoi oun pasan kakian kai panta dolon kai upokriseis kai fqonous kai pasas katalalias
1pe 2:2 ws artigennhta brefh to logikon adolon gala epipoqhsate ina en autw auchqhte eis swthrian
1pe 2:3 ei egeusasqe oti xrhstos o kurios.
1pe 2:4 pros on proserxomenoi liqon zwnta upo anqrwpwn men apodedokimasmenon para de qew eklekton entimon
1pe 2:5 kai autoi ws liqoi zwntes oikodomeisqe oikos pneumatikos eis ierateuma agion anenegkai pneumatikas qusias euprosdektous tw qew dia ihsou xristou.
1pe 2:6 dioti periexei en grafh idou tiqhmi en siwn liqon akrogwniaion eklekton entimon kai o pisteuwn ep autw ou mh kataisxunqh.
1pe 2:7 umin oun h timh tois pisteuousin apistousin de liqos on apedokimasan oi oikodomountes outos egenhqh eis kefalhn gwnias
1pe 2:8 kai liqos proskommatos kai petra skandalou oi proskoptousin tw logw apeiqountes eis o kai eteqhsan.
1pe 2:9 umeis de genos eklekton basileion ierateuma eqnos agion laos eis peripoihsin opws tas aretas ecaggeilhte tou ek skotous umas kalesantos eis to qaumaston autou fws
1pe 2:10 oi pote ou laos nun de laos qeou oi ouk hlehmenoi nun de elehqentes.
1pe 2:11 agaphtoi parakalw ws paroikous kai parepidhmous apexesqai twn sarkikwn epiqumiwn aitines strateuontai kata ths yuxhs
1pe 2:12 thn anastrofhn umwn en tois eqnesin exontes kalhn ina en w katalalousin umwn ws kakopoiwn ek twn kalwn ergwn epopteuontes docaswsin ton qeon en hmera episkophs.
1pe 2:13 upotaghte pash anqrwpinh ktisei dia ton kurion eite basilei ws uperexonti
1pe 2:14 eite hgemosin ws di autou pempomenois eis ekdikhsin kakopoiwn epainon de agaqopoiwn
1pe 2:15 oti outws estin to qelhma tou qeou agaqopoiountas fimoun thn twn afronwn anqrwpwn agnwsian
1pe 2:16 ws eleuqeroi kai mh ws epikalumma exontes ths kakias thn eleuqerian all ws qeou douloi.
1pe 2:17 pantas timhsate thn adelfothta agapate ton qeon fobeisqe ton basilea timate.
1pe 2:18 oi oiketai upotassomenoi en panti fobw tois despotais ou monon tois agaqois kai epieikesin alla kai tois skoliois.
1pe 2:19 touto gar xaris ei dia suneidhsin qeou upoferei tis lupas pasxwn adikws.
1pe 2:20 poion gar kleos ei amartanontes kai kolafizomenoi upomeneite; all ei agaqopoiountes kai pasxontes upomeneite touto xaris para qew.
1pe 2:21 eis touto gar eklhqhte oti kai xristos epaqen uper umwn umin upolimpanwn upogrammon ina epakolouqhshte tois ixnesin autou
1pe 2:22 os amartian ouk epoihsen oude eureqh dolos en tw stomati autou
1pe 2:23 os loidoroumenos ouk anteloidorei pasxwn ouk hpeilei paredidou de tw krinonti dikaiws
1pe 2:24 os tas amartias hmwn autos anhnegken en tw swmati autou epi to culon ina tais amartiais apogenomenoi th dikaiosunh zhswmen ou tw mwlwpi iaqhte.
1pe 2:25 hte gar ws probata planwmenoi alla epestrafhte nun epi ton poimena kai episkopon twn yuxwn umwn.
1pe 3:1 omoiws ai gunaikes upotassomenai tois idiois andrasin ina kai ei tines apeiqousin tw logw dia ths twn gunaikwn anastrofhs aneu logou kerdhqhsontai
1pe 3:2 epopteusantes thn en fobw agnhn anastrofhn umwn.
1pe 3:3 wn estw oux o ecwqen emplokhs trixwn kai periqesews xrusiwn h endusews imatiwn kosmos
1pe 3:4 all o kruptos ths kardias anqrwpos en tw afqartw tou praews kai hsuxiou pneumatos o estin enwpion tou qeou poluteles.
1pe 3:5 outws gar pote kai ai agiai gunaikes ai elpizousai eis qeon ekosmoun eautas upotassomenai tois idiois andrasin
1pe 3:6 ws sarra uphkousen tw abraam kurion auton kalousa hs egenhqhte tekna agaqopoiousai kai mh foboumenai mhdemian ptohsin.
1pe 3:7 oi andres omoiws sunoikountes kata gnwsin ws asqenesterw skeuei tw gunaikeiw aponemontes timhn ws kai sugklhronomois xaritos zwhs eis to mh egkoptesqai tas proseuxas umwn.
1pe 3:8 to de telos pantes omofrones sumpaqeis filadelfoi eusplagxnoi tapeinofrones
1pe 3:9 mh apodidontes kakon anti kakou h loidorian anti loidorias tounantion de eulogountes oti eis touto eklhqhte ina eulogian klhronomhshte.
1pe 3:10 o gar qelwn zwhn agapan kai idein hmeras agaqas pausatw thn glwssan apo kakou kai xeilh tou mh lalhsai dolon
1pe 3:11 ekklinatw de apo kakou kai poihsatw agaqon zhthsatw eirhnhn kai diwcatw authn.
1pe 3:12 oti ofqalmoi kuriou epi dikaious kai wta autou eis dehsin autwn proswpon de kuriou epi poiountas kaka.
1pe 3:13 kai tis o kakwswn umas ean tou agaqou zhlwtai genhsqe;
1pe 3:14 all ei kai pasxoite dia dikaiosunhn makarioi. ton de fobon autwn mh fobhqhte mhde taraxqhte
1pe 3:15 kurion de ton xriston agiasate en tais kardiais umwn etoimoi aei pros apologian panti tw aitounti umas logon peri ths en umin elpidos
1pe 3:16 alla meta prauthtos kai fobou suneidhsin exontes agaqhn ina en w katalaleisqe kataisxunqwsin oi ephreazontes umwn thn agaqhn en xristw anastrofhn.
1pe 3:17 kreitton gar agaqopoiountas ei qeloi to qelhma tou qeou pasxein h kakopoiountas.
1pe 3:18 oti kai xristos apac peri amartiwn epaqen dikaios uper adikwn ina umas prosagagh tw qew qanatwqeis men sarki zwopoihqeis de pneumati
1pe 3:19 en w kai tois en fulakh pneumasin poreuqeis ekhrucen
1pe 3:20 apeiqhsasin pote ote apecedexeto h tou qeou makroqumia en hmerais nwe kataskeuazomenhs kibwtou eis hn oligoi tout estin oktw yuxai dieswqhsan di udatos.
1pe 3:21 [--] kai umas antitupon nun swzei baptisma ou sarkos apoqesis rupou alla suneidhsews agaqhs eperwthma eis qeon di anastasews ihsou xristou
1pe 3:22 os estin en decia tou qeou poreuqeis eis ouranon upotagentwn autw aggelwn kai ecousiwn kai dunamewn.
1pe 4:1 xristou oun paqontos sarki kai umeis thn authn ennoian oplisasqe oti o paqwn sarki pepautai amartias
1pe 4:2 eis to mhketi anqrwpwn epiqumiais alla qelhmati qeou ton epiloipon en sarki biwsai xronon.
1pe 4:3 arketos gar o parelhluqws xronos to boulhma twn eqnwn kateirgasqai peporeumenous en aselgeiais epiqumiais oinoflugiais kwmois potois kai aqemitois eidwlolatriais.
1pe 4:4 en w cenizontai mh suntrexontwn umwn eis thn authn ths aswtias anaxusin blasfhmountes
1pe 4:5 oi apodwsousin logon tw etoimws exonti krinai zwntas kai nekrous.

1pe 4:11 ei tis lalei ws logia qeou ei tis diakonei ws ec isxuos hs xorhgei o qeos ina en pasin docazhtai o qeos dia ihsou xristou w estin h doca kai to kratos eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn amhn.
1pe 4:12 agaphtoi mh cenizesqe th en umin purwsei pros peirasmon umin ginomenh ws cenou umin sumbainontos

1pe 4:14 ei oneidizesqe en onomati xristou makarioi oti to ths dochs kai [dunamews kai] to tou qeou pneuma ef umas anapauetai [kata men autous blasfhmei kata de umas docazetai]..
1pe 4:15 mh gar tis umwn pasxetw ws foneus h klepths h kakopoios h ws allotriepiskopos
1pe 4:16 ei de ws xristianos mh aisxunesqw docazetw de ton qeon en tw onomati toutw.

1pe 4:18 kai ei o dikaios molis swzetai o asebhs kai amartwlos pou faneitai;
1pe 4:19 wste kai oi pasxontes kata to qelhma tou qeou pistw ktisth paratiqesqwsan tas yuxas autwn en agaqopoiia.

2pe 1:1 [sumwn] petros doulos kai apostolos ihsou xristou tois isotimon hmin laxousin pistin en dikaiosunh tou qeou hmwn kai swthros ihsou xristou

2pe 1:4 di wn ta timia kai megista hmin epaggelmata dedwrhtai ina dia toutwn genhsqe qeias koinwnoi fusews apofugontes ths en tw kosmw [epiqumian] fqoras.
2pe 1:5 kai auto touto de spoudhn pasan pareisenegkantes epixorhghsate en th pistei umwn thn arethn en de th areth thn gnwsin
2pe 1:6 en de th gnwsei thn egkrateian en de th egkrateia thn upomonhn en de th upomonh thn eusebeian
2pe 1:7 en de th eusebeia thn filadelfian en de th filadelfia thn agaphn.
2pe 1:8 tauta gar umin uparxonta kai pleonazonta ouk argous oude akarpous kaqisthsin eis thn tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou epignwsin
2pe 1:9 w gar mh parestin tauta tuflos estin muwpazwn lhqhn labwn tou kaqarismou twn palai autou amartiwn.

2pe 1:11 outws gar plousiws epixorhghqhsetai umin h eisodos eis thn aiwnion basileian tou kuriou hmwn kai swthros ihsou xristou.
2pe 1:12 dio mellhsw aei umas upomimnhskein peri toutwn kaiper eidotas kai esthrigmenous en th paroush alhqeia.
2pe 1:13 dikaion de hgoumai ef oson eimi en toutw tw skhnwmati diegeirein umas en upomnhsei

2pe 1:15 spoudasw de kai ekastote exein umas meta thn emhn ecodon thn toutwn mnhmhn poieisqai.
2pe 1:16 ou gar sesofismenois muqois ecakolouqhsantes egnwrisamen umin thn tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou dunamin kai parousian all epoptai genhqentes ths ekeinou megaleiothtos.
2pe 1:17 labwn gar para qeou patros timhn kai docan fwnhs enexqeishs autw toiasde upo ths megaloprepous dochs [outos estin] o uios mou o agaphtos mou eis on egw eudokhsa

2pe 1:20 touto prwton ginwskontes oti pasa profhteia grafhs idias epilusews ou ginetai
2pe 1:21 ou gar qelhmati anqrwpou hnexqh profhteia pote alla upo pneumatos agiou feromenoi elalhsan [agioi] qeou anqrwpoi.
2pe 2:1 egenonto de kai yeudoprofhtai en tw law ws kai en umin esontai yeudodidaskaloi oitines pareisacousin aireseis apwleias kai ton agorasanta autous despothn arnoumenoi epagontes eautois taxinhn apwleian.
2pe 2:2 kai polloi ecakolouqhsousin autwn tais aselgeiais di ous h odos ths alhqeias blasfhmhqhsetai
2pe 2:3 kai en pleonecia plastois logois umas emporeusontai ois to krima ekpalai ouk argei kai h apwleia autwn ou nustazei.
2pe 2:4 ei gar o qeos aggelwn amarthsantwn ouk efeisato alla seirais zofou tartarwsas paredwken eis krisin throumenous
2pe 2:5 kai arxaiou kosmou ouk efeisato alla ogdoon nwe dikaiosunhs khruka efulacen kataklusmon kosmw asebwn epacas
2pe 2:6 kai poleis sodomwn kai gomorras tefrwsas katastrofh katekrinen upodeigma mellontwn asebesin teqeikws
2pe 2:7 kai dikaion lwt kataponoumenon upo ths twn aqesmwn en aselgeia anastrofhs errusato
2pe 2:8 blemmati gar kai akoh o dikaios egkatoikwn en autois hmeran ec hmeras yuxhn dikaian anomois ergois ebasanizen
2pe 2:9 oiden kurios eusebeis ek peirasmou ruesqai adikous de eis hmeran krisews kolazomenous threin
2pe 2:10 malista de tous opisw sarkos en epiqumia miasmou poreuomenous kai kuriothtos katafronountas. tolmhtai auqadeis docas ou tremousin blasfhmountes
2pe 2:11 opou aggeloi isxui kai dunamei meizones ontes ou ferousin kat autwn [--] kuriou blasfhmon krisin.
2pe 2:12 outoi de ws aloga zwa gegennhmena fusika eis alwsin kai fqoran en ois agnoousin blasfhmountes en th fqora autwn kai fqarhsontai
2pe 2:13 [komioumenoi] misqon adikias hdonhn hgoumenoi thn en hmera trufhn spiloi kai mwmoi entrufwntes en tais apatais autwn suneuwxoumenoi umin
2pe 2:14 ofqalmous exontes mestous moixalidos kai akatapaustous amartias deleazontes yuxas asthriktous kardian gegumnasmenhn pleonecias exontes kataras tekna
2pe 2:15 kataleipontes euqeian odon eplanhqhsan ecakolouqhsantes th odw tou balaam tou bosor os misqon adikias hgaphsen
2pe 2:16 elegcin de esxen idias paranomias upozugion afwnon en anqrwpou fwnh fqegcamenon ekwlusen thn tou profhtou parafronian.
2pe 2:17 outoi eisin phgai anudroi kai omixlai upo lailapos elaunomenai ois o zofos tou skotous tethrhtai.
2pe 2:18 uperogka gar mataiothtos fqeggomenoi deleazousin en epiqumiais sarkos aselgeiais tous oligws apofeugontas tous en planh anastrefomenous
2pe 2:19 eleuqerian autois epaggellomenoi autoi douloi uparxontes ths fqoras w gar tis htthtai toutw dedoulwtai.
2pe 2:20 ei gar apofugontes ta miasmata tou kosmou en epignwsei tou kuriou [hmwn ihsou xristou kai swthros hmwn] toutois de palin emplakentes httwntai gegonen autois ta esxata xeirona twn prwtwn.
2pe 2:21 kreitton gar hn autois mh epegnwkenai thn odon ths dikaiosunhs h epignousin upostreyai ek ths paradoqeishs autois agias entolhs.
2pe 2:22 sumbebhken autois to ths alhqous paroimias kuwn epistreyas epi to idion ecerama kai us lousamenh eis kulismon borborou.
2pe 3:1 tauthn hdh agaphtoi deuteran umin grafw epistolhn en ais diegeirw umwn en upomnhsei thn eilikrinh dianoian
2pe 3:2 mnhsqhnai twn proeirhmenwn rhmatwn upo twn agiwn profhtwn kai ths twn apostolwn umwn entolhs tou kuriou kai swthros
2pe 3:3 touto prwton ginwskontes oti eleusontai ep esxatwn twn hmerwn en empaigmonh empaiktai kata tas idias epiqumias autwn poreuomenoi
2pe 3:4 kai legontes pou estin h epaggelia ths parousias autou; af hs gar oi pateres ekoimhqhsan panta outws diamenei ap arxhs ktisews.
2pe 3:5 lanqanei gar autous touto qelontas oti ouranoi hsan ekpalai kai gh ec udatos kai di udatos sunestwsa tw tou qeou logw
2pe 3:6 di wn o tote kosmos udati kataklusqeis apwleto
2pe 3:7 oi de nun ouranoi kai h gh tw autw logw teqhsaurismenoi eisin puri throumenoi eis hmeran krisews kai apwleias twn asebwn anqrwpwn.
2pe 3:8 en de touto mh lanqanetw umas agaphtoi oti mia hmera para kuriw ws xilia eth kai xilia eth ws hmera mia.
2pe 3:9 ou bradunei kurios ths epaggelias ws tines braduthta hgountai alla makroqumei [di] umas mh boulomenos tinas apolesqai alla pantas eis metanoian xwrhsai.
2pe 3:10 hcei de hmera kuriou ws klepths en h oi ouranoi roizhdon pareleusontai stoixeia de kausoumena luqhsetai kai gh kai ta en auth erga [oux] eureqhsetai.
2pe 3:11 toutwn [oun] outws pantwn luomenwn potapous dei uparxein umas en agiais anastrofais kai eusebeiais
2pe 3:12 prosdokwntas kai speudontas thn parousian ths tou qeou hmeras di hn ouranoi puroumenoi luqhsontai kai stoixeia kausoumena thketai.
2pe 3:13 kainous de ouranous kai ghn kainhn kata to epaggelma autou prosdokwmen en ois dikaiosunh katoikei.
2pe 3:14 dio agaphtoi tauta prosdokwntes spoudasate aspiloi kai amwmhtoi autw eureqhnai en eirhnh
2pe 3:15 kai thn tou kuriou hmwn makroqumian swthrian hgeisqe kaqws kai o agaphtos hmwn adelfos paulos kata thn doqeisan autw sofian egrayen umin
2pe 3:16 ws kai en pasais epistolais lalwn en autais peri toutwn en ais estin dusnohta tina a oi amaqeis kai asthriktoi streblousin ws kai tas loipas grafas pros thn idian autwn apwleian.
2pe 3:17 umeis oun agaphtoi proginwskontes fulassesqe ina mh th twn aqesmwn planh sunapaxqentes ekpeshte tou idiou sthrigmou
2pe 3:18 aucanete de en xariti kai gnwsei tou kuriou hmwn kai swthros ihsou xristou. autw h doca kai nun kai eis hmeran aiwnos. amhn.
1jo 1:1 o hn ap arxhs o akhkoamen o ewrakamen tois ofqalmois hmwn o eqeasameqa kai ai xeires hmwn eyhlafhsan peri tou logou ths zwhs 
1jo 1:2 kai h zwh efanerwqh kai ewrakamen kai marturoumen kai apaggellomen umin thn zwhn thn aiwnion htis hn pros ton patera kai efanerwqh hmin 
1jo 1:3 o ewrakamen kai akhkoamen apaggellomen kai umin ina kai umeis koinwnian exhte meq hmwn. kai h koinwnia de h hmetera meta tou patros kai meta tou uiou autou ihsou xristou.
1jo 1:4 kai tauta grafomen hmeis ina h xara hmwn h peplhrwmenh.
1jo 1:5 kai estin auth h aggelia hn akhkoamen ap autou kai anaggellomen umin oti o qeos fws estin kai skotia en autw ouk estin oudemia.
1jo 1:6 ean eipwmen oti koinwnian exomen met autou kai en tw skotei peripatwmen yeudomeqa kai ou poioumen thn alhqeian
1jo 1:7 ean de en tw fwti peripatwmen ws autos estin en tw fwti koinwnian exomen met allhlwn kai to aima ihsou tou uiou autou kaqarizei hmas apo pashs amartias.
1jo 1:8 ean eipwmen oti amartian ouk exomen eautous planwmen kai h alhqeia ouk estin en hmin.
1jo 1:9 ean omologwmen tas amartias hmwn pistos estin kai dikaios ina afh hmin tas amartias kai kaqarish hmas apo pashs adikias.
1jo 1:10 ean eipwmen oti oux hmarthkamen yeusthn poioumen auton kai o logos autou ouk estin en hmin.
1jo 2:1 teknia mou tauta grafw umin ina mh amarthte. kai ean tis amarth paraklhton exomen pros ton patera ihsoun xriston dikaion
1jo 2:2 kai autos ilasmos estin peri twn amartiwn hmwn ou peri twn hmeterwn de monon alla kai peri olou tou kosmou.
1jo 2:3 kai en toutw ginwskomen oti egnwkamen auton ean tas entolas autou thrwmen.
1jo 2:4 o legwn oti egnwka auton kai tas entolas autou mh thrwn yeusths estin kai en toutw h alhqeia ouk estin
1jo 2:5 os d an thrh autou ton logon alhqws en toutw h agaph tou qeou teteleiwtai. en toutw ginwskomen oti en autw esmen
1jo 2:6 o legwn en autw menein ofeilei kaqws ekeinos periepathsen kai autos [--] peripatein.
1jo 2:7 agaphtoi ouk entolhn kainhn grafw umin all entolhn palaian hn eixete ap arxhs h entolh h palaia estin o logos on hkousate.
1jo 2:8 palin entolhn kainhn grafw umin o estin alhqes en autw kai en umin oti h skotia paragetai kai to fws to alhqinon hdh fainei.
1jo 2:9 o legwn en tw fwti einai kai ton adelfon autou miswn en th skotia estin ews arti.
1jo 2:10 o agapwn ton adelfon autou en tw fwti menei kai skandalon en autw ouk estin
1jo 2:11 o de miswn ton adelfon autou en th skotia estin kai en th skotia peripatei kai ouk oiden pou upagei oti h skotia etuflwsen tous ofqalmous autou.
1jo 2:12 grafw umin teknia oti afewntai umin ai amartiai dia to onoma autou.
1jo 2:13 grafw umin pateres oti egnwkate ton ap arxhs. grafw umin neaniskoi oti nenikhkate ton ponhron.
1jo 2:14 egraya umin paidia oti egnwkate ton patera. egraya umin pateres oti egnwkate ton ap arxhs. egraya umin neaniskoi oti isxuroi este kai o logos tou qeou en umin menei kai nenikhkate ton ponhron.
1jo 2:15 mh agapate ton kosmon mhde ta en tw kosmw. ean tis agapa ton kosmon ouk estin h agaph tou patros en autw
1jo 2:16 oti pan to en tw kosmw h epiqumia ths sarkos kai h epiqumia twn ofqalmwn kai h alazoneia tou biou ouk estin ek tou patros all ek tou kosmou estin.
1jo 2:17 kai o kosmos paragetai kai h epiqumia autou o de poiwn to qelhma tou qeou menei eis ton aiwna.
1jo 2:18 paidia esxath wra estin kai kaqws hkousate oti antixristos erxetai kai nun antixristoi polloi gegonasin oqen ginwskomen oti esxath wra estin.
1jo 2:19 ec hmwn echlqan all ouk hsan ec hmwn ei gar ec hmwn hsan memenhkeisan an meq hmwn all ina fanerwqwsin oti ouk eisin pantes ec hmwn.
1jo 2:20 kai umeis xrisma exete apo tou agiou kai oidate pantes.
1jo 2:21 ouk egraya umin oti ouk oidate thn alhqeian all oti oidate authn kai oti pan yeudos ek ths alhqeias ouk estin.
1jo 2:22 tis estin o yeusths ei mh o arnoumenos oti ihsous ouk estin o xristos; outos estin o antixristos o arnoumenos ton patera kai ton uion.
1jo 2:23 pas o arnoumenos ton uion oude ton patera exei o omologwn ton uion kai ton patera exei.
1jo 2:24 umeis o hkousate ap arxhs en umin menetw ean en umin meinh o ap arxhs hkousate kai umeis en tw uiw kai en tw patri meneite.
1jo 2:25 kai auth estin h epaggelia hn autos ephggeilato hmin thn zwhn thn aiwnion.
1jo 2:26 tauta egraya umin peri twn planwntwn umas.
1jo 2:27 kai umeis to xrisma o elabete ap autou menei en umin kai ou xreian exete ina tis didaskh umas all ws to autou xrisma didaskei umas peri pantwn kai alhqes estin kai ouk estin yeudos kai kaqws edidacen umas menete en autw.
1jo 2:28 kai nun teknia menete en autw ina ean fanerwqh sxwmen parrhsian kai mh aisxunqwmen ap autou en th parousia autou.
1jo 2:29 ean eidhte oti dikaios estin ginwskete oti kai pas o poiwn thn dikaiosunhn ec autou gegennhtai.
1jo 3:1 idete potaphn agaphn dedwken hmin o pathr ina tekna qeou klhqwmen kai esmen. dia touto o kosmos ou ginwskei hmas oti ouk egnw auton.
1jo 3:2 agaphtoi nun tekna qeou esmen kai oupw efanerwqh ti esomeqa. oidamen oti ean fanerwqh omoioi autw esomeqa oti oyomeqa auton kaqws estin.
1jo 3:3 kai pas o exwn thn elpida tauthn ep autw agnizei eauton kaqws ekeinos agnos estin.
1jo 3:4 pas o poiwn thn amartian kai thn anomian poiei kai h amartia estin h anomia.
1jo 3:5 kai oidate oti ekeinos efanerwqh ina tas amartias arh kai amartia en autw ouk estin.
1jo 3:6 pas o en autw menwn oux amartanei pas o amartanwn oux ewraken auton oude egnwken auton.
1jo 3:7 teknia mhdeis planatw umas o poiwn thn dikaiosunhn dikaios estin kaqws ekeinos dikaios estin
1jo 3:8 o poiwn thn amartian ek tou diabolou estin oti ap arxhs o diabolos amartanei. eis touto efanerwqh o uios tou qeou ina lush ta erga tou diabolou.
1jo 3:9 pas o gegennhmenos ek tou qeou amartian ou poiei oti sperma autou en autw menei kai ou dunatai amartanein oti ek tou qeou gegennhtai.
1jo 3:10 en toutw fanera estin ta tekna tou qeou kai ta tekna tou diabolou pas o mh poiwn dikaiosunhn ouk estin ek tou qeou kai o mh agapwn ton adelfon autou.
1jo 3:11 oti auth estin h aggelia hn hkousate ap arxhs ina agapwmen allhlous
1jo 3:12 ou kaqws kain ek tou ponhrou hn kai esfacen ton adelfon autou kai xarin tinos esfacen auton; oti ta erga autou ponhra hn ta de tou adelfou autou dikaia.
1jo 3:13 [--] mh qaumazete adelfoi ei misei umas o kosmos.
1jo 3:14 hmeis oidamen oti metabebhkamen ek tou qanatou eis thn zwhn oti agapwmen tous adelfous o mh agapwn menei en tw qanatw.
1jo 3:15 pas o miswn ton adelfon autou anqrwpoktonos estin kai oidate oti pas anqrwpoktonos ouk exei zwhn aiwnion en autw menousan.
1jo 3:16 en toutw egnwkamen thn agaphn oti ekeinos uper hmwn thn yuxhn autou eqhken kai hmeis ofeilomen uper twn adelfwn tas yuxas qeinai.
1jo 3:17 os d an exh ton bion tou kosmou kai qewrh ton adelfon autou xreian exonta kai kleish ta splagxna autou ap autou pws h agaph tou qeou menei en autw;
1jo 3:18 teknia mh agapwmen logw mhde th glwssh alla en ergw kai alhqeia.
1jo 3:19 kai en toutw gnwsomeqa oti ek ths alhqeias esmen kai emprosqen autou peisomen thn kardian hmwn
1jo 3:20 oti ean kataginwskh hmwn h kardia oti meizwn estin o qeos ths kardias hmwn kai ginwskei panta.
1jo 3:21 agaphtoi ean h kardia hmwn mh kataginwskh [hmwn] parrhsian exomen pros ton qeon
1jo 3:22 kai o ean aitwmen lambanomen ap autou oti tas entolas autou throumen kai ta aresta enwpion autou poioumen.
1jo 3:23 kai auth estin h entolh autou ina pisteuswmen tw onomati tou uiou autou ihsou xristou kai agapwmen allhlous kaqws edwken entolhn hmin.
1jo 3:24 kai o thrwn tas entolas autou en autw menei kai autos en autw kai en toutw ginwskomen oti menei en hmin ek tou pneumatos ou hmin edwken.
1jo 4:1 agaphtoi mh panti pneumati pisteuete alla dokimazete ta pneumata ei ek tou qeou estin oti polloi yeudoprofhtai ecelhluqasin eis ton kosmon.
1jo 4:2 en toutw ginwskete to pneuma tou qeou pan pneuma o omologei ihsoun xriston en sarki elhluqota ek tou qeou estin
1jo 4:3 kai pan pneuma o mh omologei ton ihsoun [xriston] ek tou qeou ouk estin kai touto estin to tou antixristou o akhkoate oti erxetai kai nun en tw kosmw estin hdh.
1jo 4:4 umeis ek tou qeou este teknia kai nenikhkate autous oti meizwn estin o en umin h o en tw kosmw.
1jo 4:5 autoi ek tou kosmou eisin dia touto ek tou kosmou lalousin kai o kosmos autwn akouei.
1jo 4:6 hmeis ek tou qeou esmen o ginwskwn ton qeon akouei hmwn os ouk estin ek tou qeou ouk akouei hmwn. ek toutou ginwskomen to pneuma ths alhqeias kai to pneuma ths planhs.
1jo 4:7 agaphtoi agapwmen allhlous oti h agaph ek tou qeou estin kai pas o agapwn ek tou qeou gegennhtai kai ginwskei ton qeon.
1jo 4:8 o mh agapwn ouk egnw ton qeon oti o qeos agaph estin.
1jo 4:9 en toutw efanerwqh h agaph tou qeou en hmin oti ton uion autou ton monogenh apestalken o qeos eis ton kosmon ina zhswmen di autou.
1jo 4:10 en toutw estin h agaph oux oti hmeis hgaphkamen ton qeon all oti autos hgaphsen hmas kai apesteilen ton uion autou ilasmon peri twn amartiwn hmwn.
1jo 4:11 agaphtoi ei outws o qeos hgaphsen hmas kai hmeis ofeilomen allhlous agapan.
1jo 4:12 qeon oudeis pwpote teqeatai ean agapwmen allhlous o qeos en hmin menei kai h agaph autou en hmin teteleiwmenh estin.
1jo 4:13 en toutw ginwskomen oti en autw menomen kai autos en hmin oti ek tou pneumatos autou dedwken hmin.
1jo 4:14 kai hmeis teqeameqa kai marturoumen oti o pathr apestalken ton uion swthra tou kosmou.
1jo 4:15 os ean omologhsh oti ihsous estin o uios tou qeou o qeos en autw menei kai autos en tw qew.
1jo 4:16 kai hmeis egnwkamen kai pepisteukamen thn agaphn hn exei o qeos en hmin. o qeos agaph estin kai o menwn en th agaph en tw qew menei kai o qeos en autw menei.
1jo 4:17 en toutw teteleiwtai h agaph meq hmwn ina parrhsian exwmen en th hmera ths krisews oti kaqws ekeinos estin kai hmeis esmen en tw kosmw toutw.
1jo 4:18 fobos ouk estin en th agaph all h teleia agaph ecw ballei ton fobon oti o fobos kolasin exei o de foboumenos ou teteleiwtai en th agaph.
1jo 4:19 hmeis [oidamen] oti autos prwtos hgaphsen hmas.
1jo 4:20 ean tis eiph oti agapw ton qeon kai ton adelfon autou mish yeusths estin o gar mh agapwn ton adelfon autou on ewraken ton qeon on oux ewraken ou dunatai agapan.
1jo 4:21 kai tauthn thn entolhn exomen ap autou ina o agapwn ton qeon agapa kai ton adelfon autou.
1jo 5:1 pas o pisteuwn oti ihsous estin o xristos ek tou qeou gegennhtai kai pas o agapwn ton gennhsanta agapa [--] ton gegennhmenon ec autou.
1jo 5:2 en toutw ginwskomen oti agapwmen ta tekna tou qeou otan ton qeon agapwmen kai tas entolas autou poiwmen.
1jo 5:3 auth gar estin h agaph tou qeou ina tas entolas autou thrwmen kai ai entolai autou bareiai ouk eisin
1jo 5:4 oti pan to gegennhmenon ek tou qeou nika ton kosmon kai auth estin h nikh h nikhsasa ton kosmon h pistis hmwn.
1jo 5:5 tis de estin o nikwn ton kosmon ei mh o pisteuwn oti ihsous estin o uios tou qeou;
1jo 5:6 outos estin o elqwn di udatos kai aimatos [kai pneumatos] ihsous xristos ouk en tw udati monon all en tw udati kai en tw aimati kai to pneuma estin to marturoun oti to pneuma estin h alhqeia.
1jo 5:7 oti treis eisin oi marturountes
1jo 5:8 to pneuma kai to udwr kai to aima kai oi treis eis to en eisin.
1jo 5:9 ei thn marturian twn anqrwpwn lambanomen h marturia tou qeou meizwn estin oti auth estin h marturia tou qeou oti memarturhken peri tou uiou autou.
1jo 5:10 o pisteuwn eis ton uion tou qeou exei thn marturian en eautw o mh pisteuwn [eiston uion tou qeou] yeusthn pepoihken auton oti ou pepisteuken eis thn marturian hn memarturhken o qeos peri tou uiou autou.
1jo 5:11 kai auth estin h marturia oti zwhn aiwnion edwken hmin o qeos kai auth h zwh en tw uiw autou estin.
1jo 5:12 o exwn ton uion exei thn zwhn o mh exwn ton uion tou qeou thn zwhn ouk exei.
1jo 5:13 tauta egraya umin ina eidhte oti zwhn exete aiwnion tois pisteuousin eis to onoma tou uiou tou qeou.
1jo 5:14 kai auth estin h parrhsia hn exomen pros auton oti ean ti aitwmeqa kata to qelhma autou akouei hmwn.
1jo 5:15 kai ean oidamen oti akouei hmwn o ean aitwmeqa oidamen oti exomen ta aithmata a hthkamen ap autou.
1jo 5:16 ean tis idh ton adelfon autou amartanonta amartian mh pros qanaton aithsei kai dwsei autw zwhn tois amartanousin mh pros qanaton. estin amartia pros qanaton ou peri ekeinhs legw ina erwthsh.
1jo 5:17 pasa adikia amartia estin kai estin amartia [--] pros qanaton.
1jo 5:18 oidamen oti pas o gegennhmenos ek tou qeou oux amartanei all o gennhqeis ek tou qeou threi auton kai o ponhros oux aptetai autou.
1jo 5:19 oidamen oti ek tou qeou esmen kai o kosmos olos en tw ponhrw keitai.
1jo 5:20 oidamen de oti o uios tou qeou hkei kai dedwken hmin dianoian ina ginwskwmen [to] alhqinon kai esmen en tw alhqinw en tw uiw autou ihsou xristw. outos estin o alhqinos qeos kai zwh aiwnios.
1jo 5:21 teknia fulacate eauta apo twn eidwlwn.
2jo 1:1 o presbuteros eklekth kuria kai tois teknois auths ous egw agapw en alhqeia kai ouk egw monos alla kai pantes oi egnwkotes thn alhqeian
2jo 1:2 dia thn alhqeian thn menousan en hmin kai meq hmwn estai eis ton aiwna.
2jo 1:3 estai meq hmwn xaris eleos eirhnh para qeou patros kai para ihsou xristou tou uiou tou patros en alhqeia kai agaph.
2jo 1:4 exarhn lian oti eurhka ek twn teknwn sou peripatountas en alhqeia kaqws entolhn elabomen para tou patros.
2jo 1:5 kai nun erwtw se kuria oux ws entolhn kainhn grafwn soi alla hn eixomen ap arxhs ina agapwmen allhlous.
2jo 1:6 kai auth estin h agaph ina peripatwmen kata tas entolas autou auth h entolh estin kaqws hkousate ap arxhs ina en auth peripathte.
2jo 1:7 oti polloi planoi echlqon eis ton kosmon oi mh omologountes ihsoun xriston erxomenon en sarki outos estin o planos kai o antixristos.
2jo 1:8 blepete eautous ina mh apoleshte a eirgasameqa alla misqon plhrh apolabhte.
2jo 1:9 pas o proagwn kai mh menwn en th didaxh tou xristou qeon ouk exei o menwn en th didaxh outos kai ton patera kai ton uion exei.
2jo 1:10 ei tis erxetai pros umas kai tauthn thn didaxhn ou ferei mh lambanete auton eis oikian kai xairein autw mh legete
2jo 1:11 o legwn gar autw xairein koinwnei tois ergois autou tois ponhrois.
2jo 1:12 polla exwn umin grafein ouk eboulhqhn dia xartou kai melanos alla elpizw genesqai pros umas kai stoma pros stoma lalhsai ina h xara [emou] peplhrwmenh h.
2jo 1:13 aspazetai se ta tekna ths adelfhs sou ths eklekths.
3jo 1:1 o presbuteros gaiw tw agaphtw on egw agapw en alhqeia.
3jo 1:2 agaphte peri pantwn euxomai se euodousqai kai ugiainein kaqws euodoutai sou h yuxh.
3jo 1:3 exarhn gar lian erxomenwn adelfwn kai marturountwn sou th alhqeia kaqws su en alhqeia peripateis.
3jo 1:4 meizoteran toutwn ouk exw xaran ina akouw ta ema tekna en th alhqeia peripatounta.
3jo 1:5 agaphte piston poieis o ean ergash eis tous adelfous kai touto cenous
3jo 1:6 oi emarturhsan sou th agaph enwpion ekklhsias ous kalws poihseis propemyas aciws tou qeou
3jo 1:7 uper gar tou onomatos echlqon mhden lambanontes apo twn eqnikwn.
3jo 1:8 hmeis oun ofeilomen upolambanein tous toioutous ina sunergoi ginwmeqa th alhqeia.
3jo 1:9 [egrayas] ti th ekklhsia all o filoprwteuwn autwn diotrefhs ouk epidexetai hmas.
3jo 1:10 dia touto ean elqw upomnhsw autou ta erga a poiei logois ponhrois fluarwn hmas kai mh arkoumenos epi toutois oute autos epidexetai tous adelfous kai tous boulomenous kwluei kai ek ths ekklhsias ekballei.
3jo 1:11 agaphte mh mimou to kakon alla to agaqon. o agaqopoiwn ek tou qeou estin o kakopoiwn oux ewraken ton qeon.
3jo 1:12 dhmhtriw memarturhtai upo pantwn kai upo auths ths alhqeias kai hmeis de marturoumen kai oidas oti h marturia hmwn alhqhs estin.
3jo 1:13 polla eixon grayai soi all ou qelw dia melanos kai kalamou soi grafein
3jo 1:14 elpizw de euqews se idein kai stoma pros stoma lalhsomen.
3jo 1:15 eirhnh soi. aspazontai se oi filoi. aspazou tous filous kat onoma.
jud 1:1 ioudas ihsou xristou doulos adelfos de iakwbou tois en qew patri hgaphmenois kai ihsou xristw tethrhmenois klhtois
jud 1:2 eleos umin kai eirhnh kai agaph plhqunqeih.
jud 1:3 agaphtoi pasan spoudhn poioumenos grafein umin peri ths koinhs hmwn swthrias anagkhn esxon grayai umin parakalwn epagwnizesqai th apac paradoqeish tois agiois pistei.
jud 1:4 pareisedusan gar tines anqrwpoi oi palai progegrammenoi eis touto to krima asebeis thn tou qeou hmwn xarita metatiqentes eis aselgeian kai ton monon despothn kai kurion hmwn ihsoun xriston arnoumenoi.
jud 1:5 upomnhsai de umas boulomai eidotas umas panta oti [ihsous] apac laon ek ghs aiguptou swsas to deuteron tous mh pisteusantas apwlesen
jud 1:6 aggelous te tous mh thrhsantas thn eautwn arxhn alla apolipontas to idion oikhthrion eis krisin megalhs hmeras desmois aidiois upo zofon tethrhken
jud 1:7 ws sodoma kai gomorra kai ai peri autas poleis ton omoion tropon toutois ekporneusasai kai apelqousai opisw sarkos eteras prokeintai deigma puros aiwniou dikhn upexousai.
jud 1:8 omoiws mentoi kai outoi enupniazomenoi sarka men miainousin [kuriothtas] de aqetousin docas de blasfhmousin.
jud 1:9 o de mixahl o arxaggelos ote tw diabolw diakrinomenos dielegeto peri tou mwusews swmatos ouk etolmhsen krisin epenegkein blasfhmias alla eipen epitimhsai soi kurios.
jud 1:10 outoi de osa men ouk oidasin blasfhmousin osa de fusikws ws ta aloga zwa epistantai en toutois fqeirontai.
jud 1:11 ouai autois oti th odw tou kain eporeuqhsan kai th planh tou balaam misqou ecexuqhsan kai th antilogia tou kore apwlonto.
jud 1:12 outoi eisin oi en tais agapais umwn spilades suneuwxoumenoi afobws eautous poimainontes nefelai anudroi upo anemwn paraferomenai dendra fqinopwrina akarpa dis apoqanonta ekrizwqenta
jud 1:13 kumata agria qalasshs epafrizonta tas eautwn aisxunas asteres planhtai ois o zofos tou skotous eis aiwna tethrhtai.
jud 1:14 proefhteusen de kai toutois ebdomos apo adam enwx legwn idou hlqen kurios en agiais muriasin autou
jud 1:15 poihsai krisin kata pantwn kai elegcai pasan yuxhn peri pantwn twn ergwn asebeias autwn wn hsebhsan kai peri pantwn twn sklhrwn wn elalhsan kat autou amartwloi asebeis.
jud 1:16 outoi eisin goggustai memyimoiroi kata tas epiqumias eautwn poreuomenoi kai to stoma autwn lalei uperogka qaumazontes proswpa wfeleias xarin.
jud 1:17 umeis de agaphtoi mnhsqhte twn rhmatwn twn proeirhmenwn upo twn apostolwn tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou
jud 1:18 oti elegon umin oti ep esxatou tou xronou esontai empaiktai kata tas eautwn epiqumias poreuomenoi twn asebeiwn.
jud 1:19 outoi eisin oi apodiorizontes yuxikoi pneuma mh exontes.
jud 1:20 umeis de agaphtoi epoikodomountes eautous th agiwtath umwn pistei en pneumati agiw proseuxomenoi
jud 1:21 eautous en agaph qeou thrhsate prosdexomenoi to eleos tou kuriou hmwn ihsou xristou eis zwhn aiwnion.
jud 1:22 kai ous men [eleeite diakrinomenoi]
jud 1:23 [--] ek puros [arpasate] ous de eleate en fobw misountes kai ton apo ths sarkos espilwmenon xitwna.
jud 1:24 tw de dunamenw fulacai umas aptaistous kai sthsai katenwpion ths dochs autou amwmous en agalliasei
jud 1:25 monw qew swthri hmwn dia ihsou xristou tou kuriou hmwn doca megalwsunh kratos kai ecousia pro pantos tou aiwnos kai nun kai eis pantas tous aiwnas amhn.
rev 1:1 apokaluyis ihsou xristou hn edwken autw o qeos deicai tois doulois autou a dei genesqai en taxei kai eshmanen aposteilas dia tou aggelou autou tw doulw autou iwannh
rev 1:2 os emarturhsen ton logon tou qeou kai thn marturian ihsou xristou osa eiden.
rev 1:3 makarios o anaginwskwn kai oi akouontes tous logous ths profhteias kai thrountes ta en auth gegrammena o gar kairos eggus.
rev 1:4 iwannhs tais epta ekklhsiais tais en th asia xaris umin kai eirhnh apo o wn kai o hn kai o erxomenos kai apo twn epta pneumatwn a enwpion tou qronou autou
rev 1:5 kai apo ihsou xristou o martus o pistos o prwtotokos twn nekrwn kai o arxwn twn basilewn ths ghs. tw agapwnti hmas kai lusanti hmas ek twn amartiwn hmwn en tw aimati autou 
rev 1:6 kai epoihsen hmas basileian iereis tw qew kai patri autou autw h doca kai to kratos eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn amhn.
rev 1:7 idou erxetai meta twn nefelwn kai oyetai auton pas ofqalmos kai oitines auton ecekenthsan kai koyontai ep auton pasai ai fulai ths ghs. nai amhn.
rev 1:8 egw eimi to alfa kai to w legei kurios o qeos o wn kai o hn kai o erxomenos o pantokratwr.
rev 1:9 egw iwannhs o adelfos umwn kai sugkoinwnos en th qliyei kai basileia kai upomonh en ihsou egenomhn en th nhsw th kaloumenh patmw dia ton logon tou qeou kai thn marturian ihsou.
rev 1:10 egenomhn en pneumati en th kuriakh hmera kai hkousa opisw mou fwnhn megalhn ws salpiggos
rev 1:11 legoushs o blepeis grayon eis biblion kai pemyon tais epta ekklhsiais eis efeson kai eis smurnan kai eis pergamon kai eis quateira kai eis sardeis kai eis filadelfeian kai eis laodikeian.
rev 1:12 kai epestreya blepein thn fwnhn htis elalei met emou kai epistreyas eidon epta luxnias xrusas
rev 1:13 kai en mesw twn luxniwn omoion uion anqrwpou endedumenon podhrh kai periezwsmenon pros tois mastois zwnhn xrusan
rev 1:14 h de kefalh autou kai ai trixes leukai ws erion leukon ws xiwn kai oi ofqalmoi autou ws floc puros
rev 1:15 kai oi podes autou omoioi xalkolibanw ws en kaminw [pepurwmenw] kai h fwnh autou ws fwnh udatwn pollwn
rev 1:16 kai exwn en th decia xeiri autou asteras epta kai ek tou stomatos autou romfaia distomos oceia ekporeuomenh kai h oyis autou ws o hlios fainei en th dunamei autou.
rev 1:17 kai ote eidon auton epesa pros tous podas autou ws nekros kai eqhken thn decian autou ep eme legwn mh fobou egw eimi o prwtos kai o esxatos
rev 1:18 kai o zwn kai egenomhn nekros kai idou zwn eimi eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn kai exw tas kleis tou qanatou kai tou adou.
rev 1:19 grayon oun a eides kai a eisin kai a mellei genesqai meta tauta.
rev 1:20 to musthrion twn epta asterwn ous eides epi ths decias mou kai tas epta luxnias tas xrusas oi epta asteres aggeloi twn epta ekklhsiwn eisin kai ai luxniai ai epta epta ekklhsiai eisin.
rev 2:1 tw aggelw ths en efesw ekklhsias grayon tade legei o kratwn tous epta asteras en th decia autou o peripatwn en mesw twn epta luxniwn twn xruswn
rev 2:2 oida ta erga sou kai ton kopon kai thn upomonhn sou kai oti ou dunh bastasai kakous kai epeirasas tous legontas eautous apostolous kai ouk eisin kai eures autous yeudeis
rev 2:3 kai upomonhn exeis kai ebastasas dia to onoma mou kai ou kekopiakes.
rev 2:4 alla exw kata sou oti thn agaphn sou thn prwthn afhkes.
rev 2:5 mnhmoneue oun poqen peptwkas kai metanohson kai ta prwta erga poihson ei de mh erxomai soi kai kinhsw thn luxnian sou ek tou topou auths ean mh metanohshs.
rev 2:6 alla touto exeis oti miseis ta erga twn nikolaitwn a kagw misw.
rev 2:7 o exwn ous akousatw ti to pneuma legei tais ekklhsiais. tw nikwnti dwsw autw fagein ek tou culou ths zwhs o estin en tw paradeisw tou qeou [mou].
rev 2:8 kai tw aggelw ths en smurnh ekklhsias grayon tade legei o prwtos kai o esxatos os egeneto nekros kai ezhsen
rev 2:9 oida sou thn qliyin kai thn ptwxeian alla plousios ei kai thn blasfhmian ek twn legontwn ioudaious einai eautous kai ouk eisin alla sunagwgh tou satana.
rev 2:10 mhden fobou a melleis pasxein. idou mellei ballein o diabolos ec umwn eis fulakhn ina peirasqhte kai ecete qliyin hmerwn deka. ginou pistos axri qanatou kai dwsw soi ton stefanon ths zwhs.
rev 2:11 o exwn ous akousatw ti to pneuma legei tais ekklhsiais. o nikwn ou mh adikhqh ek tou qanatou tou deuterou.
rev 2:12 kai tw aggelw ths en pergamw ekklhsias grayon tade legei o exwn thn romfaian thn distomon thn oceian
rev 2:13 oida pou katoikeis opou o qronos tou satana kai krateis to onoma mou kai ouk hrnhsw thn pistin mou kai en tais hmerais antipas o martus mou o pistos mou os apektanqh par umin opou o satanas katoikei.
rev 2:14 all exw kata sou oliga oti exeis ekei kratountas thn didaxhn balaam os edidasken tw balak balein skandalon enwpion twn uiwn israhl fagein eidwloquta kai porneusai
rev 2:15 outws exeis kai su kratountas thn didaxhn twn nikolaitwn omoiws.
rev 2:16 metanohson oun ei de mh erxomai soi taxu kai polemhsw met autwn en th romfaia tou stomatos mou.
rev 2:17 o exwn ous akousatw ti to pneuma legei tais ekklhsiais. tw nikwnti dwsw autw tou manna tou kekrummenou kai dwsw autw yhfon leukhn kai epi thn yhfon onoma kainon gegrammenon o oudeis oiden ei mh o lambanwn.
rev 2:18 kai tw aggelw ths en quateirois ekklhsias grayon tade legei o uios tou qeou o exwn tous ofqalmous autou ws floga puros kai oi podes autou omoioi xalkolibanw
rev 2:19 oida sou ta erga kai thn agaphn kai thn pistin kai thn diakonian kai thn upomonhn sou kai ta erga sou ta esxata pleiona twn prwtwn.
rev 2:20 alla exw kata sou oti afeis thn gunaika iezabel h legousa eauthn profhtin kai didaskei kai plana tous emous doulous porneusai kai fagein eidwloquta.
rev 2:21 kai edwka auth xronon ina metanohsh kai ou qelei metanohsai ek ths porneias auths.
rev 2:22 idou ballw authn eis klinhn kai tous moixeuontas met auths eis qliyin megalhn ean mh metanohswsin ek twn ergwn [autwn]
rev 2:23 kai ta tekna auths apoktenw en qanatw kai gnwsontai pasai ai ekklhsiai oti egw eimi o eraunwn nefrous kai kardias kai dwsw umin ekastw kata ta erga umwn.
rev 2:24 umin de legw tois loipois tois en quateirois osoi ouk exousin thn didaxhn tauthn oitines ouk egnwsan ta baqea tou satana ws legousin ou ballw ef umas allo baros
rev 2:25 plhn o exete krathsate axris ou an hcw.
rev 2:26 kai o nikwn kai o thrwn axri telous ta erga mou dwsw autw ecousian epi twn eqnwn
rev 2:27 kai poimanei autous en rabdw sidhra ws ta skeuh ta keramika suntribetai
rev 2:28 ws kagw eilhfa para tou patros mou kai dwsw autw ton astera ton prwinon.
rev 2:29 o exwn ous akousatw ti to pneuma legei tais ekklhsiais.
rev 3:1 kai tw aggelw ths en sardesin ekklhsias grayon tade legei o exwn ta epta pneumata tou qeou kai tous epta asteras oida sou ta erga oti onoma exeis oti zhs kai nekros ei.
rev 3:2 ginou grhgorwn kai sthrison ta loipa a emellon apoqanein ou gar eurhka sou ta erga peplhrwmena enwpion tou qeou mou
rev 3:3 mnhmoneue oun pws eilhfas kai hkousas kai threi kai metanohson. ean oun mh grhgorhshs hcw ws klepths kai ou mh gnws poian wran hcw epi se.
rev 3:4 alla exeis oliga onomata en sardesin a ouk emolunan ta imatia autwn kai peripathsousin met emou en leukois oti acioi eisin.
rev 3:5 o nikwn outws peribaleitai en imatiois leukois kai ou mh ecaleiyw to onoma autou ek ths biblou ths zwhs kai omologhsw to onoma autou enwpion tou patros mou kai enwpion twn aggelwn autou.
rev 3:6 o exwn ous akousatw ti to pneuma legei tais ekklhsiais.
rev 3:7 kai tw aggelw ths en filadelfeia ekklhsias grayon tade legei o agios o alhqinos o exwn thn klein dauid o anoigwn kai oudeis kleisei kai kleiwn kai oudeis anoigei
rev 3:8 oida sou ta erga idou dedwka enwpion sou quran hnewgmenhn hn oudeis dunatai kleisai authn oti mikran exeis dunamin kai ethrhsas mou ton logon kai ouk hrnhsw to onoma mou.
rev 3:9 idou didw ek ths sunagwghs tou satana twn legontwn eautous ioudaious einai kai ouk eisin alla yeudontai idou poihsw autous ina hcousin kai proskunhsousin enwpion twn podwn sou kai gnwsin oti egw hgaphsa se.
rev 3:10 oti ethrhsas ton logon ths upomonhs mou kagw se thrhsw ek ths wras tou peirasmou ths melloushs erxesqai epi ths oikoumenhs olhs peirasai tous katoikountas epi ths ghs.
rev 3:11 erxomai taxu kratei o exeis ina mhdeis labh ton stefanon sou.
rev 3:12 o nikwn poihsw auton stulon en tw naw tou qeou mou kai ecw ou mh ecelqh eti kai grayw ep auton to onoma tou qeou mou kai to onoma ths polews tou qeou mou ths kainhs ierousalhm h katabainousa ek tou ouranou apo tou qeou mou kai to onoma mou to kainon.
rev 3:13 o exwn ous akousatw ti to pneuma legei tais ekklhsiais.
rev 3:14 kai tw aggelw ths en laodikeia ekklhsias grayon tade legei o amhn o martus o pistos kai alhqinos h arxh ths ktisews tou qeou
rev 3:15 oida sou ta erga oti oute yuxros ei oute zestos. ofelon yuxros hs h zestos.
rev 3:16 outws oti xliaros ei kai oute zestos oute yuxros mellw se emesai ek tou stomatos mou.
rev 3:17 oti legeis oti plousios eimi kai peplouthka kai ouden xreian exw kai ouk oidas oti su ei o talaipwros kai eleeinos kai ptwxos kai tuflos kai gumnos
rev 3:18 sumbouleuw soi agorasai par emou xrusion pepurwmenon ek puros ina plouthshs kai imatia leuka ina peribalh kai mh fanerwqh h aisxunh ths gumnothtos sou kai kollourion egxrisai tous ofqalmous sou ina blephs.
rev 3:19 egw osous ean filw elegxw kai paideuw zhleue oun kai metanohson.
rev 3:20 idou esthka epi thn quran kai krouw ean tis akoush ths fwnhs mou kai anoich thn quran kai eiseleusomai pros auton kai deipnhsw met autou kai autos met emou.
rev 3:21 o nikwn dwsw autw kaqisai met emou en tw qronw mou ws kagw enikhsa kai ekaqisa meta tou patros mou en tw qronw autou.
rev 3:22 o exwn ous akousatw ti to pneuma legei tais ekklhsiais.
rev 4:1 meta tauta eidon kai idou qura hnewgmenh en tw ouranw kai h fwnh h prwth hn hkousa ws salpiggos laloushs met emou legwn anaba wde kai deicw soi a dei genesqai meta tauta.
rev 4:2 euqews egenomhn en pneumati kai idou qronos ekeito en tw ouranw kai epi ton qronon kaqhmenos
rev 4:3 kai o kaqhmenos omoios orasei liqw iaspidi kai sardiw kai iris kukloqen tou qronou omoios orasei smaragdinw.
rev 4:4 kai kukloqen tou qronou qronous eikosi tessares kai epi tous qronous eikosi tessaras presbuterous kaqhmenous peribeblhmenous en imatiois leukois kai epi tas kefalas autwn stefanous xrusous.
rev 4:5 kai ek tou qronou ekporeuontai astrapai kai fwnai kai brontai kai epta lampades puros kaiomenai enwpion tou qronou a eisin ta epta pneumata tou qeou
rev 4:6 kai enwpion tou qronou ws qalassa ualinh omoia krustallw. kai en mesw tou qronou kai kuklw tou qronou tessara zwa gemonta ofqalmwn emprosqen kai opisqen
rev 4:7 kai to zwon to prwton omoion leonti kai to deuteron zwon omoion mosxw kai to triton zwon exwn to proswpon ws anqrwpou kai to tetarton zwon omoion aetw petomenw.
rev 4:8 kai ta tessara zwa en kaq en autwn exwn ana pterugas ec kukloqen kai eswqen gemousin ofqalmwn kai anapausin ouk exousin hmeras kai nuktos legontes agios agios agios kurios o qeos o pantokratwr o hn kai o wn kai o erxomenos.
rev 4:9 kai otan dwsousin ta zwa docan kai timhn kai euxaristian tw kaqhmenw epi tw qronw tw zwnti eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn
rev 4:10 pesountai oi eikosi tessares presbuteroi enwpion tou kaqhmenou epi tou qronou kai proskunhsousin tw zwnti eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn kai balousin tous stefanous autwn enwpion tou qronou legontes
rev 4:11 acios ei o kurios kai o qeos hmwn labein thn docan kai thn timhn kai thn dunamin oti su ektisas ta panta kai dia to qelhma sou [eisin] kai ektisqhsan.
rev 5:1 kai eidon epi thn decian tou kaqhmenou epi tou qronou biblion gegrammenon eswqen kai opisqen katesfragismenon sfragisin epta.
rev 5:2 kai eidon aggelon isxuron khrussonta en fwnh megalh tis acios anoicai to biblion kai lusai tas sfragidas autou;
rev 5:3 kai oudeis edunato en tw ouranw oude epi ths ghs oude upokatw ths ghs anoicai to biblion oute blepein auto.
rev 5:4 kai eklaion polu oti oudeis acios eureqh anoicai to biblion oute blepein auto.
rev 5:5 kai eis ek twn presbuterwn legei moi mh klaie idou enikhsen o lewn o ek ths fulhs iouda h riza dauid anoicai to biblion kai tas epta sfragidas autou.
rev 5:6 kai eidon en mesw tou qronou kai twn tessarwn zwwn kai en mesw twn presbuterwn arnion esthkos ws esfagmenon exwn kerata epta kai ofqalmous epta oi eisin ta epta pneumata tou qeou apestalmenoi eis pasan thn ghn.
rev 5:7 kai hlqen kai eilhfen ek ths decias tou kaqhmenou epi tou qronou.
rev 5:8 kai ote elaben to biblion ta tessara zwa kai oi eikosi tessares presbuteroi epesan enwpion tou arniou exontes ekastos kiqaran kai fialas xrusas gemousas qumiamatwn ai eisin ai proseuxai twn agiwn.
rev 5:9 kai adousin wdhn kainhn legontes acios ei labein to biblion kai anoicai tas sfragidas autou oti esfaghs kai hgorasas tw qew [hmwn] en tw aimati sou ek pashs fulhs kai glwsshs kai laou kai eqnous
rev 5:10 kai epoihsas [hmas] tw qew hmwn basileian kai iereis kai basileusousin epi ths ghs.
rev 5:11 kai eidon kai hkousa fwnhn aggelwn pollwn kuklw tou qronou kai twn zwwn kai twn presbuterwn kai hn o ariqmos autwn muriades muriadwn kai xiliades xiliadwn
rev 5:12 legontes fwnh megalh acion estin to arnion to esfagmenon labein thn dunamin kai plouton kai sofian kai isxun kai timhn kai docan kai eulogian.
rev 5:13 kai pan ktisma o en tw ouranw kai epi ths ghs kai upokatw ths ghs kai epi ths qalasshs kai ta en autois panta hkousa legontas tw kaqhmenw epi tw qronw kai tw arniw h eulogia kai h timh kai h doca kai to kratos eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn.
rev 5:14 kai ta tessara zwa elegon amhn kai oi presbuteroi epesan kai prosekunhsan.
rev 6:1 kai eidon ote hnoicen to arnion mian ek twn epta sfragidwn kai hkousa enos ek twn tessarwn zwwn legontos ws fwnh bronths erxou.
rev 6:2 kai eidon kai idou ippos leukos kai o kaqhmenos ep auton exwn tocon kai edoqh autw stefanos kai echlqen nikwn kai ina nikhsh.
rev 6:3 kai ote hnoicen thn sfragida thn deuteran hkousa tou deuterou zwou legontos erxou.
rev 6:4 kai echlqen allos ippos purros kai tw kaqhmenw ep auton edoqh autw labein thn eirhnhn ek ths ghs kai ina allhlous sfacousin kai edoqh autw maxaira megalh.
rev 6:5 kai ote hnoicen thn sfragida thn trithn hkousa tou tritou zwou legontos erxou. [--] kai idou ippos melas kai o kaqhmenos ep auton exwn zugon en th xeiri autou.
rev 6:6 kai hkousa ws fwnhn en mesw twn tessarwn zwwn legousan xoinic sitou dhnariou kai treis xoinikes kriqwn dhnariou kai to elaion kai ton oinon mh adikhshs.
rev 6:7 kai ote hnoicen thn sfragida thn tetarthn hkousa fwnhn tou tetartou zwou legontos erxou.
rev 6:8 kai eidon kai idou ippos xlwros kai o kaqhmenos epanw autou onoma autw o qanatos kai o adhs hkolouqei met autou kai edoqh autois ecousia epi to tetarton ths ghs apokteinai en romfaia kai en limw kai en qanatw kai upo twn qhriwn ths ghs.
rev 6:9 kai ote hnoicen thn pempthn sfragida eidon upokatw tou qusiasthriou tas yuxas twn esfagmenwn dia ton logon tou qeou kai dia thn marturian hn eixon.
rev 6:10 kai ekracan fwnh megalh legontes ews pote o despoths o agios kai alhqinos ou krineis kai ekdikeis to aima hmwn ek twn katoikountwn epi ths ghs;
rev 6:11 kai edoqh autois ekastw stolh leukh kai erreqh autois ina anapausontai eti xronon mikron ews plhrwqwsin kai oi sundouloi autwn kai oi adelfoi autwn oi mellontes apoktennesqai ws kai autoi.
rev 6:12 kai eidon ote hnoicen thn sfragida thn ekthn kai seismos megas egeneto kai o hlios egeneto melas ws sakkos trixinos kai h selhnh olh egeneto ws aima
rev 6:13 kai oi asteres tou ouranou epesan eis thn ghn ws sukh ballei tous olunqous auths upo anemou megalou seiomenh
rev 6:14 kai o ouranos apexwrisqh ws biblion elissomenon kai pan oros kai nhsos ek twn topwn autwn ekinhqhsan.
rev 6:15 kai oi basileis ths ghs kai oi megistanes kai oi xiliarxoi kai oi plousioi kai oi isxuroi kai pas doulos kai eleuqeros ekruyan eautous eis ta sphlaia kai eis tas petras twn orewn
rev 6:16 kai legousin tois oresin kai tais petrais pesete ef hmas kai kruyate hmas apo proswpou tou kaqhmenou epi tou qronou kai apo ths orghs tou arniou
rev 6:17 oti hlqen h hmera h megalh ths orghs autwn kai tis dunatai staqhnai;
rev 7:1 meta touto eidon tessaras aggelous estwtas epi tas tessaras gwnias ths ghs kratountas tous tessaras anemous ths ghs ina mh pneh anemos epi ths ghs mhte epi ths qalasshs mhte epi pan dendron.
rev 7:2 kai eidon allon aggelon anabainonta apo anatolhs hliou exonta sfragida qeou zwntos kai ekracen fwnh megalh tois tessarsin aggelois ois edoqh autois adikhsai thn ghn kai thn qalassan
rev 7:3 legwn mh adikhshte thn ghn mhte thn qalassan mhte ta dendra axri sfragiswmen tous doulous tou qeou hmwn epi twn metwpwn autwn.
rev 7:4 kai hkousa ton ariqmon twn esfragismenwn ekaton tesserakonta tessares xiliades esfragismenoi ek pashs fulhs uiwn israhl
rev 7:5 ek fulhs iouda dwdeka xiliades esfragismenoi ek fulhs roubhn dwdeka xiliades ek fulhs gad dwdeka xiliades
rev 7:6 ek fulhs ashr dwdeka xiliades ek fulhs nefqalim dwdeka xiliades ek fulhs manassh dwdeka xiliades
rev 7:7 ek fulhs sumewn dwdeka xiliades ek fulhs leui dwdeka xiliades ek fulhs issaxar dwdeka xiliades
rev 7:8 ek fulhs zaboulwn dwdeka xiliades ek fulhs iwshf dwdeka xiliades ek fulhs beniamin dwdeka xiliades esfragismenoi.
rev 7:9 meta tauta eidon kai idou oxlos polus on ariqmhsai auton oudeis edunato ek pantos eqnous kai fulwn kai lawn kai glwsswn estwtes enwpion tou qronou kai enwpion tou arniou peribeblhmenous stolas leukas kai foinikes en tais xersin autwn
rev 7:10 kai krazousin fwnh megalh legontes h swthria tw qew hmwn tw kaqhmenw epi tw qronw kai tw arniw.
rev 7:11 kai pantes oi aggeloi eisthkeisan kuklw tou qronou kai twn presbuterwn kai twn tessarwn zwwn kai epesan enwpion tou qronou epi ta proswpa autwn kai prosekunhsan tw qew
rev 7:12 legontes amhn h eulogia kai h doca kai h sofia kai h euxaristia kai h timh kai h dunamis kai h isxus tw qew hmwn eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn amhn.
rev 7:13 kai apekriqh eis ek twn presbuterwn legwn moi outoi oi peribeblhmenoi tas stolas tas leukas tines eisin kai poqen hlqon;
rev 7:14 kai eirhka autw kurie mou su oidas. kai eipen moi outoi eisin oi erxomenoi ek ths qliyews ths megalhs kai eplunan tas stolas autwn kai eleukanan autas en tw aimati tou arniou.
rev 7:15 dia touto eisin enwpion tou qronou tou qeou kai latreuousin autw hmeras kai nuktos en tw naw autou kai o kaqhmenos epi tou qronou skhnwsei ep autous.
rev 7:16 ou peinasousin eti oude diyhsousin eti oude mh pesh ep autous o hlios oude pan kauma
rev 7:17 oti to arnion to ana meson tou qronou poimanei autous kai odhghsei autous epi zwhs phgas udatwn kai ecaleiyei o qeos pan dakruon ek twn ofqalmwn autwn.
rev 8:1 kai otan hnoicen thn sfragida thn ebdomhn egeneto sigh en tw ouranw ws hmiwrion.
rev 8:2 kai eidon tous epta aggelous oi enwpion tou qeou esthkasin kai edoqhsan autois epta salpigges.
rev 8:3 kai allos aggelos hlqen kai estaqh epi tou qusiasthriou exwn libanwton xrusoun kai edoqh autw qumiamata polla ina dwsei tais proseuxais twn agiwn pantwn epi to qusiasthrion to xrusoun to enwpion tou qronou.
rev 8:4 kai anebh o kapnos twn qumiamatwn tais proseuxais twn agiwn ek xeiros tou aggelou enwpion tou qeou.
rev 8:5 kai eilhfen o aggelos ton libanwton kai egemisen auton ek tou puros tou qusiasthriou kai ebalen eis thn ghn kai egenonto brontai kai fwnai kai astrapai kai seismos.
rev 8:6 kai oi epta aggeloi oi exontes tas epta salpiggas htoimasan autous ina salpiswsin.
rev 8:7 kai o prwtos esalpisen kai egeneto xalaza kai pur memigmena en aimati kai eblhqh eis thn ghn kai to triton ths ghs katekah kai to triton twn dendrwn katekah kai pas xortos xlwros katekah.
rev 8:8 kai o deuteros aggelos esalpisen kai ws oros mega puri kaiomenon eblhqh eis thn qalassan kai egeneto to triton ths qalasshs aima
rev 8:9 kai apeqanen to triton twn ktismatwn twn en th qalassh ta exonta yuxas kai to triton twn ploiwn diefqarhsan.
rev 8:10 kai o tritos aggelos esalpisen kai epesen ek tou ouranou asthr megas kaiomenos ws lampas kai epesen epi to triton twn potamwn kai epi tas phgas twn udatwn.
rev 8:11 kai to onoma tou asteros legetai o ayinqos. kai egeneto to triton twn udatwn eis ayinqon kai polloi twn anqrwpwn apeqanon ek twn udatwn oti epikranqhsan.
rev 8:12 kai o tetartos aggelos esalpisen kai eplhgh to triton tou hliou kai to triton ths selhnhs kai to triton twn asterwn ina skotisqh to triton autwn kai h hmera mh fanh to triton auths kai h nuc omoiws.
rev 8:13 kai eidon kai hkousa enos aetou petomenou en mesouranhmati legontos fwnh megalh ouai ouai ouai tous katoikountas epi ths ghs ek twn loipwn fwnwn ths salpiggos twn triwn aggelwn twn mellontwn salpizein.
rev 9:1 kai o pemptos aggelos esalpisen kai eidon astera ek tou ouranou peptwkota eis thn ghn kai edoqh autw h kleis tou freatos ths abussou.
rev 9:2 kai hnoicen to frear ths abussou kai anebh kapnos ek tou freatos ws kapnos kaminou megalhs kai eskotwqh o hlios kai o ahr ek tou kapnou tou freatos.
rev 9:3 kai ek tou kapnou echlqon akrides eis thn ghn kai edoqh autais ecousia ws exousin ecousian oi skorpioi ths ghs.
rev 9:4 kai erreqh autais ina mh adikhsousin ton xorton ths ghs oude pan xlwron oude pan dendron ei mh tous anqrwpous oitines ouk exousi thn sfragida tou qeou epi twn metwpwn.
rev 9:5 kai edoqh autois ina mh apokteinwsin autous all ina basanisqhsontai mhnas pente kai o basanismos autwn ws basanismos skorpiou otan paish anqrwpon.
rev 9:6 kai en tais hmerais ekeinais zhthsousin oi anqrwpoi ton qanaton kai ou mh eurhsousin auton kai epiqumhsousin apoqanein kai feugei o qanatos ap autwn.
rev 9:7 kai ta omoiwmata twn akridwn omoia ippois htoimasmenois eis polemon kai epi tas kefalas autwn ws stefanoi omoioi xrusw kai ta proswpa autwn ws proswpa anqrwpwn
rev 9:8 kai eixon trixas ws trixas gunaikwn kai oi odontes autwn ws leontwn hsan
rev 9:9 kai eixon qwrakas ws qwrakas sidhrous kai h fwnh twn pterugwn autwn ws fwnh armatwn ippwn pollwn trexontwn eis polemon.
rev 9:10 kai exousin ouras omoias skorpiois kai kentra kai en tais ourais autwn h ecousia autwn adikhsai tous anqrwpous mhnas pente.
rev 9:11 exousin ep autwn basilea ton aggelon ths abussou onoma autw ebraisti abaddwn kai en th ellhnikh onoma exei apolluwn.
rev 9:12 h ouai h mia aphlqen idou erxetai eti duo ouai meta tauta.
rev 9:13 kai o ektos aggelos esalpisen kai hkousa fwnhn mian ek twn [--] keratwn tou qusiasthriou tou xrusou tou enwpion tou qeou
rev 9:14 legonta tw ektw aggelw o exwn thn salpigga luson tous tessaras aggelous tous dedemenous epi tw potamw tw megalw eufrath.
rev 9:15 kai eluqhsan oi tessares aggeloi oi htoimasmenoi eis thn wran kai hmeran kai mhna kai eniauton ina apokteinwsin to triton twn anqrwpwn.
rev 9:16 kai o ariqmos twn strateumatwn tou ippikou dismuriades muriadwn hkousa ton ariqmon autwn.
rev 9:17 kai outws eidon tous ippous en th orasei kai tous kaqhmenous ep autwn exontas qwrakas purinous kai uakinqinous kai qeiwdeis kai ai kefalai twn ippwn ws kefalai leontwn kai ek twn stomatwn autwn ekporeuetai pur kai kapnos kai qeion.
rev 9:18 apo twn triwn plhgwn toutwn apektanqhsan to triton twn anqrwpwn ek tou puros kai tou kapnou kai tou qeiou tou ekporeuomenou ek twn stomatwn autwn.
rev 9:19 h gar ecousia twn ippwn en tw stomati autwn estin kai en tais ourais autwn ai gar ourai autwn omoiai ofesin exousai kefalas kai en autais adikousin.
rev 9:20 kai oi loipoi twn anqrwpwn oi ouk apektanqhsan en tais plhgais tautais oude metenohsan ek twn ergwn twn xeirwn autwn ina mh proskunhsousin ta daimonia kai ta eidwla ta xrusa kai ta argura kai ta xalka kai ta liqina kai ta culina a oute blepein dunantai oute akouein oute peripatein
rev 9:21 kai ou metenohsan ek twn fonwn autwn oute ek twn farmakwn autwn oute ek ths porneias autwn oute ek twn klemmatwn autwn.
rev 10:1 kai eidon allon aggelon isxuron katabainonta ek tou ouranou peribeblhmenon nefelhn kai h iris epi ths kefalhs autou kai to proswpon autou ws o hlios kai oi podes autou ws stuloi puros
rev 10:2 kai exwn en th xeiri autou biblaridion hnewgmenon. kai eqhken ton poda autou ton decion epi ths qalasshs ton de euwnumon epi ths ghs
rev 10:3 kai ekracen fwnh megalh wsper lewn mukatai. kai ote ekracen elalhsan ai epta brontai tas eautwn fwnas.
rev 10:4 kai [osa] elalhsan ai epta brontai [emellon] grafein kai hkousa fwnhn ek tou ouranou legousan sfragison a elalhsan ai epta brontai kai mh auta grayhs.
rev 10:5 kai o aggelos on eidon estwta epi ths qalasshs kai epi ths ghs hren thn xeira autou thn decian eis ton ouranon
rev 10:6 kai wmosen en tw zwnti eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn os ektisen ton ouranon kai ta en autw kai thn ghn kai ta en auth kai thn qalassan kai ta en auth oti xronos ouketi estai
rev 10:7 all en tais hmerais ths fwnhs tou ebdomou aggelou otan mellh salpizein kai etelesqh to musthrion tou qeou ws euhggelisen tous eautou doulous tous profhtas.
rev 10:8 kai h fwnh hn hkousa ek tou ouranou palin lalousan met emou kai legousan upage labe to biblion to hnewgmenon en th xeiri tou aggelou tou estwtos epi ths qalasshs kai epi ths ghs.
rev 10:9 kai aphlqa pros ton aggelon legwn autw dounai moi to biblaridion. kai legei moi labe kai katafage auto kai pikranei sou thn koilian all en tw stomati sou estai gluku ws meli.
rev 10:10 kai elabon to biblaridion ek ths xeiros tou aggelou kai katefagon auto kai hn en tw stomati mou ws meli gluku kai ote efagon auto epikranqh h koilia mou.
rev 10:11 kai legousin moi dei se palin profhteusai epi laois kai eqnesin kai glwssais kai basileusin pollois.
rev 11:1 kai edoqh moi kalamos omoios rabdw legwn egeire kai metrhson ton naon tou qeou kai to qusiasthrion kai tous proskunountas en autw.
rev 11:2 kai thn aulhn thn ecwqen tou naou ekbale ecwqen kai mh authn metrhshs oti edoqh tois eqnesin kai thn polin thn agian pathsousin mhnas tesserakonta kai duo.
rev 11:3 kai dwsw tois dusin martusin mou kai profhteusousin hmeras xilias diakosias echkonta peribeblhmenoi sakkous.
rev 11:4 outoi eisin ai duo elaiai kai ai duo luxniai ai enwpion tou kuriou ths ghs estwtes.
rev 11:5 kai ei tis autous qelei adikhsai pur ekporeuetai ek tou stomatos autwn kai katesqiei tous exqrous autwn kai ei tis qelhsh autous adikhsai outws dei auton apoktanqhnai.
rev 11:6 outoi exousin thn ecousian kleisai ton ouranon ina mh uetos brexh tas hmeras ths profhteias autwn kai ecousian exousin epi twn udatwn strefein auta eis aima kai patacai thn ghn en pash plhgh osakis ean qelhswsin.
rev 11:7 kai otan teleswsin thn marturian autwn to qhrion to anabainon ek ths abussou poihsei met autwn polemon kai nikhsei autous kai apoktenei autous.
rev 11:8 kai to ptwma autwn epi ths plateias ths polews ths megalhs htis kaleitai pneumatikws sodoma kai aiguptos opou kai o kurios autwn estaurwqh.
rev 11:9 kai blepousin ek twn lawn kai fulwn kai glwsswn kai eqnwn to ptwma autwn hmeras treis kai hmisu kai ta ptwmata autwn ouk afiousin teqhnai eis mnhma.
rev 11:10 kai oi katoikountes epi ths ghs xairousin ep autois kai eufrainontai kai dwra pemyousin allhlois oti outoi oi duo profhtai ebasanisan tous katoikountas epi ths ghs.
rev 11:11 kai meta tas treis hmeras kai hmisu pneuma zwhs ek tou qeou eishlqen en autois kai esthsan epi tous podas autwn kai fobos megas epepesen epi tous qewrountas autous.
rev 11:12 kai [hkousa] fwnhs megalhs ek tou ouranou legoushs autois anabate wde kai anebhsan eis ton ouranon en th nefelh kai eqewrhsan autous oi exqroi autwn.
rev 11:13 kai en ekeinh th wra egeneto seismos megas kai to dekaton ths polews epesen kai apektanqhsan en tw seismw onomata anqrwpwn xiliades epta kai oi loipoi emfoboi egenonto kai edwkan docan tw qew tou ouranou.
rev 11:14 h ouai h deutera aphlqen idou h ouai h trith erxetai taxu.
rev 11:15 kai o ebdomos aggelos esalpisen kai egenonto fwnai megalai en tw ouranw legontes egeneto h basileia tou kosmou tou kuriou hmwn kai tou xristou autou kai basileusei eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn.
rev 11:16 kai oi eikosi tessares presbuteroi oi enwpion tou qeou kaqhmenoi epi tous qronous autwn epesan epi ta proswpa autwn kai prosekunhsan tw qew
rev 11:17 legontes euxaristoumen soi kurie o qeos o pantokratwr o wn kai o hn oti eilhfas thn dunamin sou thn megalhn kai ebasileusas
rev 11:18 kai ta eqnh wrgisqhsan kai hlqen h orgh sou kai o kairos twn nekrwn kriqhnai kai dounai ton misqon tois doulois sou tois profhtais kai tois agiois kai tois foboumenois to onoma sou tous mikrous kai tous megalous kai diafqeirai tous diafqeirontas thn ghn.
rev 11:19 kai hnoigh o naos tou qeou o en tw ouranw kai wfqh h kibwtos ths diaqhkhs autou en tw naw autou kai egenonto astrapai kai fwnai kai brontai kai seismos kai xalaza megalh.
rev 12:1 kai shmeion mega wfqh en tw ouranw gunh peribeblhmenh ton hlion kai h selhnh upokatw twn podwn auths kai epi ths kefalhs auths stefanos asterwn dwdeka
rev 12:2 kai en gastri exousa kai krazei wdinousa kai basanizomenh tekein.
rev 12:3 kai wfqh allo shmeion en tw ouranw kai idou drakwn megas purros exwn kefalas epta kai kerata deka kai epi tas kefalas autou epta diadhmata
rev 12:4 kai h oura autou surei to triton twn asterwn tou ouranou kai ebalen autous eis thn ghn. kai o drakwn esthken enwpion ths gunaikos ths melloushs tekein ina otan tekh to teknon auths katafagh.
rev 12:5 kai eteken uion arsen os mellei poimainein panta ta eqnh en rabdw sidhra kai hrpasqh to teknon auths pros ton qeon kai pros ton qronon autou.
rev 12:6 kai h gunh efugen eis thn erhmon opou exei ekei topon htoimasmenon apo tou qeou ina ekei trefwsin authn hmeras xilias diakosias echkonta.
rev 12:7 kai egeneto polemos en tw ouranw o mixahl kai oi aggeloi autou tou polemhsai meta tou drakontos. kai o drakwn epolemhsen kai oi aggeloi autou
rev 12:8 kai ouk isxusen oude topos eureqh autwn eti en tw ouranw.
rev 12:9 kai eblhqh o drakwn o megas o ofis o arxaios o kaloumenos diabolos kai o satanas o planwn thn oikoumenhn olhn eblhqh eis thn ghn kai oi aggeloi autou met autou eblhqhsan.
rev 12:10 kai hkousa fwnhn megalhn en tw ouranw legousan arti egeneto h swthria kai h dunamis kai h basileia tou qeou hmwn kai h ecousia tou xristou autou oti eblhqh o kathgwr twn adelfwn hmwn o kathgorwn autous enwpion tou qeou hmwn hmeras kai nuktos.
rev 12:11 kai autoi enikhsan auton dia to aima tou arniou kai dia ton logon ths marturias autwn kai ouk hgaphsan thn yuxhn autwn axri qanatou.
rev 12:12 dia touto eufrainesqe oi ouranoi kai oi en autois skhnountes ouai thn ghn kai thn qalassan oti katebh o diabolos pros umas exwn qumon megan eidws oti oligon kairon exei.
rev 12:13 kai ote eiden o drakwn oti eblhqh eis thn ghn ediwcen thn gunaika htis eteken ton arsena.
rev 12:14 kai edoqhsan th gunaiki ai duo pteruges tou aetou tou megalou ina pethtai eis thn erhmon eis ton topon auths opou trefetai ekei kairon kai kairous kai hmisu kairou apo proswpou tou ofews.
rev 12:15 kai ebalen o ofis ek tou stomatos autou opisw ths gunaikos udwr ws potamon ina authn potamoforhton poihsh.
rev 12:16 kai ebohqhsen h gh th gunaiki kai hnoicen h gh to stoma auths kai katepien ton potamon on ebalen o drakwn ek tou stomatos autou.
rev 12:17 kai wrgisqh o drakwn epi th gunaiki kai aphlqen poihsai polemon meta twn loipwn tou spermatos auths twn thrountwn tas entolas tou qeou kai exontwn thn marturian ihsou
rev 12:18 kai [estaqhn] epi thn ammon ths qalasshs.
rev 13:1 kai eidon ek ths qalasshs qhrion anabainon exon kerata deka kai kefalas epta kai epi twn keratwn autou deka diadhmata kai epi tas kefalas autou onomata blasfhmias.
rev 13:2 kai to qhrion o eidon hn omoion pardalei kai oi podes autou ws arkou kai to stoma autou ws stoma leontos. kai edwken autw o drakwn thn dunamin autou kai ton qronon autou kai ecousian megalhn.
rev 13:3 kai mian ek twn kefalwn autou ws esfagmenhn eis qanaton kai h plhgh tou qanatou autou eqerapeuqh. kai eqaumasqh olh h gh opisw tou qhriou
rev 13:4 kai prosekunhsan tw drakonti oti edwken thn ecousian tw qhriw kai prosekunhsan tw qhriw legontes tis omoios tw qhriw kai tis dunatai polemhsai met autou;
rev 13:5 kai edoqh autw stoma laloun megala kai blasfhmias kai edoqh autw ecousia poihsai mhnas tesserakonta kai duo.
rev 13:6 kai hnoicen to stoma autou eis blasfhmias pros ton qeon blasfhmhsai to onoma autou kai thn skhnhn autou [kai] tous en tw ouranw skhnountas.
rev 13:7 [--] kai edoqh autw ecousia epi pasan fulhn kai laon kai glwssan kai eqnos.
rev 13:8 kai proskunhsousin auton pantes oi katoikountes epi ths ghs ou ou gegraptai to onoma autou en tw bibliw ths zwhs tou arniou tou esfagmenou apo katabolhs kosmou.
rev 13:9 ei tis exei ous akousatw.
rev 13:10 ei tis [--] aixmalwsian eis aixmalwsian upagei ei tis en maxairh [apokttenei dei] auton en maxairh apoktanqhnai. wde estin h upomonh kai h pistis twn agiwn.
rev 13:11 kai eidon allo qhrion anabainon ek ths ghs kai eixen kerata duo omoia arniw kai elalei ws drakwn.
rev 13:12 kai thn ecousian tou prwtou qhriou pasan poiei enwpion autou. kai poiei thn ghn kai tous en auth katoikountas ina proskunhsousin to qhrion to prwton ou eqerapeuqh h plhgh tou qanatou autou.
rev 13:13 kai poiei shmeia megala ina kai pur poih ek tou ouranou katabainein eis thn ghn enwpion twn anqrwpwn.
rev 13:14 kai plana tous katoikountas epi ths ghs dia ta shmeia a edoqh autw poihsai enwpion tou qhriou legwn tois katoikousin epi ths ghs poihsai eikona tw qhriw os exei thn plhghn ths maxairhs kai ezhsen.
rev 13:15 kai edoqh autw dounai pneuma th eikoni tou qhriou ina kai lalhsh h eikwn tou qhriou kai poihsh ina osoi ean mh proskunhswsin th eikoni tou qhriou apoktanqwsin.
rev 13:16 kai poiei pantas tous mikrous kai tous megalous kai tous plousious kai tous ptwxous kai tous eleuqerous kai tous doulous ina dwsin autois xaragma epi ths xeiros autwn ths decias h epi to metwpon autwn
rev 13:17 [--] ina mh tis dunhtai agorasai h pwlhsai ei mh o exwn to xaragma to onoma tou qhriou h ton ariqmon tou onomatos autou.
rev 13:18 wde h sofia estin o exwn noun yhfisatw ton ariqmon tou qhriou ariqmos gar anqrwpou estin kai o ariqmos autou ecakosioi echkonta ec.
rev 14:1 kai eidon kai idou [--] arnion estos epi to oros siwn kai met autou ekaton tesserakonta tessares xiliades exousai to onoma autou kai to onoma tou patros autou gegrammenon epi twn metwpwn autwn.
rev 14:2 kai hkousa fwnhn ek tou ouranou ws fwnhn udatwn pollwn kai ws fwnhn bronths megalhs kai h fwnh hn hkousa ws kiqarwdwn kiqarizontwn en tais kiqarais autwn.
rev 14:3 kai adousin [--] wdhn kainhn enwpion tou qronou kai enwpion twn tessarwn zwwn kai twn presbuterwn kai oudeis edunato maqein thn wdhn ei mh ai ekaton tesserakonta tessares xiliades oi hgorasmenoi apo ths ghs.
rev 14:4 outoi eisin oi meta gunaikwn ouk emolunqhsan parqenoi gar eisin. outoi oi akolouqountes tw arniw opou an upagh. outoi hgorasqhsan apo twn anqrwpwn aparxh tw qew kai tw arniw
rev 14:5 kai en tw stomati autwn oux eureqh yeudos amwmoi eisin.
rev 14:6 kai eidon [--] aggelon petomenon en mesouranhmati exonta euaggelion aiwnion euaggelisai epi tous kaqhmenous epi ths ghs kai epi pan eqnos kai fulhn kai glwssan kai laon
rev 14:7 legwn en fwnh megalh fobhqhte ton qeon kai dote autw docan oti hlqen h wra ths krisews autou kai proskunhsate tw poihsanti ton ouranon kai thn ghn kai qalassan kai phgas udatwn.
rev 14:8 kai allos aggelos deuteros hkolouqhsen legwn epesen epesen babulwn h megalh h ek tou oinou tou qumou ths porneias auths pepotiken panta ta eqnh.
rev 14:9 kai allos aggelos tritos hkolouqhsen autois legwn en fwnh megalh ei tis proskunei to qhrion kai thn eikona autou kai lambanei xaragma epi tou metwpou autou h epi thn xeira autou
rev 14:10 kai autos pietai ek tou oinou tou qumou tou qeou tou kekerasmenou akratou en tw pothriw ths orghs autou kai basanisqhsetai en puri kai qeiw enwpion aggelwn agiwn kai enwpion tou arniou.
rev 14:11 kai o kapnos tou basanismou autwn eis aiwnas aiwnwn anabainei kai ouk exousin anapausin hmeras kai nuktos oi proskunountes to qhrion kai thn eikona autou kai ei tis lambanei to xaragma tou onomatos autou.
rev 14:12 wde h upomonh twn agiwn estin oi thrountes tas entolas tou qeou kai thn pistin ihsou.
rev 14:13 kai hkousa fwnhs ek tou ouranou legoushs grayon makarioi oi nekroi oi en kuriw apoqnhskontes ap arti. nai legei to pneuma ina anapahsontai ek twn kopwn autwn ta gar erga autwn akolouqei met autwn.
rev 14:14 kai eidon kai idou nefelh leukh kai epi thn nefelhn kaqhmenon omoion uion anqrwpou exwn epi ths kefalhs autou stefanon xrusoun kai en th xeiri autou drepanon ocu.
rev 14:15 kai allos aggelos echlqen ek tou naou krazwn en fwnh megalh tw kaqhmenw epi ths nefelhs pemyon to drepanon sou kai qerison oti hlqen h wra qerisai oti echranqh o qerismos ths ghs.
rev 14:16 kai ebalen o kaqhmenos epi ths nefelhs to drepanon autou epi thn ghn kai eqerisqh h gh.
rev 14:17 kai allos aggelos echlqen ek tou naou tou en tw ouranw exwn kai autos drepanon ocu.
rev 14:18 kai allos aggelos echlqen ek tou qusiasthriou [--] exwn ecousian epi tou puros kai efwnhsen fwnh megalh tw exonti to drepanon to ocu legwn pemyon sou to drepanon to ocu kai trughson tous botruas ths ampelou ths ghs oti hkmasan ai stafulai auths.
rev 14:19 kai ebalen o aggelos to drepanon autou eis thn ghn kai etrughsen thn ampelon ths ghs kai ebalen eis thn lhnon tou qumou tou qeou ton megan.
rev 14:20 kai epathqh h lhnos ecwqen ths polews kai echlqen aima ek ths lhnou axri twn xalinwn twn ippwn apo stadiwn xiliwn ecakosiwn.
rev 15:1 kai eidon allo shmeion en tw ouranw mega kai qaumaston aggelous epta exontas plhgas epta tas esxatas oti en autais etelesqh o qumos tou qeou.
rev 15:2 kai eidon ws qalassan ualinhn memigmenhn puri kai tous nikwntas ek tou qhriou kai ek ths eikonos autou kai ek tou ariqmou tou onomatos autou estwtas epi thn qalassan thn ualinhn exontas kiqaras tou qeou.
rev 15:3 kai adousin thn wdhn mwusews tou doulou tou qeou kai thn wdhn tou arniou legontes megala kai qaumasta ta erga sou kurie o qeos o pantokratwr dikaiai kai alhqinai ai odoi sou o basileus twn [aiwnwn].
rev 15:4 tis ou mh fobhqh kurie kai docasei to onoma sou; oti monos osios oti panta ta eqnh hcousin kai proskunhsousin enwpion sou oti ta dikaiwmata sou efanerwqhsan.
rev 15:5 kai meta tauta eidon kai hnoigh o naos ths skhnhs tou marturiou en tw ouranw
rev 15:6 kai echlqon oi epta aggeloi oi exontes tas epta plhgas ek tou naou endedumenoi linon kaqaron lampron kai periezwsmenoi peri ta sthqh zwnas xrusas.
rev 15:7 kai en ek twn tessarwn zwwn edwken tois epta aggelois epta fialas xrusas gemousas tou qumou tou qeou tou zwntos eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn.
rev 15:8 kai egemisqh o naos kapnou ek ths dochs tou qeou kai ek ths dunamews autou kai oudeis edunato eiselqein eis ton naon axri telesqwsin ai epta plhgai twn epta aggelwn.
rev 16:1 kai hkousa megalhs fwnhs ek tou naou legoushs tois epta aggelois upagete kai ekxeete tas epta fialas tou qumou tou qeou eis thn ghn.
rev 16:2 kai aphlqen o prwtos kai ecexeen thn fialhn autou eis thn ghn kai egeneto elkos kakon kai ponhron epi tous anqrwpous tous exontas to xaragma tou qhriou kai tous proskunountas th eikoni autou.
rev 16:3 kai o deuteros ecexeen thn fialhn autou eis thn qalassan kai egeneto aima ws nekrou kai pasa yuxh zwhs apeqanen ta en th qalassh.
rev 16:4 kai o tritos ecexeen thn fialhn autou eis tous potamous kai tas phgas twn udatwn kai [egenonto] aima.
rev 16:5 kai hkousa tou aggelou twn udatwn legontos dikaios ei o wn kai o hn o osios oti tauta ekrinas
rev 16:6 oti aima agiwn kai profhtwn ecexean kai aima autois dedwkas piein acioi eisin.
rev 16:7 kai hkousa tou qusiasthriou legontos nai kurie o qeos o pantokratwr alhqinai kai dikaiai ai kriseis sou.
rev 16:8 kai o tetartos ecexeen thn fialhn autou epi ton hlion kai edoqh autw kaumatisai tous anqrwpous en puri.
rev 16:9 kai ekaumatisqhsan oi anqrwpoi kauma mega kai eblasfhmhsan to onoma tou qeou tou exontos thn ecousian epi tas plhgas tautas kai ou metenohsan dounai autw docan.
rev 16:10 kai o pemptos ecexeen thn fialhn autou epi ton qronon tou qhriou kai egeneto h basileia autou eskotwmenh kai emaswnto tas glwssas autwn ek tou ponou
rev 16:11 kai eblasfhmhsan ton qeon tou ouranou ek twn ponwn autwn kai ek twn elkwn autwn kai ou metenohsan ek twn ergwn autwn.
rev 16:12 kai o ektos ecexeen thn fialhn autou epi ton potamon ton megan ton eufrathn kai echranqh to udwr autou ina etoimasqh h odos twn basilewn twn apo anatolhs hliou.
rev 16:13 kai eidon ek tou stomatos tou drakontos kai ek tou stomatos tou qhriou kai ek tou stomatos tou yeudoprofhtou pneumata tria akaqarta ws batraxoi
rev 16:14 eisin gar pneumata daimoniwn poiounta shmeia a ekporeuetai epi tous basileis ths oikoumenhs olhs sunagagein autous eis ton polemon ths hmeras ths megalhs tou qeou tou pantokratoros.
rev 16:15 idou erxomai ws klepths. makarios o grhgorwn kai thrwn ta imatia autou ina mh gumnos peripath kai blepwsin thn asxhmosunhn autou.
rev 16:16 kai sunhgagen autous eis ton [polemon] ton kaloumenon ebraisti armagedwn.
rev 16:17 kai o ebdomos ecexeen thn fialhn autou epi ton aera kai echlqen fwnh megalh ek tou naou apo tou qronou legousa gegonen.
