rev 16:18 kai egenonto astrapai kai fwnai kai brontai kai seismos egeneto megas oios ouk egeneto af ou anqrwpos egeneto epi ths ghs thlikoutos seismos outw megas.
rev 16:19 kai egeneto h polis h megalh eis tria merh kai ai poleis twn eqnwn epesan. kai babulwn h megalh emnhsqh enwpion tou qeou dounai auth to pothrion tou oinou tou qumou ths orghs autou.
rev 16:20 kai pasa nhsos efugen kai orh oux eureqhsan.
rev 16:21 kai xalaza megalh ws talantiaia katabainei ek tou ouranou epi tous anqrwpous kai eblasfhmhsan oi anqrwpoi ton qeon ek ths plhghs ths xalazhs oti megalh estin h plhgh auths sfodra.
rev 17:1 kai hlqen eis ek twn epta aggelwn twn exontwn tas epta fialas kai elalhsen met emou legwn deuro deicw soi to krima ths pornhs ths megalhs ths kaqhmenhs epi udatwn pollwn
rev 17:2 meq hs eporneusan oi basileis ths ghs kai emequsqhsan oi katoikountes thn ghn ek tou oinou ths porneias auths.
rev 17:3 kai aphnegken me eis erhmon en pneumati. kai eidon gunaika kaqhmenhn epi qhrion kokkinon gemonta onomata blasfhmias exwn kefalas epta kai kerata deka.
rev 17:4 kai h gunh hn peribeblhmenh porfuroun kai kokkinon kai kexruswmenh xrusiw kai liqw timiw kai margaritais exousa pothrion xrusoun en th xeiri auths gemon bdelugmatwn kai ta akaqarta ths porneias auths [kai ths ghs]
rev 17:5 kai epi to metwpon auths onoma gegrammenon musthrion babulwn h megalh h mhthr twn pornwn kai twn bdelugmatwn ths ghs.
rev 17:6 kai eidon thn gunaika mequousan ek tou aimatos twn agiwn kai ek tou aimatos twn marturwn ihsou. kai eqaumasa idwn authn qauma mega.
rev 17:7 kai eipen moi o aggelos dia ti eqaumasas; egw erw soi to musthrion ths gunaikos kai tou qhriou tou bastazontos authn tou exontos tas epta kefalas kai ta deka kerata
rev 17:8 to qhrion o eides hn kai ouk estin kai mellei anabainein ek ths abussou kai eis apwleian upagei kai qaumasqhsontai oi katoikountes epi ths ghs wn ou gegraptai to onoma epi to biblion ths zwhs apo katabolhs kosmou blepontwn to qhrion oti hn kai ouk estin kai parestai.
rev 17:9 wde o nous o exwn sofian. ai epta kefalai epta orh eisin opou h gunh kaqhtai ep autwn. kai basileis epta eisin
rev 17:10 oi pente epesan o eis estin o allos oupw hlqen kai otan elqh oligon auton dei meinai.
rev 17:11 kai to qhrion o hn kai ouk estin kai autos ogdoos estin kai ek twn epta estin kai eis apwleian upagei.
rev 17:12 kai ta deka kerata a eides deka basileis eisin oitines basileian oupw elabon alla ecousian ws basileis mian wran lambanousin meta tou qhriou.
rev 17:13 outoi mian gnwmhn exousin kai thn dunamin kai ecousian autwn tw qhriw didoasin.
rev 17:14 outoi meta tou arniou polemhsousin kai to arnion nikhsei autous oti kurios kuriwn estin kai basileus basilewn kai oi met autou klhtoi kai eklektoi kai pistoi.
rev 17:15 kai legei moi ta udata a eides ou h pornh kaqhtai laoi kai oxloi eisin kai eqnh kai glwssai.
rev 17:16 kai ta deka kerata a eides kai to qhrion outoi mishsousin thn pornhn kai hrhmwmenhn poihsousin authn kai gumnhn kai tas sarkas auths fagontai kai authn katakausousin en puri
rev 17:17 o gar qeos edwken eis tas kardias autwn poihsai thn gnwmhn autou kai poihsai mian gnwmhn kai dounai thn basileian autwn tw qhriw axri telesqhsontai oi logoi tou qeou.
rev 17:18 kai h gunh hn eides estin h polis h megalh h exousa basileian epi twn basilewn ths ghs.
rev 18:1 meta tauta eidon allon aggelon katabainonta ek tou ouranou exonta ecousian megalhn kai h gh efwtisqh ek ths dochs autou.
rev 18:2 kai ekracen en isxura fwnh legwn epesen epesen babulwn h megalh kai egeneto katoikhthrion daimoniwn kai fulakh pantos pneumatos akaqartou kai fulakh pantos orneou akaqartou kai fulakh pantos qhriou akaqartou kai memishmenou
rev 18:3 oti ek tou oinou tou qumou ths porneias auths pepwkan panta ta eqnh kai oi basileis ths ghs met auths eporneusan kai oi emporoi ths ghs ek ths dunamews tou strhnous auths eplouthsan.
rev 18:4 kai hkousa allhn fwnhn ek tou ouranou legousan ecelqate o laos mou ec auths ina mh sugkoinwnhshte tais amartiais auths kai ek twn plhgwn auths ina mh labhte
rev 18:5 oti ekollhqhsan auths ai amartiai axri tou ouranou kai emnhmoneusen o qeos ta adikhmata auths.
rev 18:6 apodote auth ws kai auth apedwken kai diplwsate ta dipla kata ta erga auths en tw pothriw w ekerasen kerasate auth diploun
rev 18:7 osa edocasen authn kai estrhniasen tosouton dote auth basanismon kai penqos. oti en th kardia auths legei oti kaqhmai basilissa kai xhra ouk eimi kai penqos ou mh idw
rev 18:8 dia touto en mia hmera hcousin ai plhgai auths qanatos kai penqos kai limos kai en puri katakauqhsetai oti isxuros kurios o qeos o krinas authn.
rev 18:9 kai klausousin kai koyontai ep authn oi basileis ths ghs oi met auths porneusantes kai strhniasantes otan blepwsin ton kapnon ths purwsews auths
rev 18:10 apo makroqen esthkotes dia ton fobon tou basanismou auths legontes ouai ouai h polis h megalh babulwn h polis h isxura oti mia wra hlqen h krisis sou.
rev 18:11 kai oi emporoi ths ghs klaiousin kai penqousin ep authn oti ton gomon autwn oudeis agorazei ouketi
rev 18:12 gomon xrusou kai argurou kai liqou timiou kai margaritwn kai bussinou kai porfuras kai sirikou kai kokkinou kai pan culon quinon kai pan skeuos elefantinon kai pan skeuos ek culou timiwtatou kai xalkou kai sidhrou kai marmarou
rev 18:13 kai kinnamwmon kai amwmon kai qumiamata kai muron kai libanon kai oinon kai elaion kai semidalin kai siton kai kthnh kai probata kai ippwn kai redwn kai swmatwn kai yuxas anqrwpwn.
rev 18:14 kai h opwra sou ths epiqumias ths yuxhs aphlqen apo sou kai panta ta lipara kai ta lampra apwleto apo sou kai ouketi ou mh auta eurhsousin.
rev 18:15 oi emporoi toutwn oi plouthsantes ap auths apo makroqen sthsontai dia ton fobon tou basanismou auths klaiontes kai penqountes
rev 18:16 legontes ouai ouai h polis h megalh h peribeblhmenh bussinon kai porfuroun kai kokkinon kai kexruswmenh en xrusiw kai liqw timiw kai margarith
rev 18:17 oti mia wra hrhmwqh o tosoutos ploutos. kai pas kubernhths kai pas o epi [potamon] plewn kai nautai kai osoi thn qalassan ergazontai apo makroqen esthsan
rev 18:18 kai ekrazon blepontes ton kapnon ths purwsews auths legontes tis omoia th polei th megalh;
rev 18:19 kai ebalon xoun epi tas kefalas autwn kai ekrazon klaiontes kai penqountes legontes ouai ouai h polis h megalh en h eplouthsan pantes oi exontes ta ploia en th qalassh ek ths timiothtos auths oti mia wra hrhmwqh.
rev 18:20 eufrainou ep auth ourane kai oi agioi kai oi apostoloi kai oi profhtai oti ekrinen o qeos to krima umwn ec auths.
rev 18:21 kai hren eis aggelos isxuros liqon ws mulinon megan kai ebalen eis thn qalassan legwn outws ormhmati blhqhsetai babulwn h megalh polis kai ou mh eureqh eti.
rev 18:22 kai fwnh kiqarwdwn kai mousikwn kai aulhtwn kai salpistwn ou mh akousqh en soi eti kai pas texniths pashs texnhs ou mh eureqh en soi eti kai fwnh mulou ou mh akousqh en soi eti
rev 18:23 kai fws luxnou ou mh fanh en soi eti kai fwnh numfiou kai numfhs ou mh akousqh en soi eti oti oi emporoi sou hsan oi megistanes ths ghs oti en th farmakeia sou eplanhqhsan panta ta eqnh
rev 18:24 kai en auth aima profhtwn kai agiwn eureqh kai pantwn twn esfagmenwn epi ths ghs.
rev 19:1 meta tauta hkousa ws fwnhn megalhn oxlou pollou en tw ouranw legontwn allhlouia h swthria kai h doca kai h dunamis tou qeou hmwn
rev 19:2 oti alhqinai kai dikaiai ai kriseis autou oti ekrinen thn pornhn thn megalhn htis efqeiren thn ghn en th porneia auths kai ecedikhsen to aima twn doulwn autou ek xeiros auths.
rev 19:3 kai deuteron eirhkan allhlouia kai o kapnos auths anabainei eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn.
rev 19:4 kai epesan oi presbuteroi oi eikosi tessares kai ta tessara zwa kai prosekunhsan tw qew tw kaqhmenw epi tw qronw legontes amhn allhlouia.
rev 19:5 kai fwnh apo tou qronou echlqen legousa aineite tw qew hmwn pantes oi douloi autou [--] oi foboumenoi auton oi mikroi kai oi megaloi.
rev 19:6 kai hkousa ws fwnhn oxlou pollou kai ws fwnhn udatwn pollwn kai ws fwnhn brontwn isxurwn legontwn allhlouia oti ebasileusen kurios o qeos [hmwn] o pantokratwr.
rev 19:7 xairwmen kai agalliwmen kai dwswmen thn docan autw oti hlqen o gamos tou arniou kai h gunh autou htoimasen eauthn
rev 19:8 kai edoqh auth ina peribalhtai bussinon lampron kaqaron to gar bussinon ta dikaiwmata twn agiwn estin.
rev 19:9 kai legei moi grayon makarioi oi eis to deipnon tou gamou tou arniou keklhmenoi. kai legei moi outoi oi logoi alhqinoi tou qeou eisin.
rev 19:10 kai epesa emprosqen twn podwn autou proskunhsai autw. kai legei moi ora mh sundoulos sou eimi kai twn adelfwn sou twn exontwn thn marturian ihsou tw qew proskunhson. h gar marturia ihsou estin to pneuma ths profhteias.
rev 19:11 kai eidon ton ouranon hnewgmenon kai idou ippos leukos kai o kaqhmenos ep auton kaloumenos pistos kai alhqinos kai en dikaiosunh krinei kai polemei.
rev 19:12 oi de ofqalmoi autou ws floc puros kai epi thn kefalhn autou diadhmata polla exwn onoma gegrammenon o oudeis oiden ei mh autos
rev 19:13 kai peribeblhmenos imation bebammenon aimati kai keklhtai to onoma autou o logos tou qeou.
rev 19:14 kai ta strateumata ta en tw ouranw hkolouqei autw ef ippois leukois endedumenoi bussinon leukon kaqaron.
rev 19:15 kai ek tou stomatos autou ekporeuetai romfaia oceia ina en auth patach ta eqnh kai autos poimanei autous en rabdw sidhra kai autos patei thn lhnon tou oinou tou qumou ths orghs tou qeou tou pantokratoros.
rev 19:16 kai exei epi to imation kai epi ton mhron autou onoma gegrammenon basileus basilewn kai kurios kuriwn.
rev 19:17 kai eidon ena aggelon estwta en tw hliw kai ekracen en fwnh megalh legwn pasin tois orneois tois petomenois en mesouranhmati deute sunaxqhte eis to deipnon to mega tou qeou
rev 19:18 ina faghte sarkas basilewn kai sarkas xiliarxwn kai sarkas isxurwn kai sarkas ippwn kai twn kaqhmenwn ep autwn kai sarkas pantwn eleuqerwn te kai doulwn kai mikrwn kai megalwn.
rev 19:19 kai eidon to qhrion kai tous basileis ths ghs kai ta strateumata autwn sunhgmena poihsai ton polemon meta tou kaqhmenou epi tou ippou kai meta tou strateumatos autou.
rev 19:20 kai epiasqh to qhrion kai met autou o yeudoprofhths o poihsas ta shmeia enwpion autou en ois eplanhsen tous labontas to xaragma tou qhriou kai tous proskunountas th eikoni autou zwntes eblhqhsan oi duo eis thn limnhn tou puros ths kaiomenhs en qeiw.
rev 19:21 kai oi loipoi apektanqhsan en th romfaia tou kaqhmenou epi tou ippou th ecelqoush ek tou stomatos autou kai panta ta ornea exortasqhsan ek twn sarkwn autwn.
rev 20:1 kai eidon aggelon katabainonta ek tou ouranou exonta thn klein ths abussou kai alusin megalhn epi thn xeira autou.
rev 20:2 kai ekrathsen ton drakonta o ofis o arxaios os estin diabolos kai o satanas kai edhsen auton xilia eth
rev 20:3 kai ebalen auton eis thn abusson kai ekleisen kai esfragisen epanw autou ina mh planhsh eti ta eqnh axri telesqh ta xilia eth meta tauta dei luqhnai auton mikron xronon.
rev 20:4 kai eidon qronous kai ekaqisan ep autous kai krima edoqh autois kai tas yuxas twn pepelekismenwn dia thn marturian ihsou kai dia ton logon tou qeou kai oitines ou prosekunhsan to qhrion oude thn eikona autou kai ouk elabon to xaragma epi to metwpon kai epi thn xeira autwn kai ezhsan kai ebasileusan meta tou xristou xilia eth.
rev 20:5 oi loipoi twn nekrwn ouk ezhsan axri telesqh ta xilia eth. auth h anastasis h prwth.
rev 20:6 makarios kai agios o exwn meros en th anastasei th prwth epi toutwn o deuteros qanatos ouk exei ecousian all esontai iereis tou qeou kai tou xristou kai basileusousin met autou ta xilia eth.
rev 20:7 kai otan telesqh ta xilia eth luqhsetai o satanas ek ths fulakhs autou
rev 20:8 kai eceleusetai planhsai ta eqnh ta en tais tessarsin gwniais ths ghs ton gwg kai magwg sunagagein autous eis ton polemon wn o ariqmos autwn ws h ammos ths qalasshs.
rev 20:9 kai anebhsan epi to platos ths ghs kai ekukleusan thn parembolhn twn agiwn kai thn polin thn hgaphmenhn. kai katebh pur ek tou ouranou [apo tou qeou] kai katefagen autous
rev 20:10 kai o diabolos o planwn autous eblhqh eis thn limnhn tou puros kai qeiou opou kai to qhrion kai o yeudoprofhths kai basanisqhsontai hmeras kai nuktos eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn.
rev 20:11 kai eidon qronon megan leukon kai ton kaqhmenon ep auton ou apo tou proswpou efugen h gh kai o ouranos kai topos oux eureqh autois.
rev 20:12 kai eidon tous nekrous tous megalous kai tous mikrous estwtas enwpion tou qronou kai biblia hnoixqhsan kai allo biblion hnoixqh o estin ths zwhs kai ekriqhsan oi nekroi ek twn gegrammenwn en tois bibliois kata ta erga autwn.
rev 20:13 kai edwken h qalassa tous nekrous tous en auth kai o qanatos kai o adhs edwkan tous nekrous tous en autois kai ekriqhsan ekastos kata ta erga autwn.
rev 20:14 kai o qanatos kai o adhs eblhqhsan eis thn limnhn tou puros. outos o qanatos o deuteros estin h limnh tou puros.
rev 20:15 kai ei tis oux eureqh en th biblw ths zwhs gegrammenos eblhqh eis thn limnhn tou puros.
rev 21:1 kai eidon ouranon kainon kai ghn kainhn o gar prwtos ouranos kai h prwth gh aphlqan kai h qalassa ouk estin eti.
rev 21:2 kai thn polin thn agian ierousalhm kainhn eidon katabainousan ek tou ouranou apo tou qeou htoimasmenhn ws numfhn kekosmhmenhn tw andri auths.
rev 21:3 kai hkousa fwnhs megalhs ek tou qronou legoushs idou h skhnh tou qeou meta twn anqrwpwn kai skhnwsei met autwn kai autoi [laos] autou esontai kai autos o qeos met autwn estai [--]
rev 21:4 kai ecaleiyei pan dakruon ek twn ofqalmwn autwn kai o qanatos ouk estai eti oute penqos oute kraugh oute ponos ouk estai eti oti ta prwta aphlqan.
rev 21:5 kai eipen o kaqhmenos epi tw qronw idou kaina poiw panta. kai legei grayon oti outoi oi logoi pistoi kai alhqinoi eisin.
rev 21:6 kai eipen moi gegonan. egw eimi to alfa kai to w h arxh kai to telos. egw tw diywnti dwsw ek ths phghs tou udatos ths zwhs dwrean.
rev 21:7 o nikwn klhronomhsei tauta kai esomai autw qeos kai autos estai moi uios.
rev 21:8 tois de deilois kai apistois kai ebdelugmenois kai foneusin kai pornois kai farmakois kai eidwlolatrais kai pasin tois yeudesin to meros autwn en th limnh th kaiomenh puri kai qeiw o estin o qanatos o deuteros.
rev 21:9 kai hlqen eis ek twn epta aggelwn twn exontwn tas epta fialas twn gemontwn twn epta plhgwn twn esxatwn kai elalhsen met emou legwn deuro deicw soi thn numfhn thn gunaika tou arniou.
rev 21:10 kai aphnegken me en pneumati epi oros mega kai uyhlon kai edeicen moi thn polin thn agian ierousalhm katabainousan ek tou ouranou apo tou qeou
rev 21:11 exousan thn docan tou qeou o fwsthr auths omoios liqw timiwtatw ws liqw iaspidi krustallizonti
rev 21:12 exousa teixos mega kai uyhlon exousa pulwnas dwdeka kai epi tois pulwsin aggelous dwdeka kai onomata epigegrammena a estin ta onomata twn dwdeka fulwn uiwn israhl
rev 21:13 apo anatolhs pulwnes treis kai apo borra pulwnes treis kai apo notou pulwnes treis kai apo dusmwn pulwnes treis
rev 21:14 kai to teixos ths polews exwn qemelious dwdeka kai ep autwn dwdeka onomata twn dwdeka apostolwn tou arniou.
rev 21:15 kai o lalwn met emou eixen metron kalamon xrusoun ina metrhsh thn polin kai tous pulwnas auths kai to teixos auths.
rev 21:16 kai h polis tetragwnos keitai kai to mhkos auths oson kai to platos. kai emetrhsen thn polin tw kalamw epi stadiwn dwdeka xiliadwn to mhkos kai to platos kai to uyos auths isa estin.
rev 21:17 kai emetrhsen to teixos auths ekaton tesserakonta tessarwn phxwn metron anqrwpou o estin aggelou.
rev 21:18 kai h endwmhsis tou teixous auths iaspis kai h polis xrusion kaqaron omoion ualw kaqarw.
rev 21:19 oi qemelioi tou teixous ths polews panti liqw timiw kekosmhmenoi o qemelios o prwtos iaspis o deuteros sapfiros o tritos xalkhdwn o tetartos smaragdos
rev 21:20 o pemptos sardonuc o ektos sardion o ebdomos xrusoliqos o ogdoos bhrullos o enatos topazion o dekatos xrusoprasos o endekatos uakinqos o dwdekatos amequstos.
rev 21:21 kai oi dwdeka pulwnes dwdeka margaritai ana eis ekastos twn pulwnwn hn ec enos margaritou. kai h plateia ths polews xrusion kaqaron ws ualos diaughs.
rev 21:22 kai naon ouk eidon en auth o gar kurios o qeos o pantokratwr naos auths estin kai to arnion.
rev 21:23 kai h polis ou xreian exei tou hliou oude ths selhnhs ina fainwsin auth h gar doca tou qeou efwtisen authn kai o luxnos auths to arnion.
rev 21:24 kai peripathsousin ta eqnh dia tou fwtos auths kai oi basileis ths ghs ferousin thn docan autwn eis authn
rev 21:25 kai oi pulwnes auths ou mh kleisqwsin hmeras nuc gar ouk estai ekei
rev 21:26 kai oisousin thn docan kai thn timhn twn eqnwn eis authn.
rev 21:27 kai ou mh eiselqh eis authn pan koinon kai o poiwn bdelugma kai yeudos ei mh oi gegrammenoi en tw bibliw ths zwhs tou arniou.
rev 22:1 kai edeicen moi potamon udatos zwhs lampron ws krustallon ekporeuomenon ek tou qronou tou qeou kai tou arniou.
rev 22:2 en mesw ths plateias auths kai tou potamou enteuqen kai ekeiqen culon zwhs poioun karpous dwdeka kata mhna ekaston apodidoun ton karpon autou kai ta fulla tou culou eis qerapeian twn eqnwn.
rev 22:3 kai pan kataqema ouk estai eti. kai o qronos tou qeou kai tou arniou en auth estai kai oi douloi autou latreusousin autw
rev 22:4 kai oyontai to proswpon autou kai to onoma autou epi twn metwpwn autwn.
rev 22:5 kai nuc ouk estai eti kai ouk exousin xreian fwtos luxnou kai fwtos hliou oti kurios o qeos fwtisei ep autous kai basileusousin eis tous aiwnas twn aiwnwn.
rev 22:6 kai eipen moi outoi oi logoi pistoi kai alhqinoi kai o kurios o qeos twn pneumatwn twn profhtwn apesteilen ton aggelon autou deicai tois doulois autou a dei genesqai en taxei.
rev 22:7 kai idou erxomai taxu. makarios o thrwn tous logous ths profhteias tou bibliou toutou.
rev 22:8 kagw iwannhs o akouwn kai blepwn tauta. kai ote hkousa kai ebleya epesa proskunhsai emprosqen twn podwn tou aggelou tou deiknuontos moi tauta.
rev 22:9 kai legei moi ora mh sundoulos sou eimi kai twn adelfwn sou twn profhtwn kai twn thrountwn tous logous tou bibliou toutou tw qew proskunhson.
rev 22:10 kai legei moi mh sfragishs tous logous ths profhteias tou bibliou toutou o kairos gar eggus estin.
rev 22:11 o adikwn adikhsatw eti kai o ruparos rupanqhtw eti kai o dikaios dikaiosunhn poihsatw eti kai o agios agiasqhtw eti.
rev 22:12 idou erxomai taxu kai o misqos mou met emou apodounai ekastw ws to ergon estin autou.
rev 22:13 egw to alfa kai to w o prwtos kai o esxatos h arxh kai to telos.
rev 22:14 makarioi oi plunontes tas stolas autwn ina estai h ecousia autwn epi to culon ths zwhs kai tois pulwsin eiselqwsin eis thn polin.
rev 22:15 ecw oi kunes kai oi farmakoi kai oi pornoi kai oi foneis kai oi eidwlolatrai kai pas filwn kai poiwn yeudos.
rev 22:16 egw ihsous epemya ton aggelon mou marturhsai umin tauta epi tais ekklhsiais. egw eimi h riza kai to genos dauid o asthr o lampros o prwinos.
rev 22:17 kai to pneuma kai h numfh legousin erxou. kai o akouwn eipatw erxou. kai o diywn erxesqw o qelwn labetw udwr zwhs dwrean.
rev 22:18 marturw egw panti tw akouonti tous logous ths profhteias tou bibliou toutou ean tis epiqh ep auta epiqhsei o qeos ep auton tas plhgas tas gegrammenas en tw bibliw toutw
rev 22:19 kai ean tis afelh apo twn logwn tou bibliou ths profhteias tauths afelei o qeos to meros autou apo tou culou ths zwhs kai ek ths polews ths agias twn gegrammenwn en tw bibliw toutw.
rev 22:20 legei o marturwn tauta nai erxomai taxu. amhn erxou kurie ihsou.
rev 22:21 h xaris tou kuriou [hmwn] ihsou meta pantwn.
